### [1] [Quantization of Gravity on Null Hypersurfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07785)
*Luca Ciambelli,Marc S. Klinger*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文基于特征初值问题（Characteristic Initial Value Problem, CIVP）框架，构建了广义相对论在零超曲面（null hypersurfaces）上的算子代数量子化方案。通过分别量子化两条相交的零超曲面，并利用角部对称性（corner symmetries）将其胶合，得到了一个包含超平移、超转动和超助推的内作用的量子代数，为引力子区域（gravitational subregion）的在壳代数（on-shell algebra）提供了候选构造。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义相对论在类空超曲面上的初值问题已被ADM形式体系（ADM formalism）充分刻画，但在零超曲面（null hypersurfaces）上的柯西问题——即特征初值问题（CIVP）——研究尚不充分。CIVP描述了一对相交零超曲面上的初值问题，其核心在于两条超曲面在其共享的余二维角（codimension-two corner）处的胶合蕴含着丰富的物理内容。本文旨在为此构造一个算子代数形式的量子化方案。

Method: 首先分别对每条零超曲面进行量子化，以角部对称性（corner symmetries）为指引原则；然后在初始交截面处将两者胶合。超平移（supertranslations）不被量子化为代数保持映射，而是通过Stinespring膨胀定理（Stinespring dilation theorem）的推广形式，被量子化为量子信道（quantum channels）并纳入代数。超助推（superboosts）和超转动（superrotations）的引入在量子代数层面实现了爱因斯坦方程（Einstein's equations）所施加的引力约束。

Result: 所得代数包含完整的角部对称性（半）群的内作用，该群由超助推、超转动和超平移构成。这些对称性分别对应于面积（area）、Hájiček一次型（Hájiček one-form）以及沿两条零方向的膨胀（expansion）的量子化。在局部无焦散（local caustic-free）的有效域内，该构造为被一对零超曲面所界定的引力子区域提供了在壳代数（on-shell algebra）的候选方案。

Conclusion: 本文通过算子代数量子化方法，成功将CIVP的几何结构与量子化层面的对称性实现统一，表明角部对称性（尤其是超平移作为量子信道的处理）是连接经典引力约束与量子代数的关键桥梁。该工作为引力子区域的全量子描述提供了基础框架。

Abstract: The initial value problem for general relativity on spacelike hypersurfaces is famously captured by the ADM formalism. Less well known is the Cauchy problem for general relativity on null hypersurfaces, which goes under the name of the Characteristic Initial Value Problem (CIVP). The CIVP is formulated on a pair of intersecting null hypersurfaces, encoding rich physics in the interplay between their respective initial data, and especially the gluing of these hypersurfaces at their shared codimension-two corner. In this work, we construct an operator-algebraic quantization of the CIVP. To do so, we first quantize each null hypersurface separately, using the corner symmetries as a guiding principle, and then glue them together at the joint initial cut. The resulting algebra admits an inner action of the full corner symmetry (semi)group consisting of superboosts, superrotations, and supertranslations. These are associated, respectively, with the quantization of the area, the Hájiček one-form, and the expansion along both null directions. Supertranslations do not act as algebra preserving maps, but instead are quantized to quantum channels and included into the algebra via a generalized form of the Stinespring dilation theorem. The inclusion of superboosts and superrotations implements the gravitational constraints arising from Einstein's equations at the level of the quantum algebra. By virtue of the CIVP, in its local caustic-free domain of validity, our construction yields a candidate for the on-shell algebra of a gravitational subregion subtended by a pair of null hypersurfaces.

</details>


### [2] [Chiral Tube Algebras I: Topological Defect Lines, Twisted Modules, and Finite Gauging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07786)
*Nathan Benjamin,Ho Tat Lam,Conghuan Luo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出手性管代数（chiral tube algebras）来统一并扩展二维共形场论中的手性代数（chiral algebras）与拓扑缺陷线（TDLs）两种对称性概念。手性管代数将手性代数的作用从局部希尔伯特空间推广到由TDLs扭化的缺陷希尔伯特空间，并允许由TDLs连接的非局域手性流，从而为有限规范变换下手性代数的像提供自然描述框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性代数与拓扑缺陷线（TDLs）是二维共形场论中两种互补的对称性概念，但缺乏统一的数学框架。本文旨在引入手性管代数，将这两种对称性统一起来，并拓展其适用范围。

Method: 通过推广手性代数，构建手性管代数：一方面将手性代数的作用从局部希尔伯特空间扩展到由TDLs扭化的缺陷希尔伯特空间；另一方面允许由TDLs连接的非局域手性流，从而在缺陷希尔伯特空间之间建立映射，类似于TDLs的管代数（tube algebras）。

Result: 通过多种例子（如Kac-Moody代数、𝒲代数、超共形代数及其轨形/玻色化）展示了该框架的适用性；构造了手性管代数的不可约模，这些模与对应手性代数的扭化模同构，并用于组织局部与缺陷希尔伯特空间。

Conclusion: 手性管代数为描述有限规范变换下手性代数的像提供了自然框架。后续工作将进一步研究由分数自旋非局域手性流生成的手性管代数，这类结构在手性代数中没有对应物。

Abstract: Chiral algebras and topological defect lines (TDLs) represent two complementary notions of symmetry in 2d conformal field theories. In this paper, we introduce chiral tube algebras to unify and extend these two notions. Chiral tube algebras generalize chiral algebras in two ways. First, they extend the action of chiral algebras beyond the local Hilbert space to include defect Hilbert spaces twisted by TDLs. Second, they allow for non-local chiral currents attached by TDLs and thus can map between different defect Hilbert spaces, analogous to the tube algebras of TDLs. Since local chiral currents can become non-local after finite gauging, chiral tube algebras provide a natural framework for describing the image of chiral algebras under such gauging. We illustrate this framework through a variety of examples that generalize familiar chiral algebras, including Kac-Moody algebras, $\mathcal{W}$ algebras, superconformal algebras, and their orbifolds/bosonizations. We construct their irreducible modules, which are isomorphic to twisted modules of the corresponding chiral algebras, and use them to organize local and defect Hilbert spaces. In a subsequent paper, we will study chiral tube algebras generated by non-local chiral currents with fractional spins, which have no counterparts in chiral algebras.

</details>


### [3] [No off-diagonal quantum focusing for Rényi divergences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07799)
*Tanay Kibe,Pratik Roy*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文证明了任何满足数据处理、张量可加性和匹配经典-量子条件（matched classical-quantum conditioning）的Rényi型散度（Rényi-type divergence）都无法满足完整的聚焦猜想（quantum focusing conjecture），从而否定了Rényi聚焦猜想的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子聚焦猜想（quantum focusing conjecture）的半对角部分已被证明可由纠缠熵的强次可加性（strong subadditivity）推导，而最近对角线Rényi量子零能量条件（Rényi quantum null energy condition）的证明提出了一个开放问题：是否存在完整的Rényi聚焦表述？

Method: 通过对满足数据处理（data processing）、张量可加性（tensor additivity）和匹配经典-量子条件这三类公理的任意Rényi型散度进行理论分析，检验其是否能够满足完整的聚焦单调性条件。

Result: 论文给出了否定答案：任何满足上述三项公理的Rényi型散度都无法实现完整的Rényi聚焦表述。

Conclusion: 完整的Rényi聚焦猜想不成立，这为量子聚焦猜想的适用范围和Rényi熵在广义相对论半经典引力中的角色提供了重要约束。

Abstract: The quantum focusing conjecture is a mathematical expression of the idea that semiclassical gravity remains universally attractive. Its off-diagonal part is a monotonicity condition on the double null shape variation of relative entropy on distinct null generators, and has been argued to follow from strong subadditivity of entanglement entropy. Recent proof of a diagonal Rényi quantum null energy condition raises the question: does a full Rényi focusing statement also hold? We answer this question negatively for any Rényi-type divergence satisfying data processing, tensor additivity, and matched classical--quantum conditioning.

</details>


### [4] [Relative entropy for $λφ^4$ in the Rindler wedge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07810)
*Markus B. Fröb,Albert Much,Kyriakos Papadopoulos*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文在 λφ⁴ 相互作用的量子场论中，对 Rindler 楔形区域的真空与相干态之间的相对熵（relative entropy）进行了一阶 λ 微扰计算。通过构建相互作用的 Weyl 代数，并利用 Tomita–Takesaki 模理论（modular theory）与 Araki–Uhlmann 公式，验证了相对熵约化为经典的相互作用升力 Noether 电荷（boost Noether charge），并确认了 Bekenstein 界（Bekenstein bound）成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究相互作用量子场论中 Rindler 楔形区域的相对熵，以检验该熵是否仍能由经典 Noether 电荷描述，并验证 Bekenstein 界在微扰相互作用下的有效性。

Method: 采用微扰方法，在 λφ⁴ 理论中构建了 Rindler 楔形的相互作用的 Weyl 代数，并利用 Tomita–Takesaki 模理论与 Araki–Uhlmann 公式计算真空与相干态之间的相对熵。

Result: 在一阶 λ 微扰下，相对熵约化为经典的相互作用升力 Noether 电荷，且 Bekenstein 界成立。

Conclusion: 相互作用不破坏相对熵与经典 boost Noether 电荷之间的对应关系，且 Bekenstein 界在微扰层次上依然成立。

Abstract: We consider the relative entropy between the vacuum and a coherent state in the Rindler wedge for an interacting $λφ^4$ theory to first order in $λ$. We construct the perturbatively interacting Weyl algebra of the wedge, and employ Tomita--Takesaki modular theory and the Araki--Uhlmann formula to compute the relative entropy. We verify that the relative entropy reduces to the classical (interacting) boost Noether charge, analogously to the free theory, and that the Bekenstein bound holds.

</details>


### [5] [The Energy-Momentum-News Complex near Future Null Infinity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07872)
*Jelle Hartong,Emil Have,Vijay Nenmeli,Gerben Oling*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了三维和四维渐近平坦真空广义相对论解在未来零无穷远（future null infinity）附近的几何结构，通过构建共形Carroll流形上的渐近解，定义了边界能量-动量-新闻复形（boundary energy-momentum-news complex），并导出了其满足的Ward型恒等式，最终得到了Bondi损失方程（Bondi loss equations）的Carroll协变推广。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究渐近平坦时空在零无穷远附近的几何结构，特别是Carroll几何（Carroll geometry）在广义相对论边界理论中的作用。

Method: 采用Carroll协变的Bondi-Sachs规范（Bondi-Sachs gauge），从Einstein方程允许的最一般Carroll度量数据出发，构建渐近解；通过在未来零无穷远附近的截断面上添加边界项，对重整化作用量（renormalised action）变分，定义边界能量-动量-新闻复形。

Result: 边界能量-动量-新闻复形满足三个Ward型恒等式：两个来自边界微分同胚（boundary diffeomorphism）和Weyl规范不变性（Weyl gauge invariance），第三个来自Carroll boost（Carroll boost），存在反常（anomaly）。这些恒等式共同导出Bondi损失方程的Carroll协变推广。

Conclusion: 建立了广义相对论在渐近平坦情形下未来零无穷远处的Carroll协变边界理论，为理解引力辐射和边界对称性提供了新框架。

Abstract: We study asymptotically flat vacuum solutions of general relativity in three and four dimensions, with an emphasis on the geometric structures that emerge near null infinity. We construct asymptotic solutions to the three- and four-dimensional Einstein equations near future null infinity, which is a conformal Carroll manifold, starting from the most general Carroll metric data allowed by the Einstein equations. We use a Carroll-covariant version of Bondi--Sachs gauge, whose residual transformations act on the boundary Carroll geometry and shear as boundary diffeomorphisms, Weyl transformations and Carroll boosts. We then define a boundary energy-momentum-news complex at future null infinity by varying a suitably renormalised action with respect to the boundary Carroll metric data and shear. This involves adding boundary terms to the Einstein--Hilbert action on a cut-off surface near future null infinity. The boundary energy-momentum-news complex obeys two relations due to the boundary diffeomorphism and Weyl gauge invariance of the renormalised action. A third relation, due to the Carroll boost, is anomalous, and the corresponding anomaly is obtained from the variation of the renormalised action. Together, these Ward-type identities obeyed by the boundary energy-momentum-news complex lead to a Carroll-covariant generalisation of the Bondi loss equations.

</details>


### [6] [2-Group global symmetry in the compactified M2-brane](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07924)
*F. Caro-Pérez,M. P Garcia del Moral,A. Restuccia*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究带有非平凡四形式通量的十一维背景中玻色M2膜（bosonic M2-brane）的广义全局对称性（generalized global symmetries），发现膜的单极（monopole）与缠绕（winding）对称性扇区在包含Wess-Zumino耦合后并非简单直积，而是结合成一个非平凡的2-群全局对称（2-group global symmetry），并通过量化的靶空间通量（quantized target space flux）确定相应的Postnikov类（Postnikov class）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高维膜理论中的全局对称性结构是理解M-理论（M-theory）非微扰效应的重要途径。本文旨在揭示在带有非平凡四形式通量的背景中，M2膜的单极与缠绕对称性如何因Wess-Zumino耦合而发生非平凡组合，从而探究高群对称性（higher-group symmetry）在世界体积理论（worldvolume theory）中的具体实现。

Method: 研究聚焦于$AdS_5\times S^2_{1} \times S^2_{2}\times T^2$形式的紧化（compactification）背景。通过分析包含Wess-Zumino耦合的M2膜作用量，考察单极与缠绕对称性扇区之间的代数结构，识别混合背景-规范结构（mixed background-gauge structure），并利用靶空间通量的量子化条件确定关联的Postnikov类。

Result: 结果表明，在包含Wess-Zumino耦合后，M2膜的单极与缠绕对称性并非以普通直积形式存在，而是构成一个非平凡的2-群全局对称性。该2-群结构关联的Postnikov类由量化的靶空间四形式通量唯一确定。

Conclusion: 该工作为高群对称性（higher-group symmetry）在M2膜世界体积理论中的存在提供了具体例证，表明靶空间通量量子化会诱导世界体积上的通量量子化（flux quantization），并将M2膜的全局对称性结构与M-理论中量子化通量的引入联系起来。

Abstract: We study generalized global symmetries of the bosonic M2-brane in eleven-dimensional backgrounds with non-trivial four-form flux. Focusing on compactifications of the form $AdS_5\times S^2_{1} \times S^2_{2}\times T^2$, we show that the monopole and winding symmetry sectors of the membrane do not organize as an ordinary direct product once the Wess--Zumino coupling is included. Instead, they combine into a non-trivial 2-group global symmetry. We identify the corresponding mixed background-gauge structure and show that the quantized target space flux determines the associated Postnikov class. This provides a concrete realization of higher-group symmetry in the worldvolume theory of the M2-brane induces a flux quantization on the worldvolume and relates its global symmetry structure to the introduction of a quantized flux in M-theory.

</details>


### [7] [Scalar Charges in a Self-Dual Background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07938)
*Seth Grable,Jamison Barcelona*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在常自对偶磁场背景下精确求解了3+1维标量QED模型的配分函数、β函数和传播子，首次给出了物质场传播子在自对偶背景下的闭式有限解析表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究带电粒子在平行电磁场中的行为，为3+1维手征磁效应（chiral magnetic effect）和脉冲星物理（pulsar physics）提供可精确求解的玩具模型。

Method: 采用常自对偶磁场（constant self-dual magnetic field）构型，全程工作在朗道能级基（Landau level basis）下，对配分函数、β函数和传播子进行精确闭式解析计算。

Result: 首次得到了自对偶背景下物质场传播子的闭式有限解析表达式；给出了配分函数和β函数的精确闭式结果。

Conclusion: 该标量QED模型可作为带电粒子在平行电磁场中的玩具模型，并可自然扩展至手征磁效应和脉冲星物理等研究领域。

Abstract: In this work, we present a \(3+1d\) scalar QED model in a constant self-dual magnetic field configuration. We provide exact closed form analytic calculations of the partition function, the \(β\)-function, and the propagators. To our knowledge, we present the first closed-form finite expression for the matter field propagators in a self-dual background, which is made accessible by working entirely in the Landau level basis. This theory serves as a toy model for charged particles in parallel electric and magnetic fields, with natural extensions to studies of \(3+1d\) chiral magnetic effects and pulsar physics.

</details>


### [8] [More on Majorana fields, modular localization and near saturation of the Tsirelson bound](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07949)
*J. G. A. Caribé,J. R. A. Quispe,S. P. Sorella*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 利用1+1维自由无质量马约拉纳场（Majorana field）研究量子场论（Quantum Field Theory）中的Bell-CHSH不等式，通过模楔局域化（modular wedge localization）方法展示了Tsirelson界（Tsirelson bound）的近饱和。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子场论中Bell-CHSH不等式的行为，特别关注其与Tsirelson界的关系。

Method: 采用1+1维自由无质量马约拉纳场作为研究模型，运用模楔局域化方法进行分析。

Result: 通过模楔局域化方法，展示了Tsirelson界可以被近饱和。

Conclusion: 在量子场论框架下，Bell-CHSH不等式能够接近Tsirelson界，表明该模型具有较强的非经典关联。

Abstract: The free massless Majorana field in 1+1 dimensions is employed to study the Bell-CHSH inequality in Quantum Field Theory. Use of the modular wedge localization enables us to show the near saturation of the Tsirelson bound.

</details>


### [9] [Ghosts Hunting in the Yang-Mills Vacuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07954)
*Seth Grable*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在3+1维中分析了一圈半经典杨-米尔斯理论（one-loop semi-classical Yang-Mills theory）的零模（zero-modes），发现零模由背景场的规范冗余（gauge redundancy）生成。通过引入玻色子鬼项（bosonic ghost term）和zeta函数正则化（zeta-function regularization）进行规范固定，得到了闭合形式的一圈有效理论，并再现了著名的一圈杨-米尔斯β函数（beta-function）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在杨-米尔斯理论的一圈半经典计算中，零模的出现会导致红外发散或路径积分定义上的困难，因此需要系统分析零模的起源并建立规范的有限计算方法。

Method: 采用规范固定（gauge fixing）方法，引入玻色子鬼项处理规范冗余；使用zeta函数正则化处理发散；在3+1维时空中进行一圈半经典杨-米尔斯理论的计算，并得到闭合形式的有效作用量。

Result: 发现零模源自背景场的规范冗余；通过规范固定和正则化后，得到了一组有限的一圈有效理论表达式，并以闭合形式呈现。

Conclusion: 该闭合形式的一圈有效理论正确再现了标准的一圈杨-米尔斯β函数，验证了所采用的正则化和规范固定方法的自洽性，并为半经典杨-米尔斯理论的计算提供了可行的有限方案。

Abstract: In this work I analyze the zero-modes of a one-loop semi-classical Yang-Mills theory in \(3+1d\). I find the zero-modes are generated by gauge redundancy of the background field. With proper gauge fixing, via the introduction of a bosonic ghost term, and the use of zeta-function regularization, a finite one-loop effective theory is calculated in closed form, reproducing the well known one-loop Yang-Mills beta-function.

</details>

### [11] [Gauge-Invariant Off-Shell Mass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08426)
*Kang-Sin Choi,Hyeseon Im*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在量子场论中定义了一种规范不变且重整化的离壳质量函数。通过将“捏合技术”（pinch technique）推广到任意长费米子线，构造了规范不变且与过程无关的自能和顶点函数，从而得出在壳重整化后与物理质量一致、且与Schwinger-Dyson方程及格点计算可比的质量函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的离壳自能（self-energy）依赖于规范选择，这导致质量函数在离壳情形下缺乏规范不变性，难以与Schwinger-Dyson方程和格点计算直接比较。因此，需要构建一种规范不变且与过程无关的离壳质量函数。

Method: 将捏合技术（pinch technique）从单条费米子线推广到任意长度的费米子线；利用在每个顶点局域作用的Ward-Takahashi恒等式（Ward-Takahashi identity）精确抵消规范依赖部分，从而得到Feynman规范下的自能。

Result: 在壳重整化（on-shell renormalization）后，得到的质量函数是规范不变、方案无关的，且在极点处等于物理质量；该自能还产生一个红外有限的标量质量函数，可直接与Schwinger-Dyson方程和格点（lattice）计算结果比较；该抵消在内部费米子线上是局域的，且完全在离壳情形下成立。

Conclusion: 所构造的规范不变自能在具有任意多个外部光子的振幅的每个内部分支上都有良好定义；通过计算最小离壳Compton振幅（minimal off-shell Compton amplitude）对此进行了明确验证。

Abstract: We define a gauge-invariant and renormalized off-shell mass function in quantum field theory. The conventional self-energy is gauge-dependent off-shell. We generalize the self-energy, together with the corresponding vertex function, to be gauge-invariant and process-independent. To do this, we extend the pinch technique to an arbitrarily long fermion line. The Ward-Takahashi identity acting locally at each vertex cancels the gauge-dependent piece exactly, leaving the Feynman-gauge self-energy. On-shell renormalization then yields a mass function that is gauge-invariant, scheme-independent and equal to the physical mass at the pole; the same self-energy also yields an infrared-finite scalar mass function directly comparable with Schwinger-Dyson and lattice determinations. The cancellation is local to the internal fermion line and holds entirely off-shell, so the self-energy is well-defined on each internal segment of an amplitude with arbitrarily many external photons; we demonstrate this explicitly by computing the minimal off-shell Compton amplitude.

</details>


### [12] [Gram--Wishart--Stiefel formulation of the $N=2$, large--$d$ gauge theory in 1D](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08481)

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了 BFSS/BMN 矩阵量子力学晶格模型中大 d 平面端点理论的 Gram/Wishart/Stiefel 表述，将端点自由度重组为二阶 Wishart 特征值与相对 Stiefel 角变量，并通过精确的 O(2) 角积分与 Bessel 核结构分析了大 R 对齐渐近行为，揭示了有限截断带来的大 d 微扰性界限是人为假象，最终恢复了具有物理移位质量的 Wishart 鞍点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用 Gram/Wishart/Stiefel 表述将端点自由度重组为 Wishart 特征值与 Stiefel 角变量；将 holonomy 势的线性项 −A 吸收进高斯部分，引入移位质量参数 (α_Λ)eff = α_Λ − 1/2；通过精确 O(2) 角积分得到二阶 Bessel 核结构；从精确可解的纯 −A 理论提取 Bessel/HCIZ 结构，并应用于横向 B 型展开及其非多项式玩具完整化。

Result: 有限多项式截断会产生一个与大 d 连续极限不相容的微扰性界限，但该界限是截断人为假象；通过对局部横向完整化求和并平衡补偿性的 +A 项，恢复了具有物理移位质量的 Wishart 鞍点；所得连续行为复现了 D_Λ 通道的普适 −2d 贡献，而各向异性的 β_Λ 通道则超出纯横向 B 型描述的适用范围。

Conclusion: Gram/Wishart/Stiefel 表述为分析矩阵量子力学端点理论提供了有效框架，能够正确处理 holonomy 势的大 R 渐近行为，排除截断假象，并区分普适与各向异性通道的贡献。

Abstract: We develop in this paper the Gram/Wishart/Stiefel formulation of the \(N=2\), large--\(d\) planar endpoint theory of the BFSS/BMN matrix quantum mechanics on the lattice, obtained in our previous work. In this formulation, the endpoint degrees of freedom are reorganized into rank--two Wishart eigenvalues and relative Stiefel angular variables. This allows the holonomy invariants \(A\), \(B\), and \(R^2=A^2+B^2\) to be analyzed directly in terms of radial and angular Gram data.
  A central point is the large-\(R\) aligned asymptotics of the holonomy potential. Its universal linear contribution \(-A\) is absorbed into the Gaussian sector, producing the shifted mass parameter
  \((α_Λ)_{\rm eff}=α_Λ-1/2\). In the Gram/Wishart/Stiefel variables, the exact \(O(2)\) angular integral encodes this shifted sector in a rank--two Bessel kernel. The pure \(-A\) theory, which is exactly solvable in Cartesian variables, then fixes the leading Bessel/HCIZ structure: its exponential part selects the aligned configuration, while its prefactor removes the spurious doubled Wishart entropy.
  We then apply this structure to the transverse \(B\)-type expansion and its non-polynomial toy completion. Finite polynomial truncations lead to an apparent large--\(d\) perturbativity bound incompatible with the continuum limit, but this bound is shown to be an artifact of truncation. After summing the local transverse completion and balancing the compensating \(+A\) term, the Wishart saddle is recovered with the physical shifted mass. The resulting continuum behavior reproduces the universal \(-2d\) contribution of the \(D_Λ\)-channel, while the genuinely anisotropic \(β_Λ\)-channel lies outside the scope of a pure transverse \(B\)-type description.

### [13] [Quantum corrections to the near-extremal thermodynamics of (warped) BTZ black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08482)
*Emilie Despontin,Stéphane Detournay,Robinson Mancilla,Chiara Toldo*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用三维拓扑 massive 引力（含有引力 Chern-Simons 项的高阶导数理论），结合 Newman-Penrose 形式（Newman-Penrose formulation）进行分析。对 BTZ 黑洞，将近视界（near-horizon）计算结果与全几何（full-geometry）本征值问题进行对比；随后将相同策略推广到扭曲 BTZ 黑洞。

Result: 对于 BTZ 黑洞，识别了 Schwarzian 模和转动模在低温下的提升机制；发现转动模对 BTZ 和扭曲 BTZ 黑洞的近极端处理均不可或缺，其取舍取决于边界条件。

Conclusion: 转动模在近极端黑洞热力学中具有本质重要性，不能在不指定边界条件的前提下被随意丢弃。该结论同时适用于 BTZ 和扭曲 BTZ 黑洞。

Abstract: We study one-loop effects in the near-extremal thermodynamics of BTZ and warped BTZ black holes, with particular emphasis on the fate of eigenmodes that become zero modes in the extremal throat. Our analysis is formulated in three-dimensional Topologically Massive Gravity, a higher derivative theory characterized by the presence of a gravitational Chern--Simons term, and it makes use of the Newman--Penrose formulation. For BTZ, we compare the near-horizon computation with the full-geometry eigenvalue problem and identify how the Schwarzian and rotational sectors are lifted at small temperature. We then extend the same strategy to warped BTZ. We find that rotational modes are essential for a consistent near-extremal treatment of both BTZ and warped BTZ black holes, and cannot be discarded without first specifying the boundary conditions.

### [14] [The Remnant of an Evaporating Rotating Regular Black Hole from the Generalized Entropy in the Final Stage of Evaporation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08661)
*Shingo Takeuchi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文基于广义熵（generalized entropy）的非负性假设，通过将蒸发中的旋转规则黑洞（rotating regular black hole）质量写为极极限质量与参数α之和，确定了修正项消失时α的下界（记为α₁），从而表明黑洞质量不能小于m_ext+α₁，这被解释为黑洞蒸发末期残骸（remnant）的出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究蒸发末期旋转规则黑洞的霍金辐射（Hawking radiation）广义熵的结构，旨在探讨黑洞蒸发最终阶段的物理行为，特别是残骸能否自然出现。

Method: 将黑洞质量表示为m_ext+α，基于广义熵非负且面积项与修正项在整个蒸发过程中符号不变的假设，令修正项为零以确定α的下界α₁，进而推得黑洞质量下限。

Result: 修正项消失时对应的α是有限的有限值α₁，表明黑洞质量存在下限m_ext+α₁，即蒸发末期会形成残骸。

Conclusion: 旋转规则黑洞在蒸发末期会自然产生残骸，中心区域精细结构（fine structure）在末期变得重要，从普遍性角度考虑旋转黑洞是必要的。

Abstract: We express the generalized entropy (GE) of the Hawking radiation in the final stage of an evaporating rotating regular black hole (BH) by writing the mass of the BH as $m_{\rm ext}+α$, where $m_{\rm ext}$ represents the mass at the extremal limit and $α$ is a parameter. Generally, entropy is non-negative. Based on this fact, we assume that, in the GE considered in this study, the signs of the contributions from the area term and the correction term remain unchanged throughout the entire evaporation process of the BH. Therefore, we regard $α$ at which the correction term vanishes as its lower bound and determine it. As a result, we find that such a value of $α$ is finite. Denoting this value by $α_1$, this result indicates that the mass of the BH cannot become smaller than $m_{\rm ext}+α_1$, which can be interpreted as the emergence of a remnant at the final stage of BH evaporation. The BH considered in this study is a rotating regular BH. The regularization is motivated by the fact that the fine structure of the central region becomes relevant in the final stage of evaporation. A rotating BH is considered from the viewpoint of generality.

### [15] [Entanglement Wedge Reconstruction without Holographic Quantum Error Correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08684)
*Seiji Terashima*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文论证了纠缠楔重建（entanglement wedge reconstruction）应与非全息量子纠错解释（holographic quantum error correction interpretation）分离；在有限N的全息CFT中，不存在跨边界区域的共享逻辑算符（shared logical operator），只有各边界区域各自独立的子区域互补性（subregion complementarity）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 体态重建（bulk reconstruction）是AdS/CFT对偶中的核心问题，而纠缠楔重建是其子区域版本。作者试图厘清该子区域宣称与更强的全息量子纠错解释之间的关系，并指出后者在有限N全息CFT中并不成立。

Method: 采用简单的局域性论证（locality argument），证明若存在跨区域共有的逻辑体态算符（logical bulk operator），则该算符必须与互补区域中保码的局域代数（code-preserving local algebras）对易。该机制在HaPPY型张量网络码中得以实现，但作者将此与普通有限N全息CFT进行对比分析。

Result: 在有限N全息CFT中，低能局域可观测量（如适当涂抹的应力张量）能够探测普通体态算符的物理支撑（physical support）和引力穿着（gravitational dressing），因此不存在受保护的不可见扇区（protected invisible sector）。全局和子区域HKLL公式在N→∞时的等价性仅是一个自由场论陈述（free-theory statement）。

Conclusion: 纠缠楔重建不应等同于全息量子纠错；正确的图景是子区域互补性（subregion complementarity）——每个边界区域拥有自身保码的低能代数和区域适配的体态解释，而非一个共享的逻辑算符。

Abstract: Bulk reconstruction is a central problem in AdS/CFT, and entanglement wedge reconstruction is its subregion version. We argue that this subregion statement should be separated from the stronger holographic quantum error correction interpretation, in which one region-independent logical bulk operator has code-preserving representatives in several boundary regions. A simple locality argument shows that such a common reconstruction must commute with the code-preserving local algebras in the complementary regions. This is the mechanism realized in HaPPY-type codes: the erased regions are blind to a protected logical algebra. An ordinary finite $N$ holographic CFT does not have such a protected invisible sector for supergravity fields. Its low-energy local observables, in particular, suitably smeared stress tensors, detect the physical support and gravitational dressing of ordinary bulk operators, up to possible center or superselection data. Thus, there is no such holographic quantum error correction and the $N=\infty$ agreement of global and subregion HKLL formulae is a free-theory statement. What remains is entanglement wedge reconstruction without holographic quantum error correction, or subregion complementarity: each boundary region has its own code-preserving low-energy algebra and its own region-adapted bulk interpretation, rather than a shared logical operator.

</details>


### [16] [The mini-Page Curve in Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08737)
*Ricardo Espíndola,Shoichiro Miyashita*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过二维流形几何和Type II∞因子代数构造，研究de Sitter视界中霍金对携带信息的时机，发现信息在τ≈β/8时刻开始逃逸，且代数熵与纠缠楔广义熵一致，信息被静态片观测者获取的标度为scrambling时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞信息悖论（black hole information paradox）推动了对信息从蒸发黑洞中逃逸问题的广泛研究，本文旨在将类似问题拓展到宇宙学视界（cosmological horizon），探讨单个霍金对（Hawking pair）何时开始从de Sitter视界携带信息离开。

Method: 研究在一类二维流形（flow geometries）中进行，该流形在渐近AdS2边界与dS2静态片（static patch）之间平滑插值。通过由局域算符（local operators）及其模共轭（modular conjugates）构造的探针态（probe state）模拟霍金对的发射，采用交叉积构造（crossed-product construction）将可观测量的人马座代数（centaur algebra）提升为Type II∞因子。进而计算热场双态（thermofield-double reference state）与霍金对态之间的熵差。

Result: 熵差在宇宙学视界上呈现特征性的mini-Page曲线：初始接近零，在τ≈β/8附近达到最小值后再度上升。该最小值的时刻被解释为量子信息开始逃离宇宙学视界的时间。微正则系综（microcanonical ensemble）分析表明，代数熵（algebraic entropy）与追踪沿视界辐射粒子的纠缠楔切口（entanglement wedge cut）的广义熵（generalized entropy）一致。两态间生成的相对模流（relative modular flow）给出李雅普诺夫指数（Lyapunov exponent）λ=2π/β，将scrambling时间标定为信息对静态片观测者变得可获取的标度。

Conclusion: de Sitter视界中的信息逃逸并非瞬时发生，而是在τ≈β/8时刻才开始，且该过程与纠缠楔结构及量子混沌（quantum chaos）的scrambling时间尺度密切相关。代数熵方法与广义熵在微正则系综下一致，表明该代数框架能够有效刻画宇宙学视界的信息动力学。

Abstract: The black hole information paradox has motivated extensive study of how and when information escapes from evaporating black holes. Here we address the analogous question for cosmological horizons: when does an individual Hawking pair begin to carry information out of a de Sitter horizon? We study this problem in a class of two-dimensional flow geometries that interpolate smoothly between an asymptotic AdS$ _2 $ boundary and a dS$ _2 $ static patch. Modeling the emission of a Hawking pair via a probe state constructed from local operators and their modular conjugates, we promote the centaur algebra of observables to a Type II$ _\infty $ factor through the crossed-product construction. This allows us to compute the entropy difference between the thermofield-double reference state and the Hawking-pair state. We find that this difference traces a characteristic mini-Page curve for the cosmological horizon: it starts near zero, reaches a minimum near $ τ\approx β/8 $ before increasing again. We interpret the location of the minimum as the time at which quantum information begins to escape the cosmological horizon. Extending the analysis to the microcanonical ensemble, we show that the algebraic entropy coincides with the generalized entropy of an entanglement wedge cut that tracks the emitted particle along the horizon. Furthermore, the relative modular flow generated between the two states yields a Lyapunov exponent $λ=2π/β$, identifying the scrambling time as the scale at which the information carried by the pair becomes accessible to a static-patch observer.

</details>


### [17] [Decoupling Limit of Quiver Theories and the Angular Spectra of Extreme C-metrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08747)
*Peng Yang,Kilar Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了极端带电C-度规的角特征值问题。在极端极限下，控制微分方程从具有五个正则奇点的Fuchs型方程退化为汇合扩展Heun方程。通过构造对偶四维$\mathcal{N}=2$线性箭形规范理论中的解耦极限，推导出参数词典和重整化Matone关系，并利用瞬子计数方法建立代数量子化条件，得到与数值结果一致的角特征值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极端带电C-度规的角特征值问题在极端极限下涉及奇点融合（singularity fusion），导致方程结构退化，传统解析方法难以处理。本文旨在通过规范理论中的瞬子计数方法，为这一退化问题的角谱提供解析求解方案。

Method: 首先识别在极端极限（$Q \to M$）下角方程从Fuchs型方程退化为汇合扩展Heun方程（Confluent Extended Heun Equation）。然后在对偶四维$\mathcal{N}=2$线性箭形规范理论中构造解耦极限，导出参数词典和重整化Matone关系以吸收奇点融合引起的宏观留数偏移。最后基于角方程的正则边界条件，采用瞬子计数方法（instanton counting method）建立代数量子化条件。

Result: 成功建立了一套代数量子化条件，由此计算得到的角特征值与数值结果一致，验证了该解析方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 规范理论中的瞬子计数方法可以有效解决极端带电C-度规在极端极限下由奇点融合引起的角特征值问题，扩展了该类退化方程的解析求解途径。

Abstract: We investigate the angular eigenvalue problem of the extreme charged C-metric. In the extreme limit ($Q \to M$), the governing differential equation degenerates from a Fuchsian equation with five regular singular points into a Confluent Extended Heun Equation. To evaluate the angular spectrum analytically, we formulate a decoupling limit within the dual four-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=2$, $\mathrm{SU(2)}\times \mathrm{SU(2)}$ linear quiver gauge theory. Within this framework, we derive the parameter dictionary and renormalized Matone relations, which absorb the macroscopic residue shifts induced by the singularity fusion. Based on the regular boundary conditions of the angular equation, we utilize the instanton counting method to establish an algebraic quantization condition, yielding angular eigenvalues consistent with numerical results.

</details>


### [18] [Phase-dependent kink collisions and dual critical-velocity branches in the complex sine-Gordon model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08752)
*Mohammad Mohammadi,Farnaz Eizadbaksh,Vahideh Bagheri*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟研究复正弦-戈登（complex sine-Gordon）模型中带有内部相位自由度的孤立波碰撞动力学，发现初始速度和相对相位共同决定了散射、捕获、长寿命双孤子束缚态（bion）等多种最终状态，揭示了临界速度的双分支结构与相位控制机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复正弦-戈登（complex sine-Gordon, CSG）模型因其内部相位自由度而显著改变了孤波（solitary-wave）解的动力学行为，但该内部自由度对碰撞过程的系统性影响尚未被充分理解，特别是初始速度与相对相位如何联合决定最终状态。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，对复正弦-戈登模型中的复扭结（complex kink）对撞过程进行系统研究，通过改变初始速度和相对相位来观测碰撞结果，并计算辐射轮廓（radiative profiles）携带的能量、能量密度极值、动能与梯度贡献以及碰撞中心的场模量（field modulus）。

Result: CSG模型的碰撞表现出散射、捕获、长寿命双孤子束缚态（bion formation）、呼吸子态（breather-like states）及辐射发射等多种非弹性行为。临界速度存在两个不同的相依赖分支，其中一个分支中初始速度增加促进捕获，另一个分支则恢复散射。相关物理量在临界点处呈现尖锐转变。

Conclusion: 相对相位作为有效的内部自由度，在复杂孤立子的碰撞动力学中起着关键调控作用，这与实正弦-戈登模型的弹性碰撞形成鲜明对比。

Abstract: The complex sine-Gordon (CSG) model contains an internal phase degree of freedom that strongly modifies the dynamics of its solitary-wave solutions. We present a numerical study of complex kink--kink collisions and determine how the final state depends jointly on the initial velocity and relative phase. In contrast with the elastic collisions of the real sine-Gordon model, the CSG system exhibits scattering, capture, long-lived bion formation, breather-like states, and emission of radiative profiles. The simulations reveal two distinct phase-dependent branches of critical velocity. In one branch, increasing the initial velocity promotes capture, whereas in the other it restores scattering. This dual structure highlights the rich velocity--phase dependence of the collision dynamics. We also compute the energy carried by radiative profiles and examine extreme values of the energy density, kinetic and gradient contributions, and field modulus at the collision center. These quantities show sharp transitions at critical points and provide sensitive diagnostics of phase-controlled dynamics. These results suggest that the relative phase behaves as an effective internal degree of freedom that plays an important role in the collision dynamics of complex solitons.

### [19] [A Novel Hadronic Calorimeter With A Direct Neutron Readout](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08587)
*I. Giomataris,F. Jeanneau,T. Papaevangelou,G. Tsiledakis,M. Vandenbroucke*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文通过Geant4蒙特卡洛模拟，研究了一种基于铅吸收体与钆负载液体闪烁体交替层的中子灵敏采样量热器。结果显示，延迟沉积能量与中子俘获多重性近乎完美正比，且利用延迟中子信号与瞬发量热响应之间的关联进行逐事件非线性修正，可将瞬发能量分辨率从21.8%提升至13.3%，证明钆负载采样量热器具有恢复不可见强子能量并显著改善强子能量重建与能量分辨率的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统强子量热器（hadronic calorimeter）难以直接探测强子簇射（hadronic shower）中的中子组分，导致“不可见能量”（invisible energy）损失显著影响能量分辨率。该研究旨在通过引入中子灵敏的钆负载液体闪烁体（gadolinium-loaded liquid scintillator），捕获中子慢化与俘获产生的延迟信号，从而直接获取中子信息并改善强子能量重建。

Method: 采用Geant4蒙特卡洛模拟，构建基于铅（Pb）吸收体与钆负载LAB液体闪烁体（LAB-Gd）交替层的中子灵敏采样量热器（sampling calorimeter）。将六层Pb/LAB-Gd量热器暴露于10 GeV质子束中，通过分析瞬发量热信号（prompt calorimetric signal）与中子慢化和俘获产生的延迟能量（delayed energy），表征中子响应并评估其对量热性能的影响。

Result: 延迟沉积能量与中子俘获多重性（neutron-capture multiplicity）几乎完美正比，可直接校准中子灵敏信号。逐事件分析显示瞬发量热响应与延迟中子可观测量之间存在清晰关联，后者包含大量不可见强子能量信息。利用非线性逐事件修正，瞬发能量分辨率从21.8%提升至13.3%（无需剔除事件）。此外，中子产生涨落（neutron-production fluctuations）是整体强子能量分辨率的主要贡献因素。

Conclusion: 钆负载采样量热器能够恢复部分不可见强子能量，显著提升强子能量重建精度与能量分辨率。该方案为改善强子量热器性能提供了新的技术途径。

Abstract: A neutron-sensitive sampling calorimeter based on alternating lead absorber and gadolinium-loaded liquid scintillator layers is investigated using detailed Geant4 Monte Carlo simulations. In addition to the conventional prompt calorimetric signal, the proposed detector records delayed energy from neutron moderation and capture, providing direct information on the neutron component of hadronic showers. A six-layer Pb/LAB-Gd calorimeter exposed to 10~GeV protons is studied to characterize its neutron response and evaluate its impact on calorimetric performance. The delayed deposited energy is found to be almost perfectly proportional to the neutron-capture multiplicity, providing a direct calibration of the neutron-sensitive signal. Event-by-event analyses further reveal a clear relationship between the prompt calorimetric response and the delayed neutron observable, demonstrating that the latter contains substantial information on the invisible hadronic energy. Exploiting this correlation through a simple nonlinear event-by-event correction improves the prompt-energy resolution from 21.8% to 13.3% without rejecting events. Furthermore, the analysis of events with similar neutron multiplicities indicates that neutron-production fluctuations constitute a major contribution to the overall hadronic energy resolution. These results demonstrate the potential of gadolinium-loaded sampling calorimeters to recover part of the invisible hadronic energy and significantly improve hadronic energy reconstruction and energy resolution.

</details>

Result: 通过对理论预言与电子散射实验数据的对比，凸显了不同模型之间的差异，并评估了多种核效应的影响。这些教学材料已被纳入塞维利亚大学参与的核物理校际硕士与伊拉斯谟世界联合硕士项目的相关课程。

Conclusion: 该笔记作为传统散射理论与量子场论教材的补充，旨在帮助研究生掌握相对论框架下轻子-核子与轻子-原子核散射建模的关键知识，并理解不同模型及核效应在解释实验数据中的作用。

Abstract: In these notes, basic concepts and necessary formulas for the modeling of elastic lepton-nucleon and quasielastic lepton-nucleus scattering using relativistic models are discussed. Certain theoretical developments are presented in meticulous detail, particularly those rarely found in papers or standard textbooks. In order to highlight the discrepancies between models and evaluate the impact of various nuclear effects, theoretical predictions are compared with inclusive electron scattering data.
  These notes are designed for Master's or PhD students embarking on their research in the field of neutrino-nucleus interactions at intermediate energies (ranging from several hundred MeV to a few GeV). They are intended to serve as a supplemental guide, never as a substitute for traditional textbooks on Scattering Theory and Quantum Field Theory. Currently, these notes are included in the course `Relativistic Quantum Theory: Nuclear Processes', which is integrated into both the Interuniversity Master in Nuclear Physics (https://master.us.es/fisicanuclear/index.php/) and the Erasmus Mundus Joint Master Degree in Nuclear Physics (https://www.emm-nucphys.eu/en), with the University of Seville as one of the partner institutions. Previously, this material was part of the course `Weak Interactions', within the same Master's programs.

### [21] [Deuterium-Proton Fusion in an Effective Field Theory Constructed from On-Shell Amplitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05514)
*Tim M. P. Tait*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文利用有效场论（EFT）结合现代on-shell振幅方法，对质子-氘核辐射俘获反应 d(p,γ)³He 进行建模，通过全局贝叶斯拟合给出 S(0) = 0.209 ± 0.008 eV b，并解释其与从头算基准（ab initio benchmark）偏差的来源为单个自然大小的次领头阶接触项。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大爆炸核合成（BBN）对原始氘丰度的预测精度受到氘燃烧核反应的制约，其中质子-氘核辐射俘获反应 d(p,γ)³He 的精确LUNA实验数据低于从头算基准（ab initio benchmark），而BBN反应网络在采用哪一数据上存在分歧，因此需要系统的方法来解析这一偏差。

Method: 发展了一种基于原子核有限尺度展开的有效场论（effective field theory, EFT），利用现代 on-shell 振幅方法（on-shell methods）列举所有与对称性一致的树图结构，无需显式拉格朗日量（Lagrangian）。结合核理论先验，对俘获数据进行了全局贝叶斯拟合（global Bayesian fit）。

Result: 全局贝叶斯拟合得到 S(0) = 0.209 ± 0.008 eV b，并将与从头算基准的偏移追溯至单个自然大小的次领头阶接触项（t_E1 ≈ -0.15，即电偶极振幅的分数偏移），等效于3He有效渐近归一化（asymptotic normalization）降低约15%。同时估计了领头阶EFT截断误差，并识别出可区分这些误差的弹性 d-p 观测量。

Conclusion: 研究表明，振幅方法（amplitude methods）能够实现低能核反应有效场论的系统性、完备的树图构建与匹配。

Abstract: Big Bang nucleosynthesis (BBN) predicts the primordial deuterium abundance to a precision now limited by the nuclear reactions that burn deuterium. For the simplest of them, proton-deuteron radiative capture, d + p -> γ+ 3He [d(p,γ)3He], the precise LUNA data sit below the ab initio benchmark, and BBN reaction networks split on which to adopt. We develop an effective field theory (EFT) expanding in the finite size of the nuclei, building the amplitude with modern on-shell methods that enumerate every tree-level structure consistent with symmetries without the need for an explicit Lagrangian. A global Bayesian fit to the capture data and nuclear-theory priors returns S(0) = 0.209 +/- 0.008 eV b and traces the offset from the ab initio benchmark to a single natural-sized next-to-leading contact term (t_E1 ~ -0.15, the fractional shift of the electric-dipole amplitude) -- equivalently a ~15% lower effective 3He asymptotic normalization. We estimate the leading EFT truncation errors and identify an elastic d-p observable that would separate them. Our results suggest that amplitude methods enable systematic and complete tree-level construction and matching of EFTs for low-energy nuclear reactions.

</details>


### [22] [A symmetry-based resolution of pseudo-gauge ambiguities in local equilibrium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08569)
*Carlos Hoyos*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 该研究将重离子碰撞中总角动量流分解的赝规范歧义性（pseudo-gauge ambiguity）重新表述为与总电荷为零的守恒流相对应的假对称性（spurious symmetries），并提出了一种基于真正对称性（genuine symmetries）的局域平衡密度算符的明确定义方法，该密度算符在添加改进项（improvement terms）的变换下保持不变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 总角动量流可分解为轨道贡献和自旋贡献，这种分解方式（即赝规范）具有任意性，导致局域平衡密度算符（local-equilibrium density operator）的定义存在歧义，进而影响重离子碰撞（heavy-ion collisions）中自旋极化（spin polarization）的估算。该研究旨在从假对称性的角度统一理解这些歧义，并给出消除歧义的明确定义方案。

Method: 将赝规范歧义性及其他与守恒流改进项（improvements of conserved currents）相关的歧义性，重新表述为与总电荷为零的守恒流相对应的假对称性。基于与真正对称性对应的守恒流，引入一种局域平衡密度算符的无歧义定义方案。

Result: 得到的密度算符在添加改进项（包括能量-动量张量（energy-momentum tensor）的改进）的变换下保持不变，从而消除了由赝规范歧义性导致的局域平衡描述的不确定性。

Conclusion: 通过将赝规范歧义性归因于假对称性，并采用基于真正对称性的局域平衡密度算符，可以消除重离子碰撞中自旋极化估算的理论歧义，为相关物理量的计算提供了更自洽的框架。

Abstract: The total angular momentum current can be decomposed into orbital and spin contributions in different ways, known as pseudo-gauges. This freedom leads to ambiguities in the definition of local-equilibrium density operators, which in turn affect estimates of spin polarization in heavy-ion collisions. In this work, the pseudo-gauge ambiguity, together with other ambiguities associated with improvements of conserved currents, is reformulated in terms of spurious symmetries corresponding to conserved currents with vanishing total charge. A prescription for the unambiguous definition of a local-equilibrium density operator is introduced using the currents associated with genuine symmetries. The resulting density operator is invariant under transformations that add improvement terms to local currents, including the energy-momentum tensor.

</details>


### [23] [Relativistic Mean Field Approach with Chiral Symmetry Breaking and Quark Confinement in the light of Astrophysical Observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08412)
*Bikram Keshari Pradhan,Mohamad Chamseddine,Jérôme Margueron,Hubert Hansen,Guy Chanfray,Jean-Paul Ebran,Elias Khan*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文对手征约束与禁闭相对论平均场（RMF-CC）模型进行贝叶斯分析，发现引入 ωρ 耦合能缓解大质量中子星与GW170817潮汐形变之间的张力，而非线性 ω 自耦合并非必要；在无相变前提下，标准RMF模型略优于RMF-CC模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验手征约束与禁闭相对论平均场（RMF-CC）模型在同时满足核物质饱和性质、多信使中子星观测和格点量子色动力学（lattice QCD）约束时的表现，并探究 ρ-ω 介子耦合与非线性 ω 自耦合对理论-观测张力的缓解作用。

Method: 采用贝叶斯分析（Bayesian analysis）对RMF-CC模型进行参数推断；模型约束来源包括核物质近饱和密度性质、多信使中子星天体物理观测以及格点QCD对核子质量的预言；通过贝叶斯因子（Bayes factor）分析评估不同耦合项（ωρ耦合、非线性ω自相互作用）的统计必要性。

Result: RMF-CC模型在同时重现约2倍太阳质量（~2M⊙）大质量中子星与GW170817推断的潮汐形变（tidal deformability）时存在张力；贝叶斯因子分析表明，引入 ωρ 耦合可显著缓解该张力，而非线性 ω 自相互作用对RMF-CC模型并非必要；由于手征动力学对标量场的强约束以及禁闭处理导致的高密度状态方程（equation of state）软化，RMF-CC倾向于刚性状态方程，不压缩模量（incompressibility modulus）约为300 MeV。

Conclusion: ωρ 耦合是缓解理论-观测张力的关键因素；在未考虑中子星核心相变的前提下，标准RMF模型相较于RMF-CC模型更受贝叶斯分析青睐。

Abstract: We perform a Bayesian analysis of a relativistic mean-field approach, which is an implementation of the chiral confining model with both chiral symmetry breaking and confinement effects, and which was recently proven to reproduce well the ground state properties of finite nuclei. We additionally explore the impact of couplings between $ρ$ and $ω$ mesons as well as a non-linear $ω$ coupling. Our models are simultaneously constrained by nuclear matter properties near saturation density, multi-messenger neutron star astrophysical observations, and/or lattice QCD predictions of the nucleon mass. It exhibits tension in simultaneously reproducing the $\sim 2M_{\odot}$ massive NS and the tidal deformability inferred from GW170817. We show that an additional $ωρ$ coupling, favored by Bayes factor analysis, substantially alleviates this tension, while adding a non-linear $ω$ self-interaction is not necessary for the RMF-CC model. Owing to the strong constraints on the scalar sector imposed by chiral dynamics and the softening of the equation of state at high densities induced by our treatment of confinement, the RMF-CC approach favors stiff equations of state. Since we do not consider phase transition in the core of neutron stars, this stiffening is obtained with large values of the incompressibility modulus of about $\sim300$ MeV. We finally compare the well-known RMF model with RMF-CC models with the same constraints, and we obtain a preference for the RMF model in the absence of a phase transition in the core of neutron stars.

</details>

### [24] [Dissecting Parton Showers with Multi-Point Energy Correlators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07792)
*Mark Gonzalez,Philip Harris,Kyle Lee,Ian Moult,Simon Rothman*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统探索了喷注（jet）中四点能量关联器（four-point energy correlators）的唯象学，通过投影方法区分不同因子化通道，并基于Herwig和Pythia进行详细的部分子簇射（parton shower）模拟，揭示了自旋关联（spin correlations）与运动学方位角关联（kinematic azimuthal correlations）在不同相空间中的相对贡献，为LHC实验测量及下一代部分子簇射检验奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 能量关联器（energy correlators）因其高微分特性而成为研究喷注内多共线因子化（multi-collinear factorization）和方位角结构的理想探针。本文旨在推进四点关联器的唯象学研究，以弥合理论计算与实验测量之间的空白。

Method: 识别出可在实验中实现的投影，用于探测不同因子化通道中的分裂张量（splitting tensors）和分裂函数（splitting functions）。利用Herwig和Pythia进行部分子簇射模拟，并将结果与运动学极限下的解析计算进行对比，从而分离自旋关联与运动学方位角关联。

Result: 在实验可到达的运动学区域中，自旋关联表现为次主导效应（subdominant）；同时提出了可用于实验的参数化方案和分析算法。模拟结果强有力地激励了完整的QCD四点关联器计算，以验证部分子簇射结果。

Conclusion: 本文工作为在LHC上实验测量这些可观测量（observables）奠定了基础，并表明四点关联器可作为检验下一代部分子簇射的有效探针。

Abstract: The last several years have seen tremendous progress in the ability to both compute and measure multi-point correlations in energy flux. The highly differential nature of energy correlators makes them ideal probes of multi-collinear factorization and azimuthal structure within jets. In this paper, we explore the phenomenology of four-point correlators in jet substructure. We identify experimentally realizable projections that probe different factorization channels onto splitting tensors and splitting functions. We perform a detailed phenomenological study using both Herwig and Pythia. By comparing parton shower results with analytic calculations in kinematic limits, we are able to disentangle intrinsic spin correlations from kinematic azimuthal correlations. In experimentally accessible kinematic regions, we find the spin correlations are subdominant, strongly motivating a complete calculation of the four-point correlator in QCD to provide a test of the parton shower results. We also present parameterizations and analysis algorithms that can be used experimentally. Our work sets the stage for the experimental measurement of these observables at the LHC, and their use as probes of the next generation of parton showers.

</details>


### [25] [Azimuthal momentum isotropization in the Quark-Gluon Plasma thermalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07796)
*Sergio Barrera Cabodevila,Xiaojian Du,Carlos A. Salgado,Bin Wu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用玻尔兹曼方程扩散近似（BEDA）研究重离子碰撞中初始方位角各向异性的弛豫过程，发现不同谐波系数存在明确的弛豫时间层级，且在 $p_T$ 依赖的谐波系数演化中观察到初始峰值向高动量区移动，与实验数据定性一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 历史上认为重离子碰撞初始态中的方位角各向异性（azimuthal anisotropy）会在末态相互作用中迅速被抹除，因此在热化研究中常被忽略。然而在小系统碰撞中观测到的方位角关联可能受这些初始各向异性影响，因此有必要重新审视其弛豫行为。

Method: 采用玻尔兹曼方程扩散近似（Boltzmann Equation in Diffusion Approximation, BEDA）作为理论框架，系统分析初始态方位角各向异性的时间演化，并考察不同谐波系数（harmonic coefficient）的弛豫时间尺度，以及 $p_T$ 依赖的谐波系数随时间的演化特征。

Result: 不同谐波系数的弛豫时间存在清晰的层级结构（hierarchy）；$p_T$ 依赖的谐波系数在时间演化中初始峰值向高动量方向移动，该行为在现象学模拟中与实验观测数据吻合。

Conclusion: 初始方位角各向异性在 BEDA 框架下并非被迅速完全抹除，其弛豫过程具有谐波层级性，且可以贡献于小系统碰撞中观测到的方位角关联特征，值得在热化研究中纳入考虑。

Abstract: Azimuthal anisotropies coming from the initial state of a heavy-ion collision have been historically disregarded in the study of thermalization because they are expected to be rapidly washed out due to final-state interactions. However, they may be important when one attempts to describe azimuthal correlations observed in the collisions of small systems. In this work, we study how these initial anisotropies relax in the context of the Boltzmann Equation in Diffusion Approximation (BEDA). We find a clear hierarchy in the relaxation time of the anisotropies in terms of each harmonic coefficient. We also explore the evolution of the $p_T$-dependent harmonic coefficients in time, finding a shift in the initial peak towards higher momenta that mimics the experimental data when we perform a phenomenologically motivated simulation.

</details>


### [26] [Impact of QED Radiation on SMEFT Constraints in Deep Inelastic Scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07811)
*Sonny Mantry,Jian-Wei Qiu,Jia-Yue Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了在标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）框架下，由碰撞引发的QED辐射对深非弹性散射（DIS）测量精度的影响。基于联合QCD+QED因子化方案，发现QED辐射可显著修正DIS截面，但纵向电子自旋不对称性仅受百分之几的影响，因此后者作为SMEFT观测参量更为稳健；研究为SoLID和电子-离子对撞机（EIC）提供了基准投影。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深非弹性散射（deep-inelastic scattering, DIS）是超越标准模型物理的强大探针，但碰撞引发的QED辐射可能影响基于标准模型有效场论（Standard Model Effective Field Theory, SMEFT）的精确约束提取，因此需系统评估QED辐射在联合QCD+QED因子化框架下的修正效应。

Method: 采用基于轻子分布函数（lepton distribution function）和碎裂函数（fragmentation function）的联合QCD+QED因子化（joint QCD+QED factorization）框架，分析碰撞引发的QED辐射对DIS截面和纵向电子自旋不对称性（longitudinal electron spin asymmetry）的影响，并在SoLID和电子-离子对撞机（Electron-Ion Collider, EIC）实验条件下给出基准投影。

Result: QED辐射可使DIS截面受到量级为1的修正（order-one corrections），但在某些运动学区域显著改变与因子化相关的有效动量转移（effective momentum transfer）；而纵向电子自旋不对称性仅受百分之几量级的影响，受QED辐射扰动较小。

Conclusion: 纵向电子自旋不对称性作为SMEFT研究的观测参量比截面更为稳健，在SoLID和EIC等高精度DIS分析中具有重要应用价值；同时需将QED辐射效应纳入未来SMEFT约束提取的精确计算中。

Abstract: Deep-inelastic scattering (DIS) provides a powerful probe of physics beyond the Standard Model through precision measurements interpreted within the Standard Model Effective Field Theory (SMEFT). We study the impact of collision-induced QED radiation on SMEFT constraints using the joint QCD+QED factorization framework based on lepton distribution and fragmentation functions. QED radiation can substantially modify DIS cross sections and, in some kinematic regions, significantly alter the effective momentum transfer relevant for factorization. We find that while cross sections receive order-one corrections, longitudinal electron spin asymmetries are affected only at the few-percent level, making them significantly more robust observables for SMEFT studies. Benchmark projections for SoLID and the Electron-Ion Collider are provided to demonstrate the impact of QED radiation for future precision DIS analyses and the extraction of SMEFT constraints.

</details>

Method: 采用综述性方法，系统梳理近年来量子算法在对撞机物理各子领域（包括事件生成、部分子簇射模拟、散射振幅评估、回路与相空间积分、实验分析优化问题）中的发展思路。

Abstract: Quantum computing has emerged as a promising framework for addressing computationally demanding problems in collider physics. In recent years, a growing number of quantum algorithms have been proposed for applications ranging from event generation and parton shower simulation to the evaluation of scattering amplitudes, loop and phase-space integration, and optimization problems relevant to experimental analysis. We provide a concise overview of the main ideas behind these developments, with emphasis on the potential advantages of quantum approaches in comparison with classical methods, as well as on the current limitations imposed by noisy intermediate-scale quantum hardware.

### [28] [Transformer-based machine learning using low-level calorimeter signals for collimated photon identification at collider experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08175)
*Gabriel Matos,Lauren Larson,Abhilasha Dave,Maria Bressan,Azal Amer,Cindy Liu,Nikiforos Nikiforou,Jonathan Long,Timothy Andeen,John Parsons,Julia Gonski*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本研究利用电磁量能器（electromagnetic calorimeter）的细胞级（cell-level）信息，结合多种机器学习（machine learning）架构，对来自轻轴子类似粒子（axion-like particles）衰变的高度准直双光子（diphoton）信号与孤立单光子（single-photon）簇射进行分类。结果表明细胞级机器学习方法，特别是Transformer架构，在分类能力上显著优于传统高能重建方法，并可直接进行不变质量回归（invariant mass regression），有效压制π⁰和η假光子本底。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统高能重建方法丢弃了现代量能器精细分段（fine-grained segmentation）所捕获的大量簇射内部结构信息，限制了对超越标准模型（beyond the Standard Model, SM）物理事件的识别能力。

Method: 系统比较了从高能级变量（high-level shower shape variables）到直接基于量能器细胞级（cell-level）输入的多种机器学习架构，包括Transformer、MLP Mixer等六种模型，用于分类轻轴子类似粒子衰变产生的准直双光子信号与孤立单光子信号，并利用Transformer实现直接不变质量回归。

Result: 细胞级机器学习方法在分类性能上显著优于传统方法，其中Transformer在六种架构中表现最佳；MLP Mixer作为资源受限场景下适用于实时触发（trigger-level）应用的替代方案。Transformer还可从量能器细胞直接回归不变质量，有效改善轻共振态的表征，并降低π⁰和η假光子本底。

Conclusion: 细胞级机器学习方法能够将基于量能器的粒子识别（particle identification）性能显著超越当前传统技术水平，为高能对撞机物理中的粒子鉴别和共振态分析提供了新的有效手段。

Abstract: Electromagnetic calorimeters provide essential information for reconstructing and selecting both Standard Model (SM) and potential beyond the SM physics events at high-energy particle colliders. The fine-grained segmentation of modern calorimeters captures rich information about the internal structure of particle showers, much of which is discarded by conventional high-level reconstruction methods. In this work, we leverage calorimeter cell-level information to classify highly collimated diphoton signatures, arising from the decay of light axion-like particles, from isolated single-photon showers. We systematically compare a range of machine learning architectures, spanning high-level, shower shape variable-based approaches and direct cell-level methods. Cell-level machine learning shows significantly superior classification ability, with a Transformer in particular representing the best performance among six different architectures studied, and an MLP Mixer representing a resource-constrained alternative for potential real-time, trigger-level applications. Beyond classification, the Transformer model developed enables direct invariant mass regression from calorimeter cells, improving the characterization of light resonances and providing an additional handle in reducing the $π^0$ and $η$ fake photon backgrounds. These results demonstrate that cell-level machine learning methods can extend calorimeter-based particle identification and performance well beyond the capabilities of current conventional techniques.

### [29] [Precision three-Dimensional Atmospheric Neutrino Flux Calculation Based on Honda Flux Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08310)
*Jie Cheng,Yu-Feng Li,Liang-Jian Wen*

TL;DR: 本文基于Honda等人的模拟框架，首次在三维大气中微子通量计算中纳入μ子在地球内部的传播及其衰变或核俘获过程，同时更新了初级宇宙线模型、地磁场模型和强子相互作用模型，覆盖七个探测器站点（10 MeV–10⁴ GeV），揭示了低能区显著的位置依赖性通量差异，并重新评估了强子不确定性，为多项中微子振荡和稀有事件搜索实验提供关键输入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Honda等人开发的成熟的模拟框架，首次引入μ子在地球内部的传播及其后续衰变或核俘获过程；更新了基于AMS02的初级宇宙线模型（primary cosmic ray model）、IGRF2020地磁场模型（geomagnetic field）和经μ子重新标定的强子相互作用模型（hadronic interaction model）；计算覆盖七个位于不同地磁环境中的探测器站点，能量范围为10 MeV至10⁴ GeV。

Result: 当能量E_ν < 10 GeV时，不同站点的中微子通量出现显著差异，例如在1 GeV以下，IceCube处的ν_μ通量约为JUNO的两倍。与HKKMS15相比，因输入模型更新导致2%–10%的偏差。在100 MeV以下，μ子传播对所有站点的低能中微子通量贡献了一个全球性的重要分量，且绝对增量近似与站点无关。使用更新后的强子相互作用模型重新评估了全能量范围内的强子不确定性（hadronic uncertainty），系统误差较以往计算显著降低。

Conclusion: 本文提供的大气中微子通量计算结果可作为JUNO、Super-Kamiokande/Hyper-Kamiokande、DUNE、KM3NeT/ORCA、IceCube等中微子振荡和稀有事件搜索实验，以及面临中微子雾（neutrino fog）问题的直接暗物质探测实验的关键输入。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive three-dimensional atmospheric neutrino flux calculation based on the well-recognized simulation framework develeped by Honda and his collaborators, incorporating for the first time the muon propagation inside the Earth and its subsequent decay or nuclear capture. Other updates of essential input models include: the AMS02-based primary cosmic ray model, IGRF2020 geomagnetic field, and muon-recalibrated hadronic interaction model. The calculation covers seven detector sites across diverse geomagnetic environments, spanning 10~MeV to $10^4$~GeV. Significant site-dependent differences appear at $E_ν< 10$~GeV, with $ν_μ$ flux at IceCube approximately twice that at JUNO below 1~GeV. Compared to HKKMS15, deviations of 2\%--10\% are attributed to the updated input models. Below 100~MeV, we present precise flux results, revealing that muon propagation contributes a globally significant component to the low-energy neutrino flux at all sites, with an approximately site-independent absolute increment. The hadronic uncertainty is re-estimated across the energy range using the updated hadronic interaction model, with significant reduction of the systematic error compared to previous calculations. These results provide essential inputs for neutrino oscillation and rare-event search experiments including JUNO, Super-Kamiokande/Hyper-Kamiokande, DUNE, KM3NeT/ORCA, and IceCube, as well as direct dark matter detection experiments facing the neutrino fog.

### [31] [Internal pseudospin, lepton-number superselection, and neutrino--antineutrino coherence in massive neutral-fermion one-particle states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08739)
*Ricardo Romero*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，在固定三维动量下，大质量狄拉克中微子单粒子态的四维空间（粒子-反粒子标记与螺旋度）可生成一个内部SU(2)赝自旋子代数，该代数不同于维格纳小群（Wigner little group），其电荷共轭生成元U₂的+1本征空间对应于马约拉纳条件（Majorana condition）。该框架在不假定中微子为马约拉纳粒子的前提下，对马约拉纳质量与赝狄拉克劈裂（pseudo-Dirac splitting）进行了代数分类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动机在于利用代数的完备性统一描述中微子的质量类型（马约拉纳质量与赝狄拉克劈裂），同时避免提前假设中微子为马约拉纳粒子。通过分析四维单粒子态空间中的内部对称性结构（SU(4)）及其子代数（SU(2)赝自旋），揭示螺旋度翻转、电荷共轭及其乘积的代数封闭关系。

Method: 构建固定三维动量下大质量狄拉克中微子单粒子态的16个生成元τ_μ⊗σ_ν，利用轻子数L与螺旋度算符H_h进行分级；证明螺旋度翻转、电荷共轭及其乘积在SU(4)内部形成独立的SU(2)赝自旋子代数，其生成元U₁=2LJ₂（轻子数权重的自旋转动）；通过区分保持螺旋度的方向τ_{1,2}⊗σ_{0,3}与翻转螺旋度的方向τ_{1,2}⊗σ_{1,2}，分别映射赝狄拉克混合系数κ_pD=Δm²/4E和无中微子双β衰变质量因子（neutrinoless double-beta decay mass factor）。

Result: 发现电荷共轭与SU(2)赝自旋的U₂生成元对应，马约拉纳条件退化为U₂=+1本征空间的投影，在该子空间中仅保留维格纳小群代数；螺旋度保持方向承载主动-惰性（active–sterile）中微子混合（赝狄拉克劈裂），螺旋度翻转方向承载主动-主动（active–active）混合（无中微子双β衰变质量因子）。

Conclusion: 该代数框架无需预先假设中微子为马约拉纳粒子，即可系统分类中微子的马约拉纳质量项与赝狄拉克质量劈裂，为理解中微子质量结构提供了基于群论的统一视角。

Abstract: At fixed three-momentum, massive Dirac neutrino one-particle states span a 4D space of particle--antiparticle identity and helicity. We show that helicity flip, charge conjugation, and their product close an internal $SU(2)$ pseudospin subalgebra within $SU(4)$, distinct from the Wigner little group. Its helicity generator is the lepton-number-weighted spin rotation $U_1=2LJ_2$. The lepton-number $L$ and helicity $\mathcal H_h$ grade the 16 generators $τ_μ\otimesσ_ν$, organizing the $ΔL=2$ sector. Helicity-preserving directions $τ_{1,2}\otimesσ_{0,3}$ carry the pseudo-Dirac mixing $κ_{\rm pD}=Δm^2/4E$ (active--sterile), while helicity-flipping directions $τ_{1,2}\otimesσ_{1,2}$ carry the neutrinoless double-beta decay mass factor (active--active). Furthermore, charge conjugation matches the $U_2$ generator. The Majorana condition is thus a projection onto the $U_2=+1$ eigenspace, where only the Wigner algebra survives. This framework algebraically classifies Majorana masses and pseudo-Dirac splittings without assuming neutrinos are Majorana particles.

### [32] [Lecture notes on random matrix theory: the results, the applications, and the analytical tools](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07868)
*Joseph W. Baron*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文以教学为导向，系统介绍了随机矩阵理论（Random Matrix Theory）的经典结果与多种分析技术，涵盖空穴方法（cavity method）、图解形式（diagrammatic formalism）、复制方法（replica method）、路径积分形式（path-integral formalism）、超对称形式（supersymmetric formalism）、群体动力学方法（population dynamics method）和自由概率论（free probability theory），并讨论各方法的应用场景与优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机矩阵理论在核物理、金融、生态学和无序系统等多个领域具有广泛应用，但其经典结果和分析技术分散且学习门槛较高。本文旨在以统一且教学友好的方式，系统梳理经典结果及其推导，并为研究者提供一份涵盖多种分析方法的参考指南。

Method: 第一部分采用直观的空穴方法（cavity method）推导最著名且广泛使用的经典结果，并结合具体应用展示其意义，每节附有练习题。第二部分基于第一性原理，系统介绍图解形式（diagrammatic formalism）、复制方法（replica method）、路径积分形式（path-integral formalism）和超对称形式（supersymmetric formalism），并纳入群体动力学方法（population dynamics method）和自由概率论（free probability theory）等较新工具，用半圆律（semicircle law）作为统一示例重新推导部分经典结果。

Result: 以半圆律（semicircle law）为切入点，展示了多种分析技术对该经典结果的重新推导过程，并给出了每种分析方法的优势比较及适用场景的说明。

Conclusion: 本文作为教学笔记与参考指南，系统整合了随机矩阵理论的核心结果与分析技术，阐明各方法在不同研究情境中的实用价值，有助于降低该领域的学习与研究门槛。

Abstract: Random matrix theory has established itself as a theoretical cornerstone of the mathematical sciences over the past century. It has undeniable utility in areas of research as diverse as nuclear physics, finance, ecology and disordered systems. The purpose of these notes is twofold. First, the most famous and widely used classic results are derived in a pedagogical manner, mostly using the comparatively elementary and transparent cavity method. The significance of each result is then demonstrated in the context of a particular application. There are also some select exercises at the end of each section. In the second part of these notes, a reference guide of analytical techniques for the random-matrix/disordered-systems practitioner is provided. Introducing the diagrammatic, replica, path-integral, and supersymmetric formalisms from first principles, we rederive some of the aforementioned classic results, particularly focussing on the simplest one -- the semicircle law. Innovations such as the population dynamics method and the tools of free probability theory are also included. We discuss the merits of each analytical approach, and we highlight the contexts in which each becomes particularly useful.

### [33] [Anisotropic vacancy-induced magnetization textures in altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07789)
*Ruben Burkard,Mathias S. Scheurer,Urban F. P. Seifert*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过微观模拟和低能场论，研究了交变磁体（altermagnets）中由空位（vacancy）诱导的磁纹理（magnetic textures），发现空位会产生反映交变磁态对称性的实空间各向异性畸变，为利用局域探针检测交变磁有序提供了直接途径。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索交变磁体中空位缺陷诱导的磁结构响应，旨在建立一种利用局域探测手段（如扫描探针）识别和表征交变磁有序（altermagnetic order）的新方法。

Method: 采用微观模拟（microscopic simulations）和低能场论（low-energy field theory）相结合的理论方法，分别研究经典交变磁体（classical altermagnets）和量子交变磁体模型中空位产生的磁有序畸变。

Result: 经典交变磁体中，空位在横向磁场（transverse magnetic field）下产生各向异性的磁化纹理（magnetization textures）；量子模型中，即使在零场下，量子涨落（fluctuations）也会诱导出纵向的幂律衰减磁畸变（longitudinal power-law decaying magnetic distortions）。

Conclusion: 空位响应直接编码了交变磁态的对称性信息，为利用局域分辨探针检测交变磁有序提供了可行路线。

Abstract: We study magnetic textures induced by vacancies in altermagnets using microscopic simulations and low-energy field theory. We show that a vacancy generically produces a real-space anisotropic distortion of the magnetic order, whose structure encodes the symmetry of the underlying altermagnetic state. This impurity response offers a direct route to detecting altermagnetic order with locally resolved probes. We demonstrate this for both classical altermagnets, where vacancies generate anisotropic magnetization textures in a transverse magnetic field, and quantum models, where fluctuations induce longitudinal power-law decaying magnetic distortions even at zero field.

Particularizing to the RG flow of the electron-electron interaction vertex, we treat phonon- and electron-mediated Fermi liquid instabilities on equal footing as we analyze tentative electronic order parameters related to charge, spin, nematicity, and superconducting pairing. We illustrate the approach at the example of Peierls-type transitions we find for the Hubbard model on the square lattice coupled to acoustic phonon bands. Our method allows to incorporate full electronic and phononic ab initio input, and thus lends itself to the analysis of electronic order from intertwined electronic interactions and EPC at a microscopically most substantiated level.

Result: 大多数微扰是不相关的（irrelevant），不会在性质上改变模型的精确可解性；但Kitaev相互作用与Z₂规范场耦合，使原本局域的visons变为可移动。

Abstract: I investigate the stability of the spin-orbital liquid described by the Yao-Lee model in the presence of multiple perturbations that naturally arise in a recently proposed microscopic realization. While most perturbations are irrelevant and do not qualitatively alter the exact solvability, we find that the Kitaev interaction plays a special role: it couples to the $ \mathbb{Z}_2 $ gauge field and renders the visons mobile.

### [36] [Tunable Emergent Gauge Fields from Skyrmions in a Quasicrystalline Lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07948)
*Leandro M. Chinellato,Flavia A. Gómez Albarracín,Cristian D. Batista,Pablo S. Cornaglia*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过经典海森伯模型（Heisenberg model）结合Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用（DMI）和外磁场，研究二维准晶格（quasicrystalline lattice）中的磁性斯格明子（magnetic skyrmions）。斯格明子间的排斥与准周期钉扎势（quasiperiodic pinning landscape）的竞争，导致随外场变化的序列性斯格明子晶格构型。与周期晶格上斯格明子晶体（skyrmion crystal）的一阶崩塌不同，准晶中准简并极小（quasi-degenerate minima）的势能层级使斯格明子密度随接近饱和场而准连续抑制。这一机制可直接调控拓扑荷（topological charge）及相应的巡游电子规范场（emergent gauge field），进而使霍尔电导率（Hall conductivity）随磁场小幅变化而显著可调，并在饱和附近平滑降至零。该基于多稳态（multistability）的场控可调性将准晶磁体确立为可调拓扑结构平台，可用于磁存储和磁电响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了探索拓扑磁结构（topological magnetic textures）在非周期晶格中的行为，并揭示准晶无序（quasicrystalline disorder）与磁序（magnetic order）之间的竞争机制，从而克服传统周期晶格中斯格明子晶体突然塌缩的局限性，实现更精细的拓扑荷控制。

Method: 采用经典海森伯模型（classical Heisenberg model）并引入Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用（DMI）与外磁场（external magnetic field），在二维准晶格（two-dimensional quasicrystalline lattice）中进行数值模拟，分析斯格明子晶格构型随外场变化的演化。

Result: 发现斯格明子间排斥与准周期钉扎势（quasiperiodic pinning landscape）的竞争导致一系列不同的斯格明子晶格构型；准晶中准简并极小（quasi-degenerate minima）的钉扎势层级允许斯格明子密度在接近饱和场时准连续抑制，而非周期晶格中的强一级相变（strongly first-order collapse）崩塌；霍尔电导率（Hall conductivity）可随小磁场变化而剧烈改变，并在饱和附近平滑归零。

Conclusion: 指出准晶磁体（quasicrystalline magnets）因其固有的多稳态（multistability）特性，可作为一种场控可调拓扑结构（field-controlled tunable topological textures）的平台，在磁存储（magnetic memory）和磁电响应（magnetoelectronic response）等方面具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: We study magnetic skyrmions in a two-dimensional quasicrystalline lattice using a classical Heisenberg model with Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interactions and an external magnetic field. The competition between the skyrmion-skyrmion repulsion and an emergent quasiperiodic pinning landscape gives rise to a sequence of distinct skyrmion lattice configurations as a function of field. The resulting hierarchy of quasiperiodic pinning potentials, characterized by closely spaced quasi-degenerate minima, enables a quasi-continuous suppression of the skyrmion density as the saturation field is approached, in sharp contrast to the strongly first-order collapse of skyrmion crystals on periodic lattices. This provides a direct mechanism for controlling the topological charge and, consequently, the emergent gauge field for itinerant electrons. As a consequence, the Hall conductivity can be strongly modified with small changes in the magnetic field and driven smoothly to zero near saturation. This field-controlled tunability, rooted in the underlying multistability, identifies quasicrystalline magnets as a platform for tunable topological textures, with potential applications in magnetic memory and magnetoelectronic response.

### [37] [Scalable Simulation of Strongly Correlated Electron-Phonon Systems via Non-Gaussian Matrix Product States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08176)
*Siyuan Jiang,Tao Shi*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出一种非高斯矩阵乘积态（non-Gaussian matrix product state）方法，用于研究强关联电子-声子（e-ph）耦合系统，并在一维和二维Hubbard-Holstein（HH）模型中系统地揭示了相分离（PS）、条纹相（stripe phases）及其与声子延迟效应相关的稳定化机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强关联电子-声子耦合系统中，电子与无限维希尔伯特空间（unbounded Hilbert space）的声子模式之间存在难以处理的纠缠，已有方法难以在广泛的参数区间内进行可扩展模拟，因此需要更高效的数值方法。

Method: 将非高斯态（non-Gaussian states）与矩阵乘积态（matrix product states, MPS）相结合，提出非高斯矩阵乘积态方法，以有效刻画强关联电子与声子模式之间的纠缠，实现跨参数区间的可扩展模拟。

Result: 在一维广义Hubbard-Holstein（HH）模型中，发现强烈的相分离（phase separation, PS）倾向，与掺杂铜氧化物链（cuprate chain）的角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）观测相关。在二维HH模型中：半满时构建了相图，发现非局域声子介导吸引与局域Hubbard排斥竞争产生金属相；掺杂时揭示了软声子（soft phonons）稳定条纹相的作用。在反铁磁（antiferromagnet）中，完全填充条纹的稳定化归因于局域延迟效应（local retardation effect）；在掺杂电荷密度波（charge-density-wave）区域，通过非局域延迟效应（non-local retardation effect）稳定了具有扩大晶胞的新型双极化子条纹相（bipolaronic stripe phase）。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一条系统解析电子-声子相互作用的路径，这种相互作用对于理解超导电性（superconductivity）至关重要。

Abstract: We investigate strongly correlated electron-phonon (e-ph) systems via a non-Gaussian matrix product state method. By combining non-Gaussian states with matrix product states, our method efficiently characterizes the intractable entanglement between strongly correlated electrons and phononic modes of unbounded Hilbert space, enabling scalable simulations across broad parameter regimes. In one-dimensional generalized Hubbard--Holstein (HH) models, we identify a pronounced tendency toward phase separation (PS), an instability relevant to recent angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy observations on doped cuprate chain. In two-dimensional HH models, we construct the phase diagram at half-filling featuring a metallic phase emerging from the competition between non-local phonon-mediated attraction and local Hubbard repulsion. Upon doping, we elucidate the role of soft phonons in stabilizing stripe phases. In the antiferromagnet, the stabilization of the fully filled stripe is attributed to a local retardation effect, wherein the charge order is pinned by phonons, leading to a diminished response to spin fluctuations. In the doped charge-density-wave regime, a novel bipolaronic stripe phase with an enlarged unit cell is stabilized via a non-local retardation effect, where long-range phonon-mediated interactions suppress PS. Our work establishes a systematic route to decoding the e-ph interplay that is crucial for superconductivity.

### [38] [Holographic Theory of Mixed-Dimensional Statistics and Conservation-Encoding Hopping-Operator Algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08583)
*Hanyu Xue,Xiao-Gang Wen*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本论文建立了一个适用于混合维度激发（mixed-dimensional excitations）在交织守恒律（intertwined conservation laws）下统计行为的通用理论框架，通过跳跃-算子代数（hopping-operator algebra）对统计性质进行微观定义，并证明其分类分别由上同调类（cohomology class）和融合d-范畴（fusion d-category）刻画。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的费米统计（Fermi statistics）仅适用于粒子数守恒的简单情形，但实际物理系统中存在更复杂的、涉及混合维度激发和多个交织守恒律的统计行为，缺乏统一的描述框架。

Method: 定义了一个由局域算子生成的子代数——跳跃-算子代数（hopping-operator algebra, LOsA），这些算子在不违反守恒律的前提下局域移动或形变激发。统计性质是否非平凡取决于该子代数是否非平凡。对于有指向的（pointed）守恒律，系统由更高群（higher group）G的对称缺陷（symmetry defects）刻画，其LOsA分类由上同调类[ω] ∈ H^{d+2}(BG; R/Z) 描述。更一般的非指向（non-pointed）守恒律及非可逆激发（non-invertible excitations）则由LOsA及其希尔伯特空间表示（Hilbert-space representation）构成的对偶描述，等价于广义对称性（generalized symmetry）的分类，即融合d-范畴。

Result: 证明了对于d维空间中由更高群G守恒的激发，其LOsA的分类由上同调类[ω] ∈ H^{d+2}(BG; R/Z) 给出；改变[ω]的一个上边缘（coboundary）仅对应局域算子的重新相位。此外，该统计行为可以通过(d+1)维空间中扭曲的G更高群规范理论（higher-group gauge theory）在全息（holographic）意义上实现。对于更一般的非指向情形，统计分类等价于融合d-范畴的分类。

Conclusion: 跳跃-算子代数提供了一种描述混合维度激发在复杂守恒律下统计性质的统一微观定义；有向情形对应更高群对称缺陷的上同调分类，非指向情形则推广至融合d-范畴分类，从而将统计行为与广义对称性理论建立起严格的对应关系。

Abstract: We develop a general framework for the statistics of mixed-dimensional excitations subject to intertwined conservation laws, extending the familiar Fermi statistics with conserved particle number. We define statistics microscopically through a \emph{hopping-operator algebra}: a local operator subalgebra (LOsA) generated by operators that locally move or deform excitations while preserving the conservation law. Nontrivial statistics arise when this subalgebra is nontrivial.
  We first focus on LOsAs that encode \emph{pointed} conservation laws. These give rise to invertible excitations, whose fusion rules are exactly those of the symmetry defects of a higher group $\cG$. For such $\cG$-conserved excitations in $d$-dimensional space, we show that the corresponding LOsA -- and hence the statistics it defines -- is classified by a cohomology class $[ω] \in H^{d+2}(B\cG;\R/\Z)$, where changing $[ω]$ by a coboundary corresponds merely to a rephasing of the local operators. We further provide a holographic realization: excitations with this prescribed conservation law and statistics live on the boundary of a $\cG$ higher-group gauge theory in $(d+1)$-dimensional space, twisted by $[ω]$.
  More generally, non-pointed conservation laws and the associated statistics of non-invertible excitations are defined by a pair: a LOsA together with its excitation-complex representation. This is equivalent to the pair consisting of a LOsA and its Hilbert-space representation, which is the data defining a generalized symmetry. Consequently, non-pointed conservation laws and their statistics in $d$-dimensional space are classified by fusion $d$-categories, just as generalized symmetries are. The higher-group results above are the fully-pointed special cases of this more general classification.

</details>


### [39] [Emergent Topology from Nonlocal Electronic Correlations in One Dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08278)
*Félix Fossati,Erik Linnér,Evgeny A. Stepanov*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文证明，在低维系统中，电子关联可以从拓扑平庸的非相互作用能带结构中诱导出拓扑相。通过将高级团簇图论多体方法应用于一维扩展哈伯德模型，研究发现非局域库仑相互作用驱动了键序波（BOW）和电荷密度波（CDW）相的出现，这些相虽然由相互作用驱动且对称性破缺，但可以用有效的单粒子描述来刻画，并展现出非平凡的拓扑性质，包括局域边缘态的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索电子关联（electronic correlations）如何从拓扑平庸的能带结构中产生拓扑相（topological phases），建立非局域相互作用驱动拓扑涌现的物理机制。

Method: 采用高级团簇图论多体方法（advanced cluster-diagrammatic many-body approach），应用于一维扩展哈伯德模型（one-dimensional extended Hubbard model），通过调节非局域库仑相互作用（nonlocal Coulomb interaction）来研究相变与拓扑性质。

Result: 非局域库仑相互作用驱动键序波（bond-order-wave, BOW）和电荷密度波（charge-density-wave, CDW）相的出现；BOW 相映射为有效的 Su-Schrieffer-Heeger 模型，CDW 相（具有次主导的键序关联）对应 Rice-Mele 模型；两相均具有非平凡拓扑特征，表现为局域边缘态（localized edge states）的存在。

Conclusion: 非局域电子关联（nonlocal electronic correlations）可以在关联系统中生成涌现拓扑（emergent topology），为理解相互作用驱动的拓扑相提供了新的机制。

Abstract: We demonstrate that electronic correlations in low-dimensional systems can induce topological phases starting from a topologically trivial noninteracting band structure. Using an advanced cluster-diagrammatic many-body approach applied to the one-dimensional extended Hubbard model, we show that tuning the nonlocal Coulomb interaction drives the emergence of bond-order-wave (BOW) and charge-density-wave (CDW) phases. Despite being interaction-driven and symmetry-broken, these states admit an effective low-energy single-particle description. In particular, the BOW phase maps onto an effective Su-Schrieffer-Heeger model, while the CDW phase, with subleading bond-order correlations, corresponds to a Rice-Mele model. Both phases exhibit a nontrivial topological character, manifested by the presence of localized edge states. Our results establish a mechanism by which nonlocal electronic correlations generate emergent topology in correlated systems.

</details>


### [40] [The charge density fluctuations and the Shrinking Fermi Liquid scenario for strange metallicity in cuprates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08476)
*Sergio Caprara,Sauri Bhattacharyya,Carlo Di Castro,Giovanni Mirarchi,Götz Seibold,Marco Grilli*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文基于收缩费米液体（Shrinking Fermi Liquid）理论，结合铜氧化物中实验表征的电荷密度涨落（CDF）、声子（phonons）及顺磁子（paramagnons）等微观散射机制，系统解释了过掺杂铜氧化物奇异金属（strange metal）相在输运、光学和热力学上的反常性质，并指出CDF耗散参数的对数增长可统一描述其在强磁场下的低温行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解铜氧化物高温超导体中奇异金属（strange metal, SM）相的微观机制是凝聚态物理的核心难题之一。现有理论框架难以同时解释SM相的输运、光学及热力学反常行为，亟需一个基于实验可观测微观激发（如电荷密度涨落）的自洽理论。

Method: 采用收缩费米液体（Shrinking Fermi Liquid）理论框架，将实验表征的电荷密度涨落（charge density fluctuations, CDF）、声子（phonons）和顺磁子（paramagnons）作为费米型朗道准粒子（Landau quasiparticles）的散射源，通过CDF与非临界短程关联（M/γ~10 meV）的输入参数，结合耗散参数γ随温度对数增长（logarithmic growth）的假设，计算输运、光学及热力学性质。

Result: 输运性质可由准粒子与CDF及声子的散射很好地描述；光学性质由低频CDF决定温度依赖关系，顺磁子连续谱则产生频率线性（linear-in-frequency）的散射率；在频率大于M/γ时出现ω/T标度（ω/T scaling）行为；当超导被强磁场抑制后，SM性质可延伸至几开尔文（Kelvin）的低温。

Conclusion: 基于实验可观测的电荷密度涨落、声子和顺磁子等微观散射机制，结合CDF耗散参数的对数增长假设，可自洽解释铜氧化物奇异金属相在输运（电阻率、磁阻）、光学（散射率、ω/T标度）及热力学（比热、塞贝克系数、热导）方面的全部反常性质，为过掺杂铜氧化物的SM相提供了一个统一的理论图景。

Abstract: We interpret the strange metal (SM) properties of slightly overdoped cuprates in terms of the recently proposed Shrinking Fermi Liquid theory. This is based on the pervading presence in the cuprate phase diagram of charge density fluctuations (CDF), which have been identified and characterized in RIXS. These fluctuations are abundant and have a low energy due to the proximity of the charge density wave quantum critical point hidden under the superconducting dome of cuprates, but have a short range and non-critical character with a finite energy M/γ~10 meV as measured above Tc. Here M~ ξ^-2 is determined by the short correlation length ξ, while γencodes the Landau damping ruling the lifetime of the charge fluctuations. Besides these low energy CDF, cuprates also display phonons and a broad continuum of particle-hole excitations, mostly due to spin paramagnons arising from their strongly correlated character. With these experimentally characterized ingredients we show that above Tc the SM properties in transport are well described in terms of fermionic Landau quasiparticles scattering with CDF and phonons. The optical properties can instead be interpreted by the combined effect of low energy CDF determining the temperature dependence, and of the paramagnon continuum determining a linear in frequency scattering rate. Remarkably, the combined effect of these simple ingredients also induces ω/T scaling properties for frequencies larger than M/γ. When superconductivity is suppressed by strong magnetic fields the SM properties extend down to a few Kelvin. By assuming that the CDF dissipation parameter γgrows logarithmically by lowering T, we account for all anomalous transport and thermodynamic properties of cuprates (specific heat, Seebeck, heat transport, resistivity, and magnetoresistance) thereby providing a consistent scenario for the SM phase of cuprates.

</details>


### [41] [Accurate Self-Attention Wavefunctions at Large Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08616)
*Filippo Gaggioli,Sam Azadi,Liang Fu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文证明自注意力（self-attention）神经网络波函数在最多N=169粒子的二维均匀电子气（homogeneous electron gas）中，能够获得比最先进扩散蒙特卡洛（DMC）更低的能量，并完整恢复液态集体激发谱，且有限尺寸外推到热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）的结果表现出良好收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自注意力神经网络变分波函数（self-attention neural network variational wavefunctions）虽具有超越传统变分拟设（variational ansatz）的表达能力，但其计算复杂度随系统尺度增加而升高，因而其在大尺度系统下能否保持精度成为一个亟待回答的可扩展性（scalability）问题。

Method: 将自注意力波函数应用于二维均匀电子气系统，粒子数最大至N=169；通过直接获取基态波函数计算可观测量，并与扩散蒙特卡洛（DMC）方法进行系统性能量比较。

Result: 自注意力波函数在所有测试系统尺度下均获得了系统性地低于最先进DMC方法的能量；成功恢复了液态相完整的集体激发模（collective-mode）色散关系，涵盖小q等离激元（plasmon）支到q≈2k_F处类似旋子（roton-like）的最小值；N=91与N=169的可观测量几乎完全一致。

Conclusion: 自注意力神经网络波函数在二维均匀电子气中展现出良好的可扩展性，在多达169个粒子的尺度上仍能保持高精度，且计算结果已收敛到热力学极限（thermodynamic limit），表明该类方法有望应用于更大规模的强关联量子多体系统。

Abstract: Self-attention neural networks provide powerful variational wavefunctions that surpass the expressivity of traditional variational ansatze. This expressivity, however, comes with increased computational complexity, raising a pressing question about scalability -- can such wavefunctions retain their accuracy at large system sizes? We apply self-attention wavefunctions to the two-dimensional homogeneous electron gas for up to N=169 particles, obtaining energies systematically lower than state-of-the-art DMC. Direct access to the ground state wavefunction further lets us recover the full collective-mode dispersion of the liquid phase, from the small-q plasmon branch to a roton-like minimum near q=2k_F. Observables at N=91 and N=169 are in near-perfect agreement, indicating convergence to the thermodynamic limit.

</details>
