H. Yin,K. Yoshihara,C. Z. Yuan,J. Yuan,L. Yuan,Y. Yusa,L. Zani,F. Zeng,M. Zeyrek,B. Zhang,X. Zhao,V. Zhilich,J. S. Zhou,Q. D. Zhou,X. Y. Zhou,L. Zhu,R. Žlebčík*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于Belle II探测器采集的408 fb⁻¹数据，搜索轴子类似粒子（axion-like particle, ALP）在正负电子对撞中通过过程e⁺e⁻→γa, a→γγ的产生，在0.17–9.80 GeV/c²的ALP质量范围内未发现显著信号，并在0.17–5.00 GeV/c²质量区间设定了目前最强的上限限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轴子类似粒子（ALP）是标准模型（Standard Model）多种扩展理论所预言的粒子，其与光子的耦合为可见区与隐藏区（hidden sector）之间提供了理论动机充分的相互作用通道。通过实验搜索ALP信号，可以检验超出标准模型的新物理（new physics）存在的可能性。

Method: 利用Belle II探测器在SuperKEKB e⁺e⁻对撞机上获取的积分亮度为408 fb⁻¹的数据样本。通过重建终态含三个光子的事例，提取双光子不变质量谱（di-photon invariant mass spectrum），在0.17–9.80 GeV/c²的ALP质量范围内搜索窄峰信号。

Result: 未观测到超出背景的显著过剩（significant excess）。在95%置信水平上，对ALP-光子耦合强度g_{aγγ}及其产生截面设定了上限，灵敏度达10⁻⁴ GeV⁻¹量级。该结果在0.17–5.00 GeV/c²的几乎整个质量区间内为目前最强限制，较此前最优结果改进最多达9倍。

Conclusion: 在0.17–9.80 GeV/c²质量范围内未发现ALP存在的证据；所设上限是目前在0.17–5.00 GeV/c²区间内最严格的限制，显著提高了对ALP-光子耦合参数的约束能力。

Abstract: Axion-like particles (ALPs) are predicted in many extensions of the Standard Model and provide a well-motivated portal between visible and hidden sectors through their coupling to photons. We search for ALPs produced in the process $e^{+}e^{-}\toγa$, $a\toγγ$, using a data sample corresponding to an integrated luminosity of $408~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ recorded by the Belle~II detector at the SuperKEKB $e^{+}e^{-}$ collider. Events containing three photons are used to reconstruct the ALP as a narrow peak in the di-photon invariant mass spectrum over the range $0.17 < m_{a} < 9.80~\mathrm{GeV}/c^{2}$. No significant excess above background is observed. We set 95\% confidence level upper limits on the production cross section and on the ALP-photon coupling $g_{aγγ}$, reaching sensitivities at the level of $10^{-4}~\mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$. The limits are the most restrictive to date over nearly the entire mass range $0.17 < m_{a} < 5.00~\mathrm{GeV}/c^{2}$, and improve upon previous results by up to a factor 9.

### [43] [Early Career Issues in Particle Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08131)
*Saptaparna Bhattacharya*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于早期职业研究者（ECR）的视角，概述了粒子物理学在标准模型（Standard Model）完成后所面临的关键问题、未来对撞机（collider）规划、学术就业市场、科学传播（science outreach）角色以及人工智能（artificial intelligence）带来的机遇与挑战，并强调了支持网络对ECR职业发展的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粒子物理学正处于关键转折点：2012年希格斯玻色子（Higgs boson）的发现虽完成了标准模型，却也开启了关于等级问题（hierarchy problem）、暗物质（dark matter）本质和中微子质量（neutrino masses）等根本性问题。未来数十年的实验规划将直接影响至2060年后的领域走向，因此需要了解将承担这些长期任务的最年轻研究者群体——早期职业研究者——所面临的关键问题与诉求。

Method: 本文基于一场主题演讲整理而成。首先从ECR视角概述未来对撞机（collider）规划全景；其次通过大规模问卷调查（large-scale surveys）收集ECR的直接反馈，聚焦其主要关切与可行建议；随后分析学术就业市场、科学传播（science outreach）的重要但常被忽视的角色，以及人工智能（artificial intelligence）带来的双重挑战与机遇。

Result: 提供了ECR对未来对撞机规划的直接看法；揭示了ECR在调查中表达的主要关切与具体建议；呈现了学术就业市场的分析结果；指出了科学传播工作重要但回报不足的现状；以及人工智能作为双刃剑（dual-edged challenge and opportunity）对ECR的影响。

Conclusion: 结束部分强调了现有支持网络（support networks）对ECR应对复杂且不确定的职业道路至关重要，表明这些网络是不可或缺的生存与发展的资源。

Abstract: Particle physics stands at a crossroads. The discovery of the Higgs boson in 2012 completed the Standard Model, but it also opened a new set of fundamental questions about the nature of our universe. Answering these questions, from the hierarchy problem and the nature of dark matter to the origin of neutrino masses, will require a new generation of powerful and sophisticated experiments. The global community is currently engaged in a comprehensive, long-term planning process to determine the next big machine. These discussions are not merely technical. The decisions made in the coming years will shape the field until 2060 and beyond. This extended timeline has a direct and immediate impact on the lives and careers of the field's youngest members: the graduate students, postdoctoral fellows, and other early-career researchers (ECRs) who will be tasked with designing, building, and ultimately analyzing the data from these future facilities. This proceeding provides an overview of the key issues facing ECRs in particle physics today, based on a talk delivered on the subject. It begins by surveying the future collider landscape from an ECR perspective. It then delves into the critical feedback gathered directly from ECRs through large-scale surveys, focusing on their primary concerns and actionable recommendations. Following this, it presents an analysis of the academic job market, the important but often unrewarded role of science outreach, and the emerging dual-edged challenge and opportunity of artificial intelligence. The paper concludes by highlighting the indispensable support networks available to ECRs, which are vital for navigating this complex and uncertain career path.

</details>

### [44] [Universality and Dynamical Inequivalence in Isospectral Non-Hermitian Anderson Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07714)
*Aziz Hasan,Anant Vijay Varma,Namit Anand,Sourin Das*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文证明，在一维无序环中仅需一个非厄米边界键即可驱动局域化-退局域化转变，而非此前认为需要全局非互易性。作者构建了等谱哈密顿量族，发现临界行为由总虚规范通量（imaginary gauge flux）决定而与空间分布无关，但不同构型具有截然不同的动力学行为，揭示了非厄米系统中静态与动力学普适性的分离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典的Hatano-Nelson范式认为，体态非互易性（extensive bulk nonreciprocity）通过虚规范通量可以破坏安德森局域化（Anderson localization）。本文旨在检验这一必要条件是否真正不可或缺，并探索边界效应对局域化-退局域化转变（localization-delocalization transition）的影响。

Method: 作者构造了一个精确等谱（isospectral）的非厄米哈密顿量族，该族连续插值于均匀Hatano-Nelson模型与单非厄米键极限之间。通过分析谱性质、本征态及拓扑诊断量，研究临界行为的规范不变性，并对比不同构型下的动力学演化。

Result: 仅需单个非厄米边界键即可驱动局域化-退局域化转变；整个等谱族中，普适临界行为仅由总虚规范通量决定，与空间分布无关。然而，不同构型在动力学上差异显著：单边界实现表现出快速算符混杂（operator scrambling）、振荡波包加速以及双重新入稳态纠缠转变（double re-entrant steady state entanglement transition）。

Conclusion: 非厄米系统中静态临界性质与动力学普适性存在根本分离。作者还提出基于多端拓扑输运的实验可行方案，为观测边界诱导的非厄米临界性及其非传统动力学信号提供了现实路径。

Abstract: The Hatano Nelson paradigm establishes that extensive bulk nonreciprocity can destabilize Anderson localization via an imaginary gauge flux. Here, we demonstrate that extensive nonreciprocity is not a necessary ingredient: a single non-Hermitian boundary bond in a disordered one-dimensional ring suffices to drive the localization-delocalization transition. More generally, we construct an exactly isospectral family of non-Hermitian Hamiltonians that continuously interpolates between the uniform Hatano Nelson model and the single-bond limit. We show that the universal critical behavior encompassing spectral, eigenstate, and topological diagnostics is gauge invariant and governed solely by the total imaginary gauge flux, regardless of its spatial distribution. Remarkably, despite sharing identical spectra and critical exponents, different configurations within this isospectral family exhibit qualitatively distinct quantum dynamics, establishing a fundamental separation between static and dynamical universality in non-Hermitian systems. Specifically, the single boundary realization features rapid operator scrambling, oscillatory wavepacket acceleration, and a double re-entrant steady state entanglement transition. Finally, we propose an experimentally feasible realization based on multi-terminal topological transport, providing a realistic route toward observing boundary induced non Hermitian criticality and its unconventional dynamical signatures.

</details>


### [45] [Axion-Induced Casimir Interaction Between Graphene Plates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07757)
*Ahmad Alachkar,Philippe Brax,Pierre Brun*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究轴子暗物质（axion dark matter）在平行石墨烯（graphene）界面构成的平面腔（planar cavity）中诱发的电磁响应，推导出感应电场和压强的闭式解析表达式，发现压强在特定板间距下发生共振增强，且该共振结构受石墨烯化学势（chemical potential）和阻尼参数（damping parameter）的强烈调控。高掺杂、低耗散的石墨烯构型在共振条件下可显著放大轴子信号，有望用于探测轴子暗物质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轴子暗物质可在谐振腔系统中诱导可观测的电磁效应并修正卡西米尔相互作用（Casimir interaction）。石墨烯因其可调的电磁性质和可从第一性原理（first principles）在量子场论（quantum field theory）框架下微观建模的优势，成为研究这一效应的理想平台。作者旨在探索石墨烯基卡西米尔型构型能否为探测轴子诱发的电磁现象提供灵敏手段。

Method: 在均匀外磁场存在下，考虑有限温度、化学势和耗散，通过石墨烯电导率（graphene conductivity）对平行石墨烯界面构成的平面腔进行建模。基于量子场论方法，推导出轴子诱导电场及其产生的压强的闭式解析表达式。

Result: 得到压强在板间距 $d_n=(2πn-φ(r))/m_a$（$m_a$ 为轴子质量，$φ(r)$ 由反射系数 $r$ 决定）处发生共振增强。共振结构强烈依赖于石墨烯化学势和阻尼参数：增加掺杂（如通过栅极电压）可使共振峰变锐并放大轴子信号。将共振增强信号与传统卡西米尔背景对比，确定出实验相关参数区间，其中高掺杂、低耗散石墨烯构型在近共振条件下灵敏度最高。

Conclusion: 石墨烯基卡西米尔型构型可为探测轴子诱导电磁现象提供灵敏的实验平台，揭示了轴子电动力学（axion electrodynamics）、腔共振（cavity resonances）与低维系统材料性质之间的相互作用。

Abstract: Axion dark matter may induce observable electromagnetic effects in resonant cavity systems and potentially lead to modifications of the Casimir interaction. In this context, graphene represents an attractive platform owing to its tunable electromagnetic properties, and the fact that its electromagnetic response can be modelled microscopically from first principles within quantum field theory. The electromagnetic response induced by axion dark matter is investigated in a planar cavity consisting of parallel graphene interfaces in the presence of a homogeneous external magnetic field, incorporating finite temperature, chemical potential and dissipation through the graphene conductivity. Closed analytical expressions are obtained for the induced electric field and the resulting pressure. The pressure exhibits resonant enhancement at a series of plate separations satisfying $d_n=(2πn-φ(r))/m_a$, where $m_a$ is the axion mass and the phase $φ(r)$ is determined by the reflection coefficient $r$, which depends on the graphene conductivity evaluated at $ω=m_a$. The resonant structure is strongly influenced by the graphene chemical potential and damping parameter. In particular, increased doping, for example via a gate voltage, sharpens the resonances and amplifies the axion-induced signal. By comparing the resonantly enhanced signal with the conventional Casimir background, the parametric regimes in which the effect could become experimentally relevant are identified, with the strongest sensitivity obtained for highly doped low-dissipation graphene configurations operated near resonance. These results demonstrate that graphene-based Casimir-type configurations may provide a sensitive framework for probing axion-induced electromagnetic phenomena and highlight the interplay between axion electrodynamics, cavity resonances, and material properties in low-dimensional systems.

</details>


### [46] [Monte-Carlo solution of the Kondo model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07797)
*Nicolas Paris,Oscar Bouverot-Dupuis,Christophe Mora*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种离散模型，精确再现多通道近藤模型（multichannel Kondo model）并支持高效模拟。通过团簇蒙特卡洛（cluster Monte Carlo）算法完全消除临界慢化（critical slowing down），直接获取宽参数范围内的普适交叉函数（universal crossover functions）与输运性质。该模型统一了弱耦合与强耦合描述，自然适用于大通道数、各向异性、一维相互作用导线及通道不对称等情况，并在电荷近藤器件中给出输运性质预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近藤模型（Kondo model）作为强关联电子研究中的核心量子杂质问题（quantum impurity problem），在多种实验平台上均有实现。然而传统方法在不同耦合极限下的描述相互割裂，且存在临界慢化等计算困难，亟需一种统一、高效的模拟方案。

Method: 引入一个离散模型（discrete model）精确再现多通道近藤模型，并采用团簇蒙特卡洛算法（cluster Monte Carlo algorithms）进行模拟，从而完全消除临界慢化效应。

Result: 该模型在宽参数范围内直接获取了普适交叉函数与输运性质；成功统一了弱耦合（weak-coupling）与强耦合（strong-coupling）两种传统上互补的描述；自然兼容大通道数、各向异性、一维相互作用导线及通道不对称等情形。

Conclusion: 所提离散模型与团簇蒙特卡洛方法为多通道近藤模型提供了高效且统一的模拟框架，并能在电荷近藤器件（charge-Kondo devices）等实际系统中预测输运性质。

Abstract: The Kondo model is a paradigmatic quantum impurity problem realized in a wide variety of experimental platforms and central to the study of strongly correlated electrons. We introduce a discrete model that exactly reproduces the multichannel Kondo model and demonstrate that it can be simulated efficiently. Using cluster Monte Carlo algorithms, we completely eliminate critical slowing down, providing direct access to universal crossover functions and transport properties across a broad range of parameters. Remarkably, the same model captures both the weak- and strong-coupling regimes, unifying descriptions traditionally derived in complementary limits and revealing their common origin. Our method naturally accommodates large channel numbers, anisotropy, interacting one-dimensional leads, and channel asymmetry, yielding predictions for transport properties in charge-Kondo devices.

*D. van der Bovenkamp,C. S. A. Müller,B. D. Pantiru,I. Bošnjak,M. Cignoni,Q. Torrent Nicolau,M. E. Bal,S. Wiedmann,J. Ridderbos,F. A. Zwanenburg*

Method: 通过改变铝栅厚度来调控沟道中的应变，利用舒布尼科夫-德哈斯（Shubnikov-de Haas）振荡分析子带结构的出现，并进行温度依赖的磁输运测量以提取回旋质量（cyclotron mass）。

Conclusion: 测得的回旋质量偏离了理想重空穴（HH）/轻空穴（LH）图像的理论预期，表明价带结构受到量子限域、应变和 HH-LH 混合三个因素的共同影响。

Abstract: We show the effect of gate-induced strain on the valence band of a silicon (Si) metal oxide semiconductor (MOS) confined two-dimensional hole gas (2DHG). Increasing aluminum gate thickness, and thereby the strain in the channel, results in the onset of a second subband contributing to Shubnikov-de Haas oscillations. Temperature-dependent magnetotransport measurements reveal distinct cyclotron masses of $m_c^*=(0.36\pm0.04)m_0$ and $m_c^*=(0.49\pm0.02)m_0$. ### [48] [Interplay of Quasiperiodic Criticality and the Non-Hermitian Skin Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08294)
*Zhangyuan Chen,Xianqi Tong,Xiaosen Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了Hatano-Nelson模型（准周期调制跳跃振幅）中非互易性与准周期性的联合作用，通过非幺正规范变换得到Lyapunov指数的精确解析表达式，揭示了周期性边界条件下的准周期临界态与开边界条件下的非厄米趋肤效应之间的对应关系，并将其推广至长程跳跃与多带模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准周期晶格可支持临界本征态，而非厄米晶格中的非互易跳跃可诱导非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect）。本文旨在探究准周期性、调制非互易性与边界条件如何共同塑造临界区间的非厄米趋肤效应。

Method: 采用Hatano-Nelson模型，左右跳跃振幅具有不相等的准周期调制强度以引入非互易性。通过非幺正规范变换（non-unitary gauge transformation）将非厄米系统映射为厄米准周期系统，在热力学极限下得到Lyapunov指数（Lyapunov exponent）的精确解析表达式。在周期性边界条件下，利用逆参与率（inverse participation ratio）和有限尺寸标度分析（finite-size scaling analysis）识别准周期临界区间。

Result: 在周期性边界条件下处于准周期临界态的参数区间，在开边界条件下可展现出非厄米趋肤效应。该现象在代表性长程跳跃模型（long-range hopping models）和多带扩展（multiband extensions）中也被观测到。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一个可解析控制的视角，说明准周期性、调制非互易性与边界条件如何共同塑造临界区间的非厄米趋肤效应。

Abstract: Quasiperiodic lattices can host critical eigenstates, whereas nonreciprocal hopping in non-Hermitian lattices can induce non-Hermitian skin effect. In this work, we investigate localization phenomena in a Hatano--Nelson model with quasiperiodically modulated hopping amplitudes, where nonreciprocity arises from unequal modulation strengths of the right and left hoppings. Using a non-unitary gauge transformation, we map the non-Hermitian system into a Hermitian quasiperiodic system and obtain an exact analytical expression for the Lyapunov exponent in the thermodynamic limit. Under periodic boundary conditions, inverse participation ratios and finite-size scaling analysis are used to identify the quasiperiodic critical regimes. The comparison shows that parameter regimes hosting quasiperiodic critical states under periodic boundary conditions can exhibit the non-Hermitian skin effect under open boundary conditions. Furthermore, the non-Hermitian skin effect associated with quasiperiodic critical regimes is also observed in representative long-range hopping models and multiband extensions. Our results provide an analytically controlled perspective on how quasiperiodicity, modulated nonreciprocity, and boundary conditions jointly shape the non-Hermitian skin effect in critical regimes.

### [49] [Anomalous Reflection of Caustic Spin-Wave Beams in a Magnonic Waveguide](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08295)
*Franz Vilsmeier,Christian Back*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过实验证明，在各项异性介质中，焦散自旋波束（caustic spin-wave beams）的反射遵循一种与斯涅尔定律（Snell's law）根本不同的机制：反射波束由各向异性等频轮廓（anisotropic iso-frequency contour）上的焦散点跃迁（caustic-point transition）决定，而非由动量守恒决定；通过调节外磁场可连续控制反射过程与波束路由。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统波动在界面反射由斯涅尔定律描述，该定律源于界面平行方向动量守恒。然而，该定律是否适用于各向异性介质中的焦散波束（如自旋波束）尚不明确，因此需要实验验证和理论修正。

Method: 采用时间分辨克尔显微术（time-resolved Kerr microscopy）对钇铁石榴石（yttrium iron garnet, YIG）波导进行实验测量，同时通过改变外磁场的幅值和取向来调控反射过程。

Result: 反射波束由各向异性等频轮廓上的焦散点之间的跃迁决定，而非由动量守恒决定；反射载波波矢（carrier wave vector）和波前取向（wavefront orientation）的变化趋势与斯涅尔定律的预测相反。

Conclusion: 焦散点跃迁构成各向异性波束的一种独特反射定律，为可重构的磁子束流操控（magnonic beam steering）提供了新途径。

Abstract: Reflection of waves at interfaces is conventionally governed by Snell's law, which follows from conservation of momentum parallel to the interface. Here we show experimentally that caustic spin-wave beams in anisotropic media obey a fundamentally different reflection mechanism. Applying time-resolved Kerr microscopy to a yttrium iron garnet waveguide, we observe that reflected beams are selected by transitions between caustic points on the anisotropic iso-frequency contour rather than by momentum conservation. As a consequence, the reflected carrier wave vector and wavefront orientation exhibit trends opposite to those predicted by Snell's law. By tuning the magnitude and orientation of an external magnetic field, we continuously control the resulting reflection process and beam routing. Our results establish caustic-point transitions as a distinct reflection law for anisotropic wave beams and provide a route towards reconfigurable magnonic beam steering.

### [50] [Magnetic control of Goos-Hänchen shifts and group delay time in monolayer WSe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08315)

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过求解有效低能哈密顿量（effective low-energy Hamiltonian）并计算传输系数相位，系统研究了单层WSe₂在磁势垒（magnetic barrier）存在时，外磁场对古斯-汉欣位移（Goos-Hänchen shift, GH shift）和群延迟时间（group delay time, GDT）的调控作用，揭示了显著的旋-谷依赖（spin-valley-dependent）传输特性，为自旋电子学（spintronics）和谷电子学（valleytronics）中的纳米器件设计提供了新机制。

Method: 通过求解单层WSe₂的有效低能哈密顿量获得类狄拉克载流子（Dirac-like carriers）的传输特性，计算传输系数振幅后，从中提取传输系数的相位信息，进而得到GH位移和GDT。系统分析了磁场强度、入射能量、入射角和势垒宽度等参数的影响。

Result: 磁势垒对GH位移和GDT均产生强烈调制作用，呈现出振荡行为以及显著的旋-谷依赖传输特征。磁场能够选择性控制每个自旋和谷通道的横向位移（lateral shift）和穿行时间（traversal time），实现电子波包在空间和时间上的可调分离。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一种高度可控的费米子轨迹操控机制，为设计基于自旋和谷滤波的纳米器件开辟了道路，并对自旋电子学和谷电子学平台中的信息存储与处理具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: We study the influence of an external magnetic field on the Goos-Hänchen (GH) shift and the group delay time (GDT) in monolayer WSe$_2$ in the presence of a magnetic barrier. The transport properties of Dirac-like carriers are obtained by solving the effective low-energy Hamiltonian and evaluating the corresponding transmission amplitudes. The GH shift and the GDT are subsequently extracted from the phase of the transmission coefficient. We systematically analyze their dependence on the magnetic field strength, incident energy, angle of incidence, and barrier width, with particular emphasis on the spin and valley degrees of freedom associated with the $K$ and $K'$ valleys. Our results show that the magnetic barrier strongly modulates both the GH shift and the GDT, leading to oscillatory behavior and pronounced spin-valley-dependent transport characteristics. Remarkably, the magnetic field enables selective control of the lateral shift and traversal time of carriers for each spin and valley channel, allowing for tunable spatial and temporal separation of electronic wave packets. This provides a mechanism for manipulating fermionic trajectories after transmission through the barrier in a highly controllable manner. Such tunability opens promising avenues for designing nanoscale devices based on spin and valley filtering, as well as for potential applications in information storage and processing within spintronic and valleytronic platforms.

### [51] [Charge carrier flow through trimmed graphene nanoribbon junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08471)
*Julien Leuenberger,Kristiāns Čerņevičs,Oleg V. Yazyev*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究如何在石墨烯纳米带（GNR）中设计最优尺寸的纳米结，通过修剪连接尖端且不显著影响导电性能，实现以最小空间占用连接以一定角度相交的石墨烯纳米带。研究发现尖端概率密度电流可忽略，并提出一个基于扶手椅边与锯齿边比率预测电导的简单模型。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过修剪石墨烯纳米带结（junction）的边缘，研究在不显著改变电子特性的前提下，实现以一定角度连接石墨烯纳米带的最佳尺寸设计。具体分析结尖端处的概率密度电流（probability density current），评估去除部分原子对电导（conductance）的影响，并建立电导与扶手椅边（armchair edge）和锯齿边（zigzag edge）比例之间的关系模型。

Result: 研究表明，结尖端处的概率密度电流可忽略不计，这意味着可以安全地移除尖端处的部分原子而不显著改变电导。更大范围的修剪会影响导电通道（conductance channels），导致电导主要由扶手椅边与锯齿边的比例决定。

Conclusion: 提出一个简单模型，将扶手椅边与锯齿边的比例与电导联系起来，为设计最小空间的石墨烯纳米带连接结提供了理论指导，有助于推动全石墨烯纳电子电路（nanoelectronics paradigm）的实现。

Abstract: As Moore's law approaches its fundamental limits, the development of nanoelectronic devices using low-dimension materials has become a promising avenue for further miniaturization and performance improvements. Among the various novel materials, graphene nanoribbons (GNRs) have emerged as particularly attractive candidates due to their unique electronic properties, opening up a whole new nanoelectronics paradigm consisting of circuits made entirely of graphene. However, due to the technical constraints that naturally arise when working on a two-dimensional plane, the design of efficient nanoelectronic components with a minimal spatial footprint remains a significant challenge. In particular, connecting various components can be a real architectural challenge, comparable to that of the first printed circuit boards. This paper investigates strategies for designing optimal-sized nanoribbon junctions which allow connecting GNRs at an angle, by trimming the junction edge while maintaining favorable electronic properties. Specifically, we show that the probability density current at the tip of junctions is negligible, implying that a selection of atoms can safely be removed without significantly altering the conductance. More generally, we demonstrate that larger trimmings have impacts on the conductance channels, resulting in a conductance that is mainly dictated by the ratio of armchair and zigzag edges. Finally, we propose a simple model relating this ratio to the conductance.

### [52] [The Radial Distribution Functions of Nanofluids: Molecular Dynamics Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08527)
*Özlem Öztürk*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文采用分子动力学模拟方法，研究了由非刚性（软）纳米颗粒与聚合物熔体（基液）构成的聚合物纳米流体的径向分布函数（RDF）和角度依赖径向分布函数（ARDF），并分析了不同尺寸纳米颗粒在基液中的形状稳定性。结果表明，28原子纳米颗粒在升温时发生形状不稳定，双层同心球壳结构瓦解；而42和56原子纳米颗粒则保持形状稳定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米流体是下一代液体，由纳米级或亚纳米级固体颗粒稳定悬浮于基液中构成。本文旨在利用分子动力学模拟方法，研究由非刚性（soft）纳米颗粒与聚合物熔体（polymer melt）组成的聚合物纳米流体的一维和三维角度依赖的径向分布函数，并据此探究纳米颗粒的形状稳定性。

Method: 采用分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulation）方法，考察三种不同尺寸（28、42和56个原子）的非刚性纳米颗粒。分别在基液内和无聚合物介质两种条件下进行不稳定性分析，并计算径向分布函数（radial distribution function, RDF）和角度依赖径向分布函数（angle dependent radial distribution function, ARDF）。

Result: 当系统温度从 T=1.2 升至 T=1.8 时，28原子纳米颗粒在基液内部表现出形状不稳定性，其双层同心球壳结构破裂，内外壳之间的真空消失。相比之下，42原子和56原子纳米颗粒在升温过程中保持同心壳层结构，在基液内具有形状稳定性；同时发现纳米颗粒与基液之间的亲和力（affinity）降低也会影响稳定性。

Conclusion: 纳米颗粒的尺寸是决定其在聚合物基液中形状稳定性的关键因素：小尺寸（28原子）颗粒易发生结构失稳，而较大尺寸（42和56原子）颗粒能维持同心球壳结构的完整性。这一发现对聚合物纳米流体的设计与应用具有指导意义。

Abstract: Nanofluids, which are composed of insoluble, stable, and well-dispersed solid particles of nanoscale and/or subnanometer sizes suspended in a base liquid, are the next generation of liquids of today. The purpose of this paper is to investigate the one dimensional and three dimensional angle dependent radial distribution functions RDF and ARDF of polymeric nanofluids made up of nonrigid (soft) nanoparticles and a polymer melt (base fluid) using the molecular dynamics simulation approach and to search the shape stabilities by using these results. For this purpose, we use the nanoparticles of three different sizes: 28, 42, and 56 particles. We research them both within the base fluid and without this polymeric medium for instability analysis. We found that the nanoparticles with 28 atoms show the shape instability inside the base fluid when we increase the system temperature from T=1.2 to T=1.8 and hence, the structure of two concentric spherical shell of the nanoparticle breaks down and as a result the empty vacuum between these inner and the outer shells disappears. In contrast to this findings, the nanoparticles with 42 and 56 atoms show the shape stability inside the base fluid by preserving their concentric shell structures when we rise the system temperature and decrease the affinity between the nanoparticles and the base liquid medium.

</details>


### [53] [Curvature-Controlled Topological Magnon Phases in a Folded Kagome Lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08580)
*Seif Alwan,Jonas Fransson*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文证明kagome晶格中两个共角三角形的折叠角度所编码的几何曲率可作为拓扑磁振子相（topological magnon phase）的连续调节参量。在小折叠与倾角条件下，弓形耦合（bow-tie coupling）超过Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya（DM）相互作用，形成曲率主导的拓扑相区域，从而将几何曲率确立为拓扑磁子学（topological magnonics）的内在几何控制参量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索几何曲率能否作为连续调节参数控制拓扑磁振子相，特别是寻找在DM相互作用较弱或被对称性禁止的体系中驱动拓扑磁振子效应的替代机制。

Method: 基于包含交换作用、DM相互作用和标量手性（scalar chirality）的高阶弓形耦合的扩展自旋哈密顿量，推导出依赖于折叠角和自旋倾角的、由手性介导的跳跃振幅（chirality-mediated hopping amplitude）。

Result: 在小折叠角和自旋倾角条件下，弓形耦合的强度超越DM相互作用，建立起曲率主导的拓扑相区域。表明几何曲率是拓扑磁振子相的内在几何控制参量。

Conclusion: 这项工作揭示了曲率驱动的拓扑磁振子相与手性诱导自旋选择性（chirality-induced spin selectivity, CISS）分子体系之间的直接类比，提出了跨尺度手性驱动输运的统一机制。该机制对DM作用弱或受六重螺旋轴对称性禁止的手性晶体（chiral crystals）尤为适用。

Abstract: We show that geometric curvature, encoded in the folding angle between two corner-sharing triangles on a kagome lattice, provides a continuous tuning knob for topological magnon phase. Starting from an extended spin Hamiltonian with exchange, Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya (DM) interaction, and a higher-order bow-tie coupling of scalar chiralities, we derive the chirality-mediated hopping amplitude, which depends on the folding and spin canting of the bow-tie triangles. At small folding and canting angles, the bow-tie coupling surpasses DM, establishing a curvature-dominated regime. These results establish curvature as an intrinsic geometric control parameter for topological magnonics and reveal a direct analogy with chirality-induced spin selectivity in molecular systems, pointing to a unified mechanism for chirality driven transport across scales. The mechanism is particularly relevant for chiral crystals where the DM interaction is weak or forbidden by symmetry, as in systems with a six-fold screw axis.

### [54] [Valley Hall viscosity in the integer quantum Hall phases of (2+1)D Dirac materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08648)
*M. Selch*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在零温下计算了类石墨烯体系中Lorentz不变的整数量子霍尔相的谷分辨霍尔粘度（valley-resolved Hall viscosity），发现先前报道的单谷霍尔粘度发散可通过Wigner-Weyl微积分中的能量本征函数表示被正规化，并将相对论性Hoyos-Son公式推广到单个谷，同时评估了偏置Bernal双层石墨烯中的谷（差）霍尔粘度，讨论了其在单层/双层石墨烯及VI族过渡金属硫族化合物（TMD）器件中的非局域输运测量前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作（Phys. Rev. B 100, 115421, 2019）发现，在Semenoff型半导体石墨烯类体系的Lorentz不变整数量子霍尔相中，单谷粘性霍尔贡献存在发散，只有谷求和后的霍尔粘度是有限的。本文旨在解决该发散问题，并建立谷分辨的霍尔粘度（valley-resolved Hall viscosity）的正确定义和计算方法。

Method: 采用基于Wigner-Weyl微积分（Wigner-Weyl calculus）的等效格林函数形式（Green function formulation）替代原有的久保形式（Kubo formalism），在能量本征函数和本征值的表示下计算谷分辨霍尔粘度。同时结合局部霍尔电导（local Hall conductivity）及其一阶非局域修正，将经验性的相对论Hoyos-Son公式（relativistic Hoyos-Son formula）推广至单个谷。

Result: 先前识别的单谷粘性霍尔发散在能量本征函数和本征值的恰当表示下被正规化为有限值。原Hoyos-Son公式（适用于Galilean不变流体）及其相对论版本（适用于Dirac材料）在整数量子霍尔相中结构相同，均可由局部电响应和粘性霍尔响应（viscous Hall response）表达。此外，在低能手征费米子近似（chiral fermion low energy approximation）下，计算了偏置Bernal双层石墨烯中的谷（差）霍尔粘度（valley(-difference) Hall viscosity）。

Conclusion: 谷分辨霍尔粘度在适当的表示下是有限且定义良好的；Hoyos-Son公式可推广至单谷层次，其结构在Galilean不变流体和Dirac材料中一致。该结果为在单层/双层石墨烯及VI族TMD（group-VI TMD）器件中通过非局域输运测量谷霍尔粘度（valley Hall viscosity）提供了理论依据和前景展望。

Abstract: We calculate the valley-resolved Hall viscosity for Lorentz-invariant integer quantum Hall phases in Semenoff-semiconducting graphene-like systems at zero temperature. The Kubo formalism based discussion reported in Phys. Rev. B 100, 115421 (2019) revealed the divergence of single valley viscous Hall contributions for this case with only a valley-summed Hall viscosity being finite and therefore well-defined. Our approach to the Hall viscosity calculation is based on an equivalent Green function formulation within Wigner-Weyl calculus. We find that the previously identified divergence seems to be regularized to a finite value in a proper representation of the valley-resolved Hall viscosity in terms of energy eigenfunctions and eigenvalues. Together with the local Hall conductivity and its first nonlocal correction, reported as well in Phys. Rev. B 100, 115421 (2019), we extend the empirical relativistic Hoyos-Son formula to individual valleys. Both the original Hoyos-Son formula for Galilean invariant fluids and its relativistic extension to Dirac materials are found to be structurally identical for integer quantum Hall phases and expressible in terms of local electric and viscous Hall responses. In addition we evaluate the valley(-difference) Hall viscosity for biased Bernal bilayer graphene in the chiral fermion low energy approximation. Prospects of measuring valley Hall viscosity in nonlocal transport for mono- and bilayer graphene- and group-VI TMD-based devices are discussed.

</details>

Abstract: Magnetophonon resistance oscillations (MPR) associated with the resonant scattering of electrons by optical phonons at temperatures of 77-240 K, as well as resonant scattering of electrons by acoustic phonons (PIRO) at temperatures of 10-25 K, were investigated in the same samples featuring a GaAs quantum well and AlAs/GaAs superlattice barriers doped with Si. The study of MPR demonstrated that resonant electron scattering occurs on bulk longitudinal optical phonons and does not depend on the dimensionality of the system or inter-subband transitions in systems with two subbands of size quantization. However, the amplitude of the oscillation with number $N=1$ in two-dimensional structures depends on the interplay of scattering mechanisms, which, in turn, is influenced by the structure of the system. As for PIRO, in samples with two size quantization subbands, resonant electron scattering by longitudinal acoustic phonons is observed against the background of inter-subband transitions (MISO), leading to their interference.

### [56] [Quantum-Geometric Design of Lattice Generalized Landau Levels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08702)
*Bohao Li,Fengcheng Wu*

TL;DR: 本文设计了具有定制化量子几何（quantum geometry）的晶格模型，包括满足积分迹条件的广义朗道能级（Landau levels, LLs）和具有理想量子几何的高陈数能带（higher-Chern bands）。通过精确对角化，在三种子晶格模型中发现了分数量子反常霍尔效应，包括广义第零朗道能带中的分数量子陈绝缘体、N=4模型广义第一朗道能带中的Moore-Read态，以及N=3模型理想高陈能带中多种相互作用驱动的拓扑相。该工作为在晶格系统中实现朗道能级及超越朗道能级物理提供了基于量子几何的路线。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，基于量子几何（quantum geometry）的晶格模型设计能够有效在晶格系统中实现朗道能级物理及超越朗道能级的新奇物态，为实空间晶格中实现分数化拓扑序（fractional topological order）提供了新的途径。

Abstract: We design lattice models with tailored quantum geometry, including generalized Landau levels (LLs) satisfying the integrated trace condition and higher-Chern bands with ideal quantum geometry. Our models with $N=2$, $3$, and $4$ sublattices include a generalized Haldane model ($N=2$ honeycomb lattice model) with Gaussian-decaying hoppings realizable in twisted bilayer MoTe$_2$, and $N \geq 3$ models with exponentially decaying hoppings. Informed by quantum geometry, our work provides a pathway for lattice realizations of Landau-level and beyond-Landau-level physics.

### [57] [Competing Chern states revealed by quasiparticle charging in moiré rhombohedral graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08710)
*Hongyuan Li,Zuhan Geng,Junseok Seo,Chenxi Xu,Yifan Jiang,Shenyong Ye,Zhenqi Hua,Jiabin Xie,Lujin Min,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Kenji Yasuda,Xiaomeng Liu,Long Ju,Jie Shan,Kin Fai Mak*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过介观反点（antidot）器件中的准粒子充电探测和体态电阻测量，研究了moiré菱方石墨烯（mRG）中分数陈绝缘体（FCI）随温度降低演化为扩展量子反常霍尔背景的机制。结果表明，该演化并非由边缘态未平衡导致，而是源于体态中从FCI到广义反常霍尔晶体的热力学相变，排除了边缘态平衡假说。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Moiré材料中分数陈绝缘体（FCI）在低温下演化为扩展量子反常霍尔背景的机制尚不明确：该现象究竟是由FCI边缘态未能达到平衡引起，还是由体态中从FCI到广义反常霍尔晶体的本征相变所致？这一问题亟待解决。

Method: 使用介观mRG反点（antidot）器件探测准粒子充电行为，并结合体态电阻测量。两种方法均对体态敏感，可排除边缘态效应的干扰。在填充因子ν=1和2/3的陈态（Chern states）下，通过隧穿测量确定准粒子电荷；在ν=2/3附近测量体态电阻的温度依赖性。

Result: 在低温下，填充因子ν=1和2/3的陈态中，隧穿至mRG反点显示准粒子携带单电子电荷。ν=2/3附近的体态电阻温度依赖性测量进一步表明，在约150 mK以下存在从FCI到广义反常霍尔晶体的热力学相变。

Conclusion: 结果明确排除了边缘态平衡假说，支持体态相变场景。该工作建立了介观探测方法作为揭示moiré材料中竞争基态的有效手段，并为探测FCI中的分数化激发提供了基础。

Abstract: Moiré materials realize a versatile platform for exploring the physics of fractional Chern insulators (FCIs). The recently observed evolution from FCIs to an extended quantum anomalous Hall background upon lowering the electronic temperature in moiré rhombohedral graphene (mRG)8 raises a fundamental question: Is it caused by a failure to equilibrate the edge states of an FCI or by a genuine phase transition in the bulk from an FCI to a generalized anomalous Hall crystal? Here we address this question by probing quasiparticle charging in a mesoscopic mRG antidot device and by bulk resistance measurements, both of which are bulk-sensitive and free from complications from edge states. Tunneling to the mRG antidot reveals quasiparticles carrying one electron charge for both Chern states at filling factors ν=1 and 2/3 at low temperatures. Temperature dependence measurements of the bulk resistance near ν=2/3 further suggest a thermodynamic phase transition from an FCI to a generalized anomalous Hall crystal at temperatures below about 150mK. The results clearly exclude the edge state equilibration scenario and favor the phase transition scenario. Our work establishes mesoscopic probes as a powerful approach to uncover competing ground states in moiré materials and provides a basis for probing fractionalized excitations in FCIs.

</details>

### [58] [Braiding structures on categorical multi-Interval Jones-Wassermann subfactor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08296)
*Zhengwei Liu,Yuze Ruan*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文为多区间 Jones-Wassermann 子因子平面代数构造了辫结构，并基于此给出了子因子自对偶性的新证明；进一步证明这些辫结构诱导了平衡超椭圆映射类群的射影酉表示，从而编码了底层范畴的非平凡高亏格数据；作为应用，通过平面代数的 2-盒傅里叶对偶导出了广义 Verlinde 公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解幺半模融合范畴（unitary modular fusion category）在高亏格（higher genus）曲面上的非平凡表示，是拓扑量子场论和弦论中的核心问题；现有方法对多区间子因子平面代数上的辫结构缺乏系统构造，且 Verlinde 公式的推导尚未在此框架下与傅里叶对偶（Fourier duality）建立明确联系。

Method: 采用平面代数（planar algebra）方法，在 Jones-Wassermann 子因子（subfactor）框架下显式构造辫结构（braiding structures）；利用该结构重新证明子因子的自对偶性（self-duality）；通过分析辫结构在超椭圆映射类群（superelliptic mapping class group）作用下的表现，建立射影酉表示（projective unitary representation）；将广义 Verlinde 公式表述为 2-盒平面代数的傅里叶对偶。

Result: 成功为多区间 Jones-Wassermann 子因子平面代数构造了辫结构；给出了子因子自对偶性的新证明；证明了这些辫结构诱导了平衡超椭圆映射类群（balanced superelliptic mapping class group）的射影酉表示；进而证明了这些结构编码了底层幺半模融合范畴的非平凡高亏格数据；作为应用，通过 2-盒傅里叶对偶推导出广义 Verlinde 公式。

Conclusion: 平面代数框架下的辫结构能够系统地编码幺半模融合范畴的高亏格信息，并建立子因子理论与映射类群表示之间的桥梁；广义 Verlinde 公式在此框架下自然呈现为傅里叶对偶，进一步揭示了平面代数结构与拓扑量子场论之间深刻的联系。

Abstract: In this paper, we construct braiding structures on the multi-interval Jones-Wassermann subfactor planar algebra associated with any unitary modular fusion category. Utilizing this construction, we provide a new proof of the self-duality of these subfactors. Furthermore, we demonstrate that these braidings induce a projective unitary representation of the balanced superelliptic mapping class group; consequently, these structures effectively encode the non-trivial higher-genus data of the underlying category. As an application of this correspondence, we derive a generalized Verlinde formula as 2-box Fourier duality of the planar algebra.

</details>

### [59] [Gravitational perturbations of a regular T-duality inspired black hole: Quasinormal modes, excitation factors, and time-domain evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07715)
*Bekir Can Lütfüoğlu,Mardon Abdullaev,Javlon Rayimbaev,Shokhzod Jumaniyozov,Shavkat Karshiboev*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了由非局域T-对偶性启发零点长度（zero-point length）及其引力自能产生的中性规则黑洞的轴向引力扰动。利用高阶WKB-Padé方法和时域演化计算了准正规模式（quasinormal modes），发现零点长度增大会使ADM标度频率的实部升高，从而加快环豫（ringdown）振荡速度，而阻尼率的变化则较为平缓。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在理解由非局域T-对偶性零点长度生成的中性规则黑洞（regular black hole）在引力扰动下的动力学行为，特别是零点长度对环豫阶段振荡特性的影响。

Method: 采用高阶WKB-Padé方法计算基本准正规模式及多个泛音（overtones），并通过直接时域演化验证主导模式；同时计算激发因子（excitation factors）。

Result: 零点长度开启后，对于ℓ=2,3,4的引力模式，ADM标度频率的实部增大，环豫振荡加快；阻尼率先小幅增加，后在最大变形值附近减小；激发因子的幅度变化远弱于准正规频率。

Conclusion: 零点长度导致的规则核（regular core）替代了点源，有效势垒（effective potential barrier）随变形参数增大而升高，这解释了频率实部增大及阻尼率的非单调变化行为。

Abstract: We study axial gravitational perturbations of the neutral regular black hole generated by a non-local, T-duality-inspired zero-point length and the associated gravitational self-energy. In this geometry, the usual point source is replaced by a regular core, and the zero-point length controls the departure from the Schwarzschild limit. We compute the fundamental quasinormal modes and several overtones using high-order WKB--Padé methods, and we verify the dominant mode via direct time-domain evolution. When the zero-point length is turned on, the real parts of the ADM-scaled frequencies increase for the gravitational modes with $\ell=2,3,4$, so the ringdown oscillates faster than in the Schwarzschild limit. The damping rates change more gradually: they initially increase slightly and then decrease near the largest deformation values considered here. This behavior is consistent with the effective potential, whose barrier becomes higher as the deformation parameter increases. We also compute the corresponding excitation factors and find that their magnitudes vary much less strongly than the quasinormal frequencies.

</details>


### [60] [Deformed Compact Objects in General Relativity and Modified Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07736)
*Jonathan Tejeda Quartuccio*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文系统研究了中子星（neutron stars）和奇异星（strange stars）在广义相对论（General Relativity）及其扩展框架（D-TOV 形式与 f(R,T) 引力）下的流体静力学平衡（hydrostatic equilibrium），发现有效形变参数 D 和迹相关物质-几何耦合（trace-dependent matter-geometry coupling）会显著改变致密星的质量-半径关系和最大支撑质量。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文从广义相对论中的标准 TOV（Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff）方程出发，引入了一个单参数有效形变方案，建立了形变 TOV（D-TOV）形式体系，并将流体静力学平衡框架推广至 f(R,T) 引力理论。采用 GM1 状态方程（equation of state）、MIT 袋模型（MIT Bag Model）以及多方状态方程（polytropic equation of state）来描述中子星和奇异星，并数值计算了平衡序列。

Result: 在广义相对论下，形变参数 D 显著影响整体星体性质：扁球（oblate）构型通常支撑更大的质量和半径，而长球（prolate）构型导致质量更小、更致密的恒星。在优化和线性 f(R,T) 模型中，迹依赖的物质-几何耦合进一步改变了质量-半径关系和最大支撑质量（maximum supported mass）。

Conclusion: 结果表明，有效形变和迹依赖的物质-几何耦合能够显著影响致密星的平衡结构，这为拓展对致密天体在非标准引力和形变几何下的理解提供了重要依据。

Abstract: Neutron stars and related compact objects are unique laboratories for probing matter at supranuclear densities and gravity in the strong-field regime. In this thesis, we investigate the hydrostatic equilibrium of compact stars in different geometric and gravitational scenarios, combining relativistic stellar structure, dense-matter microphysics, and numerical modeling. We derive the standard Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equation in General Relativity, introduce an effective one-parameter deformation scheme leading to the deformed TOV (D-TOV) formalism, and extend the hydrostatic equilibrium framework to f(R,T) gravity.
  Using these structure equations, we compute equilibrium sequences for neutron stars and strange stars described by the GM1 equation of state, the MIT Bag Model, and a polytropic equation of state. In General Relativity, the deformation parameter D significantly affects the global stellar properties: oblate configurations generally support larger masses and radii than the spherical case, while prolate configurations lead to less massive and more compact stars. In optimized and linear f(R,T) models, trace-dependent matter-geometry couplings further modify the mass-radius relation and the maximum supported mass. Overall, the results indicate that effective deformation and trace-dependent matter-geometry coupling can significantly affect the equilibrium structure of compact stars.

### [61] [Systematic Light Propagation Bias from the Heliosphere and Its Impact on the Hubble Tension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07741)
*Behnam Pourhassan,İzzet Sakallı,Sudhaker Upadhyay,Kairat Myrzakulov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出哈勃张力（Hubble tension）可能源于太阳系日球层（heliosphere, HS）环境对局域距离测量的系统性效应，并通过理论计算表明日球层效应可解释观测到的8–9%偏差中的约3–8%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 哈勃张力是现代宇宙学中最显著的矛盾之一：局域距离测量得到的哈勃常数$H_0 = 73.5 \pm 1.4$ km/s/Mpc，而宇宙微波背景辐射（cosmic microwave background, CMB）观测预测的$H_0 = 67.4 \pm 0.5$ km/s/Mpc，两者存在显著差异。本文旨在探索这种张力是否源于局域测量中的系统性效应。

Method: 作者提出日球层环境通过加热等离子体和高能中性原子（energetic neutral atoms, ENAs）在日球层顶（heliopause, HP）之外形成复杂介质，导致星际介质（interstellar medium, ISM）温度显著升高。这种热梯度和粒子环境可能系统性影响造父变星（Cepheid variables）和Ia型超新星（Type Ia supernovae, SNe Ia）的观测，从而偏置局域宇宙距离阶梯（cosmic distance ladder, CDL）的测量结果。作者基于此进行了理论计算。

Result: 理论计算显示，日球层效应最多可解释观测到的8–9%偏差中的约8%。在考虑各向异性（anisotropy）、部分校准抵消（partial calibration cancellation）和色散抑制（chromatic suppression）后，实际贡献范围约为3–8%。

Conclusion: 作者认为日球层环境造成的系统性偏差可能是哈勃张力的重要来源，并提出了可用于验证这一假说的观测检验方案。

Abstract: The Hubble tension (HT) represents one of the most significant discrepancies in modern cosmology, with local distance measurements yielding $H_0 = 73.5 \pm 1.4$ km/s/Mpc while cosmic microwave background (CMB) observations predict $H_0 = 67.4 \pm 0.5$ km/s/Mpc. We propose that this tension arises from systematic effects introduced by our Solar System's heliospheric (HS) environment on local distance measurements. The HS creates a complex medium of heated plasma and energetic neutral atoms (ENAs) beyond the heliopause (HP), where interstellar medium (ISM) temperatures rise significantly. This thermal gradient and particle environment may systematically affect observations of Cepheid variables and Type Ia supernovae (SNe~Ia) used in the local cosmic distance ladder (CDL), biasing distance measurements and artificially inflating the measured Hubble constant. We present theoretical calculations showing how HS effects could account for up to $\sim 8\%$ of the observed 8--9\% discrepancy, with the realistic contribution lying in the $\sim 3$--$8\%$ range once anisotropy, partial calibration cancellation, and chromatic suppression are included, and discuss observational tests to validate this hypothesis.

### [62] [Observational Limits on Einasto Dark Matter Parameters from Event Horizon Telescope Images of Sgr A$^{*}$ and M87$^{*}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07752)
*A. Errehymy,S. Hansraj,C. Hansraj*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本工作利用事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope, EHT）对 M87* 和 Sgr A* 的阴影观测数据，基于 Einasto 型暗物质晕（dark-matter halo）包围的静态球对称黑洞模型，通过贝叶斯参数估计（Bayesian parameter estimation）对暗物质内晕结构给出了约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EHT 已获取超大质量黑洞的直接成像，为检验引力理论和探测黑洞周围暗物质分布提供了新窗口。任何延展质量分布（如暗物质晕）都会扰动光子环（photon-ring）区域的零测地线（null-geodesic），因此阴影测量可用于探测内晕结构。

Method: 从 Einasto 密度轮廓出发，构造插值度规函数 $f(r)=1-2M/r+2M_\infty \tilde{g}(r)$，该函数连接黑洞视界与渐近暗物质晕；在非自旋极限下分析光子势（photon-potential）和阴影半径；利用 EHT 测量的无量纲阴影直径 $d_{\text{sh}}$ 进行贝叶斯参数估计。

Result: 对于 Sgr A*，结合恒星轨道质量先验，在 $1σ$ 置信水平下给出 $\varrho_0 \lesssim 10^{-11},M_\odot/\text{pc}^3$；对 M87* 的约束因距离不确定性而较弱；Einasto 指数 $\tildeν$ 受约束较弱，表明 EHT 精度主要限制光子球面附近的质量聚集而非轮廓斜率。

Conclusion: EHT 的阴影数据能够对暗物质晕内部密度提供有效约束，但当前精度尚不足以确定轮廓斜率参数。未来 EHT 观测将进一步提高这些约束，并有助于区分不同暗物质模型。

Abstract: The Event Horizon Telescope (EHT) has provided images of the supermassive black-holes Sgr A$^{*}$ and M87$^{*}$, enabling direct tests of gravity. Any extended mass-distribution, such as a dark-matter halo, perturbs null-geodesics in the photon-ring regime, making shadow-measurements a probe of inner-halo structure. In this work, we investigate static, spherically-symmetric black-holes surrounded by Einasto-type dark-matter halos and derive constraints from EHT shadow-data. Starting from the Einasto density-profile with parameters ${\varrho_0, \tildeα, \tildeν}$, we construct a metric-function $f(r)=1-2M/r+2M_\infty \tilde{g}(r)$ that interpolates between the black-hole horizon and the asymptotic halo, following the approach of Xu et al. (2018) but adapted specifically to the Einasto scenario. We analyze the photon-potential, null-geodesics, and shadow-radius as functions of black-hole mass $M$, in the non-spinning limit. Using the dimensionless shadow-diameter $d_{\text{sh}}\equiv Dθ/M$ measured by the EHT -- $d_{\text{sh}}^{M87*}=11.0\pm1.5$ and $d_{\text{sh}}^{SgrA*}=9.5\pm1.4$ -- we perform Bayesian parameter-estimation to identify allowed regions in the Einasto parameter-space. Combined with the independently-measured black-hole masses from stellar-dynamics, our results place constraints on the inner dark-matter distribution: for Sgr A$^{*}$, adopting the stellar-orbit mass-prior, we find $\varrho_0 \lesssim 10^{-11},M_\odot/\text{pc}^3$ at $1σ$ confidence, while for M87$^{*}$ the bounds are weaker due to distance-uncertainties. The Einasto-index $\tildeν$ is weakly-constrained, indicating that EHT precision primarily limits the mass enclosed near the photon-sphere rather than the profile-slope. Future EHT observations will refine these constraints and distinguish between competing dark-matter descriptions.

### [64] [Singularity resolution and unitarity in two-dimensional dilaton black holes with negative central charge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07806)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在负总中心荷区域，经典曲率奇点被消除，代之以视界内渐近平直区域；外部霍金辐射通量得以保持，并与来自视界内的内辐射通量存在关联，该内通量包含一段短暂的负值区间。

Conclusion: 内部与外部辐射之间的关联提示系统可能保持幺正性，前提是相关零曲面（null surface）与塌缩物质轨迹保持有限仿射距离（affine distance）；但当前框架下能量平衡尚不完全自洽，仍需进一步改进。

Abstract: We study a one-loop corrected extension of the classical Callan-Giddings-Harvey-Strominger (CGHS) model of two-dimensional dilaton gravity. The effective action combines the non-local Polyakov action for matter fluctuations, a Polyakov-type term built from an auxiliary flat metric that implements Strominger's mechanism for the Faddeev-Popov reparametrization ghosts, and a local counterterm that simultaneously preserves the flatness of the auxiliary metric, ensures exact solvability, and keeps two-dimensional Minkowski spacetime as an exact solution of the backreacted equations. In the regime of negative total central charge, the classical curvature singularity is resolved and gives way to asymptotically flat regions inside the horizon. The exterior Hawking flux is preserved and turns out to be correlated with an internal radiation flux supported on null surfaces that approach null infinity from beyond the horizon; this internal flux, in particular, presents a short interval of negative values. These correlations point to the preservation of unitarity, provided the relevant null surfaces remain at a finite affine distance from the collapsing matter trajectory. Within the present formulation, however, a fully consistent energy balance cannot yet be established. We discuss possible strategies to overcome this issue.

### [65] [Causal Horizons, Geodesic Completeness and Stability in Slow Contraction Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07815)
*Mariam Khaldieh,Anna I. Rosenzweig,Paul J. Steinhardt*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文论证了具有半无限慢收缩（ekpyrosis）阶段的宇宙学模型具备多种特性，能够解决标准大爆炸膨胀或收缩德西特（de Sitter）阶段中面临的若干基本宇宙学问题，包括因果视界问题、过去测地线不完备性以及初始涨落起源问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的大爆炸膨胀模型或收缩德西特（de Sitter）阶段存在诸多基本宇宙学问题，如因果视界问题、过去测地线不完备性（Borde-Guth-Vilenkin定理的限制）以及引力熵过大等问题。本文旨在探索慢收缩（ekpyrosis）阶段是否能够提供一种替代方案，以同时规避上述问题。

Method: 论文通过理论分析，研究具有半无限慢收缩（semi-infinite phase of slow contraction）阶段的反弹宇宙学（bouncing cosmology）模型的动力学吸引子（attractor）性质。具体分析了该收缩阶段的过去吸引子（past attractor）渐近至闵可夫斯基空间（Minkowski space）以及未来吸引子（future attractor）的平坦、均匀、各向同性且外尔曲率（Weyl curvature）可忽略的特性。

Result: 慢收缩阶段具有一个稳定的过去吸引子，渐近至闵可夫斯基空间；同时具有一个稳定的、平坦、均匀、各向同性的未来吸引子，且外尔曲率（即可忽略的引力熵）极小。该模型不存在粒子视界（particle horizon），因而避免了因果视界问题。过去闵可夫斯基吸引子能在所有波长上产生真空样量子涨落（vacuum-like quantum fluctuations）的初始谱。由于沿过去定向测地线（past-directed geodesics）的平均膨胀率为非正，该模型规避了Borde-Guth-Vilenkin定理，满足过去测地线完备性（past geodesic completeness）。相比之下，收缩德西特空间存在有限粒子视界，且在标量场、物质或辐射存在时不稳定。

Conclusion: 包含半无限慢收缩阶段的宇宙学模型在理论上能够同时解决因果视界问题、初始涨落起源问题以及过去测地线不完备性等多项基础宇宙学难题，并且通过非奇异反弹（non-singular bounce）平滑地将收缩阶段的吸引子性质转化为膨胀阶段的初始条件，为构建更为完备的宇宙学模型提供了可行途径。

Abstract: We show that cosmological models with a semi-infinite phase of slow contraction (ekpyrosis) possess a combination of properties that can address several fundamental problems in cosmology, otherwise faced in contracting de Sitter phases or standard big bang expansion. In particular, slow contraction admits a stable past attractor asymptoting to Minkowski space, as well as a stable, flat, homogeneous, and isotropic future attractor with negligible Weyl curvature (and, therefore, negligible gravitational entropy). In bouncing cosmologies, this contracting attractor is terminated by a smooth, non-singular bounce that transforms the attractor properties at the end of contraction into the initial conditions for the subsequent expanding phase. Cosmologies incorporating a slow contraction phase have no particle horizon and therefore avoid the causal horizon problem. The past Minkowski attractor also generates an initial spectrum of vacuum-like quantum fluctuations on all wavelengths. Moreover, because the averaged expansion rate along past-directed geodesics is non-positive, models incorporating a semi-infinite phase of slow contraction also evade the Borde,Guth and Vilenkin theorem and are past geodesically complete. By contrast, contracting de Sitter space possesses a finite particle horizon and becomes unstable in the presence of scalar fields, matter, or radiation.

### [66] [Charging up regular black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07831)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的正则黑洞模型（如Bardeen和Hayward黑洞）在引入电荷后是否仍能保持正则性尚不明确，因此需要建立一般性框架来构造带电正则黑洞，并检验已有模型的正则性条件。

Method: 通过在球对称下推广爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦场方程，将爱因斯坦张量（Einstein tensor）变形为一个包含引力场至二阶导数的守恒张量，从而构造带电正则黑洞的一般解。随后应用该框架检验Bardeen和Hayward黑洞的带电版本的正则性，并提出改进度量。

Result: 带电正则黑洞的正则性条件比非带电情况更严格；Bardeen和Hayward黑洞的带电版本奇异；提出了保持正则性的改进版本。

Conclusion: 真空广义相对论（general relativity）解的正则化不足以推广到其他物理情形（如带电、旋转或存在物质场）中；这对构造更真实的（如考虑旋转和物质场）正则黑洞具有重要意义。

Abstract: We present a general construction of charged regular black holes as solutions of a generalization of the Einstein--Maxwell field equations in spherical symmetry in which the Einstein tensor is deformed into an identically conserved tensor containing up to second derivatives of the gravitational field. The generality of the construction allows us to define the field equations satisfied by generic regular black holes when becoming charged. The conditions that guarantee regularity of charged solutions are evaluated and shown to be more stringent than the regularity conditions for uncharged solutions. This implies, in particular, that the charged versions of the Bardeen and Hayward black holes become singular. Improved versions of the Bardeen and Hayward metrics that remain regular when charged are proposed. Our results indicate that regularizing the vacuum solutions of general relativity is, in general, not enough to yield regular solutions in other situations of physical interest. The implications that follow for the construction of realistic regular black holes, in which aspects such as rotation and the presence of matter fields are taken into account, are discussed.

TL;DR: 本文构建了一族静态、无视界、渐近平直的双喉（two-throat）虫洞族，由一个全局度规统一描述其几何、有效源、零测地线动力学、引力透镜及标量场传播，并在有限质量框架下推导了拓扑、平均能量条件、分支分辨强透镜与波透射特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在虫洞物理中，现有模型往往需要多片度规拼接或依赖特定物质场，缺乏一个由单一全局度规描述且具有有限质量的统一框架。本文旨在构造一族静态渐近平直的双喉虫洞，以便在有限质量设定下统一研究其几何、能量条件、强引力透镜（strong gravitational lensing）及波散射现象。

Method: 通过对四次嵌入轮廓（quartic embedding profile）施加有限质量形变得出对称双喉与中间赤道结构；利用 Misner–Sharp 质量定义两端渐近质量，借助 Einstein 张量构造单一守恒各向异性源；推导全局径向平均零泛函（radial averaged null functional）与零势（null potential）并完成相位分类；解析推导对数强偏转系数（logarithmic strong deflection coefficients），并通过数值积分验证；求解标量散射问题中的相位依赖势垒与共振透射。

Result: 双喉虫洞在两端渐近处 Misner–Sharp 质量趋于同一有限值；全局零势在正质量与非负红移形变参数下存在完整的相位分类：不稳定集合包括喉环（throat rings）、四离喉环（off throat rings）及带有亚临界赤道环的外环。在四环相位中，所有不稳定环具有相同碰撞参数（impact parameter），但内外分支的 Lyapunov 指数不同。跨喉（cross throat）的强偏转系数等于光线所经所有全局极大值的贡献之和。标量散射呈现相位相关的势垒与共振透射。

Conclusion: 该模型提供了一个有限质量的统一框架，使得虫洞的拓扑、平均能量条件、分支分辨的强透镜以及波透射均可从单一时空度规导出，为虫洞物理的解析与数值研究提供了新的基准模型。

Abstract: We introduce a static, horizonless, asymptotically flat two throat wormhole family in which one global metric determines the geometry, effective source, null dynamics, lensing, and test field propagation. A finite mass deformation of a quartic embedding profile produces two symmetric throats and an intermediate equator, while the associated Misner--Sharp mass tends to the same finite value at both asymptotic ends. The temporal sector yields the same mass parameter, and the Einstein tensor defines a single conserved anisotropic source. In addition to the local flare out identity, the complete radial averaged null functional is obtained exactly and is strictly negative. The global null potential admits a complete phase classification for all positive masses and nonnegative redshift deformation. Depending on the parameters, the global unstable set consists of throat rings, four off throat rings, or exterior rings accompanied by a subcritical equatorial ring. In the four ring phase, all unstable rings have the same impact scale but the inner and outer branches have different Lyapunov exponents. We derive the logarithmic strong deflection coefficients analytically and show that the cross throat coefficient is the sum of the contributions from every global maximum traversed by the ray. Direct numerical integration verifies these coefficients. The scalar scattering problem exhibits phase dependent barriers and resonant transmission. The resulting model provides a finite mass setting in which topology, averaged energy conditions, branch resolved strong lensing, and wave transmission are derived from one spacetime.

</details>


### [68] [Nonlinear hydrodynamics in spinning neutron stars: Theoretical universal relations and equilibrium solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07943)
*Hang Yu,Giorgio Nicolini,Shu Yan Lau,K. J. Kwon,Tejaswi Venumadhav,Nils Andersson,Pantelis Pnigouras,Fabian Gittins,Amlan Nanda*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用仿射近似（affine approximation）分析双中子星（binary neutron star, BNS）并合过程中包含非线性流体动力学相互作用的潮汐效应，推导至四波阶（four-wave order）的哈密顿耦合系数，发现三波相互作用系数完全由线性潮汐决定，但忽略它们会导致引力波波形出现显著系统误差，而四波相互作用在慢自旋中子星中仅提供小修正，在快自旋情形下则可用于研究绝热指数（adiabatic exponent）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双中子星并合过程中的潮汐效应对于引力波天文学至关重要，现有研究多集中于线性潮汐，而非线性流体动力学相互作用（nonlinear hydrodynamical interactions）对引力波波形的影响尚未被充分理解，因此需要更精确的理论模型来评估其重要性和系统性误差。

Method: 采用仿射近似（affine approximation）将受扰动的中子星视为椭球体（ellipsoid），在哈密顿量框架下解析推导至四波阶的f模（f-mode）与径向模（radial mode）之间的耦合系数，允许背景星体具有任意自转；同时采用混合方法（hybrid approach）同时捕捉牛顿流体动力学中预期的模共振（mode resonances），并在低频展开（low-frequency expansion）中与相对论计算结果保持一致。

Result: 三波（next-to-leading-order）相互作用系数完全由线性潮汐性质决定，不揭示中子星的新物理；忽略三波非线性潮汐会导致引力波波形的显著系统误差。单颗中子星中非线性潮汐相比于线性潮汐模型可累积约1.7弧度的相移（phase shift）；相似质量双星系统相移约翻倍。四波相互作用在慢自旋中子星中仅提供小修正；在快自旋中子星中，非线性离心驱动与四波非简谐性（four-wave anharmonicity）可探测与内部浮力（buoyancy）相关的绝热指数，而线性潮汐与三波潮汐无法探测该参数。非简谐性不会导致f模的共振锁定（resonance locking）。

Conclusion: 高阶非线性潮汐效应在双中子星引力波建模中不可忽略，特别是三波相互作用若缺失将引入显著系统误差；四波相互作用在慢自旋系统中影响较小，但在快自旋系统中提供了一个探测中子星内部结构的独特窗口，补充了线性与三波潮汐的探测盲区。

Abstract: We study tides during the inspiral of a binary neutron star (BNS) system, including nonlinear hydrodynamical interactions. Using an affine approximation that treats the perturbed NS as an ellipsoid, we analytically derive coupling coefficients among the f-modes and the radial mode to the four-wave order (i.e., next-to-next-to-leading order) in the Hamiltonian, allowing for arbitrary rotation of the background star. Our model reveals a series of universal relations from first-principles arguments. Besides the well-known relations, we show that the three-wave (next-to-leading-order) interaction coefficients are fully determined by the properties of the linear tide. Therefore, they do not probe new physics of the NS. Nonetheless, not including the three-wave nonlinear tides can lead to significant systematic errors in the gravitational waveform. We support this claim via a hybrid approach that simultaneously captures mode resonances expected in Newtonian hydrodynamics and is consistent with relativistic calculations in the low-frequency expansion. The nonlinear tide in a single NS can cause a phase shift of around 1.7 radians accumulated up to merger compared to the linear tide model; for a binary of similar masses, the phase shift is approximately doubled. Our calculation extends to four-wave interactions, which, for a slowly spinning NS, provide only small corrections and are subdominant compared to the tidal back-reaction on the orbit. For a rapidly rotating NS, the nonlinear centrifugal drive of the f-mode and the four-wave anharmonicity provides a window to study the adiabatic exponent related to internal buoyancy that cannot be probed by the linear and three-wave tides in slowly spinning systems. The anharmonicity cannot lead to resonance locking of the f-mode.

</details>


### [69] [Wave and particle probes of a regular T-duality-inspired black hole with gravitational self-energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07955)
*Alexey Dubinsky*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究一种受T-对偶性（T-duality）启发的非局域涂抹点质量所生成的非奇异黑洞几何，分析其零点长度（zero-point length）对强场区域标量场振动、粒子轨道及黑洞阴影等可观测信号的影响，发现该正则化修正会在波动传播、黑洞阴影和圆轨道物理中留下关联印记。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索一种非局域T-对偶性启发的点质量涂抹方法生成的非奇异黑洞几何，该几何具有有限零点长度且其ADM质量包含有限自能贡献，极值普朗克尺度残骸（remnant）被提议为可能的暗物质（dark matter）成分。作者旨在研究该时空如何影响两类熟悉的物理信号：大质量标量场的振动（ringing）以及粒子和光在视界附近的运动。

Method: 通过理论分析研究零点长度对强场区域的影响：在波动方面，分析大质量标量场的振荡频率与阻尼行为；在粒子运动方面，计算光子轨道（photon orbit）、最内稳定圆轨道（innermost stable circular orbit, ISCO）、黑洞阴影（shadow）、光子环频率（photon-ring frequency）以及轨道结合能（orbital binding energy）随零点长度的变化。

Result: 零点长度平滑了中心区域并改变了视界外的强场势（strong-field potential）。在波动方面，增大标量场质量会提高振荡频率并减弱阻尼，产生长寿命振动（long-lived ringing）。在粒子运动方面，增大零点长度使光子轨道和最内稳定圆轨道在物理质量单位下更紧凑，阴影变小，光子环频率增大，轨道结合能增加。

Conclusion: 相同的正则化修正会在波动传播、黑洞阴影和圆轨道物理中留下相互关联的印记，表明该非奇异黑洞几何具有可观测的物理后果。

Abstract: Recently it was shown that a non-local T-duality-inspired smearing of the point mass introduces a finite zero-point length, while the regularized Newtonian gravitational self-energy is promoted to an additional source for the spacetime. The result is a nonsingular black-hole geometry whose ADM mass contains a finite self-energy contribution and whose extremal Planck-scale remnant sector has been proposed as a possible dark-matter component. We study how this spacetime would affect two familiar physical signals: the ringing of a massive scalar field and the motion of particles and light near the horizon. The zero-point length smooths the central region and changes the strong-field potential outside the horizon. On the wave side, we find that making the scalar field heavier increases the oscillation frequency and makes the damping weaker, a behavior associated with long-lived ringing. On the particle side, increasing the zero-point length makes the photon orbit and the innermost stable circular orbit more compact in physical mass units. The corresponding shadow becomes smaller, the photon-ring frequency becomes larger, and the orbital binding energy increases. These results show that the same regularizing correction leaves related imprints in wave propagation, black-hole shadows and circular-orbit physics.

### [70] [Acceleration in 3D Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08030)
*Cendikiawan Suryaatmadja,Dong-han Yeom,Robert Mann*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在2+1维爱因斯坦-高斯-博内引力（Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet gravity）中发现了一类推广C度规的新精确解，该解具有六种子类结构，并在零耦合极限下恢复已知结果，同时包含两种先前未知的Anti-de Sitter (AdS)时空表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高维引力理论中寻找精确解是理解时空结构的重要途径，而爱因斯坦-高斯-博内引力作为含高阶曲率修正的理论，其精确解空间尚待探索。本文旨在推广已知的C度规（C-metric）至该理论框架，以发现新的解析解结构。

Method: 通过引入与无质量标量场（massless scalar field）耦合的乘性因子，将爱因斯坦-高斯-博内引力中的C度规进行推广。该因子依赖于单一变量，该变量取值决定时空结构。解被分类为三大类，每类进一步细分为六个不同子类，并重点分析了局域AdS子类的性质。

Result: 在每个大类中识别出六种不同的解子类；在零耦合极限下，所选子类不仅能良好定义并恢复C度规，还包含了两种先前未知的AdS时空表示。此外，发现了一个畴壁（domain wall）结构并明确了其能量条件（energy conditions），还得到了若干非常曲率（non-constant curvature）的新解。

Conclusion: 本文在2+1维爱因斯坦-高斯-博内引力中扩展了精确解的类别，揭示了C度规的丰富推广结构。部分新解（特别是非常曲率解）的物理解释仍有待进一步研究。

Abstract: We present a new class of exact solutions in Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet gravity in 2+1 dimensions that generalize the C-metric. This set of metrics equals the C-metric multiplied by a factor which, along with the massless scalar field, depends on a single variable whose value governs the structure of the spacetime. As in Einstein gravity there are three classes of metrics, but within each class we find six distinct subclasses of solutions. After discussing their basic structure, we concentrate only on one subclass that is locally AdS. In the zero-coupling limit, this subclass of solutions not only remains well defined and recovers the C-metric but also encompasses two previously unknown representations of the AdS spacetime. Furthermore, we establish the existence of a domain wall and delineate its energy conditions. We also find new classes of solutions of non-constant curvature, whose interpretation remains to be understood.

### [71] [An analytic model for a total process of gravitational collapse: From star to Schwarzschild black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08088)
*Sinya Aoki,Jorge Ovalle*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一个精确解析模型，完整描述了从无视界初始条件到黑洞形成的引力坍缩全过程，揭示了视界从微观尺度形成到宏观稳定的两阶段演化机制，并证明了裸奇点被视界增长因果隐藏，在无需奇异物质的条件下维护了弱宇宙监督假设（weak cosmic censorship）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建一个精确解析模型（exact analytical model），直接求解引力坍缩的完整动力学过程，追踪视界 H(t) 从微观尺度形成（~普朗克尺度）到宏观稳定化（尺度为 2M）的全时间演化。

Result: 模型识别出两个主要阶段：（i）动态视界增长——表观视界（apparent horizon）H(t) 在临界时刻 t_b 出现并增长至最终大小 h=2M，表明俘获面（trapped surface）可在有限时间内动态形成；（ii）裸奇点消解——在 r=0 处出现可积的里奇曲率奇点（Ricci curvature singularity，R^μ_ν∼r^{-2}），但被视界增长因果隐藏，无需引入奇异物质即可保持弱宇宙监督假设。

Conclusion: 该模型可能为研究量子-经典过渡（quantum-to-classical transition，H(t)∼ℓ_Planck）提供理论框架，有助于理解黑洞形成中从微观量子效应到宏观经典行为的衔接机制。

Abstract: We present an exact analytical model describing a complete gravitational collapse of matter from horizonless initial conditions to black hole formation, tracing the full evolution of the horizon $H(t)$ from its formation at microscopic scales to macroscopic stabilization. The solution reveals two main stages: (i) a dynamical horizon growth, where an apparent horizon $H(t)$ emerges at a critical time $t_b$ until reaching its final size $h=2 M$, demonstrating how trapped surfaces form dynamically in finite time, and (ii) a {naked-}singularity resolution, where an integrable Ricci curvature singularity ($R^μ_ν\sim r^{-2}$) develops at $r=0$, but remains causally hidden by the horizon growth, preserving weak cosmic censorship without exotic matter. The model could offer a framework to study the quantum-to-classical transition ($H(t) \sim \ell_{\rm Planck}$).

Result: 在量子框架下，场不再仅仅是粒子间力的中介者，而是成为一种自主的物理实体（autonomous physical entity）；引力在量子场论中引入了一些尚未被完全澄清的新特征。

Conclusion: 从超距作用到场论、再到量子场论中场的实体化转变，构成了引力概念演化的一条重要线索；本文旨在提供概念性的梳理，而非全面的综述。

Abstract: One of the technical anchors of JVN's research was the "action-at-a-distance" view of gravitational interaction, driven by "Mach's Principle" addressing the origin of inertia. This view exorcises the concept of a field as a mediator of force between separated "particles". However, within a quantum framework, the concept of field as a mediator transcends to field as an autonomous physical entity. Beginning with a comparison between direct action view and field theoretic view in classical framework and moving over to quantum framework, I sketch the strides made in quantum field theory including the new features brought in by gravity. This is intended as a conceptual trace rather than a review.

### [73] [Spectroscopic structure of Non-Hermitian $\mathcal{PT}$-Symmetric Klein--Gordon Fields in a Magnetized Cosmic String Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08148)
*Omar Mustafa,Abdullah Guvendi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了磁化宇宙弦时空中的非厄米$\mathcal{PT}$对称Klein-Gordon场，通过引入复非最小标量相互作用构造了一个条件精确可解的$\mathcal{PT}$对称Klein-Gordon振荡子模型，并发现非厄米$\mathcal{PT}$对称化会对允许能级施加一个上限，这一特性在相应厄米情形中并不存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索曲率时空（curved spacetime）中非厄米（non-Hermitian）相对论量子场的可解模型，为理解$\mathcal{PT}$对称性（$\mathcal{PT}$-symmetry）如何调控量子系统能谱提供解析框架。

Method: 在磁化宇宙弦时空中引入具有复磁荷$q=ie$的复非最小标量相互作用$\mathcal{F}_\mu=(0,\omega r+ib,0,0)$，构造了一个$\mathcal{PT}$对称Klein-Gordon振荡子（Klein-Gordon oscillator），并添加了复数形式的库仑相互作用（Coulombic interaction）和线性相互作用（linear interaction）。通过双合流Heun级数至多项式方法（biconfluent Heun series-to-polynomial approach）条件精确求解径向方程。在$\omega=0$极限下，进一步利用合流超几何级数/多项式（confluent hypergeometric series/polynomials）实现精确求解。

Result: 对于所考虑的两种$\mathcal{PT}$对称模型，非厄米$\mathcal{PT}$对称化会引入一个允许能量的上限（upper limit），而对应的厄米情形（通过映射$e=-i\tilde e$、$b=-i\tilde b$得到）则不存在此限制。

Conclusion: 该工作为在曲率时空中研究非厄米相对论量子场提供了一个解析可解的框架，并展示了$\mathcal{PT}$对称性在调控允许能谱中所起的关键作用。

Abstract: We investigate non-Hermitian $\mathcal{PT}$-symmetric Klein--Gordon (KG) fields in a magnetized cosmic string spacetime. A complex non-minimal scalar interaction, $\mathcal{F}_μ=(0,\mathcal{F}_{r},0,0)$ with $\mathcal{F}_{r}=ωr+ib\in\mathbb{C}$, indulged with a magnetic charge $q=ie$, is shown to introduce an effective $\mathcal{PT}$-symmetric Klein--Gordon oscillator supplemented by complex Coulombic and linear interactions. The resulting radial equation is shown to be conditionally exactly solvable using a biconfluent Heun series-to-polynomial approach. To observe non-Hermitian \(\mathcal{PT}\) symmetrization, we compare with the Hermitian counterpart by mapping $e=-i\tilde e \Rightarrow q\in \mathbb R$ and $b=-i\tilde b \Rightarrow \mathcal F_r\in \mathbb R$. In the limiting case $ω=0$, the system is shown to reduce to an exactly solvable non-Hermitian \(\mathcal{PT}\) symmetric Coulomb-type KG equation using confluent hypergeometric series/polynomials. Hereby, for both \(\mathcal{PT}\) symmetric models considered, we show that non-Hermitian \(\mathcal{PT}\) symmetrization introduces an upper limit for the allowed energies, unlike the corresponding Hermitian cases. These results provide an analytically tractable framework for exploring non-Hermitian relativistic quantum fields in curved spacetimes and demonstrate the role of $\mathcal{PT}$-symmetry in regulating the allowed spectrum.

</details>


### [74] [Static regular black holes in Horndeski theories: analytic no-go and nonanalytic obstructions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08228)
*Antonio De Felice,Shinji Tsujikawa*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究霍恩德斯基理论（Horndeski theories）中的正则黑洞，发现标量场在一般情形下会被无毛定理所排除：非退化平移对称理论中只有 Schwarzschild 解，且中心奇异；仅在特定的非解析边际情形（标量-高斯-博内耦合）中，毛状黑洞（hairy black holes）得以存在，但中心仍保持奇异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究霍恩德斯基引力理论中是否存在具有稳定视界和正则中心的“正则黑洞”（regular black holes），并明确标量场在何种条件下能够产生非平凡毛发（hair）。

Method: 采用静态球对称渐近平直度规并设标量场与时间无关，分别分析视界支（horizon branch，标量动能项 X 非零）和正则支（regular branch，X 在视界处为零）的动力学行为；利用端点解析性将标量方程约化为有限组泰勒系数，并对非解析边际情形进行分类讨论。

Result: 视界支普遍存在发散传播速度或鬼/梯度不稳定性（除非特殊退化）；正则支中，对于非退化平移对称理论，得到非微扰的流无毛定理（current no-hair theorem）——标量为常数，度规为 Schwarzschild，ADM 质量非零时中心奇异；对于非平移对称的正幂次耦合，相应排除适用于与 Schwarzschild 连续连接的微扰支；标量-高斯-博内（scalar-Gauss-Bonnet）链是唯一的边际非解析完备化，在此类完成中毛状黑洞可规避解析流步骤，但中心仍为奇异。

Conclusion: 霍恩德斯基理论中正则黑洞无法在常规解析条件下实现，标量毛发受到严格无毛定理的约束；唯一的例外是标量-高斯-博内耦合的边际非解析情形，但该类解仍不具备正则中心，因此无法满足正则黑洞的双重条件（稳定视界 + 正则中心）。

Abstract: Regular black holes in Horndeski theories must have stable horizons and regular centers. We study static, spherically symmetric, asymptotically flat configurations with a time-independent scalar. The horizon branch on which the scalar kinetic term $X$ remains nonzero is generically obstructed by divergent propagation speeds or ghost/gradient instabilities, aside from special degeneracies. On the regular branch, where $X$ vanishes at the horizon, analyticity at the relevant $X=0$ endpoints reduces the leading scalar equation to finite sets of Taylor coefficients. For nondegenerate shift-symmetric theories this gives a nonperturbative current no-hair theorem: the scalar is constant and the metric is Schwarzschild, hence centrally singular for nonzero ADM mass. For non-shift-symmetric positive-power couplings, the corresponding exclusion applies to the perturbative branch continuously connected to Schwarzschild. We also classify marginal nonanalytic departures: covariant regularity fixes the scalar-Gauss-Bonnet chain as the unique marginal nonanalytic completion. Hairy black holes in this completion evade the analytic current step but remain centrally singular.

</details>


### [75] [Quasi-bound states and late-time evolution of a massive fermion around a Reissner-Nordström black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08258)
*Guang-Shang Chen,Cheng-Bo Yang,Shou-Shan Bao,Yue-Liang Wu,Hong Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过构建耦合矩阵系统和格林函数，研究了带电黑洞周围大质量费米子的准束缚态（quasi-bound state）谱，给出了弱耦合情形下的改进解析表达式，分析了极端Reissner-Nordström情形的光滑极限行为，并在时域中揭示了中间晚期和极晚期不同衰减规律（t^{-5/6}指数抑制尾端与啁啾相位共存）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 带电黑洞周围的大质量费米子提供了原子束缚态及其弛豫的引力类比（gravitational analogue），但现有解析工具对弱耦合下准束缚态谱的描述不够精确，且晚期时域行为中不同机制（准束缚态贡献与幂律尾端）的共存与过渡尚未被充分厘清。

Method: 将径向方程表述为耦合矩阵系统（coupled matrix system），并构造满足视界处入波边界条件（ingoing boundary condition）与无穷远处衰减边界条件（decaying boundary condition）的格林函数（Green's function）。在弱耦合情形|qQ|∼mM<1下，采用矩阵匹配方案（matrix matching scheme）推导准束缚态谱。针对极端Reissner-Nordström黑洞独立处理并验证其非极端谱的光滑极限。对时域格林函数的支割线贡献进行渐近分析，并辅以直接时域模拟验证。

Result: 获得了改进的准束缚态谱解析表达式，包含精细结构修正（fine-structure correction）和更精确的衰变宽度（decay width）。极端情形被证明是非极端谱的光滑极限。中间晚期（1/m < t < 1/m³M²）呈现振荡幂律（oscillatory power-law）行为；极晚期（t > 1/m³M²）准束缚态激活，产生 t^{-5/6} exp(-η t^{1/3}) 的指数抑制衰减，并伴随啁啾相位（chirping phase），最终趋于 t^{-5/6} 渐近尾端。

Conclusion: 准束缚态贡献与经典幂律分量（power-law component）在晚期时域中共存且可被区分，直接时域模拟支持这一图景，表明该引力类比体系具有丰富的弛豫动力学结构。

Abstract: A massive fermion around a charged black hole provides a gravitational analogue of atomic bound states and their relaxation. In this work, we study this system by formulating the radial equation as a coupled matrix system and constructing the Green's function with ingoing boundary conditions at the horizon and decaying boundary conditions at infinity. In the weak-coupling scenario $|qQ|\sim mM<1$, a matrix matching scheme gives an improved analytic expression of quasi-bound-state spectrum, including fine-structure corrections and more accurate decay widths. The extremal Reissner-Nordström case ($|Q|=M$) is treated separately and shown to be the smooth limiting result of the non-extremal spectrum. We further analyze the branch-cut contribution to the time-domain Green's function in the late-time limit. We confirm an oscillatory power-law behavior in intermediate late-time regime $1/m < t < 1/m^3M^2$. In the far late-time regime $t>1/m^3M^2$, the activation of the quasi-bound states produces an $t^{-5/6}\exp(-ηt^{1/3})$ suppression with a chirping phase before the asymptotic $t^{-5/6}$ tail previously found in the limit $t\to\infty$. Direct time-domain simulations support this distinction and show how the quasi-bound contribution coexists with the familiar power-law component.

### [76] [5d Schwarzschild-Tangherlini spacetime: MST-like formalism for a Reduced Confluent Heun Equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08280)
*Donato Bini,Giorgio Di Russo,Veronica Fantini*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了五维Schwarzschild-Tangherlini解的测地线结构与无质量标量扰动，在探针极限下计算了散射角、Lyapunov指数，并通过对Mano-Suzuki-Takasugi (MST) 形式论的原始扩展分析了标量扰动动力学，最终获得了2.5阶后牛顿（post-Newtonian）能流结果。

Method: 在探针极限下，对无界测地线计算散射角，采用后牛顿（post-Newtonian）和后闵可夫斯基（post-Minkowskian）型展开并用超几何函数（hypergeometric functions）重求级数；对临界圆轨道偏差导出Lyapunov指数（Lyapunov exponent），用于准正则模（quasinormal modes）的eikonal估计。标量扰动径向方程化为约化合流Heun方程（Reduced Confluent Heun equation），发展了Mano-Suzuki-Takasugi (MST) 形式论的原型扩展，并用量子Seiberg-Witten形式论独立确定重整化角动量参数ν。

Conclusion: 论文所发展的MST形式论扩展在五维Schwarzschild-Tangherlini背景下是自洽且有效的，其计算结果得到了Seiberg-Witten形式论的交叉验证。该工作为更高维黑洞的微扰理论提供了新的分析工具。

Abstract: We study the five-dimensional Schwarzschild-Tangherlini solution, with particular attention to its geodesic structure and massless scalar perturbations. In the probe limit, we present two applications. First, we compute the scattering angle for unbound geodesics showing both post-Newtonian and post-Minkowskian type expansions, and succeeding in resumming the resulting series in terms of hypergeometric functions. Second, we derive the Lyapunov exponent for deviations from a critical circular orbit, which is relevant to the eikonal estimation of quasinormal modes.
  We then investigate the dynamics of massless scalar $(s=0)$ perturbations, for which the radial equation becomes a Reduced Confluent Heun equation. In this $d=5$ Schwarzschild-Tangherlini case we develop an original extension of the standard Mano-Suzuki-Takasugi (MST) formalism and validate the construction by computing the renormalized angular-momentum parameter $ν$, whose value agrees with an independent determination based on the quantum Seiberg-Witten formalism. Finally, we analyze the energy flux from circular orbits, obtaining post-Newtonian results through 2.5PN order.

Abstract: We study linear gravito-electromagnetic perturbations of a slowly rotating 4-derivative corrected Kerr-Newman (KN) black hole (BH), using a perturbative approach beyond the KN geometry up to first order in angular momentum, first order in the higher-derivative parameters ci, i = 1,2...8, and 14th order in the BH electric charge. ### [78] [Chaplygin and Polytropic Kantowski--Sachs Solutions in Teleparallel $F(T)$ Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08343)
*Alexandre Landry*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于协变框架和Coley-Landry不变量方法，在teleparallel F(T)引力中针对Kantowski-Sachs几何，通过Chaplygin型与多方物质流体的非线性状态方程，从守恒律出发直接重构F(T)的泛函形式，得到了幂律和指数两支不变量重构分支，并将其解释为局域各向异性宇宙学扇区及黑洞内部重构分支。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在teleparallel F(T)引力中，标准重构策略通常预先指定引力拉格朗日量（gravitational Lagrangian），但缺乏从非线性物质守恒律出发、针对各向异性Kantowski-Sachs几何的协变重构方法。

Method: 采用coframe-spin-connection形式论和Coley-Landry不变量方法，将广义Chaplygin气体 p=-A/ρ^α 和多方状态方程 p=Kρ^Γ 的守恒律嵌入各向异性KS体积 V=A_2A_3^2 的演化中，再将源项代入协变teleparallel场方程的对称部分，直接重构F(T)的泛函形式。分别考虑幂律和指数两种ansätze，并引入平移不变量 X=T_0-T。

Result: 幂律分支中，Chaplygin流体产生常数加幂次的混合源项，多方流体产生由多方指数Γ控制的密度幂次项；指数分支中，自然重构变量为平移不变量X，导出平移de Sitter分支。重构模型在局域各向异性宇宙学扇区和收缩角向尺度因子的KS黑洞内部扇区均有物理诠释，领头阶可行性由 F_T>0 和 F_{TT}>0 判据评估。

Conclusion: 该重构完全由非线性物质守恒律驱动，逆转了标准重构策略中预先指定引力拉格朗日量的做法，为各向异性几何中F(T)引力的泛函形式提供了系统性的协变重构途径，但完整的扰动稳定性分析留待后续工作。

Abstract: A covariant reconstruction framework for Kantowski--Sachs (KS) geometries sourced by Chaplygin-type and polytropic fluids in teleparallel $F(T)$ gravity is developed using the coframe--spin-connection formalism and the invariant Coley--Landry approach. The matter sector is modeled by nonlinear equations of state, including the generalized Chaplygin gas $p=-A/ρ^α$ and a polytropic law $p=Kρ^Γ$. The corresponding conservation laws determine the dependence of the fluid density on the anisotropic KS volume $V=A_2A_3^2$. These source scalings are then inserted into the symmetric part of the covariant teleparallel field equations and used to reconstruct the functional form of $F(T)$ directly from the KS dynamics. Power-law and exponential ansätze generate distinct invariant reconstruction branches. In the power-law sector, the Chaplygin fluid produces mixed constant-plus-power source terms, while the polytropic sector generates density powers controlled by the polytropic index. In the exponential sector, the natural reconstruction variable is the shifted invariant $X=T_0-T$, leading to shifted teleparallel de Sitter branches. The reconstructed models are interpreted as local anisotropic cosmological sectors and, for contracting angular KS scale factors, as local Kantowski--Sachs black-hole-interior reconstruction branches. The analysis is local and branch-dependent; leading-order viability is assessed through \(F_T>0\) and \(F_{TT}>0\), while a complete perturbative stability analysis is left for future work. The reconstruction is entirely driven by nonlinear matter conservation laws, thereby reversing the standard reconstruction strategy in which the gravitational Lagrangian is prescribed a priori.

### [79] [Signal-to-Noise Ratio Contours for LISA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08445)
*Kai Schmitz,Joseph D. Romano*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对LISA自相关测量中期望最优信噪比的常用表达式仅适用于弱引力波背景信号的问题，首次推导出适用于任意信号强度的广义期望最优信噪比表达式，并发现LISA信噪比存在理论上界（SNR_max ≈ √[T_obs(f_max−f_min)]），为典型任务参数时不超过约10^4；同时给出了广义幂律积分（PLI）灵敏度曲线在不同信噪比水平下的数值结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 文献中广泛使用的LISA随机引力波背景（GWB）信噪比（SNR）表达式仅对弱信号成立，导致大量已报道的SNR数值不够准确，亟需纠正这一理论缺陷。

Method: 首次推导了一个适用于任意信号强度的LISA自相关测量期望最优SNR的广义表达式，并基于该表达式进一步计算了广义幂律积分（power-law-integrated, PLI）灵敏度曲线在不同SNR水平下的等值线。

Result: LISA自相关观测的信噪比存在上限：SNR_max = √[T_obs(f_max−f_min)]，典型任务参数下不超过约10^4；SNR等值线被LISA应变噪声曲线乘以欧拉数e所约束；广义SNR表达式适用于非弱GWB信号场景。

Conclusion: 对于不显著弱于该上限范围的引力波背景信号，必须使用本文新推导的广义SNR表达式进行评估；数值结果已在Zenodo上公开（DOI: 10.5281/zenodo.21275527）。

Abstract: The Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA) will search for a stochastic gravitational-wave (GW) background at millihertz frequencies, from both astrophysical and cosmological sources, and thereby open a new chapter in GW astronomy. In the literature, LISA's sensitivity to prospective GW background (GWB) signals is often quantified in terms of an expected signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) assuming perfect knowledge of the detector noise. The commonly employed expression for the SNR is, however, valid only in the limit of a weak GWB signal, which renders a large number of SNR values reported in the literature inaccurate. In this paper, we address this issue by deriving for the first time an expression for the expected optimal SNR of a LISA auto-correlation measurement that is valid at arbitrary signal strength. Based on our generalized expression, we conclude that LISA data worth an observing time of T_obs across the frequency band from f_min to f_max will never yield an SNR in excess of SNR_max = sqrt(T_obs(f_max-f_min)), which evaluates to SNR_max <~ 10^4 for typical mission parameters. We illustrate our findings in terms of generalized power-law-integrated (PLI) sensitivity curves at different SNR levels, i.e., LISA SNR contour lines in plots of the GW energy-density power spectrum. In contrast to earlier work on PLI sensitivity curves, we notably find that the LISA SNR contours are bounded from above, approximately by the LISA strain noise curve multiplied by a factor of Euler's number e. For GWB signals not much weaker than this range, the expected SNR for a LISA auto-correlation measurement needs to be evaluated based on our new expression. Our numerical results for the LISA SNR contours are available on Zenodo [https://doi.org/10.5281/zenodo.21275527].

</details>

*Ankur Barsode,Koustav N. Maity,Parameswaran Ajith*

Abstract: A small fraction of the gravitational waves (GWs) currently observable by LIGO, Virgo, and KAGRA (LVK) may be strongly lensed by intervening galaxies and galaxy clusters, potentially producing multiple copies of the same signal. We search for lensed pairs of binary black hole signals detected during the O1-O4a observing runs. We include the events identified by the LVK Collaboration, as well as additional events found by external groups (IAS and OGC). Our search is based on Posterior Overlap 2.0, a fast and efficient Bayesian model-selection pipeline to identify lensed candidates. The search is supplemented by realistic background and foreground simulations to characterize the robustness and detection efficiency of the pipeline, as well as the statistical significance of lensed candidates. We define new metrics to assess the statistical significance of lensing both at the individual and population levels. Our work addresses some of the limitations of previous searches. With the probability of lensing $<0.6\%$ for all pairs, we find no evidence for strong lensing in the data and consequently place a $90\%$ upper bound on the lensing fraction of $1.4\%$. With five out of the top nine lensed candidate pairs being from non-LVK catalogs, we also highlight the importance of searching among events reported by multiple GW catalogs. We forecast that the probabilities of making a $3σ$ detection in the fourth (O4), intermediate (IR1), and fifth (O5) observing runs are $\sim 20\%,\, 23\%$, and $67\%$, respectively.
