### [81] [Horizon-redshift transfer in black-hole direct-wave damping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08570)
*Wen-Biao Han,Ye Jiang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过计算黑洞并合产生的直接波（direct wave）在近地平线源驱动下的Teukolsky响应，发现其包络阻尼率（γ_eff）并非直接等于Kerr表面引力（κ），而是一种红移转移观测量；对引力波事件GW250114和GW231226的分析支持这一结论。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索黑洞并合产生的直接波是否能够用来探测视界动力学（horizon dynamics），尤其是观察到的包络是否以Kerr表面引力（surface gravity）速率衰减。

Method: 计算了自旋权重为-2、ℓ=m=2的Teukolsky响应（Teukolsky response），驱动源为红移拉伸的近地平线源（redshift-stretched near-horizon source）；通过Kerr屏蔽（Kerr screening）和源卷积（source convolution），将局域表面引力尺度κ映射为无穷远处测量的有限窗口包络阻尼γ_eff。

Result: 对GW250114的计算给出γ_eff/κ≃0.6，即γ_eff≃0.4 ms⁻¹，与QNM扣除后的残差及H1-L1联合残差分析一致；瞬时源（instantaneous-source）控制实验恢复脉冲响应阻尼接近κ，而有限持续期的汇聚源、测试粒子和径向归一化源实现均给出γ_eff<κ；GW231226的残差级别检验支持相同的有限窗口阻尼预测。

Conclusion: 直接波包络阻尼应被视为一种视界红移转移观测量（horizon-redshift transfer observable），而非表面引力的直接测量（direct measurement）。

Abstract: Direct waves from black-hole mergers may probe horizon dynamics, but their observed envelopes need not decay at the Kerr surface-gravity rate. We compute the complex-frequency spin-$-2$, $\ell=m=2$ Teukolsky response driven by a redshift-stretched near-horizon source. Through Kerr screening and source convolution, the calculation maps the local surface-gravity scale $κ$ into the finite-window envelope damping $γ_{\rm eff}$ measured at infinity. For GW250114, this calculation gives $γ_{\rm eff}/κ\simeq0.6$, or $γ_{\rm eff}\simeq0.4~{\rm ms}^{-1}$, consistent with QNM-subtracted residuals and a joint H1--L1 residual analysis. An instantaneous-source control recovers the impulse-response damping near $κ$, whereas finite-duration plunge-source, test-particle and radial-normalized source realizations give $γ_{\rm eff}<κ$. A residual-level check in GW231226 favours the same finite-window damping prediction. These results identify direct-wave envelope damping as a horizon-redshift transfer observable rather than a direct measurement of surface gravity.

</details>


### [82] [Beyond black hole spectroscopy: Quasinormal mode contamination by massless scalars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08619)
*Miguel Yulo Asuncion,Giovanni D'Addario,Thomas P. Sotiriou*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究超越广义相对论（beyond-GR）场景下黑洞铃宕（black hole ringdown）信号中，由shift-symmetric Horndeski作用量引入的新标量场（scalar field）所产生的准正则模（QNM）频率污染（contamination）效应，分析了不同耦合项在微扰展开中的贡献次序及其与频率偏移（frequency shift）的相对主导关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，利用黑洞铃宕检验广义相对论（General Relativity, GR）聚焦于探测Kerr度规准正则模（quasinormal mode, QNM）频率的偏移。但近期研究表明，在超越GR的场景中，如果新场（new fields）与非最小耦合（nonminimal coupling）项共存，铃宕信号还会受到这些新场QNM频率的污染（contamination）。本文旨在明确这一污染效应的产生条件及其与频率偏移的相对重要性。

Method: 作者选用 shift-symmetric Horndeski 作用量（shift-symmetric Horndeski action），该作用量包含了无质量标量场（massless scalar）与引力之间所有导致二阶运动方程（second order equations）的相互作用。研究采用双重视角的微扰展开：一是对场变量作线性微扰（linear perturbation），二是对标量荷与黑洞质量之比 q 作微扰展开（perturbative expansion）。

Result: 在标量振幅被 q 抑制的假设下，至 q^2 阶，标量场与 Gauss-Bonnet 不变量（Gauss-Bonnet invariant）的耦合是唯一同时贡献于频率偏移（frequency shift）和污染（contamination）的项，且两者出现在同一微扰阶。若放松标量振幅被 q 抑制的假设，污染可在 q 的最低阶出现，因此主导频率偏移；此时污染还会受到另一个额外耦合项（additional coupling）的次领头阶（subleading）修正。

Conclusion: 在 beyond-GR 铃宕分析中，标量场QNM的污染效应可能在参数空间中占据主导地位，不能仅关注Kerr度规QNM频率的偏移。结果表明，频率偏移与污染之间的相对重要性取决于标量振幅是否受到 q 的抑制，这为未来引力波观测中检验GR提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: Testing General Relativity (GR) with black hole ringdowns has conventionally focused on attempting to detect shifts away from the quasinormal mode (QNM) frequencies of the Kerr metric. It has recently been argued, however, that the ringdown signal will also be contaminated with the QNM frequencies of any new fields that are present in a beyond-GR scenario, provided that they couple nonminimally to gravity. We study black hole perturbations for the shift-symmetric Horndeski action, which includes all interactions between a massless scalar and gravity that lead to second order equations upon variation. We perturb linearly in the field and also employ a perturbative expansion in the scalar charge per unit black hole mass, $q$. Assuming that the scalar amplitude is suppressed by $q$, we demonstrate that, to order $q^2$, the coupling between the scalar and the Gauss-Bonnet invariant is the only term that contributes to both frequency shifts and contamination, and that the two effects appear at the same perturbative order. If the assumption about the suppression of the scalar amplitude is relaxed, contamination can appear at leading order in $q$, and hence dominate over frequency shifts. In this case, contamination also receives subleading corrections from an additional coupling

</details>


### [83] [Shadows and lensing signatures of a rotating black hole in a Hernquist dark matter halo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08650)
*A. A. Araújo Filho,Arun Kumar,N. Heidari,C. F. S. Pereira,Amilcar R. Queiroz,V. B. Bezerra*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过非复化的Newman-Janis方法构建了嵌入Hernquist暗物质晕的旋转黑洞时空，推导了零短程线方程与光子轨道，计算了黑洞阴影，并结合事件视界望远镜观测数据和Einsetin环对暗物质晕参数施加了观测约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究暗物质晕对黑洞光学观测特征的定量影响，并利用真实天文观测（如Sgr A*和M87*的阴影数据、ESO325-G004的Einstein环）约束暗物质晕的物理参数。

Method: 采用非复化版本的Newman-Janis方法（noncomplexification version of the Newman-Janis procedure）生成旋转黑洞时空；通过Hamilton-Jacobi方程的可分离性导出临界碰撞参数；利用黑洞阴影与强/弱场引力透镜分析，结合事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope, EHT）和Einstein环观测数据进行参数约束。

Result: 旋转参数主要使黑洞阴影偏移和变形，而Hernquist暗物质晕（Hernquist dark matter halo）会扩大光子俘获区并增大阴影表观尺寸。基于Sgr A*的1σ和2σ约束给出无量纲晕参数$\hatρ$分别约为$(2.7-3.8)\times10^{-3}$和$(4.1-5.2)\times10^{-3}$；基于ESO325-G004的Einsetin环给出$0\leq\hatρ\lesssim0.00939$（1σ）和$0\leq\hatρ\lesssim0.01963$（2σ）。

Conclusion: 暗物质晕对黑洞阴影和引力透镜均有显著影响，Sgr A*的观测数据提供了最强的参数约束；该研究为通过黑洞光学观测间接探测暗物质晕的结构提供了可行途径。

Abstract: We investigate the optical properties of a rotating black hole immersed in a Hernquist dark matter halo. The spacetime is generated from a static Hernquist black hole through the noncomplexification version of the Newman-Janis procedure, yielding a Kerr-like geometry whose halo contribution is encoded in the radial function $Δ(r)$ \cite{AraujoFilho:2026hernquist}. We derive the null geodesic equations, effective potentials, radial acceleration, and representative three-dimensional photon trajectories around the event horizon and ergoregion. Using the separability of the Hamilton-Jacobi equation, we obtain the critical impact parameters of unstable spherical photon orbits and construct the shadow contours for a distant observer. The rotation parameter mainly shifts and distorts the shadow, whereas the Hernquist halo enlarges the photon capture region and increases the apparent shadow size. Comparing the area-equivalent shadow diameter with the Event Horizon Telescope measurements of Sgr A$^\ast$ and M87$^\ast$, we constrain the dimensionless halo parameter $\hatρ=M^2ρ$. The strongest restriction comes from Sgr A$^\ast$, giving $\hatρ\sim(2.7-3.8)\times10^{-3}$ at $1σ$ and $\hatρ\sim(4.1-5.2)\times10^{-3}$ at $2σ$. We also analyze strong- and weak-field gravitational lensing. In the strong-field regime, the halo shifts the unstable photon orbit and critical impact parameter, controlling the logarithmic deflection angle and the position of relativistic images. In the weak-field regime, the halo contributes already to the leading bending angle and enhances deviations from Kerr as $ρ$ grows. From the Einstein ring of ESO325-G004, we further obtain $0\leq\hatρ\lesssim0.00939$ at $1σ$ and $0\leq\hatρ\lesssim0.01963$ at $2σ$.

</details>

### [84] [Folding-Driven Auxetic Weft Knit Textiles with Integrated Capacitive Sensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07713)
*Kausalya Mahadevan,Helen E. Read,Anya X. Zhang,Louis-Justin Tallot,Michelle C. Yuen,Katia Bertoldi*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文开发了一个降阶弹簧网络模型（reduced-order spring-network model），用于预测由罗纹（rib）与平针（garter）补丁棋盘格排列构成的针织织物在大变形下的力学响应，并结合导电纱线部分镀层（partial plating）实现可编程的电容式应变传感，从而为力学可编程且集成传感器的针织结构设计提供了一条理性设计路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器编织（machine knitting）为制造多功能纺织品提供了可扩展平台，可在针迹（stitch）级别对几何、力学和嵌入式功能进行编程。然而，能够将编织架构与大变形力学响应（large-deformation mechanical response）联系起来的设计工具仍然有限，亟需发展预测性设计方法。

Method: 提出一个降阶弹簧网络模型，仅使用线性拉伸弹簧（linear extensional springs）和扭转弹簧（torsional springs）来捕捉针织织物在松弛、展开和变形过程中的行为。模型中考虑棋盘格排列的罗纹与平针织法补丁，并结合实验进行验证。同时，在 fabrication 过程中直接通过导电纱线的部分镀层集成电容式应变传感（capacitive strain sensing），无需后处理。

Result: 模型准确预测了编织物的波纹状松弛构型（corrugated relaxed configuration）以及拉伸载荷下局部变形的演化。实验表明，程序化的波纹展开（programmed unfolding）可产生可调谐的拉胀行为（auxetic behavior），负泊松比（negative Poisson's ratio）的大小及其发生应变由单胞几何（unit-cell geometry）控制。集成传感的编织电容器在应变灵敏度（strain sensitivity）与传感范围（sensing range）之间表现出可编程的权衡关系。

Conclusion: 所提出的建模框架与制造策略为实现力学可编程且集成传感器的针织结构提供了理性设计路线，能够实现定制的形状变化（shape-morphing）与传感功能。

Abstract: Machine knitting provides a scalable platform for manufacturing multifunctional textiles in which geometry, mechanics, and embedded functionality can be programmed at the stitch level. However, predictive design tools capable of linking knit architecture to large-deformation mechanical response remain limited. Here, we develop a reduced-order spring-network model that captures the relaxation, unfolding, and deformation of knitted fabrics composed of checkerboard arrangements of rib and garter patches. The model accurately predicts the corrugated relaxed configuration of the knits and the evolution of local deformations under tensile loading using only linear extensional and torsional springs. Combining simulations with experiments, we show that the programmed unfolding of the corrugations generates tunable auxetic behavior, with both the magnitude of the negative Poisson's ratio and the strain at which it occurs governed by the unit-cell geometry. We further integrate capacitive strain sensing directly during fabrication through partial plating of conductive yarns, eliminating post-processing. The resulting knitted capacitors exhibit programmable tradeoffs between strain sensitivity and sensing range, enabling either highly sensitive sensors over narrow deformation windows or lower-sensitivity sensors capable of measuring larger strains. Together, our modeling framework and fabrication strategy provide a route toward the rational design of mechanically programmable, sensorized knits with tailored shape-morphing and sensing functionalities.

</details>


### [85] [Directed assembly of tetrahedral patchy particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07877)
*Xin Yin,Ekaterina Kostyurina,Bert Nickel,Tim Liedl,Gregor Posnjak*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于DNA折纸（DNA origami）的方法，通过调控两种设计结合构型的相对强度，可预测性地引导四面体胶体颗粒自组装为金刚石立方、孪生金刚石、堆垛无序混合物、六角金刚石及sII笼合物等多种开放晶格结构，并在特定条件下形成互穿网络结构；其中笼合物的440 nm大晶胞可将结构反射移至可见光范围，产生结构色。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 具有指定配位数（如四面体补丁颗粒）的胶体颗粒长期被视为构建百纳米尺度技术相关开放晶格结构的可行途径，但概念限制及由此产生的竞争性局域键合构型常导致混合晶格相，亟需一种可预测控制组装的方法。

Method: 采用DNA折纸（DNA origami）技术实现对四脚建筑块（tetrapod building blocks）附着方式的可预测控制；通过改变两种设计的结合构型（binding configurations）的相对强度来调控组装路径。

Result: 成功将四面体颗粒组装为金刚石立方（diamond cubic）、孪生金刚石（twinned diamonds）、堆垛无序混合物（stacking-disordered mixtures）、六角金刚石（hexagonal diamonds）及sII笼合物（sII clathrates）；在特定条件下，金刚石结构被额外网络互穿，形成三重立方（triple cubic）和三重六角金刚石（triple hexagonal diamond）结构。

Conclusion: 该DNA折基方法实现了对胶体开放晶格结构的理性设计（rationally designed）与自组装（self-assembled），其中笼合物的440 nm大晶胞可将结构反射移至可见光范围，赋予材料结构色（structural color），在光子学领域具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: Colloidal particles with prescribed valency such as the tetrahedral patchy particles have long been seen as a viable route to technologically relevant open lattice structures on the scale of hundreds of nanometers. However, conceptual limitations and resulting competing local bonding configurations often lead to mixed lattice phases. Here, we present a DNA-origami enabled approach to controlling the attachment of tetrapod building blocks in predictable ways. By varying the relative strength of two designed binding configurations we are able to direct the assembly of tetrapod particles into diamond cubic, twinned diamonds, stacking-disordered mixtures, hexagonal diamonds, and sII clathrates. Under specific conditions, the diamond structures are interpenetrated by additional networks, resulting in triple cubic and triple hexagonal diamond structures. The 440 nm large unit cell of the clathrates shifts structural reflections into the visible range, giving these rationally designed, self-assembled crystals structural color.

### [86] [Understanding quorum sensing self-organization: Clustering and defect-induced ordering of diffusing particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07906)
*Feifei Liu,Vyacheslav R. Misko,Yunyun Li,Fabio Marchesoni*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 通过数值模拟研究缺陷颗粒如何影响群体感应（quorum sensing, QS）协议下的固液相变与结构组织，发现热的缺陷可诱导具有长程有序的再入式（reentrant）固化，而冷的缺陷则导致仅具短程有序的非晶结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 群体感应（QS）是生物中一种由自诱导剂（autoinducers）介导的细胞间通讯形式，控制着从个体到集体行为的转变。已有研究尚未充分揭示缺陷颗粒如何影响这一转变过程及由此形成的菌落结构组织。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，构建了一个包含慢扩散（"冷"）和快扩散（"热"）胶体颗粒混合物的模型系统，这些颗粒遵循QS协议，同时加入具有恒定扩散系数的缺陷颗粒。

Result: 热缺陷诱导QS颗粒出现引人注目的再入式固化（reentrant solidification），并伴随长程有序结构；而冷缺陷则导致仅具有短程有序的非晶结构。

Conclusion: 这些发现加深了对QS相互作用的理解，并提供了一种控制QS系统中结构组织程度的机制，在机器人学、社会科学及医学（如克服抗菌素耐药性）等领域具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: Quorum sensing (QS) is known in biology as a form of intercellular communication mediated by signaling molecules called autoinducers. The QS protocol governs the transition from individual to collective cell behavior once a critical population density is reached. Using numerical simulations, we investigate how defects influence the QS transition and the structural organization of the resulting colonies. Our model system consists of a mixture of slow ("cold") and fast ("hot") diffusing colloidal particles that obey the QS protocol, together with defect particles characterized by a constant diffusivity. A striking reentrant solidification of QS particles, characterized by long-range order, is induced by hot defects, whereas cold defects give rise to amorphous structures with only short-range order. These findings deepen our understanding of the QS interaction and provide a mechanism to control the degree of organization in QS systems, with potential applications in robotics, social sciences, and medicine -- for instance, in overcoming antimicrobial resistance.

### [87] [Liquid Crystal Ground States on Hyperbolic Cones](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07930)
*Cheng Long,David R. Nelson*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文将液晶基态理论从常规锥面（正高斯曲率）推广到双曲锥面（负高斯曲率类δ函数），发现两种锥面上虽都存在未量子化的赝缺陷（pseudodefect），但基态存在根本差异，表现为液晶相中电荷共轭对称性（charge conjugation symmetry）的破缺。通过有无边界条件的两种实例分析，特别在切向边界条件下，双曲锥面上的正赝电荷能与同号拓扑电荷稳定结合，与常规锥面的电荷共轭情形形成鲜明对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前液晶基态研究主要集中于具有正顶点高斯曲率的常规锥面，而负曲率对液晶有序行为的影响尚不清楚。本文旨在将解析理论和模拟模型推广至双曲锥面（hyperbolic cone），以探究负高斯曲率下的液晶基态特性与对称性破缺机制。

Method: 采用解析理论推广与模拟模型相结合的方法。具体选取两个简单示例进行对比分析：(a)双曲锥面上具有自由边界条件的p-atic液晶；(b)双曲锥面上具有切向边界条件（tangential boundary conditions）的p-atic液晶。特别对p=1（矢量序参量场）情形进行精细分析。

Result: 两种锥面的顶点曲率都会在共形域（conformal domain）中产生固定且未量子化的赝缺陷，行为类似于携带相反拓扑荷（topological charges）的传统向错（disclination）。然而二者基态存在本质差异，体现为电荷共轭对称性的破缺。在切向边界的双曲锥面上，顶点曲率产生的正赝电荷能与同号拓扑荷稳定结合（尽管存在排斥相互作用），与常规锥面上电荷共轭情形完全不同。

Conclusion: 双曲锥面作为具有负高斯曲率的几何平台，为液晶系统电荷共轭对称性破缺提供了天然实现条件。该发现丰富了液晶在弯曲几何中的基态理论，并揭示了曲率符号对拓扑缺陷行为的根本性影响。

Abstract: We generalize the analytic theory and simulation models for liquid crystal ground states on conventional cones with positive apex Gaussian curvature and study liquid crystal ground states on hyperbolic cones with a delta function of negative apex Gaussian curvature. While both the local apex curvature on a conventional cone and a hyperbolic cone lead to a fixed unquantized pseudodefect in the conformal domain and behave like conventional disclinations with opposite topological charges, there are fundamental differences in the ground states as well, which can be viewed as a violation of charge conjugation symmetry in a liquid crystal phase. To illustrate the violated charge conjugation symmetry on curved surfaces, we study two simple examples: (a) $p$-atic liquid crystals on a hyperbolic cone with free boundary conditions at the cone base. (b) $p$-atic liquid crystals on a hyperbolic cone with tangential boundary conditions at the cone base. In the simple case of $p=1$ liquid crystals (a vector order parameter field) on a hyperbolic cone with tangential boundary conditions, the positive pseudocharge caused by the apex curvature can be stably bound with a topological charge of the same sign despite their repulsive interaction, in sharp contrast to the charge conjugated situation associated with conventional cones.

</details>


### [88] [A Generalized Mechanical Model for the Cycle Rank Dependence of Stretch at Break in Phantom Chain Star Polymer Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07981)
*Yuichi Masubuchi,Takato Ishida,Takashi Uneyama*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文将一个解释幻象链网络（phantom-chain network）中断裂拉伸比（stretch at break, λ_b）与环秩密度（cycle-rank density, ξ）普适性的简单力学模型重新表述为瓶颈链段（bottleneck strand）与周围网络的串联形式，得到 λ_b-1=(λ_bs-1)[1+ν_h/(1+cξ)] 公式，并通过固定几何常数 c、将 λ_bs 和 ν_h 作为拟合参数，成功再现了多种条件下的幻象链网络模拟数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期研究提出一个简单力学模型用以解释幻象链网络模拟中断裂拉伸比 λ_b 随环秩密度 ξ 变化的普适性行为[J. Non-Newtonian Fluid Mech., 349, 105620 (2026)]，本文旨在将该模型重新表述为瓶颈链段与周围网络串联的显式形式以深化其物理理解并验证其适用性。

Method: 将该力学模型重新表述为瓶颈链段与周围网络的串联形式，推导出 λ_b-1=(λ_bs-1)[1+ν_h/(1+cξ)] 公式；由于 c 和 ν_h 在所考察的 ξ 范围内难以分离，固定 c 为常数，将 λ_bs（瓶颈链段的断裂拉伸比）和 ν_h（沿断裂路径串联的刚性单元数）作为拟合参数，对多种条件下的幻象链网络模拟数据进行拟合。

Result: 该公式在所有考察条件下均能合理拟合模拟数据，且两个拟合参数 λ_bs 和 ν_h 能够反映网络特征。

Conclusion: 该串联形式的力学模型能够有效描述幻象链网络中断裂拉伸比与环秩密度之间的普适关系，其中两个拟合参数具有明确的网络物理意义。

Abstract: A simple mechanical model was recently proposed to explain the universality of stretch at break (λ_b) as a function of cycle-rank density (ξ) in phantom-chain network simulations [J Non-Newtonian Fluid Mech., 349, 105620 (2026)]. Here, that model is reformulated as a series of the bottleneck strand and the surrounding network, yielding λ_b-1=(λ_bs-1)[1+ν_h/(1+cξ)]. In this formula, λ_bsis the stretch at break of the bottleneck strand, ν_h is the number of stiff units in series along the rupture path, and c is a geometric constant for the parallel redundancy of the medium. Since c and ν_hare difficult to separate over the examined range of ξ, c is fixed, and λ_bs and ν_hare treated as fitting parameters. The formula is applied to phantom-chain simulations of networks with various conditions. In all cases, it reasonably captures the data, and the two parameters represent network characteristics.

</details>

*Ligesh Theeyancheri,Jennifer L. Ross,J. M. Schwarz*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过模拟活性粒子浴中的粘附-间隔（sticker-spacer）聚合物，发现活性驱动能够使流体凝聚体从紧凑液滴转变为系统尺度的渗透网络，并在移除活性粒子后仍保留这种拓扑结构印记，揭示了一种具有长时结构记忆的类流体状态。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用粘附-间隔聚合物在活性粒子浴（active particle bath）中的模拟，通过增强链间连通性、抑制链内塌缩以及增加链间缠绕带来的拓扑约束，研究活性对凝聚体结构演化的影响。

Conclusion: 活性能够在流体凝聚体中写入具有长寿命的结构组织与记忆，形成一种带有活性诱导拓扑印记（activity-induced topological imprinting）的类流体状态。

Abstract: Fluid condensates readily exchange components and reorganize, and in doing so typically erase structural history. Using simulations of sticker-spacer polymers in an active particle bath, we show that activity drives condensates from compact droplets into system-spanning percolated networks by enhancing interchain connectivity, suppressing intrachain collapse, and increasing topological constraints through interchain winding. The network persists after the active particles are removed, despite continued polymer exchange and contact turnover, revealing a fluid-like state with activity-induced topological imprinting. Hence, activity can write long-lived structural organization and memory into fluid condensates.

### [90] [Basin-volume distributions in monodisperse particle packings -- the soul of memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08094)
*Varda F. Hagh,Zhaoning Liu,Sidney R. Nagel*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文通过数值模拟测量了二维和三维单分散软球体系的势能景观中吸引盆（catchment basin）的体积分布，发现该分布满足幂律标度关系 $P_N(n) \approx A_N n^{-\alpha}$ 且 $\alpha \approx 1$，在全域可跨越7个数量级，并进一步分析了吸引盆的连通性与几何形貌结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解无定形颗粒体系力学稳定堆积（mechanically stable packings）所对应的势能景观（potential energy landscape）结构，特别是吸引盆的体积分布与几何性质，是揭示非晶固体记忆效应与力学响应本质的关键。

Method: 从随机初始粒子位置出发，采用基于梯度（gradient-based）的优化方法使系统弛豫至势能极小值，从而定义吸引盆（catchment basin）；在 $d=2$ 和 $d=3$ 下测量不可分辨单分散软球（indistinguishable monodisperse soft spheres）的吸引盆体积分布，按体积从大到小排序，并分析其幂律行为。

Result: 在二维和三维中，吸引盆体积分布均呈现极宽的分布范围，在最优情况下可跨越7个数量级；分布符合 $P_N(n) \approx A_N n^{-\alpha}$ 形式，指数 $\alpha \approx 1$；吸引盆具有高度扭曲（highly contorted）的结构特征。

Conclusion: 吸引盆体积的幂律标度行为与维度无关，暗示了一种普适性的势能景观拓扑结构；该结果可用于理解固体在循环应变（cyclic strain）实验中的记忆印刻（imprinting of memories）现象。

Abstract: Mechanically stable packings of $N$ particles in $d$ dimensions lie at the minima of an $Nd$-dimensional potential energy landscape. Starting from random initial particle positions, the system can relax using gradient-based optimization until it arrives at one of the equilibrium states; all initial conditions that end at the same minimum belong to the same catchment basin. We measure the distribution of the catchment basin volumes for indistinguishable monodisperse soft spheres in both $d=2$ and $d=3$. Ordering the basins at each system size, $N$, according to their volume, $P_N(n)$, from the largest at $n=1$ to smaller at larger $n$, we find a very wide distribution of volumes which is similar in both dimensions: $P_N(n) \approx A_Nn^{-α}$ with $α\approx 1$ which, in our most favorable cases, extends over $7$ decades. We explore aspects of the connectivity of the basins, show that their structure is highly contorted, and demonstrate how these results may be used to understand the imprinting of memories in cyclic strain studies of solids.

</details>


### [91] [Viscoelasticity Enhances Contactless Adhesion of Soft Substrates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08213)
*Marco Rizzo,Jacco H. Snoeijer,Vincent Bertin,Pascal Damman*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过实验、第一性原理理论和数值模拟，揭示了粘弹性松弛如何从根本上改变弹性流体动力学粘附（elastohydrodynamic adhesion），提出了由软度参数（softness parameter）和德博拉数（Deborah number）定义的新标度律与统一相图，涵盖三个不同的粘附区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解粘附力（adhesion force）对于描述系统的稳定性、摩擦和界面动力学至关重要，但粘弹性（viscoelasticity）在非接触软表面粘附中的作用尚不清晰，需要从理论上揭示其基本机制。

Method: 采用刚性球体与软表面通过粘性流体介导的非直接接触实验，结合第一性原理粘弹-弹性流体动力学理论（visco-elastohydrodynamic theory）以及数值模拟，系统研究粘附力动力学。

Result: 粘弹性使基底在瞬态行为上表现为更硬的固体，增大了最大粘附力；早期力增长的时间标度从t^(2/3)变为t^(1/3)；缩短了相互作用时间；产生了由德博拉数（Deborah number）控制的新标度律。

Conclusion: 提出的两个无量纲参数——软度参数和德博拉数——定义了一个统一相图，连接了经典雷诺润滑（Reynolds lubrication）、弹性流体动力学粘附和新发现的粘弹-弹性流体动力学（visco-elastohydrodynamic）三个粘附区域。

Abstract: Understanding adhesion is essential for describing stability, friction, and interfacial dynamics. Here, we investigate the adhesion force dynamics between a rigid sphere and a soft surface without direct contact, mediated by a viscous fluid. By combining controlled experiments, a first-principles visco-elastohydrodynamic theory, and numerical simulations, we demonstrate that viscoelastic relaxation fundamentally modifies elastohydrodynamic adhesion. Rather than simply dissipating energy, viscoelasticity causes the substrate to behave transiently as a stiffer solid, enhancing the maximum adhesive force, changing the early-time force growth for $t^{2/3}$ to $t^{1/3}$, shortening the interaction time, and giving rise to new scaling laws governed by the Deborah number. The two proposed dimensionless parameters, the softness parameter and the Deborah number, define a unified phase diagram connecting three distinct adhesion regimes: classical Reynolds lubrication, elastohydrodynamic adhesion, and the newly identified visco-elastohydrodynamic regime.

### [92] [Short Peptide Tails Modulate DNA Association and Condensation by PAMAM Dendrimers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08623)
*Corinna Dannert,Pablo M. Blanco,Sebastian P. Pineda,Peter Košovan,Rita S. Dias*

Conclusion: 肽尾修饰使G2 PAMAM树形分子从相对pH不敏感的DNA凝聚剂转变为pH响应性DNA结合系统；单个缀合物的模拟无法完全解释凝聚行为，凸显了多缀合物集体效应的重要性；研究为电荷调控、肽组成与DNA凝聚之间的相互作用提供了分子层面的理解。

Abstract: Poly(amidoamine) (PAMAM) dendrimers are promising candidates for nucleic acid delivery; however, biocompatibility and transfection efficiency remain a challenge. Here, we investigated how the composition of short peptide tails conjugated to generation 2 PAMAM (G2) dendrimers influence DNA association and condensation across a range of pH values. Using a combination of potentiometric titrations, DNA precipitation assays, and coarse-grained molecular simulations with charge regulation, we show that the ionization of G2 dendrimers is strongly affected by both pH and proximity to DNA. Although charge regulation enhances dendrimer protonation and strengthens DNA association at low pH, DNA condensation by unmodified G2 remains largely insensitive to pH within the studied range.
  In contrast, conjugation of a single peptide tail introduces a pronounced pH dependence to DNA condensation. Histidine-containing conjugates exhibit the strongest response, with condensation efficiency decreasing markedly as the pH increases. Simulations reveal that the interaction strength between conjugates and DNA depends on both peptide composition and pH and that histidine-containing peptide tails become nearly neutral at physiological pH, contributing little to DNA binding. While single-conjugate simulations explain the trends in DNA association, they do not fully account for the observed condensation behavior, highlighting the importance of collective effects involving multiple conjugates.
  Overall, peptide conjugation transforms G2 PAMAM dendrimers from relatively pH-insensitive DNA condensing agents into pH-responsive DNA-binding systems. These findings provide molecular-level insight into the interplay between charge regulation, peptide composition, and DNA condensation.

### [93] [Stochastic dynamics of particles in correlated fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08627)
*Andrea Gambassi*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文推导了浸没在复杂平衡介质中的胶体粒子有效动力学的非线性模型，该模型基于与涨落高斯场线性耦合的假设，揭示了自趋化动力学在低维空间中呈现反常扩散和“run-and-tumble”运动等特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的线性过阻尼朗之万方程（linear overdamped Langevin equation）无法描述实验中观察到的胶体粒子有效动力学的非线性行为，因此需要建立新的理论模型来解释数值模拟与实验结果之间的差异。

Method: 研究聚焦于介质可用涨落且相关的标量高斯场（fluctuating and correlated Gaussian field）描述的情形，假设该场与胶体粒子线性耦合，从而推导出有效动力学方程，并分析其在驱动粒子随机热力学（stochastic thermodynamics）中的后果。对于场由粒子自身产生（自趋化，self-chemotactic）且涨落可忽略的情景，在低空间维度下进行解析刻画。

Result: 推导得到了非线性有效动力学方程。在自趋化情形下，发现低维空间中系统呈现反常扩散（anomalous diffusion）和“run-and-tumble”运动模式，并给出了这些行为的解析描述。

Conclusion: 平衡复杂介质中胶体粒子的有效动力学本质上是非线性的，该非线性模型能够解释线性模型失效的原因，并为驱动粒子随机热力学及自推进运动（如run-and-tumble）提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The effective dynamics of a colloidal particle immersed in a complex medium at equilibrium is usually described in terms of a linear overdamped Langevin equation, possibly with memory. However, numerical simulations and experiments have shown that this linear model fails, suggesting that the effective dynamics of the probe is actually nonlinear. Focusing on the case in which the medium is described by a fluctuating and correlated Gaussian field, linearly coupled to the colloid, we derive this effective dynamics and discuss its various consequences, including those on the stochastic thermodynamics of a driven particle. When the field is generated by the particle itself, with negligible fluctuations, the resulting self-chemotactic dynamics turns out to display anomalous diffusion and run-and-tumble motion in low spatial dimension, which we characterise analytically.

### [94] [Complex dynamics perspective for birational maps of the plane arising from cluster algebra mutations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08125)
*Andrei Grigorev,Krishna Chaitanya Kalidindi,Andres Quintero Santander,Roland Roeder*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文利用全纯动力学方法研究源自簇代数和可积系统的平面双有理映射，通过计算动力度数（其中许多大于1）证明这些映射大部分不存在守恒量或不变量纤维化，并进一步构造了具有正熵和正李雅普诺夫指数的不变测度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 回答 Machacek & Ovenhouse (2024) 以及 Chen & Li (2024) 提出的问题：这些来自簇代数（cluster algebras）和可积系统（integrable systems）的平面双有理映射（birational mappings）是否具有守恒量或不变量纤维化？

Method: 采用全纯动力学（holomorphic dynamics）方法，通过计算动力度数（dynamical degree）来判断映射是否具有守恒量；利用发现超吸引周期点（superattracting periodic points）来排除不变量纤维化（invariant fibration）的存在；为映射建立代数稳定模型（algebraically stable model），并应用双有理映射遍历理论（ergodic theory of birational maps）构造不变测度。

Result: 大部分映射的动力度数大于1，表明它们不具有守恒量；通过超吸引周期点也排除了大多数例子中存在不变量纤维化的可能性。

Conclusion: 成功回答了所引文献中的开放问题；在建立了代数稳定模型并计算了动力度数后，能够进一步构造具有正熵（positive entropy）和正李雅普诺夫指数（positive Lyapunov exponents）的不变测度（invariant measures）。

Abstract: Using the methods of holomorphic dynamics we investigate planar birational mappings that arise from the theory of cluster algebras and integrable systems. Computing dynamical degrees of these mappings, many of which are greater than one, allows us to show that many of the mappings do not have a conserved quantity (nor an invariant fibration). In most of the examples, invariant fibrations can also be ruled out by finding superattracting periodic points. This answers a question posted by Machacek and Ovenhouse 2024 and by Chen and Li 2024. Moreover, having found a good algebraically stable model for the mappings and having computed the dynamical degree, we can then apply results from the ergodic theory of birational maps to produce invariant measures with positive entropy and positive Lyapunov exponents.

Abstract: We present electric-field-modulated electron paramagnetic resonance (EFM-EPR) measurements on centrosymmetric single crystals of the molecular spin triangle $\mathrm{[{Fe_3}O({O_2}CPh){_6}(py){_3}]ClO{_4}{\cdot}py}$ ($\bf{Fe_3}$). Additionally, an unexpected first harmonic EFM-EPR signal is observed. Various plausible symmetry-breaking mechanisms are discussed in an attempt to explain this feature, whose observation is unexpected in a nominally centrosymmetric crystal.

### [98] [Bulk Boundary Condition for Surface Calculations in Density Functional Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07894)
*Sayan Bhowmik,Andrew J Medford,Phanish Suryanarayana*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于体相边界条件（bulk boundary condition）的形式化方法，用于Kohn-Sham密度泛函理论（Kohn-Sham density functional theory）中的表面计算。该方法利用电子相互作用的近程性（nearsightedness），将计算限制在局部表面区域，通过密度矩阵（density matrix）的衰减特性评估电子密度，并在内部对密度和静电势施加体相值，同时求解满足体相边界条件的静电势。能量和原子力通过基于密度矩阵的表达式计算。代表性表面能和吸附能计算验证了该方法的精度与效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 表面计算在密度泛函理论（DFT）中面临计算成本高的挑战，传统方法需要处理较大的体相区域。该工作旨在通过利用电子相互作用的近程性，将计算限制在局部表面区域，从而在保持准确性的前提下提高计算效率。

Method: 提出了一种体相边界条件形式化方法（bulk boundary condition formalism）。具体而言，利用电子相互作用的实空间近程性（nearsightedness）将计算限制在局部表面区域；通过密度矩阵（density matrix）的衰减特性评估该区域内的电子密度；在内部区域对电子密度和静电势施加体相值（bulk values），并求解满足体相边界条件的静电势；能量和原子力则通过基于密度矩阵的表达式计算。

Result: 通过代表性的表面能（surface energy）和吸附能（adsorption energy）计算，展示了所提出形式化方法的准确性和计算效率。

Conclusion: 该体相边界条件形式化方法能够有效且准确地用于Kohn-Sham DFT中的表面计算，为降低表面计算成本提供了一种可行的途径。

Abstract: We present a bulk boundary condition formalism for surface calculations in Kohn--Sham density functional theory. The approach exploits the nearsightedness of electronic interactions in real space to restrict the calculation to a localized surface region. Within this region, the electron density is evaluated by leveraging the decay of the density matrix, with bulk values imposed on the density and electrostatic potential in the interior, and the electrostatic potential solved subject to bulk boundary conditions. The energy and atomic forces are computed using density-matrix-based expressions. Through representative calculations of surface and adsorption energies, we demonstrate the accuracy and efficiency of the proposed formalism.

However, new chiral phenomena can emerge uniquely at the interface, distinct from their bulk counterparts, when a chiral material forms a heterostructure. Chiral (CH)$_x$ oligomers are generated in distinct conformations which differ in their out-of-plane tonsorial ordering.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用团簇展开形式（cluster expansion formalism）整合蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）与基于密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）的计算，构建了CaₓV₂O₄（0 ≤ x ≤ 1）的温度-组分相图，并进行了迁移势垒（migration barrier）计算。

Conclusion: 钙离子在γ相中的迁移受到Ca-空位有序性和两相区的强动力学限制，导致实际容量远低于理论值。通过阳离子掺杂（cation doping）和减小颗粒尺寸（particle size reduction）有望降低γ相的势能面（potential energy landscape）起伏以改善Ca迁移率。计算结果揭示了稳定性与离子输运之间的相互作用，为CaV₂O₄作为钙离子电池正极材料的实际应用提供了设计策略。

Abstract: Calcium-ion batteries (CBs) represent an alternative to lithium-ion technology but their advancement is limited by the lack of high-performance intercalation cathodes. Identified via computational screening, post-spinel CaV$_2$O$_4$ has emerged as a promising candidate, though its practical application is hindered by limited electrochemical capacity. Hence, we investigate the thermodynamic and ionic transport characteristics of Ca$_x$V$_2$O$_4$ ($0 \leq x \leq 1$) in this work, by integrating the cluster expansion formalism with Monte Carlo simulations and density functional theory based calculations. We construct the temperature-composition phase diagram of Ca$_x$V$_2$O$_4$ revealing several stable phases ($α$ through $ζ$) that can appear during electrochemical operations at different voltages. Importantly, we observe the formation of the $\varepsilon$ phase at $x \sim 0.83$ across a 370-590~K temperature window via invariant reactions, which agrees with observations in the experimental voltage profiles. Further, migration barrier calculations confirm that Ca mobility is severely impeded within the $α$ ($x \sim 0$) and $γ$ ($x \sim 0.5$) phases. With the strong Ca-vacancy ordering contributing to the high barrier in $γ$ and the persistent two-phase region stretching across the $δ$ ($x \sim 0.67$) and the $γ$ phases, we expect the accessible electrochemical capacity in the CaV$_2$O$_4$ system to be kinetically limited to at most half the theoretical capacity at 298~K, in agreement with experiments. Strategies including cation doping and particle size reduction can be considered to flatten the potential energy landscape of $γ$ and improve Ca mobility. Our computational findings highlight the interplay between stability and transport and provide design strategies that can enable the practical use of CaV$_2$O$_4$ as a CB cathode.

### [103] [Nonlocal Electrostatic Origin of Schottky-Barrier Variability in 2D Contacts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08253)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建了非局域静电模型（nonlocal electrostatic model），并基于密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）对Ti–MoS₂和Au–MoS₂体系进行了第一性原理输运计算（density-functional-theory-based transport calculations）来支撑该模型。

Conclusion: 研究建立了由边缘邻近缺陷（edge-proximal defects）介导的非局域静电效应作为二维接触中载流子注入（carrier injection）的关键机制，为长期存在争议的实验SBH变异性提供了统一解释。

Abstract: Electrical contacts often limit the performance of atomically thin semiconductor devices. The Schottky barrier height (SBH) is conventionally treated as a local interface property, yet reported values for the same metal/2D-semiconductor contact vary by hundreds of meV. Here we show that, in top contacts, the effective SBH exhibits a pronounced nonlocal electrostatic dependence on defects near the contact edge, beyond the conventional local interface framework. A nonlocal electrostatic model, supported by density-functional-theory-based transport calculations for Ti--MoS$_2$ and Au--MoS$_2$, captures the large, metal-dependent variations in SBH as a function of defect position relative to the contact edge. These results provide a unified explanation for the longstanding variability in experimentally extracted SBHs and establish nonlocal electrostatics, mediated by edge-proximal defects, as a key mechanism governing carrier injection in 2D contacts.

### [104] [Interplay between Electronic Structure, Chemical Bonding, and Lattice Symmetry in Bismuth Vanadate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08327)

Motivation: 钒酸铋（BiVO₄）是一种典型的氧化物光催化剂，其四方相和单斜相表现出迥异的光催化和光电化学活性，但准确识别单斜相为基态（ground state）并解释其对称性破缺畸变的起源在理论上极具挑战性，文献中各种理论层次及其物理解释存在分歧。

Method: 系统评估了有无自旋-轨道耦合下精确交换的作用，通过密集采样布里渊区（Brillouin zone）计算电子能带结构，并选择最能复现晶体结构的交换关联泛函，同时考虑激子和热效应来预测带隙。

Result: 电子局域化的准确处理是稳定单斜白钨矿结构的关键；单斜畸变源自非等效氧位点间的电荷转移，该对称性破缺在半局域密度泛函理论（semi-local DFT）中会因自相互作用误差（self-interaction error）而被抑制；单斜与四方相的能带边缘远离常规高对称路径，导致带隙和载流子有效质量显著不同；最优泛函结合激子与热效应可精确预测带隙。

Conclusion: 研究结果建立了BiVO₄中交换关联泛函、电子局域化、化学键合与结构稳定性之间的直接联系，为复杂氧化物的相稳定性（phase stability）和光电子性质（optoelectronic properties）的稳健第一性原理（ab initio）描述提供了基础。

Abstract: Bismuth vanadate (BiVO$_4$) is a prototypical oxide photocatalyst that occurs in both tetragonal and monoclinic scheelite phases with markedly different photocatalytic and photoelectrochemical activities. Accurately identifying the monoclinic phase as the ground state and explaining the origin of its symmetry-breaking distortion are unusually challenging from a theoretical perspective, with various levels of theory and associated physical interpretations for this behaviour reported in the literature. Here, we resolve these discrepancies by systematically assessing the role of exact exchange with and without spin-orbit coupling, demonstrating that an accurate treatment of electronic localization is essential to stabilize the monoclinic scheelite structure. Using this framework, we compute the electronic band structure through dense sampling of the Brillouin zone and show that the band edges in monoclinic and tetragonal BiVO$_4$ lie far from conventional high-symmetry paths, leading to substantial differences in band gaps and carrier effective masses. Choosing the exchange-correlation functional that best reproduces the crystal structure leads to excellent predictions of the band gap once excitonic and thermal effects are taken into account. In addition, we show that the monoclinic distortion is driven by charge transfer between non-equivalent oxygen sites, which breaks the lattice symmetry and is suppressed by self-interaction errors when using semi-local DFT. These results establish a direct connection between the exchange-correlation functional, electronic localization, chemical bonding, and structural stability in BiVO$_4$, providing a foundation for robust ab initio descriptions of phase stability and optoelectronic properties in such complex oxides.

</details>


### [105] [Bond, orbital and spin order in d4/d6/d7 perovskite oxides: successes and limitations of foundation interatomic potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08351)
*Swagata Acharya,Dimitar Pashov,Mark van Schilfgaarde,Alin M. Elena*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究测试了三种基座机器学习原子间势（foundation MLIPs）在三种强关联ABO₃钙钛矿氧化物低温有序态上的表现，发现它们能捕获标量类有序（如NdNiO₃），在矢量类有序（如LaMnO₃）上能还原大小但无法还原对称性，而局域类有序（如LaCoO₃的低自旋-高自旋交叉）则完全无法描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基座机器学习原子间势（foundation MLIPs）正快速取代密度泛函理论（DFT）用于模拟结构和核动力学，但其在强关联系统中的保真度成为亟待回答的问题。该研究旨在评估这些势函数在描述具有不同低温有序类型的强关联钙钛矿氧化物时的能力边界。

Method: 选取三种基座势函数，对三种同构但低温度有序类型不同的ABO₃钙钛矿氧化物（LaMnO₃、LaCoO₃、NdNiO₃）进行分子动力学模拟。模拟使用80和160原子超胞，温度范围50–300 K，持续1 ns，不进行系统特异性训练。根据低温有序的几何复杂度将挑战分为标量类、矢量类和局域类三个层次。

Result: 标量类有序（NdNiO₃）因具有简单几何指纹而被成功捕获。矢量类有序（LaMnO₃）需识别每个格点上长键所在的笛卡尔轴方向，势函数能还原有序的大小但无法还原其对称性。局域类有序（LaCoO₃的低自旋到高自旋交叉）作为纯局域多重态布居转移，无空间序参量，当前MLIPs完全无法描述。

Conclusion: 基座MLIPs在处理强关联钙钛矿氧化物时表现出层次化的能力缺陷：随低温有序类型从标量到矢量再到局域类，描述难度递增。特别是与自旋态转变相关的局域电子关联效应，对现有势函数构成了根本性挑战。

Abstract: Foundation machine-learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) are rapidly replacing density-functional theory (DFT) for modeling structure and nuclear dynamics, making their fidelity in strongly correlated systems an urgent question. We test three foundation potentials on the low-temperature order of three correlated, isostructural ABO3 perovskite oxides: LaMnO3 (d4), LaCoO3 (d6), and NdNiO3 (d7). We run molecular dynamics for 1 ns on 80- and 160-atom supercells from 50 to 300 K with no system-specific training. These oxides expose three distinct classes of low-temperature order that define a hierarchy of difficulty for the potentials. The scalar class, represented by NdNiO3, has a simple geometric fingerprint and is captured. The vector class, represented by LaMnO3, requires identifying which Cartesian axis carries the long bond at each site, and is captured in magnitude but not in symmetry. The on-site class, represented by the low-spin to high-spin crossover in LaCoO3, is a purely local multiplet population shift with no spatial order parameter and remains inaccessible to present-day MLIPs.

### [106] [Bright and Dark Excitons in CrSBr: Local Ligand-Field Character and Band-Coherent Optical Selection Rules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08355)
*Swagata Acharya,Jessica McDivitt,Dimitar Pashov,Mark van Schilfgaarde,Justin C. Johnson,Jeffrey L. Blackburn*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过多体费曼图方法结合准粒子自洽GW与电子-空穴阶梯顶点修正，揭示了CrSBr中明亮激子的能带相干（band-coherent）本质：亮态与暗态伙伴是同一单粒子跃迁流形上亚晶格对称与反对称的叠加态，亮度由跃迁偶极子的对称性适应干涉规则决定，否定了早期类里德伯（Rydberg-like）激子归属。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CrSBr中明亮激子与暗态伙伴能量相差仅几十毫电子伏特（meV）但亮度相差数个数量级的原因尚不明确，需要从激子本征函数的能带相干性质出发解释这一差异。

Method: 采用基于准粒子自洽GW（quasiparticle self-consistent GW）的多体费曼图方法（many-body Feynman diagrammatic approach），并引入电子-空穴阶梯顶点修正（electron-hole ladder vertex corrections）对屏蔽库仑相互作用进行修正。

Result: 亮度是激子本征函数的能带相干属性：亮态与暗态伙伴分别是同一配位场型布洛赫跃迁（ligand-field-like Bloch transitions）的亚晶格对称（sublattice-symmetric）与亚晶格反对称（sublattice-antisymmetric）叠加态；亮态需要跃迁偶极子之间的对称性适应干涉规则（symmetry-adapted interference rule）。

Conclusion: 常用的Frenkel和Wannier-Mott标签描述激子的组成，但亮度由对称性决定的干涉规则控制；区分这一裸激子结构是解释CrSBr在包含磁振子（magnon）、声子（phonon）和光子（photon）耦合时光学响应的前提。

Abstract: Magnetic van der Waals semiconductors such as CrSBr host an intricate exciton landscape whose physical interpretation has converged only recently. A many-body Feynman diagrammatic approach based on quasiparticle self-consistent GW with electron-hole ladder vertex corrections to the screened Coulomb interaction has established the electronic band gap, excitonic orbital character, real-space extent, binding energies, and bosonic-coupling signatures of the bright XA exciton near 1.34 eV and the higher XB manifold near 1.8 eV. These results agree well with ARPES and magneto-optical experiments and supersede the early Rydberg-like assignment of the excitons. What has remained unresolved is why these intense bright excitons coexist, within a few tens of meV, with companion states that are several orders of magnitude darker despite drawing from essentially the same single-particle transition manifold. Here we show that brightness is a band-coherent property of the excitonic eigenfunctions: bright and dark partners are sublattice-symmetric and sublattice-antisymmetric superpositions of the same ligand-field-like Bloch transitions across the two Cr atoms of the orthorhombic primitive cell. The commonly used Frenkel and Wannier-Mott labels describe what an exciton is made of, but brightness requires a symmetry-adapted interference rule between transition dipoles. Disentangling this bare excitonic structure is a prerequisite for interpreting the optical response of CrSBr once magnon, phonon, and photon couplings are included.

Conclusion: 多晶CA薄膜在室温下表现出此前未在CA基器件中验证的热电性（pyroelectricity），打破了高结晶度是维持铁电、压电和热电性能前提的常见假设。该低温制备路线将沉积与封装集成为单一原位过程，简化了器件制造，且兼容柔性衬底与规模化真空技术，为低成本、无铅、多源能量收集系统的发展提供了有前景的方案。

Abstract: The development of organic ferroelectric materials through scalable and simplified fabrication routes remains a major challenge for next-generation energy-harvesting technologies. Here, polycrystalline croconic acid (CA) thin films are fabricated by vacuum sublimation onto Ar plasma-treated flexible substrates and stabilized by in situ encapsulation with an adamantane-based remote plasma polymer. This solvent-free strategy effectively suppresses surface degradation under ambient conditions, providing long-term stability. Piezoresponse force microscopy confirms robust ferroelectricity with an oblique polarization orientation, well-defined domains, and low nanoscale coercive fields. The films were integrated into multilayer piezoelectric and pyroelectric devices. The piezoelectric performance strongly depends on film thickness, while embedding the CA layer between dielectric polymeric films significantly improves the macroscopic response, reaching power densities of up to 37 microW m-2 for ca. 2 micrometer CA films. Despite the common assumption that high crystallinity is required to sustain ferro-, piezo-, and pyroelectricity, these polycrystalline CA films exhibit remarkable RT pyroelectricity, a property not previously demonstrated in CA-based devices. A pyroelectric coefficient of ca. 10 microC m-2 K-1 highlights a functional response comparable to that of well-established organic and inorganic pyroelectric materials, demonstrating the potential of CA thin films for thermal energy harvesting. Beyond their functional performance, the proposed low-T fabrication route combines deposition and encapsulation in a single in situ process, simplifying device fabrication. Its compatibility with scalable vacuum technologies, flexible substrates, and further process optimization makes this approach highly promising for developing low-cost, lead-free, multisource energy-harvesting systems.

### [108] [Quantum weight and low-loss EELS signatures of Wannier quantum geometry in black phosphorus](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08438)
*Vinayak M. Kulkarni,Sharona Horta*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，建立了黑磷（black phosphorus）中动量分辨量子度规（quantum metric）与低损耗电子能量损失谱（EELS）可测量的方向分辨量子权重（quantum weight）之间的理论联系。研究发现，原始单带量子度规因能带折叠和近简并而不具有全局意义，必须使用掩膜映射和占据流形投影子；引入的实验驱动的受限量子权重满足相应的Souza-Wilkens-Martin求和规则，是低损耗EELS的合适可观测量。尽管黑磷存在强能带质量各向异性和仅扶手椅方向的光吸收，但其面内受限量子权重近乎各向同性，而Hubbard-Hartree修正则在亚百分比水平上产生微小的扶手椅方向漂移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子几何（quantum geometry）已在晶体固体中通过实验可及，黑磷是极化分辨角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）的关键平台。本文旨在建立连接动量分辨量子度规与体相可观测量——方向分辨量子权重——的理论框架，使得低损耗EELS可作为各向异性层状材料中集成量子几何的实用探测手段。

Method: 采用32带DFT-Wannier哈密顿量，通过解析动量导数计算单带和占据流形几何量。引入实验驱动的受限量子权重K_ii(ω_c)，排除零损耗区域后满足相应的受限Souza-Wilkens-Martin求和规则。采用轨道分辨的Hubbard-Hartree修正评估电子关联效应。

Result: 原始单带量子度规因折叠简并和带内近简并产生真实孤立带奇点，需用掩膜映射和占据流形投影子处理。受限面内量子权重近乎各向同性，K_zz/K_xx=0.972±0.005，与强带质量各向异性和仅扶手椅方向吸收起始形成对比。轨道分辨Hubbard-Hartree修正使绝对量子权重在亚百分比水平保持刚性，但产生微小的扶手椅方向漂移，约每eV的U增加+0.46%。

Conclusion: 低损耗EELS谱矩可作为各向异性层状材料中集成量子几何的实用探针。实验驱动的受限量子权重是排除零损耗区域后合适的可观测量，其近乎各向同性的特征揭示了黑磷量子几何性质与传统带质量各向异性之间的显著差异。

Abstract: Quantum geometry is now experimentally accessible in crystalline solids, with black phosphorus providing a key platform through polarization-resolved angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy. We develop a first-principles framework that connects the momentum-resolved quantum metric of black phosphorus to a complementary bulk observable: the direction-resolved quantum weight measurable through low-loss electron energy-loss spectroscopy (EELS). A 32-band DFT--Wannier Hamiltonian is used to compute both single-band and occupied-manifold geometric quantities from analytic momentum derivatives. We show that the raw single-band quantum metric of the top valence band is not globally meaningful in the conventional cell because folding degeneracies and intra-valence near degeneracies produce true isolated-band singularities; masked maps and occupied-manifold projectors are therefore essential. Because semilocal PBE produces near-gap semimetallic pockets and spurious subgap interpolation features, we introduce an experimentally motivated restricted quantum weight $K_{ii}(ω_c)$, which obeys the corresponding restricted Souza--Wilkens--Martin sum rule and is the appropriate quantity for low-loss EELS once the zero-loss region is excluded. The restricted in-plane quantum weight is nearly isotropic, $K_{zz}/K_{xx}=0.972\pm0.005$ (armchair/zigzag), despite the strong band-mass anisotropy and armchair-only absorption onset of black phosphorus. Orbital-resolved Hubbard--Hartree corrections leave the absolute quantum weights rigid at the sub-percent level while producing a small but resolved armchair-directed drift of $K_{zz}/K_{xx}$, approximately $+0.46\%$ per eV of $U$. These results identify low-loss EELS spectral moments as a practical probe of integrated quantum geometry in an anisotropic layered material.

### [109] [Exciton valley depolarization in monolayer MoS2: non-Markovian quantum dynamics, intervalley scattering, and the breakdown of the Dyakonov-Perel mechanism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08479)
*Yang-hao Chan,Jonah B. Haber,Mit H. Naik,Felipe H. da Jornada,Diana Y. Qiu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理非平衡激子格林函数（NEGF）结合广义Kadanoff-Baym ansatz（GKBA）方法，系统研究了单层过渡金属二硫化物（TMD）中的激子谷弛豫机制。结果表明，传统认为占主导的Dyakonov-Perel（DP）机制并不成立，大动量区间谷散射（intervalley scattering）才是谷弛豫的主要路径，并揭示了Markovian Lindblad框架在谷赝自旋基下的偏差性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单层过渡金属二硫化物（monolayer transition metal dichalcogenides）中激子（exciton）的谷弛豫（valley relaxation）传统上被归因于Dyakonov-Perel（DP）机制，但该机制对区间谷散射（intervalley scattering）的作用估计不足，且缺乏对全布里渊区激子-声子散射与交换驱动进动的统一处理。作者旨在通过第一性原理方法，在同等水平上全面考察各散射机制，澄清谷弛豫的真正主导路径。

Method: 采用第一性原理非平衡激子格林函数（nonequilibrium exciton Green's function, NEGF）方法，结合广义Kadanoff-Baym ansatz（GKBA），在全布里渊区（full Brillouin zone）内将交换驱动的进动（exchange-driven precession）与激子-声子散射（exciton-phonon scattering）置于同等地位处理。同时与Lindblad型碰撞框架进行对比，以揭示非马尔可夫效应（non-Markovian effects）的作用。

Result: 即使在最有利于DP物理的小动量区域，真实激子-声子散射强度不足以引起DP机制所需的运动窄化（motional narrowing）。考虑全布里渊区激子后，大动量区间谷散射成为谷弛豫的主导路径，使得退极化时间（depolarization time）相比仅考虑谷内散射的模型缩短3–4倍。300 K时谷退极化和退相干时间（decoherence time）约为50 fs，10 K时延长至130 fs。Markovian Lindblad框架在谷赝自旋基（valley-pseudospin basis）下会人为放大散射诱导的平衡化，从而偏向DP解释。

Conclusion: 单层TMD中的激子谷弛豫并非由DP机制主导，而是由大动量区间谷散射主导。NEGF+GKBA导出的激子密度矩阵方法为研究超快激子动力学（ultrafast exciton dynamics）提供了有力工具，且揭示了Markovian近似在特定基矢选择下的局限性。

Abstract: In monolayer transition metal dichalcogenides, exciton valley relaxation is typically attributed to the Dyakonov-Perel (DP) mechanism, where frequent intravalley scattering with phonons or defects suppresses the intervalley exchange-induced precession and the role of intervalley scattering is considered secondary. Employing a first-principles nonequilibrium exciton Green's function (NEGF) approach with the generalized Kadanoff-Baym ansatz (GKBA), which treats exchange-driven precession and exciton-phonon scattering on an equal footing across the full Brillouin zone, we demonstrate that even in the small momentum regime most favorable to DP physics, realistic exciton-phonon scattering is too weak to induce the motional narrowing that defines the DP regime. Upon accounting for excitons across the entire Brillouin zone, large momentum intervalley scattering becomes the dominant pathway for valley relaxation, shortening the depolarization by a factor of 3-4 relative to intravalley-only models. We find that valley depolarization and decoherence time are approximately 50 fs at 300 K and lengthen to 130 fs at 10 K. By comparing our results with a Lindblad-type collision framework, we explicitly demonstrate the role of non-Markovian effects and reveal that the Markovian Lindblad framework is highly basis dependent. In the valley-pseudospin basis underlying prior analyses, the Lindblad approach artificially amplifies scattering-induced equilibration, biasing the dynamics toward a DP interpretation. Our study provides a comprehensive picture of valley relaxation, and establishes the exciton density matrix approach derived from NEGF+GKBA as a powerful tool for investigating ultrafast exciton dynamics.

### [110] [PhononScore: a phonon-aware scoring function for dynamical stability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08518)
*Xiao-Qi Han,Ze-Feng Gao,Zhong-Yi Lu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出PhononScore，一种基于声子谱感知（phonon-aware）的评分函数，用于快速评估晶体生成结构的动力学稳定性（dynamical stability）。该方法在秒级计算成本下，将候选结构的平均稳定性率从30.7%提升至83.7%，Top-10候选稳定性率达97.5%，可作为高效稳定性评估工具用于高通量材料发现、主动学习（active learning）和强化学习（reinforcement learning）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有晶体生成模型（crystal generation models）能够设计大量候选材料，但生成结构的动力学稳定性严重不足，已成为阻碍其实际应用于材料发现的主要瓶颈。传统的显式声子计算（explicit phonon calculations）计算成本高昂，无法满足大规模筛选需求。

Method: 构建包含157,463个晶体结构的多保真度声子数据集（multi-fidelity phonon dataset）；基于该数据集训练PhononScore模型，从晶体结构直接预测统一的稳定性评分（stability score），避免显式声子计算。提供PhononBench基准测试集，并针对高保真DFT-PBE声子基准微调PhononScore-DFT版本。

Result: 在PhononBench上，PhononScore将9种晶体生成模型候选池的平均动力学稳定性率从30.7%提升至83.7%，实现2.72倍的稳定结构富集；Top-10候选平均稳定性率达97.5%。PhononScore-DFT在DFT-PBE高保真基准上将Top-100稳定性率提升至93.0%，在极端不平衡硬筛选场景下实现5-6倍稳定结构富集。

Conclusion: PhononScore可作为类似于药物发现中评分函数（scoring function）的材料筛选工具，直接为晶体生成、主动学习和强化学习提供动力学稳定性反馈信号，实现秒级稳定性感知重排序（stability-aware reranking），为高通量材料发现和闭环逆向设计（closed-loop inverse design）提供统一高效的动力学稳定性评估器。

Abstract: In recent years, crystal generation models have enabled the design of massive numbers of candidate materials. However, the lack of dynamical stability among generated structures has become a major bottleneck preventing their translation into practical materials discovery. To address this challenge, we propose PhononScore, a phonon-aware scoring function for crystal generation. Unlike computationally expensive explicit phonon calculations, PhononScore predicts a unified stability score from crystal structures, enabling ranking of candidate materials dynamical stability with second-level computational cost. We construct a multi-fidelity phonon dataset containing 157,463 crystal structures. On the PhononBench benchmark, PhononScore improves the average dynamical stability rate of candidate pools generated by nine crystal generation models from 30.7% to 83.7%, achieving a 2.72-fold enrichment of stable structures, while the average stability rate of the Top-10 candidates reaches 97.5%. On a high-fidelity DFT-PBE phonon benchmark, the DFT-finetuned PhononScore-DFT increases the Top-100 stability rate to 93.0% and achieves 5-6-fold enrichment of dynamically stable structures under an extremely imbalanced hard-screening scenario. As a materials-screening tool analogous to scoring functions in drug discovery, PhononScore can serve directly as a dynamical-stability feedback signal for crystal generation, active learning, and reinforcement learning, enabling second-level stability-aware reranking without explicit phonon calculations and providing a unified and efficient dynamical stability evaluator for high-throughput materials discovery, active learning, reinforcement learning, and closed-loop inverse design. The online PhononScore platform is available at: http://phononbench.cn/phononscore/

</details>


### [111] [A crystal-field route to THz-driven magnetization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08519)
*T. Zalewski,M. S. Mrudul,Y. Lee,M. Weissenhofer,A. V. Boris,P. M. Oppeneer,A. Kirilyuk,C. S. Davies*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过超快法拉第光谱学实验证明，稀土绝缘体CeF₃中的晶场激发（crystal-field excitations）是圆偏振太赫兹光产生磁化（magnetization）的微观途径，并展示了该响应随激发波长调谐呈现色散性反转，揭示了晶场激发作为光学角动量动力学储层的新角色。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光携带角动量，但将其转化为磁化（magnetization）的微观路径尚不明确；本文旨在探索晶场激发（crystal-field excitations）是否构成其中一条活性微观渠道。

Method: 采用波长选择性的超快法拉第光谱学（ultrafast Faraday spectroscopy），对顺磁性绝缘体（paramagnetic insulator）CeF₃进行实验，通过共振激发局域化4f晶场跃迁（crystal-field transitions），测量螺旋依赖性磁化（helicity-dependent magnetization）的响应特征。

Result: 共振激发4f晶场跃迁产生持续约100皮秒（ps）的螺旋依赖性磁化；在固定光学螺旋度（optical helicity）条件下，THz驱动的响应随激发波长调谐跨过晶场共振时发生符号反转；该色散谱响应遵循晶场激发谱而非光学声子谱。

Conclusion: 晶场激发是此前未被认识到的光学角动量动力学储层（dynamical reservoir for optical angular momentum），拓宽了THz光产生和调控磁性态的微观路径；该结果可由逆法拉第效应（inverse Faraday effect）的共振电子理论（resonant electronic theory）捕获。

Abstract: Light carries angular momentum, but the microscopic pathways that transform it into magnetization remain elusive. Here we establish that crystal-field excitations, historically viewed primarily as equilibrium spectroscopic fingerprints of localized 4$f$ electrons, constitute an active microscopic route through which circularly-polarized terahertz (THz) light creates magnetic polarization. Using wavelength-selective ultrafast Faraday spectroscopy on the paramagnetic insulator CeF$_3$, we show that resonant excitation of localized 4$f$ crystal-field transitions generates a helicity-dependent magnetization that survives for up to about 100 ps. Most strikingly, while the optical helicity is held fixed, the THz-driven response reverses sign as the excitation wavelength is tuned across the crystal-field resonance. The resulting dispersive spectral response follows the crystal-field excitation spectrum rather than that of optical phonons, and is captured by resonant electronic theory of the inverse Faraday effect. Our results identify crystal-field excitations as a previously unrecognized dynamical reservoir for optical angular momentum and broaden the microscopic pathways through which THz light can create and manipulate magnetic states.

### [112] [Barnett effect generated by a rotating electric field in a ferromagnetic film](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08597)
*Jorge F. Soriano,Eugene M. Chudnovsky*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用经典连续介质电动力学（classical electrodynamics of continuous media）与连续弹性理论（continuous elastic theory）进行解析分析，同时利用原子晶格上离散化的Landau-Lifshitz自旋动力学（Landau-Lifshitz spin dynamics）进行数值模拟。

Result: 在典型磁性氧化物参数下，研究了不同场频率、场振幅、磁各向异性（magnetic anisotropy）、交换作用（exchange）和阻尼（damping）强度对效应的影响，并证实了使用电场脉冲反转岛磁化的可能性。

Conclusion: 旋转电场脉冲可通过Barnett效应在铁磁岛中诱导磁化，且在一定条件下能够实现磁化方向的反转，这为电场驱动的磁化操控提供了新的途径。

Abstract: We investigate the space-time evolution of the magnetization induced in a 2D ferromagnetic island by a short pulse of a rotating electric field. The field generates elastic twists that act on the magnetization via the Barnett effect: magnetization by rotation. Analytical studies are conducted within classical electrodynamics of continuous media and continuous elastic theory, while numerical studies are performed using discretized Landau-Lifshitz spin dynamics on the atomic lattice. The effect is studied for typical parameters of magnetic oxides at various field frequencies and amplitudes, and for various strengths of magnetic anisotropy, exchange, and damping. The possibility of reversing the island magnetization with an electric-field pulse is demonstrated.

### [113] [An Efficient Method for Gibbs Free Energy Evaluation under Volume Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08608)
*Zhiyuan Gao,Yong Yang,Yoshiyuki Kawazoe*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 提出一种基于插值的吉布斯自由能高效计算方法，仅需在少数体积点计算声子谱，通过有效 Grüneisen 参数重构静态-零点能分支、分模式 Grüneisen 斜率重构有限温度振动分支，在保持与准谐近似（QHA）基准相当精度（平均 MAE 0.148 meV/atom）的同时，将显式声子体积点从约 20–21 个降至 3 个，速度提升约 5.9–9.0 倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确计算吉布斯自由能（Gibbs free energy）对于构建压力-温度相图至关重要，但基于准谐近似（quasi-harmonic approximation, QHA）的传统方法需要在大量体积点上计算声子谱，计算成本高昂。因此，亟需一种更高效的方法来评估体积压缩下的吉布斯自由能。

Method: 基于少量第一性原理数据点的插值方法：仅在选定体积上计算声子谱；利用从零点能（zero-point energy, ZPE）导出的有效 Grüneisen 参数重构静态-零点能分支（static-ZPE branch）；利用分模式解析的 Grüneisen 斜率（piecewise mode-resolved Grüneisen slopes）在目标体积网格上重构有限温度振动分支（finite-temperature vibrational branches）。

Result: 对金刚石（C）、Al、Si、Ge、金红石 TiO₂、β-PtO₂ 等简单体系，吉布斯自由能相对于 QHA 基准的平均绝对误差（MAE）均低于 0.53 meV/atom，六体系平均值为 0.148 meV/atom，而显式声子体积点从约 20–21 个减少至 3 个；对更复杂的 Ta₂O₅ 多晶型，尽管相位依赖误差较大，仍能重构主要的相稳定性拓扑结构。相对于 QHA 工作流，速度提升 5.911–9.023 倍，在声子频率随体积平滑变化的中等压缩范围内保持可靠。

Conclusion: 该插值方法显著降低了吉布斯自由能计算的计算成本，同时保持了与 QHA 基准相当的精度，尤其适用于中等压缩范围、声子频率随体积平滑变化的体系。

Abstract: Accurate evaluation of Gibbs free energies is essential for constructing pressure-temperature phase diagrams. Conventional methods based on the quasi-harmonic approximation (QHA) require phonon spectra at many volume points and are therefore expensive in general. Here we develop an efficient method based on the interpolation of a few ab initio data points for Gibbs free energy evaluation under volume compression. Phonon spectra are calculated only at selected volumes. An effective Gruneisen parameter derived from the zero-point energy (ZPE) reconstructs the static-ZPE branch, while piecewise mode-resolved Gruneisen slopes reconstruct the finite-temperature vibrational branches on the target volume grids. The method is validated against QHA benchmarks for diamond (C), Al, Si, Ge, rutile TiO2, beta-PtO2, and Ta2O5 polymorphs. For simple benchmark systems (C, Al, Si, Ge, rutile TiO2, and beta-PtO2), the Gibbs free energy mean absolute errors (MAEs) relative to the QHA benchmarks remain below 0.53 meV/atom, with a six-system average of 0.148 meV/atom, while the number of explicit phonon volume points is reduced from about 20-21 to 3 in the lowest-cost implementation. For the more complex Ta2O5 polymorphs, the reconstructed free energies reproduce the main phase-stability topology despite larger phase-dependent errors. With reference to the QHA workflows, the interpolation method in this work achieves speedups of 5.911-9.023 times and remains reliable for moderate compression ranges where phonon frequencies vary smoothly with volume.

Method: 开发了基于MACE的机器学习原子间势，通过第一性原理分子动力学（first-principles molecular dynamics）轨迹训练，生成并分析了含有多达5120个原子的大尺度非晶结构。

Conclusion: 建立了非晶氧化铟的全面结构-性质关系（structure-property picture），提供了可直接实验验证的预测，并表明可控非晶化（controlled amorphization）是提升a-In$_2$O$_3$光电化学活性的可行策略。

Abstract: Amorphous indium oxide (a-In$_2$O$_3$) is a high-electron-mobility semiconductor of central importance in thin-film transistors and a promising photoanode for solar-driven water oxidation. Despite sustained experimental and computational investigations, the structural motifs underlying its unusual transport properties and the existence of O-O peroxide-like bonds within its network have remained unresolved. Here we develop a MACE-based machine-learned interatomic potential trained on first-principles molecular dynamics trajectories and use it to generate and analyze amorphous structures containing up to 5120 atoms, two orders of magnitude larger than those adopted in typical ab initio studies. We find X-ray structure factors in excellent quantitative agreement with experiment and we confirm that In$_2$O$_3$ is a poor glass former, with the likely presence of quasi-crystalline regions in amorphous samples. Our large-scale structural analysis reveals extended chains of edge-sharing InO$_k$ polyhedra providing a concrete structural basis for the high electron mobility of a-In$_2$O$_3$. Our results strongly support the formation of O-O peroxide-like bonds in the amorphous network, with a mean length of 1.5 Å. We show that these bonds introduce localized in-gap states near the conduction band minimum, acting as a source of intrinsic n-type self-doping and enhancing sub-gap optical absorption. These effects are detectable via a distinct Raman feature near 850 cm$^{-1}$ that is absent in the IR spectrum. Overall, our results establish a comprehensive structure-property picture of a-In$_2$O$_3$, provide directly testable experimental predictions, and suggest that controlled amorphization is a viable strategy for improving the photoelectrochemical activity of a-In$_2$O$_3$.

### [115] [Harnessing orbital Hall effect for energy-efficient magnetization switching in room-temperature van der Waals ferromagnet Fe3GaTe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08618)

Method: 采用Fe₃GaTe₂/Pt(1.5 nm)/Cr(4.5 nm)三层结构：以Cr作为轨道电流（orbital current）源，产生的轨道电流经由超薄Pt层转化为自旋电流（spin current），进而对二维范德华铁磁体Fe₃GaTe₂施加扭矩实现磁化翻转。

Electrically manipulating the magnetization of vdW magnets is key to realizing 2D SOT-MRAM, whereas conventional spin Hall materials such as heavy metals and topological insulators suffer from limitations in torque efficiency and energy consumption. Although recent studies show that the orbital Hall conductivity in light metals greatly exceeds the spin Hall conductivity, direct experimental demonstrations that the orbital Hall effect (OHE) can induce more energy-efficient SOT switching than the spin Hall effect in vdW magnets remain scarce. Here, we utilize Cr as the orbital current source to efficiently manipulate the magnetization of the vdW ferromagnet Fe3GaTe2 at room temperature. In the Fe3GaTe2/Pt (1.5 nm)/Cr (4.5 nm) trilayer structure, the orbital current originating from Cr is converted into the spin current via Pt, which then exerts a torque on Fe3GaTe2. Compared with control samples using 6 nm Pt as the spin current source, the switching current density in OHE-based devices is reduced by 3.9 times, resulting in a 52% reduction in power consumption. This work presents the promising potential of harnessing orbital currents to realize energy-efficient 2D SOT-MRAM.

### [116] [Physical aging of glasses of an organic semiconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08653)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: All glasses, including organic semiconductor glasses, are non-equilibrium materials whose properties will change with time. This physical aging process is poorly understood for organic semiconductors, hindering the rational design of highly durable devices. In this study, we investigated the volume and enthalpy recovery processes in both thin films and bulk glasses of N,N'-Bis(3-methylphenyl)-N,N'-diphenylbenzidine (TPD). Our results revealed that volume recovery kinetics exhibit negligible dependence on film thickness for liquid-cooled TPD films between 400 nm and 100 nm. Additionally, the volume recovery process in TPD films was strongly coupled to the enthalpy recovery observed in bulk TPD glasses during annealing near the glass transition temperature. Remarkably, TPD films prepared by physical vapor deposition at room temperature demonstrated exceptional resistance to physical aging, with an aging rate approximately one order of magnitude lower than that of their liquid-cooled counterparts. These results not only enhance our understanding of the non-equilibrium dynamics in amorphous systems but also offer valuable insights for the design of next-generation organic devices with significantly improved stability and durability.

### [117] [Best Practices for First-Principles Modeling of Amorphous Oxide Semiconductors: A Statistical Framework and Application to Zn-Sn-O](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08667)
*Michiel J. van Setten,Tonglin L. Newsom,Christopher Pashartis,Vera van Noort,Rebecca L. Peterson,Geoffrey Pourtois*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文以Zn-Sn-O体系为例，指出对非晶氧化物半导体进行第一性原理计算时需注意的陷阱，强调理解晶相与非晶相物理差异及统计采样的重要性，并预测该材料可能具有类似IGZO的氢致掺杂敏感性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三元及四元非晶氧化物半导体（amorphous oxide semiconductors）在显示、存储及后段逻辑等电子应用中极具潜力，但如何针对具体应用筛选材料并优化其性能，需深入理解相关物理与化学机制。第一性原理计算（first principles computations）若能正确执行，可有效提升这种理解。

Method: 以Zn-Sn-O体系为案例，运用第一性原理计算，系统性地分析了研究中常见的若干陷阱，重点考察了晶相与非晶/无序相物理本质的区别，并对结构模型进行了恰当的统计采样（statistical sampling）。

Result: 计算结果表明，从迁移率（mobility）和初始阈值电压（initial threshold voltage）等性能指标来看，Zn-Sn-O体系是一类有前景的材料。然而，该材料可能表现出与IGZO类似的氢致掺杂（hydrogen induced doping）敏感性。

Conclusion: 对非晶氧化物半导体进行第一性原理计算时，必须正确理解晶相与非晶相之间的基本物理差异，并对结构模型进行充分统计采样，否则可能导致误导性结论。Zn-Sn-O体系性能良好，但需警惕其氢致掺杂效应。

Abstract: Ternary and quaternary amorphous oxide semiconductors have many properties that make them promising candidates for use in electronic applications like display, memory, and back end of line logic. However, finding the right material for a given application and optimizing its properties, deposition, and integration, requires a thorough understanding of the physics and chemistry at play. When properly carried out, first principles computations can play a crucial role in enhancing this understanding. In this work, we highlight several pitfalls often observed in research applying these computations, with the Zn-Sn-O system as an example. We show that a proper understanding of the fundamental differences between the physics of the crystalline and amorphous or disordered phases is crucial, as is a proper statistical sampling of structural models. For the Zn-Sn-O system we conclude that from a performance point of view, mobility and initial threshold voltage, it is a promising material class. However, our computed results show that a similar sensitivity to hydrogen induced doping may be present as in IGZO.

</details>


### [118] [Microwave Studies of Single Crystal TeO2 at Cryogenic Temperatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08668)
*Timothy Holt,Maxim Goryachev,William Campbell,Michael E. Tobar*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用回音壁模式（whispering-gallery-mode）分析，在低温环境下表征单晶TeO₂的微波介电性质，将其损耗性能与其他低损耗介电材料进行比较。通过有限元建模与室温、4 K和20 mK下的测量相结合，提取出各向异性介电常数，并测得超高品质因子（quality factor）和极低损耗角正切（loss tangent），表明TeO₂是低温微波应用中有潜力的低损耗介电材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找在低温微波应用中具有极低介电损耗的新材料，并系统性地评估单晶TeO₂在该领域中的性能表现。

Method: 采用回音壁模式（whispering-gallery-mode）分析法表征微波介电性质；结合有限元建模（finite-element modelling）与室温、4 K、20 mK三个温度点的测量，提取各向异性介电常数（anisotropic dielectric permittivities）；使用电子自旋共振（electron-spin-resonance, ESR）光谱评估自旋环境纯净度。

Result: 测得各向异性介电常数：$\varepsilon_\parallel=25.75\pm0.08$，$\varepsilon_\perp=20.90\pm0.07$；损耗测量显示品质因子（quality factor）高达$9\times10^6$，最小损耗角正切（loss tangent）接近$3\times10^{-8}$；ESR光谱表明自旋环境洁净，并识别出与晶体已知性质一致的多个自旋系统。

Conclusion: 单晶TeO₂具备极高的品质因子和极低的损耗角正切，同时拥有洁净的自旋环境，是一种有前景的低温微波低损耗介电材料。

Abstract: We use whispering-gallery-mode analysis to characterise the microwave dielectric properties of single-crystal TeO$_2$ at cryogenic temperatures and compare its loss performance with other low-loss dielectric materials. Finite-element modelling is combined with measurements at room temperature, 4 K, and 20 mK to develop accurate cryogenic simulations and extract the anisotropic dielectric permittivities, giving $\varepsilon_\parallel=25.75\pm0.08$ and $\varepsilon_\perp=20.90\pm0.07$. Loss measurements reveal quality factors as high as $9\times10^6$ and minimum loss tangents approaching $3\times10^{-8}$, placing TeO$_2$ among promising low-loss dielectrics for cryogenic microwave applications. Electron-spin-resonance spectroscopy further indicates a clean spin environment, while identifying distinct spin systems consistent with the known properties of the crystal.

### [119] [Complex polar superstructure controlled thermal conductivity in ferroelectric PbTiO3/SrTiO3 superlattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08683)
*Noa Varela-Domínguez,Marcel S. Claro,Araceli Gutiérrez-Llorente,Eric Langenberg,Xinxin Hu,Núria Bagués,Anthony Edgeton,Chang Beom-Eom,Jordi Arbiol,José Santiso,Francisco Rivadulla*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文发现PTO/STO超晶格中极性涡旋的三维超晶体排列能够显著抑制热导率，其温度依赖性反映了极性超结构的演变，且热导率随超晶格厚度增加而异常降低，类似声子波安德森局域化现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将铁电PbTiO3与顺电SrTiO3的外延薄膜集成到人工层状周期性超晶格中，为调控应变、去极化场及界面/表面能提供了独特平台，从而可获得拓扑极性结构（topological polar structures）和超结构（superstructures）的丰富相图。然而，这些极性超结构对热输运性质的影响尚不清楚。

Method: 制备了PTO/STO超晶格（SLs），通过测量热导率（thermal conductivity, k）的温度依赖性，并结合X射线衍射（X-ray diffraction）和透射电子显微镜（transmission electron microscopy）表征极性超结构的演变。同时，与其他超晶格进行对比实验，并研究了超晶格厚度对热导率的影响。

Result: 超晶体中极性涡旋（polar vortices）的三维排列显著抑制了热导率；热导率的温度依赖性反映了极性超结构的演化；与其他超晶格的对比表明，三维排列对调控热导率的作用超越常规的界面散射（interfacial scattering）；此外，观察到热导率随超晶格厚度增加而意外降低，该现象类似于声子波安德森局域化（phonon-wave Anderson localization）。

Conclusion: 复杂的极性超结构可作为有效的主动元件，用于调控需要精确控制热耗散（heat dissipation）的技术中的热传输（heat transport）。

Abstract: Integrating epitaxial thin films of ferroelectric PbTiO3 and paraelectric SrTiO3 into artificially layered periodic superlattices provides a unique platform for tuning strain, depolarization, and interfacial/surface energies, thereby accessing a rich phase diagram of topological polar structures (skyrmions, vortices, merons, or sinusoidal waves) and superstructures (polar supercrystals). Here we show that the 3D arrangement of polar vortices in a supercrystal suppresses thermal conductivity (k) of PTO/STO superlattices (SLs). The temperature dependence of k reflects the evolution of the polar superstructure, as determined by X-ray diffraction and transmission electron microscopy. The comparison with other SLs suggests that the 3D arrangement is crucial for controlling thermal conductivity beyond the usual interfacial scattering. Moreover, we observed an unexpected reduction in thermal conductivity with increasing superlattice thickness, a phenomenon reminiscent of phonon-wave Anderson localization. Our results show that complex polar superstructures can be useful active elements for modulating heat transport in technologies where control over heat dissipation is critical.

</details>

### [120] [Seven- and eight-loop critical exponents of the three-dimensional Ising model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07776)
*D. Shapoval,Yu. Honchar,B. Delamotte,M. Dudka,Yu. Holovatch*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文通过共形映射（conformal mapping）结合同调变换（homographic transformation）对三维伊辛普适类（three-dimensional Ising universality class）的七环与八环重整化群（renormalization group）ε-展开级数进行重求和（resummation），精确估算了临界指数 η、ν 和修正标度指数 ω。研究发现 η 的误差随环数快速减小，但 ν 和 ω 收敛较慢，导致与共形自举（conformal bootstrap）基准估计值之间存在轻微但系统的张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维伊辛普适类的临界指数（critical exponents）是统计力学（statistical mechanics）和量子场论中的核心可观测量，但高阶微扰级数收敛性差，需要可靠的重求和方法来获得精确估计。已有共形自举（conformal bootstrap）方法提供了被广泛视为基准的结果，但微扰重整化群（perturbative renormalization group）方法的最新高阶计算（七环和八环）尚需与之系统比较。

Method: 采用共形映射（conformal mapping）结合同调变换（homographic transformation）作为重求和（resummation）方法，并依据两个互补性判据（complementary criteria）优化重求和参数，处理最近计算出的 ε=4-d 展开下的七环和八环重整化群级数。

Result: 获得了临界指数 η、ν 和修正标度指数 ω 的精确估计值及定量不确定度。η 的误差棒（error bar）随环数增加快速减小，但 ν 和 ω 的误差棒并未表现出同样的快速收敛。估计值在绝对意义上足够准确，但由于随环数收敛较慢，与目前作为基准的共形自举（conformal bootstrap）估计值之间存在轻微但系统的张力。

Conclusion: 讨论了这一张力可能的若干起源，包括高阶微扰级数的收敛特性及其对高阶重求和（high-order resummation）的启示。该研究为理解微扰重整化群（perturbative renormalization group）方法在高阶下的行为以及不同计算框架之间的一致性提供了重要参考。

Abstract: We determine the critical exponents $η$, $ν$, and the correction-to-scaling exponent $ω$ of the three-dimensional Ising universality class by resumming the recently computed seven- and eight-loop renormalization-group series in the $ε=4-d$ expansion (O.~Schnetz, \textit{Phys. Rev. D} \textbf{97}, 085018 (2018); O.~Schnetz, \textit{Phys. Rev. D} \textbf{107}, 036002 (2023)). The resummation combines conformal mapping with a homographic transformation, while the resummation parameters are optimized according to two complementary criteria. This approach yields precise estimates of the critical exponents together with quantitative uncertainty estimates. We find that the error bar on $η$ decreases rapidly with increasing loop order, whereas this is the case neither for $ν$ nor for $ω$. Unexpectedly, although the estimated values are accurate in absolute terms, their slow convergence with the loop order leads to a slight but systematic tension with the conformal bootstrap estimates that are currently considered as the benchmark. We discuss several possible origins of this behavior and its implications for high-order resummations of perturbative renormalization-group series.
