### [121] [Fluctuation theorems for autonomous work](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07843)
*Christopher Jarzynski,Sebastian Deffner,Saar Rahav*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文在自治框架（autonomous framework）中推导出功和熵产生的涨落定理（fluctuation theorems），该框架下系统与可逆功源（reversible work source）在无外部干预的条件下通过哈密顿或随机动力学（Hamiltonian or stochastic dynamics）相互作用，并考虑了系统对功源的反作用（back-action）。当功源的惯性趋于无穷大时，自治涨落定理约化为非自治（non-autonomous）形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典功涨落定理在非自治框架下已得到理论和实验验证，但该框架依赖外部对功参数（如活塞位置）的操控。本研究旨在将涨落定理推广到自治框架，即系统与可逆功源在无外部干预下自发相互作用，从而更真实地描述无外部操控的热力学过程。

Method: 采用自治框架，将系统（𝒮）与可逆功源（ℛ）视为两个相互作用的子系统，二者在哈密顿动力学或随机动力学下共同演化。在此设置中，纳入系统对功源的反作用，这是非自治框架所缺失的要素。通过分析自治动力学的统计性质，推导出功和熵产生的涨落定理。

Result: 获得了功和熵产生在自治框架下的标准涨落定理，并发现当功源（ℛ）的惯性趋于无穷大时，自治涨落定理约化为已知的非自治涨落定理。

Conclusion: 自治涨落定理统一了自治与非自治框架，揭示了功源惯性在两种表述之间的关键作用，为理解无外部操控的热力学涨落提供了更基础的理论基础。

Abstract: Classical fluctuation theorems for work have been obtained theoretically, and verified experimentally, within a non-autonomous framework in which work is performed on a system of interest, ${\cal S}$, by the external manipulation of a work parameter, such as a piston's position. Here we obtain fluctuation theorems within an autonomous framework in which ${\cal S}$ exchanges energy with a reversible work source, ${\cal R}$. The two subsystems, ${\cal R}$ and ${\cal S}$, interact with one another as they evolve under Hamiltonian or stochastic dynamics, without external intervention. In this setting, we must account for the back-action of ${\cal S}$ on ${\cal R}$, which is absent in the non-autonomous setting. We obtain autonomous versions of standard fluctuation theorems for work and entropy production. In each case, we argue, the autonomous fluctuation theorem reduces to its non-autonomous counterpart when ${\cal R}$'s inertia becomes infinitely large.

</details>


### [122] [Equilibrium in a Reaction Network of Assemblies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07959)
*Giampaolo Folena,Germán Kruszewski*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个平均场反应网络，其物种由相同原子通过可逆凝聚与碎裂（coagulation and fragmentation）组装成有序二叉树，物种数量随长度呈卡塔兰数（Catalan numbers）增长。模型存在显式平衡态和易处理的随机动力学，有限体积V定义了交叉长度l_c ~ ln V，将平衡态分为两个区域：低于l_c时出现Zipf分布（Zipf-like），高于l_c时物种稀少且受涨落主导。稀有区的统计权重随体积缓慢衰减，控制了多样性、香农熵（Shannon entropy）等可观测量的有限尺寸标度。该平衡态可作为衡量更复杂组装网络中选择和驱动的受控中性基线（neutral baseline）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提出一个兼具组合复杂性和解析可解性的均值场反应网络模型，以理解物种组装过程中的统计行为和有限尺寸效应，并为更复杂的网络中自然选择（selection）和外部驱动（driving）的效应提供中性基线。

Method: 定义物种为有序二叉树，物种数量由卡塔兰数描述；考虑可逆凝聚和碎裂反应；引入有限体积V定义交叉长度l_c；通过解析和随机动力学方法分析平衡态性质。

Result: 模型存在显式平衡态。当物种长度低于l_c时，每个组装体出现多次，秩-频分布呈现Zipf-like特征；高于l_c时，物种稀少且受涨落主导。稀有区统计权重视体积缓慢衰减，控制着多样性和香农熵的有限尺寸标度。平衡态可用键能（bond energy）和原子化学势（atomic chemical potential）进行巨正则描述。

Conclusion: 该模型构成了一个受控的中性基线，可用于衡量更丰富的组装网络中选择和驱动的影响。

Abstract: We study a mean-field reaction network whose species are assemblies built from identical atoms by reversible coagulation and fragmentation. Each assembly is an ordered binary tree, so the number of species of a given length grows combinatorially, as the Catalan numbers. The model nonetheless admits an explicit equilibrium and tractable stochastic dynamics. A finite volume $V$ sets a crossover length $l_c \sim \ln V$ that splits the equilibrium into two sectors. Below $l_c$ each assembly occurs in many copies and the rank-frequency distribution is Zipf-like; above $l_c$ individual species are rare and fluctuation-dominated. The statistical weight of the rare sector decays slowly with volume, controlling the finite-size scaling of diversity, Shannon entropy, and other assembly-weighted observables. The equilibrium also admits a transparent grand-canonical description in terms of a bond energy and an atomic chemical potential. Together these results make the model a controlled neutral baseline against which selection and driving in richer assembly networks can be measured.

</details>


### [123] [Universality of Measurement-Induced Criticality under Symmetry-Breaking Measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08589)
*Angelo Russotto,Filiberto Ares,Pasquale Calabrese*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有U(1)对称性的随机量子电路在局域投影测量破坏该对称性时的临界性质，发现对称性破缺测量在测量诱导相变中充当相关扰动，导致与非对称幺正动力学电路相同的普适临界性质。在局域希尔伯特空间维度无穷大极限下，电荷关联长度在任何测量率下均有限，排除了电荷锐化相变的存在，并通过数值有限尺寸标度分析验证了有限维度下的结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索具有U(1)对称性的随机量子电路中，局域投影测量明确破坏该对称性时系统的临界性质，特别是对称性破缺测量对测量诱导相变（measurement-induced phase transition）和电荷锐化相变（charge-sharpening transition）的影响。

Method: 利用局域希尔伯特空间维度无穷大极限下的经典统计力学（statistical mechanics）模型精确求解轨迹平均纠缠熵，其中守恒律对应的电荷服从对称简单排斥过程（symmetric simple exclusion process），对称性破缺测量对应无序缺陷；结合有限维度下的Haar随机电路与稳定子随机电路（stabilizer random circuit）进行数值有限尺寸标度分析。

Result: 对称性破缺测量在测量诱导相变处充当相关扰动（relevant perturbation），导致与非对称幺正动力学电路相同的普适临界性质；电荷关联长度（charge correlation length）在任何测量率下均有限，从而排除了电荷锐化相变；有限维度下的数值分析进一步支持了上述结论。

Conclusion: 对称性破缺测量不会引发电荷锐化相变，但会改变测量诱导相变的普适类，使其等价于非对称幺正动力学情形下的相变行为。

Abstract: We study the critical properties of random quantum circuits with a $U(1)$ symmetry subject to local projective measurements that explicitly break this symmetry. We find that, at the measurement-induced phase transition, symmetry-breaking measurements act as a relevant perturbation at large scales, leading to the same universal critical properties as the corresponding monitored random circuit with non-symmetric unitary dynamics. In particular, we consider monitored $U(1)$-symmetric Haar-random circuits in the limit of large local Hilbert-space dimension, where the trajectory-averaged entanglement entropy can be exactly obtained in terms of a classical statistical mechanics model. In this model, the charge associated with the conservation law follows a symmetric simple exclusion process, in which symmetry-breaking measurements correspond to disordered defects that create and destroy charges. We prove that the charge correlation length remains finite for any measurement rate, ruling out a charge-sharpening transition, in contrast to the case of symmetry-preserving measurements. We further support our predictions at finite local Hilbert-space dimension through numerical finite-size scaling analyses of the entanglement transition in monitored $U(1)$-symmetric Haar and stabilizer random circuits.

</details>

### [124] [The Status of Single Scalar Field Dark Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07777)
*Carlos García-García,Pedro G. Ferreira,William J. Wolf*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文对单标量场（single scalar field）暗能量模型的当前观测现状进行了评估。在有效场论（effective field theory, EFT）框架下，论证了宇宙学观测只能约束少量参数；显示精粹场（quintessence）与宇宙学常数仅勉强可区分，更一般的EFT扩展模型虽有微弱统计偏好，但受数据集选择和先验假设影响显著，并面临第五力（fifth forces）与结构增长修正等天体物理约束的挑战。未来第四阶段巡天（Stage IV surveys）虽能略收紧约束，但欠定问题（underdetermination）仍将持续。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受最新宇宙学测量（重子声学振荡、Ia型超新星、宇宙微波背景辐射数据）的驱动，检验动力学标量场是否为宇宙加速膨胀提供可行解释。

Method: 在有效场论（effective field theory, EFT）框架下分析单标量场暗能量模型，利用重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillations）、Ia型超新星（Type Ia supernovae）和宇宙微波背景辐射（CMB）数据，结合结构增长速率测量、Integrated Sachs-Wolfe（ISW）效应及太阳系约束进行比较。

Result: 精粹场（quintessence）与宇宙学常数仅勉强可区分；更一般的EFT扩展模型呈现微弱统计偏好，但该证据对数据集选择和先验假设敏感。当前ISW与增长数据大体一致。未来第四阶段巡天（Stage IV surveys）对暗能量约束有所收紧，但欠定问题（underdetermination）仍将持续。

Conclusion: 单标量场暗能量模型虽是一个自然且灵活的框架，但其最终可行性将取决于改进的低红移（low-redshift）结构增长测量以及对引力屏蔽（gravitational screening）机制的更清晰理解。

Abstract: We present an assessment of the current observational status of single scalar field models of dark energy. Motivated by recent cosmological measurements -- including baryon acoustic oscillations, Type Ia supernovae, and CMB data -- we examine whether a dynamical scalar field offers a viable explanation for the accelerated expansion of the Universe. Working within an effective field theory (EFT) framework, we argue that cosmological observations are fundamentally limited and can at most constrain a small number of parameters that govern scalar field dynamics. We show that quintessence remains only marginally distinguishable from a cosmological constant, $Λ$, and that more general EFT extensions exhibit modest statistical preference, though such evidence is sensitive to data set selection and prior assumptions. These extended models generically predict fifth forces and modifications to the growth of structure, raising challenges from astrophysical constraints. We compare their predictions with current growth rate measurements, Integrated Sachs-Wolfe (ISW) effect and Solar System constraints. We emphasize that viable screening mechanisms remain theoretically non-trivial and observationally testable. On the other hand, we find that current ISW and growth data remain largely in agreement. Looking ahead to Stage IV surveys we forecast improvements in constraints on the dark energy behaviour; although there will be some tightening of bounds, we argue that the problem of underdetermination will persist. We conclude that while single scalar field dark energy remains a natural and flexible framework, its ultimate viability will hinge on improved low-redshift growth measurements and a clearer understanding of gravitational screening.

</details>


### [125] [Phantom crossing from the Standard Model and General Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08120)
*Jinglong Liu,Tucker Manton,Yifu Cai,Antonino Marciano*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于费米子凝聚（fermion condensation）和广义相对论（general relativity）的低红移（low redshift）幻像穿越（phantom crossing）暗能量模型。该模型利用类五元暗能量（quintom-like dark energy）与非线性结构形成反作用（backreaction）的相互作用，在低红移处实现暗能量状态方程（equation of state）从上方和下方两次穿越 $w_{\text{DE}}=-1$，与DESI+CMB+SNIa联合观测及CPL参数化结果一致。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用费米子凝聚（fermion condensation）与广义相对论（general relativity）构造一种新的类五元暗能量（quintom-like dark energy）模型，并通过非线性结构形成（non-linear structure formation）的反作用效应（backreaction）驱动低红移处的动力学演化。

Abstract: Suggestions of a late-time phantom crossing from DESI baryon acoustic oscillation measurements, combined with cosmic microwave background and Type-Ia supernova observations, have renewed interest in non-standard dark energy models. In this Letter, we propose a new realization of a low redshift phantom crossing using only well understood ingredients from fermion condensation and general relativity. Our construction relies on the interplay between effective quintom-like dark energy and backreaction from non-linear structure formation. The full cosmological evolution is consistent with $Λ$CDM until low redshift, where the backreaction starts to become prominent and a phase transition occurs. At this point, the total dark energy equation of state first crosses $w_{\text{DE}}=-1$ from above. For benchmark values of the backreaction energy density, a second crossing from below occurs at a lower redshift, as suggested by recent observation. Fitting our theoretical model with CPL parametrization, we find the result is consistent with the combined DESI+CMB+SNIa data analysis with DESY5, PantheonPlus, and Union3 datasets. Specifically, for backreaction density parameter $Ω_{\rm BR}(z=0) = 0.0572$, the CPL parametrization gives the phantom crossing redshift $z_* \simeq 0.35$, $w_0 \simeq -0.76 $ and $w_a \simeq -0.93$.

### [126] [The statistics of curvature-profile dispersion in primordial black hole formation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08738)
*Albert Escrivà*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个有限作用量（finite-action）框架，用以描述原初黑洞（PBH）形成过程中曲率轮廓的色散（dispersion）效应。研究发现，轮廓形状的随机涨落会显著影响PBH丰度，背景轮廓并非唯一主导因素，而是由高斯统计代价与塌缩阈值降低之间的竞争共同决定。在宽谱和负非高斯性条件下，稀有的形状变形可以主导丰度，并将总丰度提升数个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准曲率扰动（curvature-perturbation）场景中，原初黑洞（PBH）的预测丰度对塌缩阈值（collapse threshold）及原初曲率轮廓（primordial curvature profile）的形状极其敏感（指数依赖），因此需要系统描述轮廓偏离平均形状的色散效应。

Method: 采用多极傅里叶-贝塞尔分解（multipolar Fourier–Bessel decomposition）将高斯场的局部峰变量（peak variables）与残留的径向和角向变形（radial and angular deformations）分离，并用高斯作用量（Gaussian action）归一化；结合球形数值塌缩算例和峰统计（peak statistics）进行分析。

Result: 有限宽度谱及对数局域非高斯性（logarithmic local non-Gaussianity）下，PBH丰度的主导贡献并非来自平均轮廓或最低阈值轮廓，而是由高斯代价与塌缩阈值降低之间的竞争决定；宽谱和负非高斯性可使稀有形状变形主导丰度，将积分丰度提升数个数量级，并降低获得固定PBH丰度所需的功率谱振幅（power-spectrum amplitude）。

Conclusion: 轮廓残差色散（residual profile dispersion）是PBH形成中一项真实的统计要素，对精确估算PBH丰度具有定量上的重要意义。

Abstract: In the standard curvature-perturbation scenario, PBHs form from the collapse of superhorizon curvature fluctuations after horizon re-entry. The predicted abundance is exponentially sensitive to the collapse threshold and hence to the shape of the primordial curvature profile. In this work we develop a finite-action framework to describe curvature-profile dispersion around representative peak profiles. Using a multipolar Fourier--Bessel decomposition, we separate the local peak variables of the Gaussian field from residual radial and angular deformations, normalized by their Gaussian action. We apply the formalism to spherical numerical-collapse examples in order to isolate the effect of radial shape dispersion. For finite-width spectra, and in the presence of logarithmic local non-Gaussianity, we compute the collapse threshold as a function of a coherent shape variable and combine the result with peak statistics. We find that the dominant contribution to the PBH abundance is not necessarily the mean profile, nor simply the profile with the lowest threshold. Instead, it is selected by a competition between the Gaussian cost of realizing a coherent deformation and the exponential gain associated with lowering the collapse threshold. Broad spectra and negative non-Gaussianity can make rare shape deformations dominate the abundance. In the examples studied here, the dominant branches can correspond to several-sigma coherent shape fluctuations while enhancing the integrated abundance by orders of magnitude. Equivalently, including shape dispersion can reduce the power-spectrum amplitude required to obtain a fixed PBH abundance. Our results show that residual profile dispersion is a genuine statistical ingredient in PBH formation and can be quantitatively important for accurate abundance estimates.

</details>

### [127] [Parameter-Space Heat Flow, Gaussian Density Ratios, and Sharp Hermite Truncation Rates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07712)
*Jae Wan Shim*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文将经典 Hermite 生成函数重新解释为相对于单位高斯参考的高斯密度比（Gaussian density ratio），并通过热半群（heat semigroup）在均值参数上的作用引入温度变化。由此建立了 Hermite 逼近误差的抛物型控制原理，并推导了非高斯扰动下 Hermite 系数的加权齐次性，最终给出了 Ornstein–Uhlenbeck 协方差、总阶 Hermite 块能量的精确生成函数以及尖锐的几何 Hermite 截断速率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重新诠释经典 Hermite 生成函数的内在结构，将其与高斯密度比和热半群联系起来，从而为 Hermite 逼近误差提供统一的参数空间分析框架，并解决非高斯扰动下缺乏可用闭合系数公式的问题。

Method: 将 Hermite 生成函数重新定义为相对于单位高斯参考的均值平移高斯密度比；在均值参数变量上施加热半群以产生温度变化；利用参数空间的热方程（heat equation）建立 Hermite 块能量与截断尾部的抛物型控制原理；针对一般协方差的高斯密度比，建立 Hermite 系数的加权齐次性。

Result: 获得了 Ornstein–Uhlenbeck 协方差；推导出总阶 Hermite 块能量的精确生成函数；得到了尖锐的几何 Hermite 截断速率，等于最大绝对协方差缺陷（covariance defect）的平方根；导出了各向同性块与尾部的精确渐近行为。

Conclusion: 该参数空间公式为 Hermite 逼近提供了新的分析工具，尤其适用于接近高斯的动力学分布（kinetic distributions），并在无需闭合系数公式的情况下依然有效。

Abstract: We reinterpret the classical Hermite generating function as a Gaussian density ratio: relative to the unit Gaussian reference, it is the density ratio of a Gaussian with shifted mean and unchanged covariance. Applying the heat semigroup in the mean-parameter variable to this generating function produces the corresponding temperature variation. Thus the heat-semigroup time variable is reinterpreted as the temperature variation of the Gaussian density ratio.
  This parameter-space formulation also gives a parabolic control principle for Hermite approximation errors. Since Hermite projections act in the velocity variable and the heat flow acts in the mean variable, Hermite block energies and truncation tails are subsolutions of the same parameter-space heat equation. This remains useful for heat-evolved non-Gaussian perturbations where no usable closed coefficient formula is available.
  For Gaussian density ratios with general covariance, the Hermite coefficients satisfy a weighted homogeneity in the mean and covariance-defect parameters. This yields Ornstein--Uhlenbeck covariance, an exact generating function for total-degree Hermite block energies, and the sharp geometric Hermite truncation rate, equal to the square root of the largest absolute covariance defect. We also derive precise isotropic block and tail asymptotics and interpret the estimates for near-Gaussian kinetic distributions.

</details>


### [128] [Weak Poincaré Inequalities via Approximate Stochastic Localization: Application to Sampling the Sherrington-Kirkpatrick Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08160)
*Ewan Davies,Holden Lee,Juspreet Singh Sandhu,Jonathan Shi*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种证明弱泛函不等式的新方法：先对逼近随机定域化（stochastic localization, SL）过程的正则分布序列证明该不等式，再通过SL过程的正则性和传导（conductance）论证将其转移至目标分布。利用该策略，本文证明了当逆温度β < 1/2时，Sherrington-Kirkpatrick模型的吉布斯测度（Gibbs measure）满足弱庞加莱不等式（weak Poincaré inequality, WPI）。作为推论，一种更简单的算法——带暖启动的格劳伯动力学（Glauber dynamics with a warm-start）——能够在β < 1/2时高效采样SK模型的吉布斯测度。这是朝着解决“在副本对称（replica-symmetric）区域内SK模型的Glauber动力学快速混合”这一猜想的重要结构性步骤。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有结果[arXiv:2605.03718, 2026]证明了SK模型的增广随机定域化（ASL）过程满足所需的正则性条件；本文旨在利用该正则性，发展一种将弱泛函不等式从正则分布序列转移至目标分布的一般性方法，并具体证明SK模型吉布斯测度的弱庞加莱不等式（WPI），从而为Glauber动力学的快速混合猜想提供关键结构性支撑。

Method: 发展了一种两步证明策略：首先对一个逼近随机定域化（SL）过程的足够正则的分布序列证明弱泛函不等式，然后利用SL过程本身的正则性和传导（conductance）论证，将该不等式转移至目标分布。该策略被应用于Sherrington-Kirkpatrick模型的吉布斯测度。

Result: 证明了当逆温度β < 1/2时，Sherrington-Kirkpatrick模型的吉布斯测度满足弱庞加莱不等式（WPI）。作为推论，带暖启动的Glauber动力学能够在β < 1/2时高效采样该吉布斯测度。

Conclusion: 本文的结果是朝着解决“在副本对称（replica-symmetric）区域内SK模型的Glauber动力学快速混合”这一公开猜想[arXiv:2504.20539, Open-Problem 15, 2025]的重要结构性步骤。

Abstract: We develop a new method for proving a weak functional inequality by first proving it for a sufficiently regular sequence of distributions approximating the stochastic localization (SL) process, and then transferring it to the desired distribution via regularity of the SL process and conductance arguments. We use this strategy to prove a weak Poincaré inequality (WPI) holds for the Gibbs measure of the Sherrington-Kirkpatrick model when $β< \frac{1}{2}$. A prior result of the authors [arXiv:2605.03718, 2026] proves the ASL process for the Sherrington-Kirkpatrick model satisfies the required regularity conditions.
  A consequence of the WPI is that a much simpler algorithm -- Glauber dynamics with a warm-start -- efficiently samples the Gibbs measure of the SK model at $β< \frac{1}{2}$. This is a significant structural step towards resolution of the conjecture that Glauber dynamics mixes fast in the replica-symmetric regime for the Sherrington-Kirkpatrick model [arXiv:2504.20539, Open-Problem 15, 2025].

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用Heisenberg群（Heisenberg group）的表示理论（representation theory）进行构造，该方法与欧氏情形不同，关键区别在于Heisenberg群中存在无限维不可约酉表示（infinite-dimensional unitary irreducible representations）。

Result: 在Heisenberg群 $\mathbb{H}$ 上构造了一族新的随机场，这些场是子拉普拉斯算子（sub-Laplacian）的广义随机本征函数（generalized random eigenfunctions），构成子黎曼空间版本的Berry随机波模型。

Abstract: We construct a new family of random fields on the Heisenberg group $\mathbb{H}$, the sub-Riemannian analog of $\mathbb{R}^{n}$. These fields are generalized random eigenfunctions of the sub-Laplacian on $\mathbb{H}$, and can be viewed as the sub-Riemannian counterpart to the Berry random wave model in $\mathbb{R}^{n}$. The construction of such waves relies on the representation theory of $\mathbb{H}$, and differs from the Euclidean case because of the presence of infinite-dimensional unitary irreducible representations. This work represents a first step towards studying random waves and their geometry in sub-Riemannian spaces.

### [130] [Zero-temperature stochastic Ising model on one-dimensional quasi-transitive graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08330)
*Emilio De Santis*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究一维拟传递图上的零温随机伊辛过程，证明图具有收缩性质（shrink property）是出现Type I行为（所有顶点无限翻转）的充要条件；对于无此性质的图，基于辅助空间自动机提出算法框架，可区分Type F（局部固定）和Type M（混合态，存在闪烁子）行为，并证明三类行为的分类是算法可判定的，同时构造了支持任意大闪烁子的图例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解零温Glauber动力学（Glauber dynamics）在无限拟传递图（quasi-transitive graph）上的行为分类，特别是图结构与动力学长期行为（无限翻转、局部固定或混合态）之间的内在联系。

Method: 基于交互作用范围有限的一维无限拟传递图上的零温随机伊辛过程（Ising process），首先建立Type I行为与收缩性质（shrink property）之间的等价性证明；对于不具备收缩性质的图，引入辅助空间自动机（auxiliary spatial automaton）框架，从而在有限时间内区分Type F与Type M行为。

Result: Type I行为（所有顶点自旋无限次翻转）发生的充要条件是图具有收缩性质；三类动力学行为（Type I、Type F、Type M）的分类是算法可判定的；存在一类图支持任意大尺寸的闪烁子（blinkers）。

Conclusion: 图结构的收缩性质完全决定了零温伊辛动力学是否呈现全顶点无限翻转；基于自动机的框架为有限时间分类提供了有效的判定方法；闪烁子的存在性表明混合型行为在拟传递图中具有丰富的结构可能性。

Abstract: We consider the zero-temperature stochastic Ising process describing $\pm 1$ spin-flip dynamics on an infinite one-dimensional quasi-transitive graph $G=(V,E)$ with finite interaction range $K$. We prove that the zero-temperature limit of the Glauber dynamics for this Ising model exhibits a Type $\mathcal{I}$ behavior (infinite fluctuations of all vertices) if and only if the graph possesses the so-called \emph{shrink property}. For graphs lacking this property, we introduce an algorithmic framework based on an auxiliary spatial automaton to distinguish, in finite time, between Type $\mathcal{F}$ behavior (almost sure local fixation) and Type $\mathcal{M}$ behavior (a mixed regime characterized by the presence of blinkers). We prove that the classification among these three regimes is algorithmically decidable. Furthermore, we provide a constructive example of a graph supporting blinkers of arbitrarily large size.

### [131] [Soft edge limit of the Laguerre beta-ensemble at the lower edge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08536)
*Yun Li,Benedek Valkó,Jiaming Xu*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明了当参数 $a_n$ 满足 $a_n\to \infty$ 且 $\tfrac{a_n}{n}\to 0$ 时，适当缩放的 Laguerre $\beta$-系综（Laguerre beta-ensemble）的下边缘收敛到 Airy$_β$ 过程（Airy$_β$ process），从而完整刻画了固定 $\beta>0$ 情形下该系综可能的边缘标度极限（edge scaling limits）。当 $a_n\gg (\log \log n)^3$ 时，通过逆缩放 Dumitriu-Edelman 三对角矩阵在算子层面的收敛到随机 Airy 算子（stochastic Airy operator）的逆来证明；当 $a_n\le (\log n)^{1/2}$ 时，则借助耦合（coupling）及 Dumaz-Li-Valko 关于 Laguerre $\beta$-系综硬-软边缘过渡的结果给出另一种论证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 完成对固定 $\beta>0$ 的 Laguerre $\beta$-系综边缘标度极限（edge scaling limits）全景图的刻画，填补此前未知的参数区间。

Method: 针对不同参数范围分别采用两种方法：当 $a_n\gg (\log \log n)^3$ 时，建立缩放后的 Dumitriu-Edelman 三对角矩阵（Dumitriu-Edelman tridiagonal matrix）的逆在算子层面的收敛到随机 Airy 算子（stochastic Airy operator）的逆；当 $a_n\le (\log n)^{1/2}$ 时，使用耦合（coupling）技术以及 Dumaz-Li-Valko 关于 Laguerre $\beta$-系综硬边缘与软边缘之间过渡的结果。

Result: 证明了当 $a_n\to \infty$ 且 $\tfrac{a_n}{n}\to 0$ 时，适当缩放的 $n$ 维 Laguerre $\beta$-系综的下边缘分布收敛到 Airy$_β$ 过程（Airy$_β$ process）。此外，该方法同样适用于已知的 Laguerre 和 Gaussian $\beta$-系综（Gaussian beta-ensembles）的软边缘标度极限（soft edge scaling limits），并得到类似的算子层面极限。

Conclusion: 该结果补全了固定 $\beta>0$ 的 Laguerre $\beta$-系综在不同 $a_n$ 参数行为下的边缘标度极限（edge scaling limits）分类，表明 Airy$_β$ 过程是 $a_n$ 介于常数增长与线性增长之间的中间区域的控制极限过程。

Abstract: We show that the lower edge of the appropriately scaled size $n$ Laguerre beta-ensemble with parameter $a=a_n$ converges to the $\operatorname{Airy}_β$ process as $n\to \infty$ when $a_n\to \infty$ and $\tfrac{a_n}{n}\to 0$. This completes the picture of the possible edge scaling limits of the Laguerre beta-ensemble with a fixed $β>0$. When $a_n\gg (\log \log n)^3$ our proof establishes operator level convergence of the inverse of the scaled Dumitriu-Edelman tridiagonal matrix to the inverse of the stochastic Airy operator. Our methods allow us to prove similar operator level limits for the known soft edge scaling limits of the Laguerre and Gaussian beta-ensembles. For $a_n\le (\log n)^{1/2}$ we give a different argument that relies on coupling and a result of Dumaz-Li-Valko for the transition between the hard and soft edge limits of the Laguerre beta-ensemble.

</details>


### [132] [Mixing of Glauber Dynamics on High Overlap Gibbs Measures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06813)
*Afonso S. Bandeira,Ahmed El Alaoui,Almut Rödder*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明，对于具有强外场的特定二次吉布斯测度（quadratic Gibbs measures），Glauber动力学（Glauber dynamics）能够快速混合。关键工具是一个重叠条件（overlap condition），通过控制相互作用矩阵小块的范数来统一控制所有钉扎（pinning）下的相关矩阵。利用随机局域化（stochastic localization）方法，进一步得到谱间隙（spectral gap）的下界，从而证明Glauber动力学的多项式时间混合。作为直接应用，针对相互作用矩阵为缩放GOE矩阵的Sherrington-Kirkpatrick模型，证明对于任意固定有限逆温度β，存在一个不依赖于系统大小的外场强度θ，使得Glauber动力学以高概率（关于相互作用矩阵的实现）在多项式时间内混合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有强外场的二次吉布斯测度下Glauber动力学的混合时间，特别是Sherrington-Kirkpatrick（SK）模型在有限温度及外场下的可混合性。此前对于SK模型在有限温度下Glauber动力学是否能在多项式时间内混合尚不清楚，本文旨在给出正面的理论保证。

Method: 提出一个重叠条件（overlap condition），通过控制相互作用矩阵中小子矩阵的范数来统一控制所有钉扎条件下的相关矩阵；结合随机局域化（stochastic localization）技术，推导出谱间隙（spectral gap）的下界，进而证明Glauber动力学的多项式时间混合。

Result: 对于满足重叠条件的二次吉布斯测度，Glauber动力学在多项式时间内混合。对于Sherrington-Kirkpatrick模型（相互作用矩阵为缩放GOE矩阵），存在不依赖于系统大小的外场强度θ，使得对于任意固定有限逆温度β，Glauber动力学以高概率在多项式时间内混合。

Conclusion: 证明了在强外场条件下，一类二次吉布斯测度的Glauber动力学可实现快速混合，并为SK模型在有限温度下的多项式时间混合提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We show fast mixing of Glauber dynamics for certain quadratic Gibbs measures with large external fields. The main ingredient is an overlap condition that allows us to control correlation matrices uniformly over all pinnings, by controlling norms of small submatrices of the interaction matrix. Using stochastic localization, we then obtain a lower bound on the spectral gap and, consequently, polynomial-time mixing of Glauber dynamics. As a direct application, we consider the Sherrington-Kirkpatrick model, whose interaction matrix is a scaled GOE matrix. For this model, we show that for any fixed finite inverse temperature $β$, there exists a strength of external field $θ$, not depending on the size of the system, for which Glauber dynamics mixes in polynomial time (with high probability on the draw of the interaction matrix).

</details>

### [133] [Instability of gray solitons in a Gross-Pitaevskii model with a moving impurity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08190)
*Paolo Antonelli,Martino Caliaro*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文通过一维Gross-Pitaevskii模型研究稀薄玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体中运动杂质的影响，证明了亚音速区域中与灰孤子分支相关的时间无关解的存在性，并利用Evans函数方法分析了谱稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解运动杂质对稀薄玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）中超流行为的影响，具体通过研究亚音速区域中时间无关解的存在性与稳定性。

Method: 采用具有非零边界条件的一维Gross-Pitaevskii（GP）模型，将杂质建模为以恒定速度运动的局域外势；在随动参考系中研究时间无关解，并运用Evans函数方法分析谱稳定性。

Result: 对亚音速区域中每个非零速度，证明存在一族从（位移）灰孤子分岔的时间无关解，其位置由有效势的极值点决定；对于小强度势，源自有效势极大值点的解族是谱不稳定的。

Conclusion: 所得不稳定结果可形式化地应用于排斥δ势情况，为理解凝聚体中超流行为的破坏机制提供理论依据。

Abstract: The effect of a moving impurity in a dilute Bose-Einstein condensate is investigated by means of the one-dimensional Gross-Pitaevskii model (GP) with non-zero boundary conditions at infinity. The impurity is modeled as a localized external potential, that travels at constant speed $v \in \mathbf{R}$. In a co-moving reference frame, we study the existence and stability of time-independent solutions. The latter are of physical relevance, being associated with the superfluid behavior of the condensate.
  For every non-zero velocity $v$ in the subsonic regime, we show the existence of a family of time-independent solutions which bifurcates from a (displaced) gray soliton $φ_{0,v}(x-s_0)$, with $s_0 \in \mathbf{R}$, of the GP equation. The position $s_0$ is determined as an extremal point of an effective potential explicitly defined. Moreover, we study the spectral stability of these states. For small values of the potential strength, we show that the families originating from the maxima of the effective potential are spectrally unstable. For this last result, we employ an Evans function approach. Finally, we formally apply the instability result to the case of a repulsive delta potential.

</details>

### [134] [Rotation Sensing via Josephson-frequency Splitting in a Toroidal Superfluid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08345)
*Giulio Nesti,Luca Pezzè*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文证明，一个被 n 个隧穿势垒（tunneling barriers）中断的环形超流体可实现一个紧凑型约瑟夫森陀螺仪（Josephson gyroscope），其对旋转的响应与 n 成正比。在小振幅条件下，解析推导了耦合数-相位振荡的简正模谱；旋转通过多普勒效应（Doppler shift）解除模式简并，产生与 Ω 和 n 均成正比的频率分裂。数值模拟确认了这一预测，并揭示了长寿命的双频拍频（two-frequency beatings），可作为直接的旋转信号，其估算不确定度标度为 ΔΩ ∼ n^{-3/2}，且对缺陷和动力学激发具有鲁棒性。这些结果将多结环形超流体定位为与现有实验平台兼容的可扩展、微米级旋转传感器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有旋转传感器在微米尺度下灵敏度受限；本文旨在利用多势垒环形超流体中约瑟夫森效应的集体行为，实现一种尺度可扩展（scalable）、对旋转响应增强的紧凑型陀螺仪。

Method: 在小振幅区域内解析推导耦合数-相位振荡的简正模谱；通过多普勒效应解释旋转对简并模式的解除机制；利用全数值模拟验证解析预测并观察双频拍频现象；基于拍频信号建立旋转估算不确定度的标度关系。

Result: 频率分裂随角速度 Ω 和势垒数 n 线性增长；非旋转系统呈现单色约瑟夫森振荡，旋转系统出现长寿命双频拍频；旋转估算不确定度标度为 ΔΩ ∼ n^{-3/2}。

Conclusion: 多结环形超流体可作为可扩展、微米级旋转传感器，与现有实验平台兼容，且对缺陷和动力学激发具有鲁棒性。

Abstract: We show that a toroidal superfluid interrupted by $n$ tunneling barriers realizes a compact Josephson gyroscope with an $n$-enhanced response to rotation. In the small-amplitude regime, we derive analytically the normal mode spectrum of the coupled population-phase oscillations. In the absence of rotation, pairs of modes are degenerate: a finite angular velocity $Ω$ lifts this degeneracy through a Doppler shift, producing a frequency splitting that grows linearly with both $Ω$ and $n$. Full numerical simulations confirm this prediction and reveal long-lived two-frequency beatings, in sharp contrast with the monochromatic Josephson oscillations of the nonrotating system. These beatings provide a direct rotation signal with estimation uncertainty scaling as $ΔΩ\sim n^{-3/2}$, while remaining robust against imperfections and dynamical excitations. These results identify multi-junction toroidal superfluids as scalable, micrometer-size rotation sensors compatible with current experimental platforms.

</details>

# physics.flu-dyn [[Back]](#toc)

### [135] [On the rectification of oscillatory flows by flexible leaflets in a confined geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08394)
*Omar Abukabsha,Simon Gsell,Martin Brandenbourger*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟研究低雷诺数（low-Reynolds number）通道中多个非对称叶片（asymmetric leaflets）的集体相互作用，开发了描述稳态与动态流固耦合的分析框架，揭示了叶片密度和弹粘性数（elastoviscous number）对净流体输运的关键影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物系统中的流固耦合（fluid-structure interactions）在柔性通道和受限几何结构中控制着流体输运，但时变流场与多个相互作用的柔性结构之间的动态耦合难以建模，当前对集体行为的预测主要局限于稳态表征。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，在低雷诺数通道中利用对称振荡板（symmetrically oscillating plates）而非压力驱动流来隔离背景不对称性，研究多个非对称叶片的集体相互作用；开发了稳态极限下的解析框架，并扩展至包含时间依赖的通道振荡，提供完整的动态描述。

Result: 高叶片密度（high leaflet densities）能最大化集体相互作用和净输运量；定义了弹性-粘性数（elastoviscous number，比较粘性水动力与叶片弹性回复力），并发现存在最大化净流量的最优值。

Conclusion: 所建立的框架为分析集体柔性结构在粘性环境中的动态相互作用奠定了基础，可用于未来生物流体输运和微流控设计（microfluidic design）中的流动控制研究。

Abstract: Inspired by biological systems, extensive research has explored how fluid-structure interactions in compliant channels and confined geometries control fluid transport. While local nonlinearities can be induced by individual components, arranging these elements into larger architectures gives rise to increasingly complex, collective responses. Predicting these collective behaviors, however, remains largely restricted to steady-state characterization, as the dynamic coupling between time-varying flows and multiple interacting structures is difficult to model. In this paper, we investigate numerically the collective interaction of multiple asymmetric leaflets within a channel at low-Reynolds number. By utilizing symmetrically oscillating plates rather than a pressure-driven flow to isolate the system from background asymmetries, we characterize how these interacting structures generate a net fluid transport. We develop an analytical framework to evaluate transport in the steady limit, which we subsequently extend to account for time-dependent channel oscillations, providing a complete dynamic description of the coupled fluid-structure system. Our results demonstrate that high leaflet densities maximize collective interactions and net transport. Furthermore, we define an elastoviscous number comparing viscous hydrodynamic forces to the restorative elastic forces of the leaflets, and uncover an optimal value that maximizes the net flow. This framework establishes a foundation for analyzing how collective slender structures interact dynamically within viscous environments, laying the groundwork for future studies on flow control in biological fluid transport and microfluidic design.

</details>

### [136] [The 20 GeV Galactic Halo Excess: Pixel-Level Confirmation and Consistency with Sub-TeV WIMP Annihilation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08552)
*Trinity Rosebud Stenhouse,Chamkaur Ghag,Frank F. Deppisch*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文独立复现了Fermi-LAT 15年数据中约20GeV的银晕状弥漫发射成分，并通过像素级似然分析确认其光谱形态，指出该信号在亚TeV暗物质湮灭、衰减及速度依赖的共振增强模型下的解释可能性，以及各类模型与矮椭球星系限值之间的张力程度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于Fermi-LAT 15年数据中报道的一个球对称、晕状、峰值约20GeV的银道弥散发射成分，本文旨在独立复现该结果，并通过更高分辨率的像素级分析验证其真实性，进而系统评估该信号是否来自暗物质（dark matter）湮灭或衰变，以及不同暗物质模型与现有天体物理限值之间的兼容性。

Method: 首先复现原文的“cell-aggregated”分析（单元聚合分析），然后扩展到原生0.125°像素级的似然分析（pixel-level likelihood），引入能量依赖的点扩散函数前向折叠（energy-dependent point-spread-function forward folding）并掩蔽亮源。使用NFW辐射强度缩放ρ^p（p∈1,2,2.5）拟合不同暗物质密度轮廓，并对比s波湮灭、p波湮灭、衰变以及共振增强（resonant Sommerfeld或Breit-Wigner）模型。

Result: 两种方法均复现了20GeV晕光谱；像素级归一化比单元聚合拟合高约20%。信号呈高纬度分布，与内银河过剩（inner-Galaxy excess）不同，中心集中，排除河外起源。s波湮灭的最佳拟合质量为m_χ≈0.55TeV（W^+W^-）和0.72TeV（b\bar{b}），⟨σv⟩≈1×10^{-24} cm^3 s^{-1}，与矮椭球星系（dwarf spheroidal galaxy）限值之间存在约4-5倍张力；考虑前景建模和J因子系统不确定性后，张力窗口R扩大至1.6-9.3。p波湮灭缺失遗迹丰度约束约7个数量级；衰变解释被各向同性伽马射线背景所排除。唯一可行的速度结构是低速度增强的湮灭（共振Sommerfeld或Breit-Wigner），提供从热遗迹（thermal relic）所需的约45倍增强。

Conclusion: 20GeV晕状信号在亚TeV暗物质s波湮灭解释下仍可存活于矮椭球星系限值内，但必须计入较大的系统不确定性。完全解决矮椭球星系张力需要精细调节的共振峰位于晕速度附近并在更冷系统中衰减，而共振增强的低速湮灭模型是目前唯一能与遗迹密度及当前晕速率一致的暗物质解释方案。

Abstract: A recent analysis of 15 years of Fermi-LAT data reported a spherically symmetric, halo-like component of the Galactic diffuse emission that peaks near 20GeV. We independently reproduce this cell-aggregated analysis, then extend it to a pixel-level likelihood on the native $0.125^\circ$ maps, adding energy-dependent point-spread-function forward folding and masking bright sources. Both methods replicate the 20GeV halo spectrum, with the pixel-level normalisation ${\sim}20\%$ above the cellwise fit across NFW emissivity scalings $ρ^p$, $p \in 1,2,2.5$. This 20GeV halo is a high-latitude feature, distinct from the inner-Galaxy excess, and consistent with sub-TeV dark matter (WIMP) annihilation. It is centrally concentrated, strongly disfavouring extragalactic emission. Fitting prompt $s$-wave annihilation spectra, best-fit masses are $m_χ\simeq 0.55$TeV ($W^+W^-$) and $0.72$TeV ($b\bar{b}$) with $\langleσv\rangle \simeq 1\times10^{-24}~\mathrm{cm^3\,s^{-1}}$, in $\sim\!4$-$5\times$ tension with dwarf spheroidal galaxy limits. However, accounting for foreground modelling and $J$-factor systematic uncertainties widens the tension window to $R\simeq1.6$-$9.3$, leaving the $s$-wave interpretation viable. To close the tension, we consider alternative particle dark matter models. $p$-wave annihilation misses relic abundance constraints by $\sim\!7$ orders of magnitude. A decay interpretation evades dwarf limits but is disfavoured by the isotropic gamma-ray background. The only viable velocity structure consistent with dwarf limits, present-day halo rates, and relic density is low-velocity-enhanced annihilation (resonant Sommerfeld or Breit-Wigner). This supplies the required $\approx\!45\times$ boost from a thermal relic. Fully resolving the dwarf tension requires a fine-tuned resonance peaking at the halo velocity and falling for colder systems.

</details>

Vetrano,A. Veutro,A. Viceré,S. Vidyant,A. D. Viets,A. Vijaykumar,A. Vilkha,N. Villanueva Espinosa,V. Villa-Ortega,E. T. Vincent,J. -Y. Vinet,S. Viret,S. Vitale,A. Vives,L. Vizmeg,H. Vocca,D. Voigt,E. Wong,K. Wong,T. Wouters,J. L. Wright,M. Wright,B. Wu,C. Wu,D. S. Wu,H. Wu,K. Wu,Q. Wu,Z. Wu,E. Wuchner,D. M. Wysocki,V. A. Xu,Y. Xu,N. Yadav,H. Yamamoto,K. Yamamoto,T. S. Yamamoto,T. Yamamoto,R. Yamazaki,T. Yan,H. Yang,K. Z. Yang,Y. Yang,Z. Yarbrough,J. Yebana,S. -W. Yeh,A. B. Yelikar,X. Yin,J. Yokoyama,T. Yokozawa,S. Yuan,H. Yuzurihara,M. Zanolin,M. Zeeshan,T. Zelenova,J. -P. Zendri,M. E. Zucker,T. L. Killestein,D. Steeghs,J. Casares,D. K. Galloway*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文利用LIGO第四轮观测期（O4）第一部分数据，通过重采样版互相关流水线搜索来自低质量X射线双星天蝎座X-1的连续引力波，在50–200 Hz频率范围设置了低于标准转矩平衡（torque balance）水平的上限，最灵敏的引力波振幅上限接近5×10⁻²⁶（倾角边缘化）和2×10⁻²⁶（最有利倾角），显著提升了搜索灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低质量X射线双星（low-mass X-ray binary）天蝎座X-1（Scorpius X-1）是连续引力波（continuous gravitational waves）搜索的重要目标天体，其自旋频率可通过吸积转矩达到平衡，此前搜索尚未在标准转矩平衡水平以下探测到信号，因此需要利用新数据（LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA第四轮观测期）和更灵敏的方法进行深入搜索。

Method: 采用重采样版（resampling version）的互相关流水线（cross-correlation pipeline）搜索信号频率f₀在25–200 Hz（对应中子星自旋频率12.5–100 Hz（三轴形变）或约15–20至约120–150 Hz（r-模（r-mode）））范围内的连续引力波，并结合层次化后续分析（hierarchical followup）和观测期后期额外数据来排除候选异常值（outliers）。

Result: 在50 Hz ≲ f₀ ≲ 200 Hz频率范围内设置了低于标准转矩平衡水平、且与中子星自旋倾角无关的上限；最灵敏的引力波振幅h₀上限在频率高端接近5×10⁻²⁶（倾角边缘化）和2×10⁻²⁶（最有利倾角）；边缘化上限对应的灵敏度深度（sensitivity depth）为70–75 Hz⁻¹/²；在f₀=75 Hz和200 Hz处对应的椭率（ellipticity）上限分别为3×10⁻⁵和3×10⁻⁶。

Conclusion: 尽管转矩和物态方程（equation of state）建模的不确定性限制了推断的强度，但结果仍然反对在该自旋频率范围内、由强子物态方程（hadronic equation of state）描述的中子星符合转矩平衡；搜索灵敏度较以往显著提升，逼近普通核物质所能支持的形变水平；所有候选异常值均被后续分析排除。

Abstract: We present the results of a search for continuous gravitational waves from the low-mass X-ray binary Scorpius X-1 using LIGO data from the first part of the fourth LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA observing run. By applying the resampling version of the cross-correlation pipeline to search for signal frequencies $f_0$ between $25$ and $200\un{Hz}$ (corresponding to neutron star spin frequencies of $12.5$ to $100\un{Hz}$ for GW due to triaxiality, or $\sim15-20$ to $\sim120-150\un{Hz}$ for GW due to $r$-modes), we set upper limits below the standard torque balance level, independent of neutron star spin inclination, for $50\un{Hz}\lesssim f_0\lesssim200\un{Hz}$. While uncertainties in the modelling of torque and equation of state limit the strength of our inference, our results nonetheless argue against torque balance in this spin range for a neutron star described by a hadronic equation of state. The most sensitive upper limits on the gravitational wave amplitude $h_0$, at the upper end of the frequency band searched, approach $5\times10^{-26}$ marginalized over inclination angle and $2\times10^{-26}$ assuming the most favorable inclination. The marginalized upper limits correspond to a sensitivity depth of $70-75\un{Hz}^{-1/2}$, improving sensitivity considerably over previous searches. Expressed as constraints on the triaxial deformation of the neutron star, the limits correspond to an ellipticity of $3\times10^{-5}$ if the GW frequency $f_0$ is $75\un{Hz}$ and $3\times10^{-6}$ if $f_0=200\un{Hz}$, approaching deformations which could be supported by ordinary nuclear matter. Outliers from the search were ruled out as potential signals by a combination of hierarchical followup and analysis of additional data from later in the observing run.

</details>


### [138] [Tilted thin accretion disks in the full Kerr spacetime and their implications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08728)
*K. S. Sruthy,Chandrachur Chakraborty,Sudip Bhattacharyya*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文在完整的Kerr时空中推导了稳态翘曲盘方程，用以研究围绕自旋坍缩天体的薄黏性吸积盘的倾斜动力学。该方程适用于从Kerr黑洞到Kerr裸奇点的全参数范围，数值解揭示出裸奇点情形下盘倾斜廓线存在内区峰状结构，该特征可为区分两类致密天体提供潜在的观测途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有吸积盘倾斜动力学研究多采用慢自旋或弱场近似，无法准确描述强引力区域（strong gravity regime）中相对论效应占主导时的盘倾斜行为。本文旨在建立无需上述近似的统一框架，以涵盖Kerr黑洞（Kerr black hole）和Kerr裸奇点（Kerr naked singularity）两种情形。

Method: 基于Pringle框架，在完整Kerr时空中推导稳态翘曲盘方程（steady-state warped-disk equation）；引入精确的开普勒频率（Keplerian frequency）和Lense-Thirring进动频率（Lense-Thirring precession frequency），避免慢自旋或弱场近似；对所得方程在真实边界条件下进行数值求解。

Result: 数值解显示，慢自旋近似在内盘区域存在显著偏差。在扩散区（diffusive regime），Kerr裸奇点的倾斜廓线（tilt profile）在比角动量（specific angular momentum）为零的半径附近出现内区峰状结构（inner hump），该特征在Kerr黑洞情形中不存在。

Conclusion: 内盘倾斜会影响对X射线光谱、时变和偏振特征的观测解释，这些观测对探测强引力区域和推断中心天体自旋至关重要。仅凭内区峰状结构本身不足以唯一区分Kerr黑洞与Kerr裸奇点，但结合吸积盘状态的约束可能为鉴别吸积坍缩天体的本质提供潜在的观测手段。

Abstract: We derive a steady-state warped-disk equation in the full Kerr spacetime to study the tilt dynamics of a thin, viscous accretion disk around a spinning collapsed object. The formulation, based on Pringle's framework, remains valid for all values of the Kerr parameter $a$, thereby encompassing both Kerr black holes (BHs; $0 < a \le 1$) and Kerr naked singularities ($a > 1$). By incorporating the exact Keplerian and Lense-Thirring precession frequencies, we analytically obtain the radial tilt profiles of the disk without invoking slow-spin or weak-field approximations. Numerical solutions of the resulting equations, obtained under realistic boundary conditions, reveal significant deviations from slow-spin approximations, particularly in the inner disk where the relativistic effects dominate. In the diffusive regime, we find that for Kerr naked singularities the tilt profile exhibits distinct inner hump(s) near the radius where the specific angular momentum vanishes -- a feature absent for Kerr BHs. Consideration of a tilt in the inner disk could significantly influence the interpretations from observed X-ray spectral, timing, and polarization features, which are crucial to probe the strong gravity regime and to infer the spin of the central object. While such a distinct hump feature alone does not uniquely distinguish Kerr BHs from Kerr naked singularities, their interpretation in conjunction with constraints on the disk regime may provide a potential observational handle on the nature of the accreting collapsed object.

</details>


### [139] [SACRA-K: A Performance-Portable Numerical Relativity Code with Kokkos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08743)
*Ming-Zhe Han,Kenta Kiuchi,Masaru Shibata*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文介绍SACRA-K，一个基于Kokkos库从Fortran迁移至C++的性能可移植数值相对论（numerical relativity）代码，在保持原物理算法与精度的同时实现了跨厂商硬件移植，并在双黑洞、黑洞-中子星及双中子星等构型中验证了波形一致性、对称性与收敛性，在加速器集群上获得约一个数量级的加速比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数值相对论代码（如SACRA-MPI）通常依赖特定硬件架构（如CPU集群），缺乏跨平台性能可移植性（performance portability），难以高效利用异构加速器（如GPU、APU）。

Method: 将Fortran编写的SACRA-MPI代码通过Kokkos库重构为C++版本SACRA-K。保留原始的Baumgarte-Shapiro-Shibata-Nakamura（BSSN）时空演化、Z4c约束传播、box-in-box Berger-Oliger自适应网格加密（adaptive mesh refinement）以及来自NANASI的广义相对论流体力学（general relativistic hydrodynamics）高分辨率激波捕捉方案。

Result: 在双黑洞、黑洞-中子星和双中子星构型中，SACRA-K与SACRA-MPI的波形差异远低于独立代码间的散射和同代码分辨率依赖变化，处于或低于当前引力波探测器可区分阈值；π对称性在位级（bitwise level）精确保持；双中子星并合的引力波相位呈现二阶收敛（second order convergence）。在最小测试构型中，SACRA-K在NVIDIA A100 GPU集群或AMD MI300A APU集群上的运行速度比Fortran SACRA-MPI在CPU集群上快约一个数量级，且可扩展至256个加速器设备。

Conclusion: SACRA-K成功实现了数值相对论代码的性能可移植性，在不牺牲物理精度和数值方法的前提下，显著提升了在异构加速器上的运行效率，并具有良好的跨厂商硬件兼容性和可扩展性。

Abstract: We present SACRA-K (SimulAtor for Compact objects in Relativistic Astrophysics with Kokkos), a performance-portable numerical relativity code ported from the Fortran code SACRA-MPI to C++ with the Kokkos library. SACRA-K retains the physics and numerical methods of SACRA-MPI, namely a Baumgarte-Shapiro-Shibata-Nakamura (BSSN) spacetime evolution with Z4c constraint propagation and a box-in-box Berger-Oliger adaptive mesh refinement, together with the high resolution shock capturing scheme for the general relativistic hydrodynamics from NANASI, while gaining cross vendor portability. We validate the port against SACRA-MPI across binary black hole, black hole neutron star, and binary neutron star configurations. Across these tests, the waveform discrepancies are well below both the scatter among independent numerical relativity codes and the resolution dependent variation within a given code, and remain at or below the distinguishability threshold of current gravitational-wave detectors; the $π$ symmetry is preserved exactly at the bitwise level; and the gravitational wave phase of the binary neutron star merger exhibits second order convergence. In the smallest test configuration, SACRA-K runs about an order of magnitude faster on the NVIDIA A100 GPU cluster or the AMD MI300A APU cluster than the Fortran SACRA-MPI on the CPU cluster, and we measure its scaling up to 256 accelerator devices.

</details>

### [140] [Kime-Representation Formulations of Three Open Problems in the Foundations of Classical Mechanics: Uncertainty, Invariant Entropy, and Directional Degrees of Freedom](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07851)
*Ivo D. Dinov*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在复时间（kime）表示下，为经典力学基础中的三个开放问题提供了数学自洽的表述，并通过kime锥与单自由度相空间作用-角图的辛同构，建立了统一的数学框架，推导了尖锐的熵不确定关系、非正则不确定关系及多自由度聚合界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典力学基础中仍存在三个开放问题：经典熵不确定原理（classical entropic uncertainty principle）向非正则变量和多自由度的推广；坐标不变测度与熵的表征，即连续物理量为何必须配对才能定义不变熵；以及经典相对论性定向自由度的构造（自旋1/2系统的经典类比）。

Method: 采用复时间（kime）表示，将kime相（phase）统计解释为潜在圆随机变量，其分布律Φ建模重复实验中由试验到试验（trial-to-trial）的变异性。通过kime锥与单自由度相空间作用-角图（action-angle chart）的精确辛同构（symplectic identification），使kime测度对应于Liouville测度（Liouville measure），相律成为Liouville密度的角条件分布。

Result: (i) 证明了kime圆柱上的尖锐熵不确定关系，极值族为von Mises×Gaussian分布，以及由von Mises律恰好饱和的尖锐圆Fisher信息不等式；(ii) 证明了精确的非正则不确定关系，修正项为Poisson括号的几何均值，阐明了期望括号的推测作用；(iii) 通过Williamson标准型和Fischer不等式证明了多自由度聚合界，并将单自由度精细化归结为辛Schur-Horn型精确开放问题；(iv) 证明了kime相的扩散产生单调熵增长，伴随等分（Haar均匀）相律。

Conclusion: 本文为经典力学中的三个基础开放问题提供了统一且严格的数学框架，揭示了kime表示在经典不确定性、不变性和相对论自由度问题中的深层辛结构联系。

Abstract: We give mathematically self-contained formulations, in the complex-time (kime) representation, of three open problems from the foundations of classical mechanics: (I) the extension of the classical entropic uncertainty principle to non-canonical variables and to multiple degrees of freedom; (II) the characterization of coordinate-invariant measures and entropies, i.e., the question of why continuous physical quantities must be paired for an invariant entropy to exist; and (III) the construction of a classical relativistic directional degree of freedom (a classical analogue of a spin-1/2 system). Throughout, the kime phase is interpreted {statistically as a latent circular random variable whose law Φmodels the intrinsic trial-to-trial variability of repeated, identically controlled experiments indexed by the kime magnitude. The mathematical bridge is an exact symplectic identification of the kime cone with the action-angle chart of a one-degree-of-freedom phase space, under which the kime measure is the Liouville measure and the phase law becomes the angular conditional of a Liouville density. Specifically, we (i) prove a sharp entropic uncertainty relation on the kime cylinder whose extremal family is von Mises x Gaussian, together with a sharp circular Fisher-information inequality saturated exactly by von Mises laws; (ii) prove an exact non-canonical uncertainty relation in which the correction term is the geometric mean of the Poisson bracket, clarifying the conjectured role of the expected bracket; (iii) prove aggregate multi-degree-of-freedom bounds via the Williamson normal form and Fischer's inequality, and isolate the per-degree-of-freedom refinement as a precise open problem of symplectic Schur-Horn type; (iv) prove that diffusion of the kime phase produces monotone entropy growth with the equipartitioned (Haar-uniform) phase law.

</details>


### [141] [An edge-bicolored graph approach to the Ising model on random regular graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07867)
*Michael Borinsky,Shiyue Ren,Maximilian Wiesmann*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 通过解析组合学（analytic combinatorics）方法，在随机正则图系综（random regular graph ensemble）上精确求解了铁磁Ising模型（ferromagnetic Ising model），将配分函数（partition function）表示为有标号边双色图（labeled edge-bicolored graphs）的生成函数，从渐近计数中得到了热力学极限下的自由能，并揭示出平均场普适类（mean-field universality class）的二阶相变（second-order phase transition）及临界指数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在随机正则图这类复杂网络上精确求解统计力学模型具有挑战性，作者旨在利用解析组合学工具提供铁磁Ising模型的精确解，以严格分析其相变行为。

Method: 将配分函数表达为有标号边双色图的生成函数（generating function），通过组合计数方法对图进行渐近枚举（asymptotic enumeration），进而得到热力学极限下的自由能。

Result: 所得自由能解析公式直接揭示出系统存在二阶相变，其临界指数属于平均场普适类（mean-field universality class）。

Conclusion: 该精确解证实了随机正则图上的Ising模型相变行为与平均场理论预期一致，展示了解析组合学在统计力学网络模型中的有效应用。

Abstract: We give an exact solution of the ferromagnetic Ising model on a random regular graph ensemble via analytic combinatorics. Expressing the partition function as the generating function of labeled edge-bicolored graphs, we obtain the free energy in the thermodynamic limit from the asymptotic enumeration of these graphs. A simple analysis of the resulting formula reveals a second-order phase transition with critical exponents of the mean-field universality class.

</details>


### [142] [The Periodic Table and the Group SO(4,4): II. Double SO(4,2)-tower](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08105)
*V. V. Varlamov*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于李代数 $\mathfrak{so}(4,4)$ 的权重图（weight diagram）框架，为元素周期表（periodic system of elements）提供了群论解释。四个量子数 $n, l, m, s$ 对应于该代数的嘉当生成元（Cartan generators）的本征值（权重）。代数 $\mathfrak{so}(4,4)$ 的根系（root system）形成一个四维正二十四胞体（24-cell）。与自旋相关的第四嘉当生成元的作用导致代数基分裂为两个结构相同的子基，每个子基同构于共形群（conformal group）的李代数 $\mathfrak{so}(4,2)$ 的姚基（Yao basis），四维正二十四胞体随之投影为两个三维立方八面体（cuboctahedra）。该分裂在物理上对应自旋二重性（spin doubling）。研究还表明，反物质（antimatter）可自然纳入该群论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为元素周期表提供严格的群论（group theory）数学基础，而非仅依赖经验规律，从而统一解释周期表中周期长度加倍（period doubling）等结构特征，并探索反物质元素在理论框架中的自然位置。

Method: 利用秩为4的李代数 $\mathfrak{so}(4,4)$ 的权重图结构，将四个量子数映射为嘉当子代数（Cartan subalgebra）的本征值。通过分析第四嘉当生成元的作用，展示嘉当-魏尔基（Cartan-Weyl basis）分裂为两个同构于 $\mathfrak{so}(4,2)$ 姚基的子基，并研究该分裂对应的正二十四胞体向立方八面体的投影。在此基础上，分析周期系统能级结构，并考察门捷列夫、西博格（Seaborg）以及10周期扩展的双SO(4,2)-塔结构。

Result: 元素周期表的周期长度序列 2, 8, 8, 18, 18, 32, 32, … 中的周期加倍现象可由第四嘉当生成元的自旋作用解释。反物质元素（反氢、反氦、反锂等）可自然包含于 $\mathfrak{so}(4,4)$ 的群论描述方案中。

Conclusion: 李代数 $\mathfrak{so}(4,4)$ 的权重图框架能够统一描述元素周期表的结构，包括自旋二重性、周期加倍以及反物质元素，为化学元素系统提供了深刻的对称性（symmetry）理论基础。

Abstract: A group-theoretic interpretation of the periodic system of elements is given within the framework of the weight diagram of the Lie algebra $\mathfrak{so}(4,4)$ of the fourth rank, where the four quantum numbers $n$, $l$, $m$, $s$ correspond to the eigenvalues (weights) of the Cartan generators of the maximal Abelian subalgebra (the maximal torus of the group SO(4,4)). It is shown that the root system of the algebra $\mathfrak{so}(4,4)$ forms a regular four-dimensional self-dual polyhedron (24-cell). The action of the fourth Cartan generator associated with spin leads to a splitting of the Cartan-Weyl basis of the algebra $\mathfrak{so}(4,4)$ into two structurally identical bases, each of which is isomorphic to the Yao basis of the subalgebra $\mathfrak{so}(4,2)$ (the Lie algebra of the conformal group). At this point, a four-dimensional 24-cell is projected onto two three-dimensional cuboctahedra, each of which defines the root system of the subalgebra $\mathfrak{so}(4,2)$. This splitting physically corresponds to spin doubling (two-valuedness). The structure of the energy levels of a periodic system is studied, the states of which (chemical elements) are represented as nodes of the weight diagram of the group algebra $\mathfrak{so}(4,4)$. The structure of the double SO(4,2)-towers of Mendeleev, Seaborg, and 10-periodic extension is examined in detail. The period doubling associated with the sequence of period lengths 2, 8, 8, 18, 18, 32, 32, $\ldots$ of the periodic system of elements is explained by the action of the fourth Cartan generator. It is shown that antimatter (Mendeleev anti-table consisting of antihydrogen, antihelium, antilitium, $\ldots$) is naturally included in the general group-theoretic scheme of description of the periodic table.

</details>


### [143] [Wigner symmetries single out symmetric Wasserstein distances in all finite dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08298)
*Gergely Bunth*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了由自伴可观测量族定义的二次型代价算子（quadratic cost operators）所诱导的量子Wasserstein距离（quantum Wasserstein distances），证明了纯态距离的几何不变性直接决定代价算子的不变性，并建立了Wasserstein等距幺半群（isometry monoid）与Wigner对称性（Wigner symmetries）之间的等价关系。进一步构造了代价算子与Hilbert–Schmidt框架型算子（frame-type operators）之间的互逆映射，揭示了各向同性（isotropy）、紧框架（tight frame）与规范正交基之间的内在联系，最终将几何、表示论、算子理论和框架理论中的对称性概念统一到同一单参数族中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子Wasserstein距离是非交换概率论与量子信息几何中的重要度量工具，但二次代价算子的结构特征及其对称性尚未被充分理解。本文旨在系统刻画代价算子由纯态距离唯一决定的条件，并建立等距对称性与Wigner对称性之间的等价关系，从而统一不同数学分支对量子Wasserstein距离对称性的描述。

Method: 首先证明任意半正定代价算子完全由其在一对纯态（pure states）上的Wasserstein距离的约束所决定，从而将纯态距离的几何不变性直接转化为代价算子的不变性。接着在至多d²-1个可观测量生成的代价算子类中，利用酉共轭不变性条件，证明Wasserstein等距幺半群恰好由Wigner对称性（幺正与反幺正共轭）构成。进一步构造代价算子与其无迹部分对应的Hilbert–Schmidt框架型算子之间的显式互逆映射，并在此对应下论证各向同性等价于紧框架性质。

Result: （1）任意半正定代价算子完全由其在纯态对上的Wasserstein距离决定；（2）在非零二次代价算子类中，Wasserstein等距幺半群等于Wigner对称性当且仅当该距离在纯态上对酉共轭不变，或等价地，代价算子在无迹子空间上为恒等算子的正标量倍；（3）各向同性非零代价至少需要d²-1个自伴生成元，且达到下界时其无迹部分（至多一个公共标度）构成Hilbert–Schmidt规范正交基。

Conclusion: 几何、表示论、算子理论与框架理论中的对称性概念最终指向同一个单参数的量子Wasserstein距离族，这为量子态空间上的度量结构提供了统一且深刻的数学刻画。

Abstract: We study the quantum Wasserstein distances introduced by De Palma and Trevisan associated with quadratic cost operators generated by families of self-adjoint observables. We first show that an arbitrary positive semidefinite cost operator is completely determined by the restriction of the corresponding Wasserstein distance to pairs of pure states. This allows geometric invariance of the pure-state distance to be translated directly into invariance of the cost operator.
  Within the class of nonzero quadratic costs generated by at most $d^2-1$ observables on a $d$-dimensional Hilbert space, we prove that the Wasserstein isometry monoid consists exactly of the Wigner symmetries, that is, unitary and antiunitary conjugations, if and only if the distance is invariant under unitary conjugations on pure states. Equivalently, the cost operator intertwines the adjoint representation of the unitary group and is a positive scalar multiple of the identity on the traceless subspace.
  We further construct explicit mutually inverse maps between quadratic cost operators generated by observables and Hilbert--Schmidt frame-type operators formed from their traceless parts. Under this correspondence, isotropy of the cost is equivalent to the tight frame property of the associated Hilbert--Schmidt operator. Consequently, a nonzero isotropic cost requires at least $d^2-1$ self-adjoint generators, and equality holds precisely when their traceless parts form, up to a common scale, a Hilbert--Schmidt orthonormal basis. Thus the geometric, representation-theoretic, operator-theoretic, and frame-theoretic notions of symmetry all determine the same one-parameter family of quantum Wasserstein distances.

</details>


### [144] [Approximate eigenfunctions for some aperiodic crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08320)
*Long Meng*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对非周期晶体（aperiodic crystals）中的一类算子族 H_ε，在特定假设下构造了局部化近似本征函数 Φ_ε，并证明了其近似本征值的误差阶为 O(ε^{m/2+1/4})。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将 H_ε 分解为依赖于快变量 x 和慢变量 εx 的周期算子，并引入含双参数 (k,X) 的族算子 h(k,X) 作用于周期边界空间 L^2_per。在此基础上，通过分析 h(k,X) 在特定能级 e_0 和参数点 (k_0,X_0) 附近的性质，构造局部化近似本征函数。

Abstract: In this paper, we consider Hamiltonians for aperiodic crystals of the form \begin{align*}
  H_\varepsilon:=T(-i\nabla_x+{\mathbf A}(x,\varepsilon x))+V(x,\varepsilon x),\qquad x\in {\mathbb R}^d \end{align*} where $T$ represents either a Dirac operators or a Schrödinger operator, and $x\mapsto {\mathbf A}(x,X)$ and $x\mapsto V(x,X)$ are $\mathbb L$-periodic with respect to some lattice $\mathbb L\subset{\mathbb R}^d$.
  Let \begin{align*}
  (k,X)\ni {\mathbb R}^d\times {\mathbb R}^d\mapsto h(k,X):=T(-i\nabla_x+k+{\mathbf A}(x,X))+V(x,X) \end{align*} be a family of operators acting on $L^2_{\rm per}(\mathbb{R}^d/\mathbb{L})$ with periodic boundary conditions. We show that, under some suitable assumptions on the family of operators $ (h(k,X))_{k,X}$ around an energy level $e_0\in {\mathbb R}$ and some points $(k_0,X_0)\in {\mathbb R}^d\times {\mathbb R}^d$, one can construct localized approximate eigenfunctions $Φ_\varepsilon\in L^2({\mathbb R}^d)$ of the operator $H_\varepsilon$ such that for $\varepsilon$ small enough and for some $m\in \{1,2\}$ and $μ\in {\mathbb R}$, \begin{align}\label{eq:abstract}
  \|(H_\varepsilon-e_0-\varepsilon^{\frac{m}{2}}μ)Φ_\varepsilon\|_{L^2({\mathbb R}^d)}={\mathcal O}(\varepsilon^{\frac{m}{2}+\frac{1}{4}}). \end{align} with \begin{align*}
  \|Φ_\varepsilon\|_{L^2({\mathbb R}^d)}=\frac{1}{|{\mathbb R}^d/\mathbb L|^{1/2}}+{\mathcal O}(\sqrt{\varepsilon}). \end{align*}

We also prove a constructive result for quasi-equilateral star graphs. ### [148] [Renormalization flows for 1D mixed states and a quantum Goursat lemma](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08568)
*Léo Le-Nestour,David Pérez-García,Alberto Ruiz-de-Alarcón*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究非手征二维拓扑有序模型边界态的重整化流，通过C*-Hopf代数上的完全正映射及其卷积迭代，证明收敛轨迹生成由有限*-量子超群描述的矩阵乘积密度算子不动点，并给出了有限群代数情形的显式分类及C*-Hopf代数量子Goursat引理的推广。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重整化（renormalization）是联系微观物理模型与大尺度有效描述的核心框架，但针对非手征二维拓扑有序模型（non-chiral two-dimensional topologically ordered models）边界态的重整化过程尚未得到系统研究。本文旨在从代数角度描述该过程中的流动、不动点及其分类。

Method: 以表示有限维C*-Hopf代数（C*-Hopf algebra）的重整化不动点为初始数据，施加均匀局域噪声量子信道（uniform on-site noise quantum channels）扰动，并进行反复粗粒化（coarse-grained）。利用C*-Hopf代数上的完全正映射（completely positive maps）或其包络C*-Hopf代数上的正线性泛函（positive linear functionals）描述流动，通过卷积幂（convolution powers）迭代，并借助有限群情形的Goursat引理（Goursat's lemma）及推广的量子版本进行分类。

Result: 收敛的迭代轨迹生成新的矩阵乘积密度算子（matrix product density operator，MPDO）不动点，由有限*-量子超群（finite *-quantum hypergroups）描述。对有限群代数及其对偶情形，基于Goursat引理给出了显式分类。此外，独立地证明了一个有限维C*-Hopf代数的量子Goursat引理（quantum generalization of Goursat's lemma），给出了所有收敛重整化轨迹的显式结构描述。

Conclusion: 该工作为非手征二维拓扑有序边界态的重整化流提供了一个自洽的代数框架，赋予有限*-量子超群以具体的物理意义，并通过量子Goursat引理统一了收敛轨迹的结构分类。

Abstract: Renormalization provides a framework for relating microscopic models of physical systems to effective descriptions at larger length scales. This procedure is studied for the boundary states of non-chiral two-dimensional topologically ordered models. The initial data consist of renormalization fixed points built from representations of finite-dimensional $C^*$-Hopf algebras, which are then perturbed by uniform on-site noise quantum channels and repeatedly coarse-grained. The resulting flows admit an intrinsic algebraic description in terms of completely positive maps on the $C^*$-Hopf algebra or, equivalently, positive linear functionals on its enveloping $C^*$-Hopf algebra. Their iteration is governed by convolution powers, and convergent trajectories yield new matrix product density operator fixed points, described by finite $*$-quantum hypergroups. This provides a concrete physical interpretation of such structures. For finite group algebras and their duals, we provide explicit classifications via Goursat's lemma for groups. Finally, we formulate and prove a quantum generalization of Goursat's lemma for finite-dimensional $C^*$-Hopf algebras, a result of independent interest, which gives an explicit structural description of all convergent renormalization trajectories.

### [149] [Parity Anomaly of Preformed Pairs Governs the Thermal Hall Effect above $T_c$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07807)
*Kumar Ghosh*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文提出，赝能隙相铜氧化物中观测到的大负热霍尔信号可由(2+1)维量子场论的奇偶性异常（parity anomaly）精确解释，无需自由参数。作者推导出热霍尔电导率解析公式，其中赝能隙Δpg(T)直接取自ARPES或STM独立测量，Coleman-Hill非重整化定理保证了结果的高阶稳定性，数值验证精度达0.2%。该理论预测热霍尔效应在T*而非Tc开启，并可为扭曲双层石墨烯提供定量靶标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多个铜氧化物家族在赝能隙相（pseudogap phase）中观测到大负热霍尔信号（negative thermal Hall signal），但现有微观理论（如手性声子、自旋子或环电流方案）均需引入未确定的耦合常数，且无法用独立测量的谱学能隙预测温度依赖关系，因此需要一种无自由参数的根本性解释。

Method: 从(2+1)维量子场论的奇偶性异常出发，将预成对赝能隙Δpg(T)等同于凝聚体质量（condensate mass）进入奇宇称费米子行列式，推导出无自由参数的热霍尔电导率公式κxy/T = (π²kB²/6h) C tanh[Δpg(T)/(2kBT)]，其中C为手性配对通道的陈数（Chern number）。利用Coleman-Hill非重整化定理保证结果不受高圈修正影响，并通过Wilson环通量穿透和p+ip圆柱上的DMRG数值模拟进行验证。

Result: 两个独立的数值测试（Wilson环通量穿透和密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）对p+ip圆柱的模拟）确认反常关联长度（anomaly correlation length）精度达0.2%，且无幂律有限尺寸修正。理论预测热霍尔效应在赝能隙温度T*而非超导转变温度Tc处开启。

Conclusion: 所提理论解决了铜氧化物赝能隙相热霍尔效应长期悬而未决的疑难，提供了可直接与ARPES数据对比的可证伪对数导数检验，并为魔角扭曲双层石墨烯（magic-angle twisted bilayer graphene）中的热霍尔效应给出了明确的定量预测靶标。

Abstract: A large negative thermal Hall signal has been reported across multiple cuprate families in the pseudogap phase where the superconducting order parameter has vanished, with a magnitude that no existing microscopic theory reproduces without free parameters. Competing proposals based on chiral phonons, spinons, or loop currents each require undetermined coupling constants and do not predict the temperature dependence in terms of an independently measured spectroscopic gap. We show that the parity anomaly of $(2+1)$-dimensional quantum field theory resolves this long-standing puzzle: the preformed-pair pseudogap $Δ_{\rm pg}(T)$ enters the parity-odd fermion determinant identically to a condensate mass, yielding the exact parameter-free formula $κ_{xy}/T = (π^2 k_B^2/6h)\,C\,\tanh[Δ_{\rm pg}(T)/(2k_BT)]$, where $C$ is the Chern number of the chiral pairing channel and $Δ_{\rm pg}(T)$ is directly measurable by ARPES or STM. Coleman-Hill non-renormalization protects the result against higher-loop corrections, and two independent numerical tests, Wilson-loop flux threading and DMRG on $p+ip$ cylinders, confirm the anomaly correlation length to $0.2\%$ accuracy with no power-law finite-size corrections. The theory predicts thermal Hall onset at $T^*$ rather than $T_c$, provides a falsifiable logarithmic-derivative test against ARPES data, and yields a concrete quantitative target for magic-angle twisted bilayer graphene.

</details>


### [150] [Bogolyubov excitons as a microscopic origin of two-level systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07812)
*Andrey Grankin,Victor Galitski*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出约瑟夫森结量子比特中二能级系统（two-level systems, TLS）的一个全新候选机制：由 Bogolyubov 准粒子（Bogolyubov quasiparticles）形成的亚gap束缚态（subgap bound states），即 Bogolyubov 激子（Bogolyubov excitons）。该机制源于常规超导体中高角动量通道的排斥相互作用，无需缺陷即可产生，且无法通过退火或屏蔽消除，表明TLS型激发可能是超导体的本征性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 约瑟夫森结量子比特（Josephson-junction qubits）中的退相干与介电损耗主要由二能级系统（TLS）引起，然而其微观起源长期以来尚未解决。本文旨在提出一种不依赖于缺陷的、纯电子的内在TLS候选机制。

Method: 采用常规超导体模型，包含s波通道的电子-电子吸引相互作用及高角动量通道的排斥相互作用。研究排斥相互作用导致的Bogolyubov准粒子之间的有效吸引，进而形成束缚态（Bogolyubov激子）。分析体态激子与表面激子的不同特性，并引入一个理想化模型：体超导体与二维排斥性金属近邻耦合（proximity-coupled），后者代表外部金属/半导体层或超导体的欠屏蔽区域。

Result: 体态Bogolyubov激子难以通过单粒子隧穿（single-particle tunneling）等常规探针检测；但表面激子能与外电场耦合，表现为二能级系统。这两个能级对应单个激子的不存在与存在，携带电偶极矩，并与谐振器发生避免交叉（avoided crossing），与实验观测到的TLS行为一致。

Conclusion: 该机制不依赖缺陷，且无法通过屏蔽或退火消除，因此推测TLS型激发可能是超导体的一种本征（intrinsic）属性。

Abstract: Two-level systems (TLS) are a leading source of decoherence and dielectric loss in Josephson-junction qubits, yet their microscopic origin remains unresolved. We propose an intrinsic, purely electronic TLS candidate: subgap bound states of Bogolyubov quasiparticles. We show that, in a model of a conventional superconductor with electron-electron attraction in the $s$-wave channel and repulsion in higher-angular-momentum channels, the latter produce an effective attraction between Bogolyubov quasiparticles, forming bound states. These Bogolyubov excitons resemble Bardasis--Schrieffer excitons but are driven by repulsive interactions. Bulk Bogolyubov excitons are not easily detectable through single-particle tunneling or other conventional probes, but we show that surface excitons couple to an external electric field and behave as two-level systems. We examine an idealized model of a bulk superconductor proximity-coupled to a two-dimensional repulsive metal, which could represent an external metallic or semiconductor layer or an underscreened region of the superconductor. The two levels correspond to the absence and presence of a single exciton, which carries an electric dipole moment and exhibits an avoided crossing with a resonator, as observed for TLS. Because this mechanism requires no defects and cannot be eliminated by screening or annealing, it suggests that TLS-like excitations may be intrinsic to superconductors.

</details>


### [151] [Observation of giant nonvolatile magneto-thermal switching in superconductor-ferromagnet hybrids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08005)
*Yui Sakamoto,Fuyuki Ando,Keigo Ito,Hossein Sepehri-Amin,Takamasa Hirai,Yuto Watanabe,Poonam Rani,Yoshikazu Mizuguchi,Ken-ichi Uchida*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究报告了在铁磁Fe-超导Pb混合体系中实现了巨大且非易失性的磁热开关效应（giant nonvolatile magneto-thermal switching），最大非易失性磁热开关比达到719%，是此前Pb-Sn复合材料记录值的两倍以上，也超过了纯Pb中的易失性开关比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁热开关（magneto-thermal switch）可通过外加磁场控制热传导，具有重要的热管理应用前景。但在第二类超导体（type-II superconductor）和相分离超导体中，非易失性（nonvolatile）磁热开关比远低于传统材料中的易失性（volatile）开关比，亟需提升非易失性开关性能以实现高效节能的热控制技术。

Method: 在铁磁Fe-超导Pb混合体系中，通过分散纯Fe颗粒，增加电子对热导率（thermal conductivity）的贡献并减少声子的贡献，从而增强超导-正常态相变（superconducting-to-normal conducting phase transition）时的磁热开关比。同时，利用超电流（supercurrent）捕获的磁通（trapped magnetic flux）与Fe的铁磁矩（ferromagnetic moment）协同作用，在零磁场下破坏Pb基质的超导性，实现显著的非易失性。

Result: 当Fe含量为8.7 vol%时，非易失性磁热开关比达到最大值719%，是此前Pb-Sn复合材料记录值的两倍以上，也超过了纯Pb中的易失性开关比。

Conclusion: 该工作为开发巨大的非易失性磁热开关材料拓宽了探索空间和策略方向。

Abstract: Magneto-thermal switch is a crucial thermal component which enables heat transfer control by the application of an external magnetic field. Recently, a nonvolatile behavior in magneto-thermal conductivity at zero magnetic field was observed in type-II and phase-separated superconductors owing to magnetic flux pinning nature, leading to an energy-efficient thermal control technology. However, the nonvolatile magneto-thermal switching ratio has been much lower than the volatile one in conventional materials. Here, we demonstrate a giant nonvolatile magneto-thermal switching in ferromagnetic Fe-superconducting Pb hybrids. The dispersion of pure Fe particles realizes increased electron and decreased phonon contributions in the thermal conductivity, which enhances the magneto-thermal switching ratio at the superconducting-to-normal conducting phase transition. Furthermore, in concert with trapped magnetic flux by supercurrent, ferromagnetic moment of Fe breaks the superconductivity of Pb matrix at zero magnetic field, enabling a significantly large nonvolatility even with a slight amount of Fe inclusions. Consequently, the nonvolatile magneto-thermal switching ratio reaches 719% in maximum at the Fe ratio of 8.7 vol%, which is more than twice the previous record value observed in Pb-Sn composites and the volatile one in pure Pb. This work broadens the exploration space and strategy for giant nonvolatile magneto-thermal switching materials.

</details>


### [152] [Signature in sound-mode of the exciton bilayer two-dimensional superfluid transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08353)
*Giovanni Midei,Filippo Pascucci,Milorad V. Milosevìc,Jacques Tempere,David Neilson,Andrea Perali*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出通过安德森-博戈留波夫声速（Anderson-Bogoliubov sound velocity）的动态迹象来探测电子-空穴双层系统中激子超流（exciton superfluidity）的存在，并结合有限温度屏蔽和重整化群方法计算了BCS-BEC渡越区（crossover）中声速在BKT相变处的跳变行为，进一步发现涡旋-反涡旋激发对声速和转变温度有显著重整化效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 零磁场下电子-空穴双层（electron-hole bilayers）中的激子超流由于凝聚体电中性，其相位相干性难以直接探测，因此寻找确凿的实验证据是一个长期挑战。

Method: 利用安德森-博戈留波夫声速作为激子超流的动态探针；在BCS-BEC渡越区中，结合有限温度屏蔽（finite-temperature screening）效应，采用重整化群方法（renormalization-group approach）确定BKT转变。

Result: 在BKT转变处，声速存在不连续跳变至零的现象，且跳变幅度具有强烈的密度依赖性；涡旋-反涡旋激发（vortex-antivortex excitations）在特定温度窗口内显著重整化声速和转变温度。

Conclusion: 安德森-博戈留波夫声速可为激子超流提供可实验检测的动态特征，且存在一个实验可访问的温度窗口，其中涡旋激发效应不可忽略。

Abstract: Obtaining definitive evidence of exciton superfluidity in electron-hole bilayers in zero magnetic field remains a major longstanding challenge since the condensate is electrically neutral, making its phase coherence difficult to detect directly. We show that the Anderson-Bogoliubov sound velocity provides a dynamical signature of exciton superfluidity. Across the BCS-BEC crossover, the velocity is known to discontinuously drop to zero at the Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless (BKT) transition. The magnitude of the drop has a strong density dependence. We compute this behavior, with the inclusion of finite-temperature screening, and determine the BKT transition using a renormalization-group approach. We further identify a temperature window which is experimentally accessible, where vortex-antivortex excitations strongly renormalize both the sound velocity and the transition temperature.

Result: 识别出五种最低焓多晶型物（polymorphs），分别结晶于 C2、P-1 和 P21/c 空间群（space groups）。所有多晶型物均呈反铁磁基态（antiferromagnetic ground state），其中 AgBeF4_4 和 AgBeF4_5 表现出前所未有的强超交换相互作用（superexchange interactions），J 值分别约为 -460 meV 和 -359 meV。这些高 J 值源于 [Ag2F7] 单元（AgBeF4_4）或无限 [AgF2/2+2/1]²⁻ 链（AgBeF4_5）的存在。

Conclusion: 尽管这些相相对于二元二氟化物（binary difluorides）呈亚稳态（metastable），但热力学分析表明，通过采用氟自由基（fluorine radicals）的合成路径，反应焓（reaction enthalpies）可达 -370 kJ/mol，因此有望实现靶向合成。

Abstract: The search for novel silver(II) fluorides is driven by their potential as electronic and magnetic analogues to high temperature cuprate(II) superconductor precursors. Here, we explore the previously uncharted Be Ag(II) F chemical space using global structure prediction algorithms combined with first principles calculations. Focusing on the AgBeF4 stoichiometry, we identify the five lowest enthalpy polymorphs crystallizing in the C2, P minus 1, and P 21/c space groups. All polymorphs show an antiferromagnetic ground state, with AgBeF4_4 and AgBeF4_5 exhibiting unprecedented strong superexchange interactions of J equal circa to minus 460meV and J equal circa to minus 359meV respectively. Those high J values are due to the presence of either [Ag2F7] for AgBeF4_4, or related infinite [AgF2/2+2/1]2 minus chains for AgBeF4_5. Although the phases are found to be metastable with respect to binary difluorides, the thermodynamic analysis suggests that they could be targeted via synthetic routes employing fluorine radicals, with reaction enthalpies reaching minus 370 kJ/mol.

### [154] [Influence of electronic correlations on disorder-induced loop currents in high-Tc superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08451)
*Marius Paul,Götz Seibold*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过无限制Gutzwiller近似研究铜氧化物超导体中由杂质诱导的环路电流（loop currents），发现关联效应会抑制环路电流，但Gutzwiller方法在维持此类态方面优于Hartree-Fock近似，并估算了局部磁矩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导系统中时间反演对称性破缺（time-reversal symmetry breaking, TRSB）可表现为由电荷及序参量分布不均匀性诱导的电流。针对铜氧化物（cuprates），此类态在相图过掺杂区已有理论研究，但局域关联效应对环路电流的影响尚未充分探索。

Method: 采用无限制Gutzwiller近似（unrestricted Gutzwiller approximation）引入局域关联，扩展了此前基于Hartree-Fock近似的研究；同时，考虑次近邻跳跃（next-nearest neighbor hopping）对TRSB相向半填充（half-filling）方向扩展的影响。

Result: 关联效应总体上导致环路电流被抑制；然而，与Hartree-Fock近似相比，Gutzwiller方法能够在更大的局域在位排斥（local on-site repulsion）参数下维持此类TRSB态。此外，次近邻跳跃可将TRSB相扩展至半填充区域。

Conclusion: 本研究为铜氧化物超导体中由杂质诱导的环路电流所产生的局部磁矩（local magnetic moment）提供了定量估计。

Abstract: Time-reversal symmetry breaking in superconducting systems can manifest itself in the form of currents which are induced by inhomogeneities in the charge and order parameter distribution. With regard to cuprates such states have been theoretically studied in the overdoped region of the phase diagram where the inhomogeneities are related to out-of plane dopants. In this paper we will extend previous work by including local correlations within the unrestricted Gutzwiller approximation in order to study its impact on the induced loop currents. In addition, we investigate the effect of next-nearest neighbor hopping which extends the TRSB phase towards half-filling. We find that in general correlations lead to a suppression of loop currents, however, the Gutzwiller approach can sustain such states to larger values of the local on-site repulsion as compared to the Hartree-Fock approximation. Our investigations allow for an estimation of the local magnetic moment emerging from impurity-induced loop currents for cuprate superconductors.

</details>


### [155] [Layer-resolved Electronic Structure and Correlation of Low-$n$ Square-planar Nickelates: A DFT+DMFT Prediction of Superconducting Candidates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08474)
*Jian-Hong She,Rong-Qiang He,Zhong-Yi Lu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）结合动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory, DMFT），对电子补偿后的 n=2 和 n=3 La 基镍酸盐进行电子结构计算，并与超导的高层数 n=6 体系进行对比。

Abstract: Multi-layer square-planar nickelates provide a rare platform in which the nominal Ni valence, dimensionality, and layer-resolved electronic structure can be tuned within the same structural family. Recent experiments have found superconductivity in $n=4$--8 $R_{n+1}Ni_nO_{2n+2}$ compounds, with the highest $T_c$ near $n=6$, whereas the more heavily hole-doped $n=3$ member remains nonsuperconducting. Here we propose spacer-layer Cl doping as a route to convert low-$n$ nickelates into superconducting candidates. Compared with changing the layer number $n$, Cl substitution on the spacer-layer oxygen sites offers a chemically natural way to continuously tune the Ni valence while leaving the NiO$_2$ planes largely intact; the lower-$n$ compounds may also be more accessible for synthesis. Using density functional theory combined with dynamical mean-field theory, we show that electron-compensated $n=2$ and $n=3$ La-based nickelates, targeted to the nominal Ni valence of superconducting $n=6$, develop Ni-$d$ correlations comparable to those of superconducting higher-$n$ compounds while preserving the characteristic low-energy Ni-$d$ electronic structure. These results suggest spacer-layer Cl doping as a promising strategy for designing low-$n$ square-planar nickelate superconductors.

### [156] [Heterostructuring as Gateway to Electron Doping of Nickelate Superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08553)

Abstract: Despite enormous expenditures in the research field, the electron-doped side of nickelate superconductors remains uncharted territory. Substituting the trivalent rare-earth cations by a tetravalent one hitherto failed. Here, we demonstrate by first-principles calculations a disorder-free route to electron dope Ruddlesden-Popper nickelates. When intercalating wide-band-gap insulating layers such as La$X$O$_3$ ($X$=Al, Ga, Sc) into La$_2$NiO$_4$, the extra (LaO)$^+$ layers act as electron donors, releasing carriers into the Ni-3$d$ orbitals. This electron doping puts La$_2$NiO$_4$:La$_2$AlO$_4$ naturally in the optimal region for $d_{x^2-y^2}$-wave superconductivity with T$_c$ exceeding 50 K. ### [157] [Vortex Dynamics in Magic-Angle Twisted Graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08585)
*Marta Perego,Peter Koopmann,Clara Galante Agero,Alexandra Mestre Torà,Takashi Taniguchi,Kenji Watanabe,Vadim Geshkenbein,Gianni Blatter,Thomas Ihn,Klaus Ensslin*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究报告了利用由扭曲双层石墨烯（twisted-layer graphene）构造的门控约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction, JJ）器件，用于探测二维体系中的涡旋动力学。通过测量磁场依赖的临界电流 Fraunhofer 干涉图案的位移及时间序列中的电报噪声，区分了准静态涡旋与快速涡旋涨落的多涡旋过程。实验发现，涡旋蠕动（creep-type motion）在约 100 mK 以上呈热激活行为，而在约 80 mK 以下速率趋于饱和，暗示存在向宏观量子隧穿（macroscopic quantum tunneling）的剧烈转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维体系中涡旋动力学的研究对于理解超导体的量子相变和耗散机制至关重要，但实验上实时分辨单个涡旋的快速涨落及其不同时间尺度过程存在技术难点。本文旨在利用门控扭曲石墨烯约瑟夫森结作为高灵敏度传感器，实现对近邻超导引线中涡旋的个体探测及动力学过程的时间尺度分离与定量分析。

Method: 采用门控定义的扭曲双层石墨烯约瑟夫森结器件，通过测量随磁场变化的临界电流 $I_c(B)$ 的 Fraunhofer 干涉图案（Fraunhofer interference pattern）中的位移来感应单个涡旋。同时，记录结电压 $V(t)$ 的时间轨迹，将快速涡旋涨落表现为的电报噪声（telegraph-type noise）作为多涡旋过程的信号，利用不同过程的时间尺度差异进行解耦分析。

Result: 在 $T = 7$ mK 至 120 mK 温度范围内追踪涡旋动力学速率：当温度高于约 100 mK 时，涡旋蠕动表现为热激活行为（thermally activated creep）；当温度低于约 80 mK 后，涡旋运动速率趋于饱和，暗示系统进入宏观量子隧穿（macroscopic quantum tunneling of vortices）主导的区域。

Conclusion: 扭曲石墨烯约瑟夫森结可作为二维涡旋动力学的有效探测工具，能够区分不同类型的多涡旋过程。实验结果表明，涡旋运动随温度降低从热激活经典蠕动向宏观量子隧穿发生急剧转变，为研究超导系统中的量子耗散与相变提供了关键实验依据。

Abstract: We use a gate-defined Josephson junction (JJ) device made from twisted-layer graphene for studying vortex dynamics in two dimensions. The JJ sensor signals the presence of individual vortices in the superconducting leads nearby the junction through shifts in the Fraunhofer interference pattern of the magnetic-field-dependent critical current $I_c(B)$ across the junction. Rapid vortex fluctuations manifest as telegraph-type noise in time traces of the junction voltage $V(t)$. Measurements of $I_c(B)$ and $V(t)$ are interpreted in terms of multi-vortex processes where fast vortex fluctuations in the leads are modulated by quasi-stationary vortices trapped in the leads. The different timescales associated with these processes allow for their disentangling and quantitative analysis. Tracking the temperature dependence of the vortex-dynamical rates between $T = 7$ mK and $T = 120$ mK, we find that the creep type vortex motion is thermally activated above $T \approx 100$ mK, while the saturation of rates below $T \approx 80$ mK is suggestive of a sharp transition to macroscopic quantum tunneling of vortices.

</details>

### [158] [Comment on 'Quantum Monge-Kantorovich Problem and Transport Distance between Density Matrices'](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07764)
*Tomasz Miller*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过构造显式的态三元组反例，证明 Friedland 等人提出的量子 p-Wasserstein 半距离（quantum p-Wasserstein semidistance）在特定量子成本矩阵（quantum cost matrix）及其邻域内不满足三角不等式，从而否定了其作为真正距离（true distance）的猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验 Friedland 等人 [PRL 129, 110402 (2022)] 关于量子 p-Wasserstein 距离（quantum p-Wasserstein distance）的猜想，即该量在某个特定量子成本矩阵（quantum cost matrix）及其小邻域内是真正的距离（满足三角不等式）。

Method: 构造一个显式的三元态族（explicit family of triples of states），并直接验证该三元组违反三角不等式（triangle inequality），从而提供反例。

Result: 成功构造出反例，证明对于所考虑的特定量子成本矩阵及其邻域内的成本矩阵，该量子 p-Wasserstein 量不满足三角不等式。

Conclusion: 否定了 Friedland 等人的猜想，表明该量子 p-Wasserstein 量在所述条件下仍仅为半距离（semidistance），而非真正的距离。

Abstract: Friedland et al. [PRL 129, 110402 (2022)] proposed and studied a quantum analogue of the $p$-Wasserstein distance based on quantum cost matrices and quantum couplings. They conjectured that, despite being only a semidistance in general, this quantity is a true distance for a particular quantum cost matrix and for cost matrices in a small neighborhood of it. We disprove these conjectures by exhibiting an explicit family of triples of states for which the triangle inequality fails.

Abstract: We present the analytical, exact, explicit, and assumption free formulas for the evolution operators corresponding to four instances of time-dependent Hamiltonians relevant to quantum spin batteries including two stochastic cases. We demonstrate how to recover and go beyond existing expansions and approximations directly from the exact solutions giving, for example, an explicit exact formula for Floquet Hamiltonians at all orders. The exact solutions are obtained through a completely novel combination of three mathematical techniques, the $\star$-algebra, path-sums and Omega calculus, which we briefly overview. These are widely applicable to other non-autonomous differential systems.
