### [160] [Temperature Beyond Equilibrium in Isolated Quantum Many-Body Systems and Their Subsystems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08655)
*Maurizio Fagotti*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文针对孤立的量子多体系统远离平衡态时温度概念模糊的问题，提出温度应基于状态的能量相干结构（energy-coherence structure）来定义；逆温度（inverse temperature）不再等于熵对能量的导数，最大熵原理（maximum entropy principle）被最小区分信息原理（principle of minimum discrimination information）取代；子系统温度不能仅由约化状态（reduced state）推断，而需由局域热力学结构（local thermodynamic structure）确定，边界歧义在热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）下消除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 温度是热力学（thermodynamics）的核心概念之一，但在远离平衡态时其含义仍不明确，这一问题在孤立量子多体系统（isolated quantum many-body systems）中尤为突出：此类系统经历幺正演化（unitary evolution），不必接近平衡态，且可保留能量相干性（energy coherence），一种经典热力学中不存在的特征。

Method: 论文提出温度应基于能量相干结构来定位该状态所属的正则状态族（regular states family）；由此导出的逆温度一般不等于热力学熵（thermodynamic entropy）对能量的导数；最大熵原理被替换为最小区分信息原理。对于子系统，温度不能仅由约化状态推断，而需通过诱导的局域热力学结构来确定，边界歧义在热力学极限下消除。

Result: 非定态（non-stationary quantum state）包含两种能量涨落（energy fluctuations）：一种与能量布居（energy populations）相关，具有通常的热力学解释；另一种源于能量本征态之间的相干性，驱动时间演化。据此定义的逆温度一般不等于熵对能量的导数，且最大熵原理不再适用。

Conclusion: 论文为远离平衡态的量子系统提供了温度的自然定义，并揭示了传统热力学概念（如熵与温度关系、最大熵原理）在非平衡态下的局限性，同时建立了子系统温度的局域热力学判定框架。

Abstract: Temperature is one of the central concepts of thermodynamics, yet its meaning away from equilibrium remains elusive. This problem is particularly acute in isolated quantum many-body systems: their states evolve unitarily, need not be close to equilibrium, and can retain energy coherence, a feature with no classical thermodynamic analogue. A non-stationary quantum state contains two kinds of energy fluctuations. One is associated with energy populations and has the usual thermodynamic interpretation; the other arises from coherence between energy sectors and drives time dependence. We propose that temperature, also out of equilibrium, locates the state within the family of regular states compatible with its energy-coherence structure. This leads to a natural definition of temperature for regular nonequilibrium states. The resulting inverse temperature is not generally the derivative of thermodynamic entropy with respect to energy. Indeed the principle of maximum entropy does not extend in its usual form; it is replaced by a principle of minimum discrimination information. We also develop the corresponding theory for subsystems, where temperature cannot in general be inferred from the reduced state alone. Instead, it is determined by the induced local thermodynamic structure, with boundary ambiguities removed in the thermodynamic limit.

</details>


### [161] [The Geometry of Quantum Complexity in Open Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08411)
*Ezra Acalapati,Kausik Ghosh,Giuseppe Policastro*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文将Nielsen的量子复杂性几何方法从封闭系统扩展到开放量子系统，建立了基于Lindbladian演化的混合态空间最优控制框架，揭示开放系统中复杂性几何本质上是子-芬斯勒（sub-Finslerian）而非黎曼（Riemannian）的，并通过退极化通道、振幅阻尼通道及阻尼谐振子等实例验证了耗散导致的不可逆性与曲率变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子复杂性（quantum complexity）的几何方法主要适用于封闭量子系统的幺正演化（unitary evolution），而实际量子系统不可避免地与环境耦合，受耗散（dissipation）影响。因此需要将复杂性几何框架推广到开放量子系统，以刻画Lindbladian演化下混合态空间的复杂性。

Method: 在混合态空间上构建最优控制问题，为幺正生成元（unitary generators）和非幺正生成元（non-unitary generators）分配成本；通过分析允许的切方向（admissible tangent directions）和代价泛函中的惩罚因子（penalty factors），推导开放系统的几何结构，并使用旗曲率（flag curvature）（芬斯勒几何中截面曲率的类比）刻画几何性质的变化。

Result: 开放量子系统的自然几何是子-芬斯勒（sub-Finslerian）的，而非封闭系统下的黎曼几何；耗散使得测地线（geodesics）不可逆（non-reversible），且物理允许的控制限制了切空间的允许方向。在退极化通道（depolarizing channel）、振幅阻尼通道（amplitude-damping channel）和阻尼谐振子（damped harmonic oscillator）等实例中，惩罚因子的变化会导致旗曲率改变，从而影响几何性质。

Conclusion: 该工作为耗散量子系统中抽象复杂性概念的量化提供了几何框架，并有望与实验可实现的装置建立联系。

Abstract: We extend Nielsen's geometric approach for quantum complexity from closed to open quantum systems, whose dynamics is governed by Lindbladian evolution. In this framework, complexity is defined through an optimal-control problem on the space of mixed states, with a cost assigned to both unitary and non-unitary generators. We show that the resulting geometric structure differs fundamentally from the Riemannian geometry that emerges in the case of unitary evolution. In the open-system setting, the natural geometry is typically sub-Finslerian. Dissipation makes the geodesics non-reversible, while the admissible tangent directions are restricted by the physically allowed controls. We analyze several physically motivated examples, including a single qubit subject to depolarizing and amplitude-damping channels, as well as the damped harmonic oscillator. We show that, similarly to the unitary case, varying the penalty factors in the cost functional modifies the geometric properties through changes in the flag curvature, the Finslerian analog of sectional curvature. Our results provide a geometric framework for quantifying the abstract notion of complexity in dissipative quantum systems, with potential connections to experimentally realizable setups.

</details>

*Fumio Hiai,Milán Mosonyi,Marco Tomamichel*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文对基于量子曲棍球散度（quantum hockey stick divergences）定义的量子f-散度（quantum f-divergences）进行了系统且统一的处理与扩展，涵盖了非归一化态、von Neumann代数框架下的推广，以及多个核心结果的延伸，包括Neyman-Pearson误差概率表示、量子信道可逆性检测的Jenčová结果推广，以及正则化曲棍球Rényi散度与Petz型及夹心型Rényi散度的等价性证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子f-散度是量子信息论中的重要工具，但现有理论散布于不同工作中，缺乏统一处理；此外，该理论需要在非归一化态、更一般的积分表示以及von Neumann代数框架下进行系统推广，以增强其适用性和完备性。

Method: 本文采用系统化的统一处理方法，将量子曲棍球散度的定义扩展至非归一化态（non-normalized states），引入附加实参数以推广积分表示形式，并将整个理论框架推广到一般的von Neumann代数（von Neumann algebras）上，在此基础上重新证明和推广已有的关键结果。

Result: 主要结果包括：(1) 在一般von Neumann代数框架下，给出了曲棍球f-散度基于Neyman-Pearson误差概率的表示；(2) 将Jenčová关于量子信道可逆性检测的结果推广到曲棍球散度情形；(3) 证明了正则化曲棍球Rényi α-散度在α∈(0,1)时与Petz型Rényi散度（Petz-type Rényi divergences）重合，在α>1时与夹心型Rényi散度（sandwiched Rényi divergences）重合；(4) 部分刻画了不同量子f-散度在量子态对上给出相同值的条件。

Conclusion: 本文为量子f-散度理论提供了更统一和更一般化的数学基础，拓展了其适用场景（非归一化态、von Neumann代数），并建立了多个重要散度概念之间的等价关系，为量子信息理论中的统计推断与信道分析提供了更坚实的工具。

Abstract: In this paper we give a systematic and unified treatment and extensions of various results on a new notion of quantum $f$-divergences defined from quantum hockey stick divergences, the theory of which has been developed recently in \cite{BHT_fdiv,HircheTomamichel_integral,LiuHircheCheng2025}. In particular, we consider non-normalized states and hockey stick $f$-divergences defined from more general notions of quantum hockey stick divergences, as well as a somewhat more general form of the integral representation defined in terms of an additional real parameter. We also consider the extension of the theory to general von Neumann algebras, and extend various results from \cite{HircheTomamichel_integral,LiuHircheCheng2025} to this setting. Our main results here are the representation of the hockey stick $f$-divergences in terms of Neyman-Pearson error probabilities, which was given in the finite-dimensional case in \cite{LiuHircheCheng2025}, an extension of Jen\v cová's result \cite{Jencova2023} on the detection of reversibility of a quantum channel on a pair of states in terms of the hockey stick divergences, and an extension of a result in \cite{HircheTomamichel_integral} showing that the regularized hockey stick Rényi $α$-divergences coincide with the Petz-type Rényi divergences for $α\in(0,1)$ and with the sandwiched Rényi divergences for $α>1$. Moreover, we give some partial results on the characterization of when different notions of quantum $f$-divergences give the same value on a pair of quantum states.

### [163] [Extracting conformal data from Loschmidt echoes after critical quenches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08649)
*Aleix Bou-Comas,Stefano Carignano,Sergio Cerezo-Roquebrún,Esperanza Lopez,Luca Tagliacozzo*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于共形场论（conformal field theory），提出了一套从实时动力学中提取共形数据的通用方法，无需制备临界低能态。通过分析Loschmidt振幅及其解析延拓、局域时空微扰和广义时间熵，系统展示了如何从有限链Loschmidt回波的系统尺寸依赖和有限尺寸标度协议中恢复边界算符谱、中心荷（central charge）和临界指数（critical exponents）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 共形场论对从乘积态淬火到临界哈密顿量后的Loschmidt振幅提供了普适性预言，但如何从实时动力学中直接提取共形数据（如中心荷和边界算符谱）尚未建立系统性框架。本文旨在填补这一空白，发展一种无需制备临界低能态即可获取共形信息的通用方法。

Method: 首先，对Loschmidt振幅进行解析延拓（analytic continuation），使其由条形区域上的边界共形场论（boundary CFT）配分函数描述，其横向转移矩阵（transverse transfer matrix）编码边界算符谱与中心荷。其次，通过引入局域时空微扰，将振幅的响应与平衡关联函数（equilibrium correlation functions）相联系，从而提取临界指数。同时，定义广义时间熵（generalized temporal entropies），展示其随时间标度行为与平衡空间纠缠熵的类似标度律。最后，提出基于有限链Loschmidt回波（finite-chain Loschmidt echoes）系统尺寸依赖的有限尺寸标度协议，通过阻尼振荡的频率提取边界标度维数（boundary scaling dimensions）的差值。

Result: 理论分析表明，Loschmidt振幅的解析延拓与边界CFT配分函数等价，其横向转移矩阵可直接给出中心荷和边界算符谱。局域时空微扰的响应由平衡关联函数控制，从而提供临界指数的提取途径。广义时间熵的时间标度行为与空间纠缠熵的平衡标度律类似。有限链Loschmidt回波的阻尼振荡频率与边界标度维数差值相对应，通过有限尺寸标度协议可从尺寸依赖性中重建低能边界谱。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一套从非平衡实时动力学中提取共形数据的系统方案，涵盖中心荷、边界算符谱和临界指数等关键共形信息，且无需制备临界低能态。基于有限尺寸标度协议的提出，该框架可直接应用于当前量子平台（如量子模拟器和量子计算机）上的模拟或实验。

Abstract: Conformal field theory provides universal predictions for Loschmidt amplitudes following quenches from product states to critical Hamiltonians. Building on this observation, we develop a route to extracting conformal data from real-time dynamics without preparing critical low-energy states. After analytic continuation, the Loschmidt amplitude is described by a boundary-CFT partition function on a strip, whose transverse transfer matrix encodes both the boundary operator spectrum and the central charge. Local space-time perturbations of the amplitude are governed by equilibrium correlation functions, and therefore provide access to critical exponents. In parallel, generalized temporal entropies exhibit scaling with time analogous to the equilibrium scaling of spatial entanglement entropy. We show that the low-lying boundary spectrum can be reconstructed from the system-size dependence of finite-chain Loschmidt echoes, whose damped oscillations encode differences of boundary scaling dimensions. Finally, we propose a finite-size scaling protocol that can extract these quantities from simulations or experiments on state-of-the-art quantum platforms.

### [164] [Observation of coherent flux-charge interaction in a gate-tunable fluxonium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07798)
*Brian D. Isakov,Shikhar Singh,Adrian Parra-Rodriguez,David Feldstein-Bofill,Zhenhai Sun,Anders Kringhøj,Svend Krøjer,Alexandre Blais,Morten Kjaergaard,András Gyenis*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过利用电压可调约瑟夫森结（voltage-tunable Josephson junction）和参量调制临界电流（parametrically modulated critical current），在超导电路（superconducting circuit）中实验实现了一种本征的磁通-电荷耦合（flux-charge coupling），即共轭变量之间的直接相互作用。该耦合在线性驱动幅度下实现，同时跃迁能量对栅极电压保持一阶不敏感，从而填补了超导电路元件库中的关键缺失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在超导电路中，电容器连接电荷与电荷，电感器连接磁通与磁通，但缺少一种两端元件能够直接耦合磁通与电荷这一对共轭变量（conjugate variables）。这种本征的磁通-电荷耦合作为电路基本元件，有望开辟非互易性（non-reciprocity）、保护模（protected modes）和非常规读出（unconventional readout）的直接途径。

Method: 利用电压可调约瑟夫森结，通过参量调制其临界电流（critical current）来实现磁通-电荷耦合。在混合超导-半导体磁通量子位（hybrid superconducting-semiconductor fluxonium）中，借助宇称选择定则（parity-selection rules）将磁通-电荷耦合与其他寄生电容贡献分离，并进行交叉正交激活（cross-quadrature-activated）的相干态控制。

Result: 实现了随驱动幅度线性变化的磁通-电荷耦合，同时跃迁能量（transition energy）对栅极电压（gate voltage）保持一阶不敏感（first-order-insensitive）。

Conclusion: 这种非传统相互作用（unconventional interaction）扩展了超导电路的元件工具箱，添补了一种能够实现共轭变量相干耦合的关键缺失元件。

Abstract: Interactions that mix conjugate variables, such as the flux through a circuit element and the charge across it, lie outside the reach of the elementary couplings of superconducting circuits. Capacitors connect charge to charge, and inductors connect flux to flux, while no two-terminal element couples flux to charge directly. A native flux-charge coupling would thus serve as a circuit primitive in its own right, opening direct routes to non-reciprocity, protected modes, and unconventional readout. In this work, we demonstrate a flux-charge coupling by harnessing a voltage-tunable Josephson junction with parametrically modulated critical current, which mediates the interaction between a classical charge variable and a quantum flux operator. Relying on parity-selection rules in a hybrid superconducting-semiconductor fluxonium, we isolate the flux-charge coupling from other parasitic capacitive contributions and perform cross-quadrature-activated coherent control of states. Critically, we realize a flux-charge coupling that scales linearly with driving amplitude while keeping the transition energy first-order-insensitive to gate voltage. Such unconventional interaction broadens the toolbox of superconducting circuits with a critical missing component that enables the coherent coupling of conjugate variables.

### [165] [Topology from Decoherence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07801)
*Alexandre Chaduteau,Derek Lee,Frank Schindler,Abhinav Prem*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究证明，传统上被视为阻碍的退相干（decoherence）实际上可以在开放多体系统中诱导拓扑现象，具体表现为晶格系统中环境导致的退相位（dephasing）通过相互作用产生由缠绕数（winding number）表征的拓扑相和非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect），且该效应为纯开放系统现象，无有效哈密顿量描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为退相干是实现拓扑量子相（topological quantum phases）的障碍，因此大量工作致力于抑制拓扑候选材料和器件中的噪声。该研究旨在挑战这一观念，探索退相干是否反而能够诱导拓扑现象。

Method: 研究在一个受环境诱导退相位（environment-induced dephasing）影响的晶格系统中进行，噪声平均动力学由相互作用的量子主方程（interacting quantum master equation）描述，从而实现对拓扑相和非厄米趋肤效应的理论分析。

Result: 噪声平均动力学实现了由缠绕数和非厄米趋肤效应表征的拓扑相。相关随机噪声的相关性导致不对称扩散（asymmetric diffusion），其方向由缠绕数决定且仅能通过拓扑相变（topological phase transition）反转。该效应由相互作用诱导，区别于以往的自由（有效单粒子）系统研究，且在投射后选择（postselecting）测量结果时消失，确认其为纯开放系统现象。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了相关量子噪声（correlated quantum noise）作为开放多体系统中实现拓扑的途径，超越了自由粒子（free-particle）和非厄米哈密顿量（non-Hermitian Hamiltonian）范式，且模型具有解析可解性。

Abstract: Decoherence is conventionally regarded as an obstacle to realizing topological quantum phases. This has motivated extensive efforts to suppress noise in candidate topological materials and devices. Here, we show that decoherence can instead induce topological phenomena. We demonstrate this in a lattice system subject to environment-induced dephasing. The noise-averaged dynamics, governed by an interacting quantum master equation, realize a topological phase characterized by a winding number and the non-Hermitian skin effect. The dynamical consequence is striking: the correlated nature of the stochastic noise yields asymmetric diffusion, whose direction is fixed by the winding number and is reversible only through a topological phase transition. This effect is induced purely by interactions, distinguishing it from previous studies of free, effectively single-particle systems. It also disappears upon postselecting measurement outcomes, confirming that it is a genuinely open-system phenomenon with no effective Hamiltonian description. Remarkably, the model remains analytically tractable. Our results establish correlated quantum noise as a route to topology in open many-body systems, beyond free-particle and non-Hermitian Hamiltonian paradigms.

</details>


### [166] [Shortcuts to Adiabaticity for non-Hermitian systems in Krylov Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07802)
*Ankit W. Shrestha,Budhaditya Bhattacharjee,Adolfo del Campo*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文发展了一种在非厄米（non-Hermitian）系统中工程化绝热捷径（shortcuts to adiabaticity, STA）的通用框架，通过将绝热规范势（adiabatic gauge potential, AGP）表示在Krylov空间中，避免了直接对角化，并利用双Lanczos和Arnoldi算法将AGP简化为稀疏三对角或上Hessenberg矩阵方程。该方法在多个非厄米模型（包括衰减二能级原子、Hatano-Nelson模型和PT对称海森堡链）中验证了有效性和收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 绝热捷径（STA）虽能在有限时间内重现绝热动力学，但其反绝热（counterdiabatic）实现依赖于绝热规范势（AGP），而在多体系统中AGP难以计算和实现，且其向开放系统和非厄米（non-Hermitian）系统的推广长期局限于特定模型。因此，需要一种通用的、免对角化的理论框架来在非厄米系统中工程化STA。

Method: 从反绝热控制的积分表示出发，将AGP重新表示为具有可控局域性的嵌套对易子级数（nested-commutator series），并利用双Lanczos（bi-Lanczos）和Arnoldi算法生成相应的Krylov基。这将精确或截断的AGP简化为稀疏三对角或上Hessenberg矩阵方程，从而推广了厄米（Hermitian）情形下的构造方法。

Result: 在衰减二能级原子中，该方法恢复了精确驱动并信号化了异常点（exceptional point）；在相互作用Hatano-Nelson模型中，截断控制快速抑制了非绝热激发；在PT对称海森堡链中，AGP范数检测到了PT对称性破缺相变。在所有模型中，展开仅需完整的Krylov空间的一小部分即可收敛。

Conclusion: 该框架为非厄米多体系统的快速、精确控制提供了一条实用途径，其Krylov空间展开的高效收敛性表明该方法具有较好的可扩展性和实际应用潜力。

Abstract: Shortcuts to adiabaticity (STA) reproduce adiabatic dynamics in finite time, but their counterdiabatic implementation relies on the adiabatic gauge potential (AGP), which is difficult to compute and implement in many-body systems and whose extension to open and non-Hermitian settings has remained largely model-specific. Here, we develop a general, diagonalization-free framework for engineering STA in non-Hermitian systems by representing the AGP in Krylov space. Starting from an integral representation of the counterdiabatic control, we recast the AGP as a nested-commutator series with controlled locality and generate the associated Krylov basis using the bi-Lanczos and Arnoldi algorithms. This reduces the exact or truncated AGP to a sparse tridiagonal or upper-Hessenberg matrix equation that generalizes the Hermitian construction. We demonstrate the method on a decaying two-level atom, where it recovers the exact drive and signals the exceptional point; on the interacting Hatano-Nelson model, where truncated controls rapidly suppress nonadiabatic excitations; and on a PT-symmetric Heisenberg chain, whose AGP norm detects the PT-symmetry-breaking transition. Throughout, the expansion converges with only a small fraction of the full Krylov space, offering a practical route to fast, accurate control of many-body non-Hermitian systems.

### [167] [Super-Logarithmic Entanglement Scaling in a Monitored Superconducting Chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07835)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建Keldysh-副本非线性sigma模型（Keldysh-replica NLSM），从辛鞍点（symplectic saddle）出发，结合测量反作用（measurement backaction）和配对振幅（pairing amplitude）的互补质量约束，投影出SO(R)靶流形上的无质量模式，并执行单圈重整化群（renormalization group）分析。

Result: 在副本极限R→1下，beta函数为负，产生弱反局域化（weak-anti-localization）流；稳态纠缠熵呈现超对数标度S(L)~ln²L，与同期数值结果一致。

Abstract: We develop a Keldysh-replica non-linear sigma model (NLSM) for the entanglement dynamics of a monitored one-dimensional spinful $s$-wave BCS chain in the rare-measurement regime, $γ\ll J,Δ$. Although the clean spinful $s$-wave BCS Hamiltonian belongs to symmetry class CI, spin-resolved measurements and projection to a conserved $f$-sector reduce the effective problem to class C. Starting from the corresponding parent symplectic saddle, we show that measurement backaction and the pairing amplitude impose complementary mass constraints that gap out different fluctuation channels. Their interplay dynamically projects the surviving massless modes onto an $\textrm{SO(R)}$ target manifold in replica space. A one-loop renormalization group analysis of this $\textrm{SO(R)}$ NLSM shows that, in the replica limit $R\to1$, the beta function becomes negative, producing a weak-anti-localization flow. This flow yields a super-logarithmic steady-state entanglement scaling $S(L)\sim \ln^2 L$ in the rare-measurement regime. Our field-theoretic result explains the numerical evidence reported in the companion Letter [arXiv:2604.04375] and shows that a topologically trivial monitored $s$-wave superconductor can realize an $\textrm{SO(R)}$ weak-anti-localizing critical phase without relying on a Wess-Zumino-Witten term.

Abstract: The advancement of chemistry and materials science relies on transformative analytical tools which can overcome the sensitivity, spatial resolution, and throughput limitations of conventional techniques. This review explores the application of quantum sensors - specifically optically pumped magnetometers (OPMs) and nitrogen-vacancy (NV) centers in diamond - as robust platforms for molecular and materials analysis. We contrast the extreme magnetic sensitivity of macroscopic OPM ensembles with the atomic-scale resolution and multimodal capabilities of solid-state NV centers. We highlight their deployment in zero- to ultralow-field and nanoscale NMR spectroscopy, real-time reaction monitoring, and transient radical and pH detection. ### [169] [Complex spacing ratio statistics in the partially open asymmetric quantum baker map](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07878)
*Leonardo Ermann,Pablo Sesin,Alejandro M. F. Rivas,Pablo D. Bergamasco,Gabriel G. Carlo*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有部分投影开孔的不对称量子面包师映射（asymmetric quantum baker map）的复本征值统计。通过三种开孔几何构型（局域、随机、均匀）与可调反射率参数ρ，发现复间距比（complex spacing ratio）z的分布呈现从准一维谱区到二维Ginibre-like区的平滑交叉(crossover），该交叉由开孔通道数M与反射率ρ共同调控，且在大M下三种模型均收敛于部分截断圆系综（PTCUE）的随机矩阵理论预言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典不对称面包师映射在q=2/3处存在间断点，具有完全混沌、无反射对称性、可调逃逸率与分形排斥子维数等特性，为研究开放量子混沌系统的本征值统计提供了干净可控的理论平台。现有研究对开孔几何形状如何影响复本征值统计行为尚缺乏系统理解，尤其是在连续可调反射率下的交叉行为。

Method: 采用三种位置空间开孔几何：局域式（contiguous channels）、随机式（random）和均匀式（equispaced channels），均由振幅反射率参数ρ（0到1）插值控制。以部分截断圆系综（PTCUE）作为随机矩阵理论基准。主要分析复间距比（complex spacing ratio）z的联合分布，z定义为复平面上本征值到最近邻和次近邻距离之比。

Result: 发现从准一维谱区（本征值聚集于单位圆附近，z的相位分布呈尖峰）到二维Ginibre-like区（分布近均匀，能级排斥完全发展）的平滑交叉，无突变相变证据。开孔通道数M与反射率ρ共同调控该交叉，ρ即使在固定开孔大小时也提供额外连续控制。三种开孔模型在大M下均收敛于PTCUE统计，局域模型在小M下差异最显著。

Conclusion: 该交叉行为暗示了开放量子与波混沌系统中的普适性（universality），对开放量子系统和波混沌实验具有深远意义。

Abstract: We study the complex eigenvalue statistics of the asymmetric quantum baker map with partial projective openings. The classical asymmetric baker map, with its discontinuity at $q=2/3$, is fully chaotic, has no reflection symmetry, and provides a clean setting with tunable escape rate and fractal repeller dimension. We consider three distinct opening geometries in position space: localized (contiguous channels), random, and uniform (equispaced channels), all controlled by a tunable amplitude reflectivity parameter $ρ$ that interpolates between the fully open ($ρ=0$) and the closed ($ρ=1$) limits. We use the partially truncated circular unitary ensemble (PTCUE) as the random matrix theory benchmark. The main focus is on the joint distribution of the complex spacing ratio $z$, defined as the ratio of the distances from an eigenvalue to its nearest and next-nearest neighbors in the complex plane. We find a smooth crossover from a quasi-1D spectral regime, where eigenvalues cluster near the unit circle and the phase distribution of $z$ is peaked, to a two-dimensional Ginibre-like regime, where the distribution becomes nearly uniform and level repulsion is fully developed. Both the number of open channels $M$ and the reflectivity $ρ$ modulate this crossover, and $ρ$ provides an additional continuous control even at fixed opening size. All three opening models converge to PTCUE statistics at large $M$, while differences are most pronounced for the localized model at small $M$. No evidence of an abrupt transition is found. This crossover which suggests a universal behavior, has deep consequences for open quantum and wave-chaotic experiments.

Abstract: Quantum gates based on resonant Rabi oscillations are inherently slow for small-frequency qubits. They are also prone to errors due to counter-rotating terms. However, when the anharmonicity is sufficiently high, as in the fluxonium architecture, alternative manipulation protocols can outperform standard resonant driving. In this work, we implement fast, high-fidelity quantum gates based on a one-period Landau-Zener-Stückelberg-Majorana (LZSM) driving protocol. We derive analytical expressions that simplify the exploration of the parameter space while accounting for the multi-level structure of the circuit. Furthermore, we analyze the role of leakage, discussing strategies to mitigate it and identifying regimes in which it becomes the dominant source of error. Finally, to evaluate the impact of dissipation on gate fidelity, we develop a robust formalism suitable for analyzing the open-system performance of quantum gates in the strong driving regime.

### [171] [Robust Quantum Learning through Hamiltonian Reservoir Computing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08037)
*Youya Xu,Chengyong Yu,Sanjib Ghosh*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种哈密顿量编码（Hamiltonian-encoding）框架用于量子储层计算（quantum reservoir computing），同时解决量子学习中的可训练性、硬件效率和信息稳定性三大挑战。该框架通过将输入数据直接映射到固定哈密顿量并利用量子动力学演化生成非线性特征，自然规避了贫瘠高原（barren plateau）问题。在模拟超导阵列处理器和数字门基量子电路两种平台上验证，两者表现出相当的表征能力和学习性能，其中模拟处理器在硬件效率上更具优势。研究发现有限耗散（finite dissipation）能抑制量子扰动弹散（quantum-scrambling）引起的不稳定性，并在长时间演化下提升学习性能，揭示了环境耦合在稳定量子学习动力学中的建设性作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用哈密顿量编码框架：将输入数据直接映射到固定哈密顿量上，通过量子动力学演化（quantum dynamical evolution）将其变换为表达性非线性特征（expressive nonlinear features）。基于储层计算（reservoir computing）范式，自然规避量子学习景观中的贫瘠高原问题。在两种互补平台——模拟超导阵列处理器（analog superconducting array processor）和数字门基量子电路（digital gate-based quantum circuit）——上分别实现验证。

Result: 两种平台尽管实现方式根本不同，但均表现出相当的表征能力和竞争性的学习性能。模拟处理器通过绕过门基分解的时间开销，更有效地利用有限相干时间（coherence times），在硬件效率上更具优势，但牺牲了通用性。有限耗散能抑制量子扰动弹散在长时间演化下引入的不稳定性，并提升学习性能。

Conclusion: 哈密顿量编码储层计算为当前量子平台提供了一种紧凑（compact）、高表达性（expressive）且硬件高效（hardware-efficient）的量子学习范式，并揭示了环境耦合在稳定量子学习动力学中的建设性作用。

Abstract: Quantum learning provides a versatile paradigm for information processing by exploiting the intrinsic representational capacity of high-dimensional Hilbert spaces. Here, we investigate a Hamiltonian-encoding framework for quantum reservoir computing that simultaneously addresses three key challenges in quantum learning: trainability, hardware efficiency, and information stability. In this framework, input data are directly mapped onto a fixed Hamiltonian and transformed into expressive nonlinear features through quantum dynamical evolution. By employing the reservoir-computing paradigm, the approach naturally circumvents the barren plateau problem in quantum learning landscapes. We validate the framework across two complementary platforms: an analog superconducting array processor and a digital gate-based quantum circuit implementation. Despite their fundamentally different realizations, both platforms exhibit comparable representational power and achieve competitive learning performance, establishing a unified framework for cross-platform quantum learning. While both implementations achieve comparable performance, the analog processor may offer a more hardware-efficient realization by bypassing the temporal overhead of gate-based decomposition and thereby making more effective use of finite coherence times, albeit at the expense of universality. Furthermore, we find that finite dissipation suppresses quantum-scrambling-induced instabilities at long evolution times and can enhance learning performance, revealing a constructive role for environmental coupling in stabilizing quantum learning dynamics. Collectively, these results establish Hamiltonian-encoded reservoir computing as a compact, expressive, and hardware-efficient paradigm for quantum learning on current-generation quantum platforms.

### [172] [Quantum and Classical Potts Criticality in Driven-Dissipative Bosonic Lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08425)
*Jacopo Tosca,Zejian Li,Cristiano Ciuti*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究受三光子参量驱动的玻色-哈伯德（Bose-Hubbard）晶格中的非平衡稳态相变，发现其临界行为分别对应二维经典三态波茨模型和一维量子三态波茨模型的普适类，并表明多光子耗散可将非平衡临界行为从经典普适类提升至量子普适类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非平衡动力学如何涌现出平衡态的普适性（universality）是一个基本未解问题，亟需通过可控的非平衡模型来探索这一机制。

Method: 采用基于变分多高斯（Variational Multi-Gaussian）近似的变分相空间方法（variational phase-space approach），在一维和二维玻色-哈伯德晶格中进行有限尺寸标度分析（finite-size scaling analysis），系统控制计算精度。

Result: 在具有单光子损耗的二维晶格中，非平衡稳态相变属于二维经典三态波茨模型（three-state Potts model）的普适类；在具有三光子损耗的一维晶格中，相变则归入一维量子三态波茨模型的普适类。

Conclusion: 驱动-耗散玻色子晶格可作为涌现波茨临界性（Potts criticality）的平台，且多光子耗散（multiphoton dissipation）是一种将非平衡临界行为从经典普适类推向量子普适类的机制。

Abstract: The emergence of equilibrium universality from intrinsically nonequilibrium dynamics is a fundamental open problem. Bose-Hubbard lattices realized in photonic and circuit-QED platforms provide a versatile setting to engineer nonlinear interactions, dissipation, and multiphoton processes. Here we investigate a Bose-Hubbard lattice subject to three-photon parametric driving, whose nonequilibrium steady state spontaneously breaks a $\mathbb Z_3$ symmetry and realizes the criticality of the three-state Potts model, a three-state generalization of the Ising model. Using a variational phase-space approach with systematically controllable accuracy based on a Variational Multi-Gaussian ansatz, we perform finite-size scaling analyses in one and two spatial dimensions. We find that, in two-dimensional lattices with single-photon losses, the nonequilibrium steady-state transition belongs to the universality class of the 2D classical three-state Potts model. In contrast, in one-dimensional lattices with three-photon losses, the transition is governed by the one-dimensional quantum three-state Potts universality class. These results establish driven-dissipative bosonic lattices as a platform for emergent Potts criticality and identify multiphoton dissipation as a mechanism that promotes nonequilibrium critical behavior from classical to quantum universality classes.

Result: 发现了动量依赖的恒等项会主动变形广义布里渊区，挑战了依赖固定复值轮廓（complex contours）的传统拓扑判据；揭示了跨胞自旋-轨道耦合与恒等项协同可在完全无手征对称性的系统中诱导拓扑边缘态和稳健零模。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一个超越对称性保护（symmetry protection）的非厄米拓扑精确可解范式，并为测试含动量依赖恒等项系统的拓扑不变量（topological invariants）提供了严格基准。

Abstract: An identity term in the Hamiltonian is conventionally regarded as spectrally inert-it shifts energies but does not alter eigenstate topology. We show that under non-Hermitian skin pumping, this paradigm fails: a momentum-dependent identity term actively deforms the generalized Brillouin zone, thereby challenging established topological criteria that rely on fixed complex contours. Here, by introducing spin-orbit coupling into a Hatano-Nelson chain, we present an exact analytical solution for the entire non-Hermitian eigensystem under open boundary conditions. Our solution reveals how inter-cell spin-orbit coupling, synergizing with this non-trivial identity term, induces topological edge states and robust zero modes in the complete absence of chiral symmetry. This work establishes an exactly solvable paradigm for non-Hermitian topology beyond symmetry protection, and provides a rigorous benchmark for testing topological invariants in systems with momentum-dependent identity terms.

### [174] [Operational meaning of Markov gap in tripartite entanglement of quantum dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08615)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 以马尔可夫间隙（Markov gap）作为不可约三体纠缠（IrTE）的探针，分析自由费米子链中的动力学行为；基于利布-罗宾逊界（Lieb-Robinson bound）给出 IrTE 起始时间的可达上下界；引入三体本质费米子（essential tripartite fermion, ETF）及三体零矩阵（tripartite null matrix），通过小奇异值数目解释马尔可夫间隙的取值。

Conclusion: 不可约三体纠缠从短程动力学中涌现的饱和时间尺度（L²）揭示了其与双体纠缠在传播机制上的本质差异；三体本质费米子与三体零矩阵为马尔可夫间隙提供了透明且可操作的物理诠释；该特征对相互作用体系具有鲁棒性。

Abstract: We investigate how irreducible multipartite entanglement, a long-range correlation by nature, can emerge from short-range dynamics far from equilibrium. Focusing on the Markov gap as a probe of irreducible tripartite entanglement (IrTE) in free-fermion chains, we uncover qualitatively distinct dynamical behaviors: the Markov gap grows either quasi-linearly or in staircase-like jumps depending on the initial state. We also propose attainable upper and lower bounds for the onset time of IrTE based on the Lieb-Robinson bound. Strikingly, the Markov gap saturates to a volume-law value on a timescale $t\sim\! L^2$, much slower than the ballistic spreading of bipartite correlations. To understand what information about the wavefunctions is revealed by the Markov gap calculation, we introduce the concept of essential tripartite fermion (ETF) and an associated tripartite null matrix. The value of Markov gap closely tracks the number of small singular values of this tripartite null matrix, yielding a transparent, operational physical interpretation of the measure. We further demonstrate that several dynamical signatures persist in the interacting XXZ chain.

Finally, we compute two-phonon contributions to inter-system crossing at 300 K for2 as a luminescent prototype, and find that it is highly spin-selective, supporting the possibility to engineer optical read out and spin initialization. ### [176] [Symmetry as a route to generalized bosonic Kitaev chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08638)
*Gideon Lee,Tony Jin,Aashish A. Clerk*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文揭示了玻色子Kitaev链（BKC）模型中对称性的关键作用，指出二次玻色子配对哈密顿量在具有子格（手征）对称性时，其动力学矩阵必然具有一种有效的时间反演对称性，并讨论了另一有效对称性——粒子-空穴对称性——如何导致正交动力学解耦。此外，论文对所有平移不变的一维配对哈密顿量进行了分类，并建立了BKC与辛Hatano-Nelson模型之间的联系。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过对称性分析识别BKC模型中动力学矩阵所具有的有效时间反演对称性（effective time reversal symmetry）和有效粒子-空穴对称性（effective particle-hole symmetry），并利用这两种有效对称性的区分来构造广义BKC模型。同时，对所有平移不变的一维玻色子配对哈密顿量进行分类。

Result: 发现任何具有子格（手征）对称性（sublattice/chiral symmetry）的二次玻色子配对哈密顿量，其动力学矩阵必然具有一种与物理时间反演无关的有效时间反演对称性，该对称性使非平凡拓扑不变量成为可能。另一关键性质——正交动力学解耦（decoupling of quadrature dynamics）——则归因于一种有效粒子-空穴对称性。论文还给出了所有平移不变一维配对哈密顿量的完整分类，并将BKC与辛Hatano-Nelson模型（symplectic Hatano-Nelson model）联系起来。

Conclusion: 对称性是理解BKC模型中非厄米拓扑现象的核心；两种有效对称性（有效时间反演对称性与有效粒子-空穴对称性）各自独立且分别对应不同的物理性质。广义BKC模型和完整的哈密顿量分类为研究玻色子拓扑系统提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: The bosonic Kitaev chain (BKC) model is a deceptively simple looking quadratic pairing Hamiltonian. Despite being purely Hermitian, it exhibits a number of striking non-Hermitian topological phenomena, including skin effects. We show here how symmetries play a key role in this model, and how identifying these allows one to develop generalized BKC-like models. We emphasize the surprising fact that any quadratic bosonic pairing Hamiltonian with a sublattice (chiral) symmetry necessarily has a dynamical matrix with an effective time reversal symmetry. This symmetry is unrelated to physical time-reversal, but enables non-trivial topological invariants. We also discuss how this symmetry is unrelated to another key property of the BKC, the decoupling of quadrature dynamics. This feature can instead be connected to a distinct symmetry, namely an effective particle-hole symmetry of the dynamical matrix. We discuss non-trivial generalized BKC models that only keep one of these two effective symmetries intact. We also provide a classification of all translationally-invariant 1D pairing Hamiltonians, and show connections between the BKC and a well-studied non-Hermitian fermionic system, the symplectic Hatano-Nelson model.

### [177] [Absence of quantum advantage for approximate spin glass optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08708)
*Dries Sels,Flaviano Morone*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用半经典大自旋分析和截断Wigner近似，研究了量子近似优化算法（QAOA）在Sherrington-Kirkpatrick（SK）模型上的表现，发现最终能量随自旋S呈非单调变化，最优平衡点出现在S~p量级，最终能量以log(p)/p速率收敛至Parisi值；移除初始噪声并重新优化参数后可实现1/p收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索QAOA在SK模型上的深度-性能缩放行为，特别是通过半经典大自旋S分析揭示自旋大小对算法性能的影响机制。

Method: 采用半经典（semiclassical）大自旋S分析，结合截断Wigner近似（truncated Wigner approximation）对QAOA进行解析和数值研究。固定QAOA角度至先前确定的S=1/2最优值，分析不同自旋S下的性能表现。

Result: 最终能量随自旋S呈现非单调依赖：小S区域半经典结果受噪声主导，大S区域受初始波动指数增长制约。对于深度为p的QAOA，最优平衡发生在S~p量级，此时最终能量以log(p)/p速率收敛至Parisi值。半经典方法略优于真实的S=1/2 QAOA。移除初始噪声并重新优化参数后，可实现1/p收敛。

Conclusion: 半经典分析表明QAOA与真实自旋1/2 QAOA均以相同方式（log(p)/p）收敛至Parisi值；消除初始噪声及参数重优化可显著提升收敛速率至1/p，暗示噪声控制是提升QAOA性能的关键因素。

Abstract: We perform a semiclassical, large-spin S, analysis of the quantum approximate optimization algorithm (QAOA) on the Sherrington-Kirkpatrick (SK) model, using the truncated Wigner approximation. Fixing the QAOA angles to their previously determined optimal S=1/2 values, we observe a non-monotonic dependence of the final energy on the spin. At small S the semiclassics is dominated by noise, while the large-S limit is constrained by the exponential growth of the initial fluctuations. For a depth-p QAOA one achieves the optimal balance at S of order p, resulting in a convergence of the final energy to the Parisi value like log(p)/p. We find that the semiclassics slightly outperforms the true spin-1/2 QAOA, and thus suggest they both converge to the Parisi value in the same way. Finally, removing all the initial noise, and re-optimizing the parameters to account for that change, results in superior performance with 1/p convergence.

### [178] [Approaching Carnot Efficiency at Finite Power in an Experimentally Feasible Quantum Heat Engine](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08713)

TL;DR: 该论文提出一种基于超导电路（superconducting circuit）的热机，通过模拟集体增强（collective enhancement）机制，在有限功率下渐进逼近卡诺效率（Carnot efficiency），从而规避经典马尔可夫热机（classical Markovian heat engine）的功率-效率权衡（power-efficiency trade-off），并将有限时间热力学（finite-time thermodynamics）的抽象界限与具体的电路量子电动力学（circuit-QED）平台联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在有限时间热力学中，经典马尔可夫热机因局域相互作用（local interactions）而无法在有限功率下渐近逼近卡诺效率。尽管量子系统中利用简并性（degeneracy）、对称性（symmetry）和集体跳跃（collective jumps）理论上可能实现这种渐近逼近，但该机制能否在实验上可实现的热机中实现仍是一个未解问题。

Result: 该可实现的超导电路热机模型表明，集体增强的耗散机制（enhanced dissipative mechanism）能够规避经典马尔可夫热机的功率-效率权衡，在有限功率下渐近逼近卡诺效率。

Conclusion: 该工作将有限时间热力学中的抽象界限与具体的电路量子电动力学平台相连接，并指出了基于集体增强耗散过程进行量子器件设计的可行路径。

Abstract: Whether a heat engine can approach Carnot efficiency while maintaining finite power is a fundamental question in finite-time thermodynamics. For classical Markovian heat engines with local interactions, the power-efficiency trade-off forbids an asymptotic approach to Carnot efficiency at finite power. In quantum systems, by contrast, degeneracy, symmetry, and collective jumps have been theoretically predicted to enable such an asymptotic attainment by enhancing activity. It has remained open, however, whether this mechanism can be realized in an experimentally implementable heat engine. In this Letter, we propose a superconducting-circuit heat engine that emulates the collective enhancement, thereby enabling an asymptotic approach to Carnot efficiency at finite power. This result demonstrates that, in an implementable model, such an enhanced dissipative mechanism circumvents the power-efficiency trade-off of classical Markovian engines. Our work connects abstract bounds in finite-time thermodynamics to a concrete circuit-QED platform and suggests a route toward quantum-device design based on collectively enhanced dissipative processes.

### [179] [Irreducible Geometry of Higher-Order Correlator Families](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08761)
*Kaito Kobayashi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个几何框架，用于对高阶量子多体关联函数族进行集体分析。通过将关联函数表示为算符词（operator words）的内积，引入条件化子空间（conditioning subspaces）将关联函数几何分解为可约信息（reducible information）与不可约信息（irreducible information），并定义不可约体积轮廓（irreducible volume profiles）来量化不可解释部分的几何展布。该框架包括规范条件化、目标条件化、Krylov条件化与交叉条件化等多种形式，揭示了单个关联函数值层面隐藏的不可约结构，并将关联函数几何确立为量子多体动力学的更高层描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可编程量子模拟器已能获取从四点时间顺序外关联函数（out-of-time-ordered correlators, OTOC）到更高阶多体关联函数等复杂度递增的关联量，但解释这些数据的理论框架仍相对不成熟。高阶关联函数虽可直观构造，其物理意义却往往难以推断；不同关联函数之间并非独立，部分相互冗余，部分编码截然不同的信息——因此需要将关联函数视为一个有结构的家族而非孤立量进行分析。

Method: 建立了一个几何框架：将关联函数表示为算符词之间的内积，从而将每个关联函数族重铸为算符空间中的几何结构。核心方法是引入条件化子空间，将该几何分离为已由选定可解扇区（resolved sector）解释的可约信息与残差关联函数几何中编码的不可约信息。针对后者定义不可约体积轮廓，用以量化关联函数族中未被解释的部分在独立几何方向上的展布程度。衍生出多种互补的条件化形式：规范条件化（canonical conditioning）最优地解释整个关联函数族；目标条件化（targeted conditioning）固定可解扇区以孤立特定物理特征；Krylov条件化与交叉条件化（Krylov and cross conditioning）将框架从单个关联函数族扩展到不同关联函数几何之间的比较。

Result: 该框架揭示了隐藏在单个关联函数值层面的不可约结构，建立了关联函数几何作为量子多体动力学更高层描述的有效性。通过定义不可约体积轮廓，量化了关联函数族中未被选定扇区解释的信息在独立几何方向上的分布，实现了对关联函数冗余与不可约结构的系统区分。

Conclusion: 关联函数不应被视为孤立量，而应作为一个有结构的几何家族加以分析。本文发展的几何框架为高阶关联函数族的集体分析提供了系统工具，能够提取单个关联函数值层面不可见的不可约结构，将关联函数几何确立为量子多体动力学的一种更高层次的描述语言。

Abstract: Programmable quantum simulators are beginning to access correlators of increasing complexity, ranging from four-point out-of-time-ordered correlators to even higher-order many-body correlators. The theoretical framework for interpreting such data, however, remains comparatively underdeveloped. Although a variety of higher-order correlators can be constructed straightforwardly, their physical meaning is often difficult to infer. A further complication is that different correlators are generally not independent: some may be mutually redundant, while others may encode genuinely distinct information. These features make it necessary to analyze correlators not as isolated quantities, but as a structured family. In this work, we develop a geometric framework for the collective analysis of higher-order correlator families. By representing correlators as inner products between operator words, we recast each family as a geometry in operator space. The key idea is to introduce conditioning subspaces that separate this geometry into reducible information, already explained by a chosen resolved sector, and irreducible information, encoded in the residual correlator geometry. Focusing on the latter component, we define irreducible volume profiles that quantify how broadly the unexplained part of a correlator family spreads over independent geometric directions. This perspective leads to several complementary forms of conditioning. Canonical conditioning optimally explains a correlator family. Targeted conditioning fixes the resolved sector to isolate a chosen physical feature. Krylov and cross conditioning extend the framework from a single correlator family to comparisons among correlator geometries. Our framework reveals irreducible structures hidden at the level of individual correlator values and establishes correlator geometry as a higher-level description of quantum many-body dynamics.

</details>

### [180] [Explaining Near-Zero Hessian Eigenvalues Through Approximate Symmetries in Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07845)
*Marcel Kühn,Bernd Rosenow*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文论证训练损失的海森矩阵（Hessian）中大量趋零特征值来源于网络参数化连续对称性（continuous symmetries）被弱提升（weakly lifted）后的赝戈德斯通模（pseudo-Goldstone modes）。线性网络中这些对称性精确，对应零模（zero modes）；引入ReLU非线性后对称性被弱破缺，形成海森矩阵的体（bulk）特征值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有工作解释了训练损失海森矩阵最大特征值的来源，但大量趋零小特征值的起源尚不明确。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 在深度线性网络中构造精确零模的本征向量；将ReLU非线性视为微扰，分析其对连续对称性的弱破缺效应；通过本征向量分量的空间分解，区分高曲率方向与对称性子空间；在两层ReLU师生模型（student–teacher model）和CIFAR-10训练的网络中验证机制，并在卷积网络案例中证明诊断方法可扩展至全连接层以外。

Result: 高曲率方向与对称性子空间正交，而海森矩阵体（bulk）几乎完全位于对称性子空间内；在两层ReLU师生模型、CIFAR-10训练网络及卷积网络实例中均观察到该现象。

Conclusion: 海森矩阵体与弱破缺对称性相关联，这一发现阐明了近零模（near-zero modes）的起源。

Abstract: The Hessian of the training loss governs the local geometry of the loss landscape, yet despite existing explanations for its largest eigenvalues, the origin of the vast multitude of vanishingly small eigenvalues remains elusive. We argue that the bulk consists of the weakly lifted pseudo-Goldstone modes of the continuous symmetries of the network parametrization. In deep linear networks these symmetries are exact: they generate flat directions and hence exact zero modes, whose eigenvectors we construct explicitly. Introducing a ReLU nonlinearity as a perturbation, we show that it breaks these symmetries weakly and explicitly. Resolving the spectrum at the level of eigenvectors, we find that the high-curvature directions are orthogonal to the symmetry subspace, while the bulk lies almost entirely within it. We demonstrate the mechanism in a two-layer ReLU student--teacher model and in a network trained on CIFAR-10. A convolutional example demonstrates that the same diagnostic extends beyond fully connected layers. Together, these results link the Hessian bulk to weakly broken symmetries and clarify the origin of near-zero modes.

</details>


### [181] [An exact information theory of generalization phase transitions in Bayesian diffusion models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08041)
*Henry Hunt,Mason Kamb,Surya Ganguli*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出贝叶斯信息受限扩散（BIRD）模型，通过信息限制解释扩散模型如何规避维度灾难，并识别出记忆与泛化之间的信息论相边界，发现生成过程运行在该边界附近。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散模型能在有限训练集上学习高维空间中的复杂分布而不发生记忆，这一机制尚不清楚。本文旨在从理论上解释扩散模型如何规避维度灾难（curse of dimensionality）。

Method: 引入贝叶斯信息受限扩散（BIRD）模型，每个像素仅观测带噪数据中的受限信息，通过贝叶斯后验推断产生当前受限观测的训练样本来逆转扩散过程。该模型推广了现有使用空间局部信息限制的分析扩散模型。

Result: 在数据分布的最小假设下，识别出训练数据量、逆生成过程时间与信息限制量三者联合空间中的记忆-泛化信息论相边界：当受限观测与训练数据之间的互信息（mutual information）超过训练点数的对数时模型记忆，否则泛化。实验验证了相变位置的理论预测，且生成过程运行在记忆化边界附近。

Conclusion: 信息限制在生成式AI中规避维度灾难中发挥了根本性作用。空间局部BIRD模型和早期训练扩散模型均随时间推移增加信息限制，追踪记忆-泛化相边界。

Abstract: How diffusion models circumvent the curse of dimensionality to learn complex distributions over high dimensional spaces from a finite training set, instead of memorizing it, remains a fundamental mystery. To address this, we introduce analytically tractable Bayesian information restricted diffusion (BIRD) models, in which each pixel observes restricted information about noisy data. A BIRD model time-reverses diffusion by inferring which past training sample produced its current restricted observation using the Bayesian posterior. This model class generalizes existing analytical diffusion models that use spatially local information restriction. We show that spatially local BIRD models closely approximate trained diffusion models \textit{early in training}, across different architectures such as UNets and DiTs. Under minimal assumptions on the data distribution, we identify an information-theoretic phase boundary between memorization and generalization in the joint space of amount of training data, time in the reverse generative process, and amount of information restriction: a BIRD model memorizes when the mutual information between its restricted noisy observations and the training data exceeds the log number of training points, and it generalizes otherwise. Experiments across a range of datasets confirm our theoretically predicted location for the transition. We find that generation proceeds near the edge of memorization: both spatially local BIRD models and early-training diffusion models track the memorization-generalization phase boundary by increasingly restricting information over time. Overall, our results reveal a fundamental role for information restriction in generative AI to circumvent the curse of dimensionality.

</details>

### [182] [A study of neutrinoless double electron capture in $^{40}$Ca from the AMoRE experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08039)
*AMoRE Collaboration,A. Agrawal,V. V. Alenkov,P. Aryal,J. Beyer,B. Bhandari,R. S. Boiko,K. Boonin,O. Buzanov,C. R. Byeon,N. Chanthima,M. K. Cheoun,J. S. Choe,Seonho Choi,S. Choudhury,J. S. Chung,F. A. Danevich,M. Djamal,D. Drung,C. Enss,A. Fleischmann,A. M. Gangapshev,L. Gastaldo,Y. M. Gavrilyuk,A. M. Gezhaev,O. Gileva,V. D. Grigorieva,V. I. Gurentsov,C. Ha,D. H. Ha,E. J. Ha,D. H. Hwang,E. J. Kim,S. R. Kim,W. T. Kim,Y. D. Kim,Y. H. Kim,K. Kirdsiri,Y. J. Ko,V. V. Kobychev,V. Kornoukhov,V. V. Kuzminov,D. H. Kwon,C. H. Lee,DongYeup Lee,E. K. Lee,H. J. Lee,H. S. Lee,J. Lee,J. Y. Lee,K. B. Lee,M. H. Lee,M. K. Lee,S. W. Lee,Y. C. Lee,D. S. Leonard,H. S. Lim,B. Mailyan,E. P. Makarov,P. B. Nyanda,Y. Oh,S. L. Olsen,S. I. Panasenko,H. K. Park,H. S. Park,K. S. Park,S. Y. Park,O. G. Polischuk,H. Prihtiadi,S. Ra,S. S. Ratkevich,G. Rooh,E. Sala,M. B. Sari,J. Seo,K. M. Seo,B. Sharma,K. A. Shin,V. N. Shlegel,K. Siyeon,J. So,N. V. Sokur,J. K. Son,J. W. Song,N. Srisittipokakun,V. I. Tretyak,R. Wirawan,K. R. Woo,H. J. Yeon,Y. S. Yoon,Q. Yue*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 基于AMoRE-I实验的7.32 kg·yr曝光数据，利用CaMoO₄晶体探测器研究⁴⁰Ca的无中微子双电子俘获（0ν2EC）衰变，未发现显著信号，给出半衰期下限T^{0ν}_{1/2} > 1.7 × 10²² yr（90%置信水平）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无中微子双电子俘获（0ν2EC）是探测轻子数破坏（lepton-number violation）和中微子马约拉纳性质（Majorana nature）的灵敏探针；AMoRE实验利用CaMoO₄探测器在主要¹⁰⁰Mo无中微子双β衰变（0νββ）搜索之外，同时探索⁴⁰Ca的0ν2EC稀有衰变过程。

Method: 使用AMoRE-I实验中的低温探测器（cryogenic detectors），配备金属磁量热计（metallic magnetic calorimeters），基于十三块⁴⁰Ca¹⁰⁰MoO₄晶体、总曝光量7.32 kg·yr的物理数据集进行0ν2EC衰变分析。

Result: 未观察到显著信号，在90%置信水平（confidence level）下给出⁴⁰Ca半衰期下限T^{0ν}_{1/2} > 1.7 × 10²² yr。

Conclusion: CaMoO₄探测器在搜索主要¹⁰⁰Mo衰变外，具备探索稀有衰变过程的潜力；预计即将开展的AMoRE-II实验将获得更高的灵敏度。

Abstract: The search for neutrinoless double electron capture ($0ν\mathrm{2EC}$) provides a sensitive probe of lepton-number violation and the Majorana nature of neutrinos. We investigate the $0ν\mathrm{2EC}$ decay of $^{40}$Ca using cryogenic detectors equipped with metallic magnetic calorimeters in the AMoRE-I experiment. The analysis is based on a physics dataset corresponding to a total exposure of 7.32 kg$\cdot$yr from thirteen $^{40}$Ca$^{100}$MoO$_4$ crystals. No significant excess is observed, and a lower limit on the half-life is obtained as $T^{0ν}_{1/2} > 1.7 \times 10^{22}$ yr at 90$\%$ confidence level. An improved sensitivity is expected for the upcoming AMoRE-II experiment. These results demonstrate the potential of CaMoO$_4$ detectors to explore rare decay processes beyond the primary $^{100}$Mo $0νββ$ search program.

### [183] [Twofold universality of large-$N$ melonic random tensors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08677)
*Carlos I. Perez-Sanchez*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文构造了一种新型普适性（universality）测度，用于大幅简化大$N$极限下张量（tensor）积分的计算。研究表明，在张量迹（trace）满足“甜瓜性（melonicity）”递归构造条件时，积分的领头阶与张量迹的详细组合结构无关，且在$D\geq 3$时与张量指标数$D$无关，仅依赖于顶点数$2p_i$所定义的甜瓜多项式（melonic polynomials）。该测度实现了两类普适性：不同张量模型在大$N$下不可区分，且交互作用的精细结构不影响最终结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 矩阵积分（matrix integration）中迹（trace）可直接构造被积函数，但张量积分需要$D$色图（$D$-coloured graph）$B$来收缩指标并形成张量迹$B(T)$，其组合结构通常非常复杂。本文旨在寻找一种能显著简化大$N$下张量积分的普适性方法。

Method: 作者构造了一个普适测度（universal measure），将每个满足甜瓜性（melonicity）条件的张量迹$B_i$替换为仅依赖于顶点数$2p_i$的规范迹（canonical trace）。核心观察是：当每个$B_1,\ldots,B_n$均可通过甜瓜性递归构造得到时，积分$\int B_1(T)\cdots B_n(T)$在大$N$下的领头阶既独立于$B_i$的精细组合结构，也在$D\geq 3$时独立于维数$D$，仅表现为甜瓜多项式。

Result: 在大$N$极限下，任意两个甜瓜张量模型（melonic tensor model）不可区分，且该结果独立于张量指标数$D$（第一类普适性）以及交互作用的精细粒度（第二类普适性）。充分条件是模型的耦合参数（$g_i$）一致，且各自的迹为关于$T$的相同次数的单项式（monomial）。

Conclusion: 本文建立的普适测度为甜瓜型张量模型在大$N$下的分析与比较提供了统一框架，揭示了张量积分中此前未发现的、独立于维数与交互细节的深层结构。

Abstract: We construct a measure that exhibits two aspects of a new type of universality and dramatically simplifies the integration of tensors $T_{a_1,a_2,\ldots,a_D} \in \mathbb{C}$ ($a_1,\ldots,a_D=1,\ldots,N$) at large $N$. In contrast to matrix integration, in which matrix traces canonically yield the integrand, tensors need additional information (equivalent to a $D$-coloured graph $B$) to contract their indices and form a tensor trace $B(T)$. We show that, whenever each $B_1,\ldots, B_n$ can be obtained by a recursive construction known as melonicity, then the leading order in $N$ of the integral of $ {B_1}(T) {B_2}(T) \cdots {B_n}(T) $ is independent of the -- often intricate -- combinatorics of the traces $B_i$, but also, to our surprise, independent of $D$ as far as $D\geq 3$. Instead, at large $N$, these integrals are some functions (indexed by $n$) of the number of vertices $2p_i$ of $B_i$ which we call melonic polynomials. Melonic traces cumulants with respect to any ('interacting') measure \[ \exp\Big\{-N^{D-1} \sum_{i=1}^m g_i {B_i}(T)\Big\} \mathrm{d}μ_0(T) \quad (g_1,\ldots,g_m \in \mathbb{R}, \mathrm{d}μ_0(T) =\text{the tensor Gaussian}) \] with each $B_i$ melonic, can be computed with our universal measure that replaces each $B_i$ by a canonical trace depending only on $p_i$. We prove that any two melonic tensor models are indistinguishable at large-$N$, independently of the number of tensor indices (first universality aspect), and of the fine-grainedness of their interactions (second universality), being a sufficient condition that the couplings (the parameters $g_i$ above) agree and their respective traces are monomials with the same degree in $T$.

</details>

### [184] [Thermodynamic Structure and Composition in Nonlinear Convection-Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07829)
*J. J. Segura*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文针对开放非线性对流–扩散系统（nonlinear convection–diffusion systems），建立了一个以连续介质力学优先（continuum-first）的框架，将热力学一致性（thermodynamic consistency）表述为具有非负体耗散和显式边界及源贡献的自由能平衡（free-energy balance）。证明了该热力学平衡在子域限制、接口耦合、线性近似和离散化等操作下保持不变，从而构建了一个从连续建模到数值计算均保持第二定律可见的组合式输运框架（compositional transport framework）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非线性对流–扩散系统在传质、传热、多孔介质输运等众多输运现象中扮演核心角色。关键问题不仅在于选择何种偏微分方程（partial differential equation）作为控制方程，更在于模型在自然出现的输运分析操作（如子域限制、跨接口耦合、近平衡线性化和计算离散化）下，能否保持一致的热力学平衡（thermodynamic balance）。

Method: 论文发展了一种连续介质优先框架，将热力学一致性形式化为自由能平衡，包含非负体耗散（bulk dissipation）以及显式的边界和源贡献。非线性输运系统被定义为由可容许状态场（admissible state fields）、存储泛函（storage functionals）、本构流分解（constitutive flux decompositions）、源和边界端口（boundary ports）构成的结构化对象。研究在精确保持结构的变换、子域限制、相容域分解下的局部到全局重构以及开放子系统间的功率守恒互连中，证明热力学平衡的保持性。进一步将经典线性对流–扩散模型推导为平衡态附近的切向热力学后代（tangent thermodynamic descendants），并证明当数值设计尊重热力学结构时，同一不变量在弱形式、半离散化和全离散时间步进中仍然成立。

Result: 论文的核心结果是证明了热力学平衡在以下过程中保持不变：精确的结构保持变换、子域限制、相容域分解下的局部到全局重构，以及开放子系统间的功率守恒互连。同时表明，经典线性对流–扩散模型是平衡态附近的切向热力学后代，并且该热力学不变量在尊重热力学结构的弱形式、半离散化和全离散时间步进中依然成立。非线性漂移–扩散（drift–diffusion）和多孔介质对流–扩散（porous-medium convection–diffusion）作为显式示例被讨论。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个组合式输运框架，在该框架中，第二定律（the second law）在连续介质建模、子系统耦合、线性近似和数值计算的全过程中始终可见（visible）。这为开放非线性对流–扩散系统的热力学一致建模与计算提供了系统化的方法论基础。

Abstract: Nonlinear convection--diffusion systems play a central role in transport phenomena, including mass transfer, heat transfer, porous-media transport, and coupled continuum processes with source, exchange, and interface effects. In such systems, the key question is often not only which governing partial differential equation is used, but whether the model preserves a consistent thermodynamic balance under the operations that arise naturally in transport analysis: restriction to subdomains, coupling across interfaces, linearization near equilibrium, and discretization for computation.
  This paper develops a continuum-first framework for open nonlinear convection--diffusion systems in which thermodynamic consistency is formulated as a free-energy balance with nonnegative bulk dissipation and explicit boundary and source contributions. Within this setting, nonlinear transport systems are defined as structured objects built from admissible state fields, storage functionals, constitutive flux decompositions, sources, and boundary ports. We prove that the thermodynamic balance is preserved under exact structure-preserving transformations, restriction to subdomains, local-to-global reconstruction over compatible domain decompositions, and power-conserving interconnection of open subsystems. We then derive classical linear convection--diffusion models as tangent thermodynamic descendants at equilibrium and show that the same invariant survives weak formulation, semidiscretization, and fully discrete time stepping when the numerical design respects thermodynamic structure. Nonlinear drift--diffusion and porous-medium convection--diffusion are used as explicit examples. The resulting contribution is a compositional transport framework in which the second law remains visible across continuum modeling, subsystem coupling, linear approximation, and computation.

</details>

# nlin.CD [[Back]](#toc)

### [185] [Chaos in the Order of Finite Bernoulli Convolutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08676)
*Nadav Shrayer*

Main category: nlin.CD

TL;DR: 本文对有限伯努利卷积（finite Bernoulli convolutions）进行数值探索，展示了其在特定参数下可作为充分发展湍流中能量级串（intermittent energy cascade）的玩具模型。分析了β-展开（β-expansions）中穿越点（crossings）在β上的分布，并引入基于N-二元词（N-binary words）词典序（lexicographical order）的序概念（order），观察到当β从2降至1时相邻对的序距离呈指数增长，暗示混沌行为且Lyapunov指数聚成若干依赖于N的簇。最后给出“序图”（order plots）并在β等于黄金比例（golden ratio）g的有限β-紧集（finite β-compactum）与二进制反射格雷码（binary reflected Gray code）之间建立了有趣联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索有限伯努利卷积作为充分发展湍流中能量级串现象的玩具模型，并研究β-展开中穿越点的分布规律及其与奇异连续测度（singular continuous measures）的关系。

Method: 采用数值实验方法，通过分析β-展开的穿越点分布、基于词典序的N-二元词序距离，以及有限β-紧集的结构，系统考察参数β变化下的行为特征。

Result: 当β从2降至1时，相邻对的序距离呈指数增长，表现出“混沌”行为，且Lyapunov指数聚集成若干依赖于N的簇。发现了有限β-紧集在β=g（黄金比例）时与二进制反射格雷码之间的有趣联系。

Conclusion: 有限伯努利卷积在特定参数下可作为湍流级串的玩具模型；β-展开的序结构揭示了参数变化中的混沌动力学特征，并为奇异连续测度相关参数提供了新的刻画视角。

Abstract: In this note we explore numerically the finite Bernoulli convolutions. We show that with a suitable choice of parameter, it might serve as a toy model for intermittent energy cascade in fully developed turbulence. We then show how the crossings of $β$-expansions distribute in $β$, and suggest that it might highlight the parameters with enhanced overlap structure that are related to measures that are singular continuous. We later introduce a notion of order to the $β$-expansions based on the lexicographical order of the $N$-binary words, and observe that for most sampled adjacent pairs when $β=2$, the distance in their order increases exponentially when $β$ decreases from 2 to 1. This suggests 'chaotic' behavior, with the 'Lyapunov exponents' bunched into several clusters that depend on $N$. We end the note with some 'order plots' and an interesting connection between the finite $β$-compactum with $β=g$ (g being the golden ratio) and binary reflected Gray code.

</details>
